rudhiraṃ gātrair vimastiṣkekṣaṇā yudhia dantapūrṇaiḥ sarudhirair vaktrair dāḍimasaṃnibhaiḥc jīvanta iva cāpy ete tasthuḥ śastropabṛṃhitāḥa parasparaṃ cāpy apare paṭṭiśair asibhis tathāc śaktibhir bhiṇḍipālaiś ca nakharaprāsatomaraiḥa tatakṣuś cicchiduś cānye bibhiduś cikṣipus tathāc saṃcakartuś ca jaghnuś ca kruddhā nirbibhiduś ca haa petur anyonyanihatā vyasavo rudhirokṣitāḥc kṣarantaḥ svarasaṃ raktaṃ prakṛtāś candanā ivaa rathai rathā vinihatā hastinaś cāpi hastibhiḥc narā naravaraiḥ petur aśvāś cāśvaiḥ sahasraśaḥa dhvajāḥ śirāṃsi cchatrāṇi dvipahastā nṛṇāṃ bhujāḥc kṣurair bhallārdhacandraiś ca chinnāḥ śastrāṇi tatyajuḥd vadhyatāṃ dāruṇaḥ śabdaḥ patatāṃ stanatām apid narāśvebharathānāṃ hi narāśvebharathais tadāa narāṃś ca nāgāṃś ca rathān hayān mamṛdur āhaveb tathā hatā rathāḥ petur aśvārohaiḥ sahasraśaḥc aśvārohair hatāḥ śūrāś chinnahastāś ca dantinaḥa sapatākā dhvajāḥ petur viśīrṇā iva parvatāḥc pattibhiś ca samāplutya dviradāḥ syandanās tathāa prahatā hanyamānāś ca patitāś caiva sarvaśaḥc aśvārohāḥ samāsādya tvaritāḥ pattibhir hatāḥe sādibhiḥ pattisaṃghāś ca nihatā yudhi śeratea mṛditānīva padmāni pramlānā iva ca srajaḥc hatānāṃ vadanāny āsan gātrāṇi ca mahāmatea rūpāṇy atyarthakāmyāni dviradāśvanṛṇāṃ nṛpac samunnānīva vastrāṇi prāpur durdarśatāṃ paramd tathaiva mukhavarṇaś ca keṣāṃ cit tatra dṛśyated madād iva prasuptānāṃ vikṣiptābharaṇasrajām saṃjaya uvācaa hastibhis tu mahāmātrās tava putreṇa coditāḥc dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ jighāṃsantaḥ kruddhāḥ pārṣatam abhyayuḥa prācyāś ca dākṣiṇātyāś ca pravīrā gajayodhinaḥc aṅgā vaṅgāś ca puṇḍrāś ca māgadhās tāmraliptakāḥa mekalāḥ kośalā madrā daśārṇā niṣadhās tathāc gajayuddheṣu kuśalāḥ kaliṅgaiḥ saha bhārataa śaratomaranārācair vṛṣṭimanta ivāmbudāḥc siṣicus te tataḥ sarve pāñcālācalam āhavea tān saṃmimardiṣur nāgān pārṣṇyaṅguṣṭhāṅkuśair bhṛśamc pothitān pārṣato bāṇair nārācaiś cābhyavīvṛṣata ekaikaṃ daśabhiḥ ṣaḍbhir aṣṭābhir api bhāratac dviradān abhivivyādha kṣiptair girinibhāñ śaraiḥe pracchādyamāno dviradair meghair iva divākaraḥa paryāsuḥ pāṇḍupāñcālā nadanto niśitāyudhāḥc tān nāgān abhivarṣanto jyātantrīśaranāditaiḥd vīranṛtyaṃ pranṛtyantaḥ śūratālapracoditaiḥa nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca draupadeyāḥ prabhadrakāḥc sātyakiś ca śikhaṇḍī ca cekitānaś ca vīryavānd samantāt siṣicur vīrā meghās toyair ivācalāna te mlecchaiḥ preṣitā nāgā narān aśvān rathān apic hastair ākṣipya mamṛduḥ padbhiś cāpy atimanyavaḥa bibhiduś ca viṣāṇāgraiḥ samākṣipya ca cikṣipuḥc viṣāṇalagnaiś cāpy anye paripetur vibhīṣaṇāḥa pramukhe vartamānaṃ tu dvipaṃ vaṅgasya sātyakiḥc nārācenogravegena bhittvā marmaṇy apātayata tasyāvarjitanāgasya dviradād utpatiṣyataḥc nārācenābhinad vakṣaḥ so patad bhuvi sātyakeḥa puṇḍrasyāpatato nāgaṃ calantam iva parvatamc sahadevaḥ prayatnāt tair nārācair vyahanat tribhiḥa vipatākaṃ viyantāraṃ vivarmadhvajajīvitamc taṃ kṛtvā dviradaṃ bhūyaḥ sahadevo ṅgam abhyagāta sahadevaṃ tu nakulo vārayitvāṅgam ārdayatc nārācair yamadaṇḍābhais tribhir nāgaṃ śatena caa divākarakaraprakhyān aṅgaś cikṣepa tomarānc nakulāya śatāny aṣṭau tridhaikaikaṃ tu so cchinata tathārdhacandreṇa śiras tasya ciccheda pāṇḍavaḥc sa papāta hato mlecchas tenaiva saha dantināa ācāryaputre nihate hastiśikṣāviśāradec aṅgāḥ kruddhā mahāmātrā nāgair nakulam abhyayuḥa calatpatākaiḥ pramukhair hemakakṣyātanucchadaiḥc mimardiśantas tvaritāḥ pradīptair iva parvataiḥa mekalotkalakāliṅgā niṣādās tāmraliptakāḥc śaratomaravarṣāṇi vimuñcanto jighāṃsavaḥa taiś chādyamānaṃ nakulaṃ divākaram ivāmbudaiḥc pari petuḥ susaṃrabdhāḥ pāṇḍupāñcālasomakāḥa tatas tad abhavad yuddhaṃ rathināṃ hastibhiḥ sahac sṛjatāṃ śaravarṣāṇi tomarāṃś ca sahasraśaḥa nāgānāṃ prasphuṭuḥ kumbhā marmāṇi vividhāni cac dantāś caivātividdhānāṃ nārācair bhūṣaṇāni caa teṣām aṣṭau mahānāgāṃś catuḥṣaṣṭyā sutejanaiḥc sahadevo jaghānāśu te petuḥ saha sādibhiḥa añjogatibhir āyamya prayatnād dhanur uttamamc nārācair ahanan nāgān nakulaḥ kuranandanaa tataḥ śaineyapāñcālyau draupadeyāḥ prabhadrakāḥc śikhaṇḍī ca mahānāgān siṣicuḥ śaravṛṣṭibhiḥa te pāṇḍuyodhāmbudharaiḥ śatrudviradaparvatāḥc bāṇavarṣair hatāḥ petur vajravarṣair ivācalāḥa evaṃ hatvā tava gajāṃs te pāṇḍunarakuñjarāḥc drutaṃ senām avaikṣanta bhinnakūlām ivāpagāma te tāṃ senām avālokya pāṇḍuputrasya sainikāḥc vikṣobhayitvā ca punaḥ karṇam evābhidudruvuḥa sahadevaṃ tataḥ kruddhaṃ dahantaṃ tava vāhinīmc duḥśāsano mahārāja bhrātā bhrātaram abhyayāta tau sametau mahāyuddhe dṛṣṭvā tatra narādhipāḥc siṃhanādaravāṃś cakrur vāsāṃsy ādudhuvuś ca haa tato bhārata kruddhena tava putreṇa dhanvināc pāṇḍuputras tribhir bāṇair vakṣasy abhihato balīa sahadevas tato rājan nārācena tavātmajamc viddhvā vivyādha saptatyā sārathiṃ ca tribhis tribhiḥa duḥśāsanas tadā rājaṃś chittvā cāpaṃ mahāhavec sahadevaṃ trisaptatyā bāhvor urasi cārdayata sahadevas tataḥ kruddhaḥ khaḍgaṃ gṛhya mahāhavec vyāvidhyata yudhāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ śrīmāṃs tava sutaṃ pratia samārgaṇagaṇaṃ cāpaṃ chittvā tasya mahān asiḥc nipapāta tato bhūmau cyutaḥ sarpa ivāmbarāta athānyad dhanur ādāya sahadevaḥ pratāpavānc duḥśāsanāya cikṣepa bāṇam antakaraṃ tataḥa tam āpatantaṃ viśikhaṃ yamadaṇḍopamatviṣamc khaḍgena śitadhāreṇa dvidhā ciccheda kauravaḥd tatas taṃ niśitaṃ khaḍgam āvidhya yudhi satvaraḥd dhanuś cānyat samādāya śaraṃ jagrāha vīryavāna tam āpatantaṃ sahasā nistriṃśaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc pātayām āsa samare sahadevo hasann ivaa tato bāṇāṃś catuḥṣaṣṭiṃ tava putro mahāraṇec sahadevarathe tūrṇaṃ pātayām āsa bhārataa tāñ śarān samare rājan vegenāpatato bahūnc ekaikaṃ pañcabhir bāṇaiḥ sahadevo nyakṛntataa sa nivārya mahābāṇāṃs tava putreṇa preṣitānc athāsmai subahūn bāṇān mādrīputraḥ samācinotc   preṣayām āsa saṃyugec tān bāṇāṃs tava putro pi chittvaikaikaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥc nanāda sumahānādaṃ dārayāṇo vasuṃdharāmc tato duḥśāsano rājan viddhvā pāṇḍusutaṃ raṇec sārathiṃ navabhir bāṇaira tataḥ kruddho mahārāja sahadevaḥ pratāpavānc samādhatta śaraṃ ghoraṃ mṛtyukālāntakopamame vikṛṣya balavac cāpaṃ tava putrāya so sṛjata sa taṃ nirbhidya vegena bhittvā ca kavacaṃ mahatc prāviśad dharaṇīṃ rājan valmīkam iva pannagaḥe tataḥ sa mumuhe rājaṃs tava putro mahārathaḥa mūḍhaṃ cainaṃ samālakṣya sārathis tvarito rathamc apovāha bhṛśaṃ trasto vadhyamānaṃ śitaiḥ śaraiḥd nādas tu sumahān āsīn nādayan vai vasuṃdharāma parājitya raṇe taṃ tu pāṇḍavaḥ pāṇḍupūrvajac duryodhanabalaṃ hṛṣṭaḥ prāmathad vai samantataḥa pipīlikāpuṭaṃ rājan yathāmṛdnān naro ruṣāc tathā sā kauravī senā mṛditā tena bhārataa nakulaṃ rabhasaṃ yuddhe dārayantaṃ varūthinīmc karṇo vaikartano rājan vārayām āsa vai tadāa nakulaś ca tadā karṇaṃ prahasann idam abravītc cirasya bata dṛṣṭo haṃ daivataiḥ saumyacakṣuṣāa yasya me tvaṃ raṇe pāpa cakṣurviṣayam āgataḥc tvaṃ hi mūlam anarthānāṃ vairasya kalahasya caa tvaddoṣāt kuravaḥ kṣīṇāḥ samāsādya parasparamc tvām adya samare hatvā kṛtakṛtyo smi vijvaraḥa evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca nakulaṃ sūtanandanaḥc sadṛśaṃ rājaputrasya dhanvinaś ca viśeṣataḥa praharasva raṇe bāla paśyāmas tava pauruṣamc karma kṛtvā raṇe śūra tataḥ katthitum arhasia anuktvā samare tāta śūrā yudhyanti śaktitaḥc sa yudhyasva mayā śaktyā vineṣye darpam adya tea ity uktvā prāharat tūrṇaṃ pāṇḍuputrāya sūtajaḥc vivyādha cainaṃ samare trisaptatyā śilīmukhaiḥa nakulas tu tato viddhaḥ sūtaputreṇa bhāratac aśītyāśīviṣaprakhyaiḥ sūtaputram avidhyataa tasya karṇo dhanuś chittvā svarṇapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaiḥc triṃśatā parameṣvāsaḥ śaraiḥ pāṇḍavam ārdayata te tasya kavacaṃ bhittvā papuḥ śoṇitam āhavec āśīviṣā yathā nāgā bhittvā gāṃ salilaṃ papuḥa athānyad dhanur ādāya hemapṛṣṭhaṃ durāsadamc karṇaṃ vivyādha viṃśatyā sārathiṃ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥa tataḥ kruddho mahārāja nakulaḥ paravīrahāc kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena karṇasya dhanur acchinata athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ sāyakānāṃ śatais tribhiḥc ājaghne prahasan vīraḥ sarvalokamahārathama karṇam abhyarditaṃ dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍuputreṇa māriṣac vismayaṃ paramaṃ jagmū rathinaḥ saha daivataiḥa athānyad dhanur ādāya karṇo vaikartanas tadāc nakulaṃ pañcabhir bāṇair jatrudeśe samārdayata uraḥsthair atha tair bāṇair mādrīputro vyarocatac svaraśmibhir ivādityo bhuvane visṛjan prabhāma nakulas tu tataḥ karṇaṃ viddhvā saptabhir āyasaiḥc athāsya dhanuṣaḥ koṭiṃ punaś ciccheda māriṣaa so nyat kārmukam ādāya samare vegavattaramc nakulasya tato bāṇaiḥ sarvato vārayad diśaḥa saṃchādyamānaḥ sahasā karṇacāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥc ciccheda sa śarāṃs tūrṇaṃ śarair eva mahārathaḥa tato bāṇamayaṃ jālaṃ vitataṃ vyomny adṛśyatac khadyotānāṃ gaṇair eva saṃpatadbhir yathā nabhaḥa tair vimuktaiḥ śaraśataiś chāditaṃ gaganaṃ tadāc śalabhānāṃ yathā vrātais tadvad āsīt samākulama te śarā hemavikṛtāḥ saṃpatanto muhur muhuḥc śreṇīkṛtā abhāsanta haṃsāḥ śreṇīgatā ivaa bāṇajālāvṛte vyomni chādite ca divākarec samasarpat tato bhūtaṃ kiṃ cid eva viśāṃ patea niruddhe tatra mārge tu śarasaṃghaiḥ samantataḥc vyarocatāṃ mahābhāgau bālasūryāv ivoditaua karṇacāpacyutair bāṇair vadhyamānās tu somakāḥc avālīyanta rājendra vedanārtāḥ śarārditāḥa nakulasya tathā bāṇair vadhyamānā camūs tavac vyaśīryata diśo rājan vātanunnā ivāmbudāḥa te sene vadhyamāne tu tābhyāṃ divyair mahāśaraiḥc śarapātam apakramya tataḥ prekṣakavat sthitea protsārite jane tasmin karṇapāṇḍavayoḥ śaraiḥc vivyādhāte mahātmānāv anyonyaṃ śaravṛṣṭibhiḥa nidarśayantau tv astrāṇi divyāni raṇamūrdhanic chādayantau ca sahasā parasparavadhaiṣiṇaua nakulena śarā muktāḥ kaṅkabarhiṇavāsasaḥc te tu karṇam avacchādya vyatiṣṭhanta yathā pared tathaiva sūtaputreṇa preṣitāḥ paramāhaved pāṇḍuputram avacchādya vyatiṣṭhantāmbare śarāḥa śaraveśmapraviṣṭau tau dadṛśāte na kaiś canac candrasūryau yathā rājaṃś chādyamānau jalāgamea tataḥ kruddho raṇe karṇaḥ kṛtvā ghorataraṃ vapuḥc pāṇḍavaṃ chādayām āsa samantāc charavṛṣṭibhiḥa sa cchādyamānaḥ samare sūtaputreṇa pāṇḍavaḥc na cakāra vyathāṃ rājan bhāskaro jaladair yathāa tataḥ prahasyādhirathiḥ śarajālāni māriṣac preṣayām āsa samare śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa ekacchāyam abhūt sarvaṃ tasya bāṇair mahātmanaḥc abhracchāyeva saṃjajñe saṃpatadbhiḥ śarottamaiḥa tataḥ karṇo mahārāja dhanuś chittvā mahātmanaḥc sārathiṃ pātayām āsa rathanīḍād dhasann ivaa tathāśvāṃś caturaś cāsya caturbhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc yamasya sadanaṃ tūrṇaṃ preṣayām āsa bhārataa athāsya taṃ rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ tilaśo vyadhamac charaiḥc patākāṃ cakrarakṣau ca dhvajaṃ khaḍgaṃ ca māriṣae śatacandraṃ tataś carma sarvopakaraṇāni caf suvarṇavikṛtaṃ tac ca dhanuḥ saśaram āhavea hatāśvo virathaś caiva vivarmā ca viśāṃ patec avatīrya rathāt tūrṇaṃ parighaṃ gṛhya viṣṭhitaḥa tam udyataṃ mahāghoraṃ parighaṃ tasya sūtajaḥc vyahanat sāyakai rājañ śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa vyāyudhaṃ cainam ālakṣya śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc ārdayad bahuśaḥ karṇo na cainaṃ samapīḍayata sa vadhyamānaḥ samare kṛtāstreṇa balīyasāc prādravat sahasā rājan nakulo vyākulendriyaḥa tam abhidrutya rādheyaḥ prahasan vai punaḥ punaḥc sajyam asya dhanuḥ kaṇṭhe so vāsṛjata bhārataa tataḥ sa śuśubhe rājan kaṇṭhāsaktamahādhanuḥc pariveṣam anuprāpto yathā syād vyomni candramāḥe yathaiva ca sito meghaḥ śakracāpena śobhitaḥf aśobhata mahārāja pāṇḍuputras tathā raṇea tam abravīt tadā karṇo vyarthaṃ vyāhṛtavān asic vadedānīṃ punar hṛṣṭo vadhyaṃ māṃ tvaṃ punaḥ punaḥa mā yotsīr gurubhiḥ sārdhaṃ balavadbhiś ca pāṇḍavac sadṛśais tāta yudhyasva vrīḍāṃ mā kuru pāṇḍavae gṛhaṃ vā gaccha mādreya yatra vā kṛṣṇaphalgunaua evam uktvā mahārāja vyasarjayata taṃ tataḥc vadhaprāptaṃ tu taṃ rājan nāvadhīt sūtanandanaḥe smṛtvā kuntyā vaco rājaṃs tata enaṃ vyasarjayata visṛṣṭaḥ pāṇḍavo rājan sūtaputreṇa dhanvināc vrīḍann iva jagāmātha yudhiṣṭhirarathaṃ pratia āruroha rathaṃ cāpi sūtaputrapratāpitaḥc niḥśvasan duḥkhasaṃtaptaḥ kumbhe kṣipta ivoragaḥa taṃ visṛjya raṇe karṇaḥ pāñcālāṃs tvarito yayauc rathenātipatākena candravarṇahayena caa tatrākrando mahān āsīt pāṇḍavānāṃ viśāṃ patec dṛṣṭvā senāpatiṃ yāntaṃ pāñcālānāṃ rathavrajāna tatrākaron mahārāja kadanaṃ sūtanandanaḥc madhyaṃ gate dinakare cakravat pracaran prabhuḥa bhagnacakrai rathaiḥ ke cic chinnadhvajapatākibhiḥc sasūtair hatasūtaiś ca bhagnākṣaiś caiva māriṣae hriyamāṇān apaśyāma pāñcālānāṃ rathavrajāna tatra tatra ca saṃbhrāntā vicerur mattakuñjarāḥc davāgninā parītāṅgā yathaiva syur mahāvanea bhinnakumbhā virudhirāś chinnahastāś ca vāraṇāḥc bhinnagātravarāś caiva cchinnavālāś ca māriṣae chinnābhrāṇīva saṃpetur vadhyamānā mahātmanāa apare trāsitā nāgā nārācaśatatomaraiḥc tam evābhimukhā yānti śalabhā iva pāvakama apare niṣṭanantaḥ sma vyadṛśyanta mahādvipāḥc kṣarantaḥ śoṇitaṃ gātrair nagā iva jalaplavama uraśchadair vimuktāś ca vālabandhaiś ca vājinaḥc rājataiś ca tathā kāṃsyaiḥ sauvarṇaiś caiva bhūṣaṇaiḥa hīnā āstaraṇaiś caiva khalīnaiś ca vivarjitāḥc cāmaraiś ca kuthābhiś ca tūṇīraiḥ patitair apia nihataiḥ sādibhiś caiva śūrair āhavaśobhibhiḥb vātāyamānān sahasā prapaśyāma hayottamānc apaśyāma raṇe tatra bhrāmyamāṇān hayottamāna prāsaiḥ khaḍgaiś ca saṃsyūtān ṛṣṭibhiś ca narādhipac hayayodhān apaśyāma kañcukoṣṇīṣadhāriṇaḥd nihatān vadhyamānāṃś ca vepamānāṃś ca bhāratad nānāṅgāvayavair hīnāṃs tatra tatraiva bhāratad vihayān sahayāṃś cāpi veṣṭamānāṃs tatas tataḥa rathān hemapariṣkārān suyuktāñ javanair hayaiḥc bhramamāṇān apaśyāma hateṣu rathiṣu drutama bhagnākṣakūbarān kāṃś cic chinnacakrāṃś ca māriṣac vipatākādhvajāṃś cānyāñ chinneṣāyugabandhurāna vihīnān rathinas tatra dhāvamānān samantataḥb rathāṃs tu tatra vicchinnāṃs tilaśaḥ karṇavikramaiḥc sūryaputraśarais trastān apaśyāma viśāṃ patea viśastrāṃś ca tathaivānyān saśastrāṃś ca bahūn hatānc tāvakāñ jālasaṃchannān uroghaṇṭāvibhūṣitāna nānāvarṇavicitrābhiḥ patākābhir alaṃkṛtānc padātīn anvapaśyāma dhāvamānān samantataḥa śirāṃsi bāhūn ūrūṃś ca chinnān anyāṃs tathā yudhib chinnāñ śarais tathā bāhūn ūrūś cāpāñ janādhipab śirobhir bāhubhiś chinnaiś citrair ūrubhir eva cac karṇacāpacyutair bāṇair apaśyāma vinākṛtāna mahān vyatikaro raudro yodhānām anvadṛśyatac karṇasāyakanunnānāṃ hatānāṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa te vadhyamānāḥ samare sūtaputreṇa sṛñjayāḥc tam evābhimukhā yānti pataṃgā iva pāvakama taṃ dahantam anīkāni tatra tatra mahārathamc kṣatriyā varjayām āsur yugāntāgnim ivolbaṇama hataśeṣās tu ye vīrāḥ pāñcālānāṃ mahārathāḥc tān prabhagnān drutān karṇaḥ pṛṣṭhato vikirañ śaraiḥe abhyadhāvata tejasvī viśīrṇakavacadhvajāna tāpayām āsa tān bāṇaiḥ sūtaputro mahārathaḥc madhyaṃdinam anuprāpto bhūtānīva tamonudaḥ saṃjaya uvācaa yuyutsuṃ tava putraṃ tu prādravantaṃ mahad balamc ulūko bhyapatat tūrṇaṃ tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīta yuyutsus tu tato rājañ śitadhāreṇa patriṇāc ulūkaṃ tāḍayām āsa vajreṇendra ivācalama ulūkas tu tataḥ kruddhas tava putrasya saṃyugec kṣurapreṇa dhanuś chittvā tāḍayām āsa karṇināa tad apāsya dhanuś chinnaṃ yuyutsur vegavattaramc anyad ādatta sumahac cāpaṃ saṃraktalocanaḥa śākuniṃ ca tataḥ ṣaṣṭyā vivyādha bharatarṣabhac sārathiṃ tribhir ānarchat taṃ ca bhūyo vyavidhyataa ulūkas taṃ tu viṃśatyā viddhvā hemavibhūṣitaiḥc athāsya samare kruddho dhvajaṃ ciccheda kāñcanama sa cchinnayaṣṭiḥ sumahāñ śīryamāṇo mahādhvajaḥc papāta pramukhe rājan yuyutsoḥ kāñcanojjvalaḥa dhvajam unmathitaṃ dṛṣṭvā yuyutsuḥ krodhamūrchitaḥc ulūkaṃ pañcabhir bāṇair ājaghāna stanāntarea ulūkas tasya bhallena tailadhautena māriṣac śiraś ciccheda sahasā yantur bharatasattamad tac chinnam apatad bhūmau yuyutsoḥ sārathes tadād tārārūpaṃ yathā citraṃ nipapāta mahītaled yantuś ciccheda samare śiraḥ krodhasamanvitaḥa jaghāna caturo śvāṃś ca taṃ ca vivyādha pañcabhiḥc so tividdho balavatā pratyapāyād rathāntarama taṃ nirjitya raṇe rājann ulūkas tvarito yayauc pāñcālān sṛñjayāṃś caiva vinighnan niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa śatānīkaṃ mahārāja śrutakarmā sutas tavac vyaśvasūtarathaṃ cakre nimeṣārdhād asaṃbhramama hatāśve tu rathe tiṣṭhañ śatānīko mahābalaḥc gadāṃ cikṣepa saṃkruddhas tava putrasya māriṣaa sā kṛtvā syandanaṃ bhasma hayāṃś caiva sasārathīnc papāta dharaṇīṃ tūrṇaṃ dārayantīva bhārataa tāv ubhau virathau vīrau kurūṇāṃ kīrtivardhanauc apākrametāṃ yuddhārtau prekṣamāṇau parasparama putras tu tava saṃbhrānto vivitso ratham āviśatc śatānīko pi tvaritaḥ prativindhyarathaṃ gataḥa sutasomas tu śakuniṃ vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc nākampayata saṃrabdho vāryogha iva parvatama sutasomas tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā pitur atyantavairiṇamc śarair anekasāhasraiś chādayām āsa bhārataa tāñ śarāñ śakunis tūrṇaṃ cicchedānyaiḥ patatribhiḥc laghvastraś citrayodhī ca jitakāśī ca saṃyugea nivārya samare cāpi śarāṃs tān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc ājaghāna susaṃkruddhaḥ sutasomaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥa tasyāśvān ketanaṃ sūtaṃ tilaśo vyadhamac charaiḥc syālas tava mahāvīryas tatas te cukruśur janāḥa hatāśvo virathaś caiva chinnadhanvā ca māriṣac dhanvī dhanurvaraṃ gṛhya rathād bhūmāv atiṣṭhatae vyasṛjat sāyakāṃś caiva svarṇapuṅkhāñ śilāśitāna chādayām āsur atha te tava syālasya taṃ rathamc pataṃgānām iva vrātāḥ śaravrātā mahārathama rathopasthān samīkṣyāpi vivyathe naiva saubalaḥc pramṛdnaṃś ca śarāṃs tāṃs tāñ śaravrātair mahāyaśāḥa tatrātuṣyanta yodhāś ca siddhāś cāpi divi sthitāḥc sutasomasya tat karma dṛṣṭvāśraddheyam adbhutame rathasthaṃ nṛpatiṃ taṃ tu padātiḥ sann ayodhayata tasya tīkṣṇair mahāvegair bhallaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc vyahanat kārmukaṃ rājā tūṇīraṃ caiva sarvaśaḥa sa cchinnadhanvā samare khaḍgam udyamya nānadanc vaiḍūryotpalavarṇābhaṃ hastidantamayatsaruma bhrāmyamāṇaṃ tatas taṃ tu vimalāmbbaravarcasamc kālopamaṃ tato mene sutasomasya dhīmataḥa so carat sahasā khaḍgī maṇḍalāni sahasraśaḥc caturviṃśan mahārāja śikṣābalasamanvitaḥd bhrāntam udbhrāntam āviddham āplutaṃ viplutaṃ sṛtamd saṃpātaṃ samudīryaṃ ca darśayām āsa saṃyugea saubalas tu tatas tasya śarāṃś cikṣepa vīryavānc tān āpatata evāśu ciccheda paramāsināa tataḥ kruddho mahārāja saubalaḥ paravīrahāc prāhiṇot sutasomasya śarān āśīviṣopamāna ciccheda tāṃś ca khaḍgena śikṣayā ca balena cac darśayaṃl lāghavaṃ yuddhe tārkṣyavīryasamadyutiḥa tasya saṃcarato rājan maṇḍalāvartane tadāc kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena khaḍgaṃ ciccheda suprabhama sa cchinnaḥ sahasā bhūmau nipapāta mahān asiḥc avaśasya sthitaṃ haste taṃ khaḍgaṃ satsaruṃ tadāa chinnam ājñāya nistriṃśam avaplutya padāni ṣaṭb so nyat kārmukam ādāya sudṛḍhaṃ vegavattaramc prāvidhyata tataḥ śeṣaṃ sutasomo mahārathaḥa sa cchittvā saguṇaṃ cāpaṃ raṇe tasya mahātmanaḥc papāta dharaṇīṃ tūrṇaṃ svarṇavajravibhūṣitaḥe sutasomas tato gacchac chrutakīrter mahārathama saubalo pi dhanur gṛhya ghoram anyat suduḥsahamc abhyayāt pāṇḍavānīkaṃ nighnañ śatrugaṇān bahūna tatra nādo mahān āsīt pāṇḍavānāṃ viśāṃ patec saubalaṃ samare dṛṣṭvā vicarantam abhītavata tāny anīkāni dṛptāni śastravanti mahānti cac drāvyamāṇāny adṛśyanta saubalena mahātmanāa yathā daityacamūṃ rājan devarājo mamarda hac tathaiva pāṇḍavīṃ senāṃ saubaleyo vyanāśayata dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ kṛpo rājan vārayām āsa saṃyugec yathā dṛptaṃ vane nāgaṃ śarabho vārayed yudhia niruddhaḥ pārṣatas tena gautamena balīyasāc padāt padaṃ vicalituṃ nāśaknot tatra bhārataa gautamasya vapur dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭadyumnarathaṃ pratic vitresuḥ sarvabhūtāni kṣayaṃ prāptaṃ ca menirea tatrāvocan vimanaso rathinaḥ sādinas tathāc droṇasya nidhane nūnaṃ saṃkruddho dvipadāṃ varaḥa śāradvato mahātejā divyāstravid udāradhīḥc api svasti bhaved adya dhṛṣṭadyumnasya gautamāta apīyaṃ vāhinī kṛtsnā mucyeta mahato bhayātc apy ayaṃ brāhmaṇaḥ sarvān na no hanyāt samāgatāna yādṛśaṃ dṛśyate rūpam antakapratimaṃ bhṛśamc gamiṣyaty adya padavīṃ bhāradvājasya saṃyugea ācāryaḥ kṣiprahastaś ca vijayī ca sadā yudhic astravān vīryasaṃpannaḥ krodhena ca samanvitaḥa pārṣataś ca bhṛśaṃ yuddhe vimukho dyāpi lakṣyatec ity evaṃ vividhā vācas tāvakānāṃ paraiḥ sahad vyaśrūyanta mahārāja tayos tatra samāgamed vicerus tatra samare gautamād bhayaśaṃsakāḥa viniḥśvasya tataḥ kruddhaḥ kṛpaḥ śāradvato nṛpac pārṣataṃ chādayām āsa niśceṣṭaṃ sarvamarmasua sa vadhyamānaḥ samare gautamena mahātmanāc kartavyaṃ na prajānāti mohitaḥ paramāhavea tam abravīt tato yantā kaccit kṣemaṃ nu pārṣatac īdṛśaṃ vyasanaṃ yuddhe na te dṛṣṭaṃ kadā canaa daivayogāt tu te bāṇā nātaran marmabhedinaḥc preṣitā dvijamukhyena marmāṇy uddiśya sarvaśaḥa vyāvartaye tatra rathaṃ nadīvegam ivārṇavātc avadhyaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ manye yena te vikramo hataḥa dhṛṣṭadyumnas tato rājañ śanakair abravīd vacaḥc muhyate me manas tāta gātre svedaś ca jāyatea vepathuṃ ca śarīre me romaharṣaṃ ca paśya vaic varjayan brāhmaṇaṃ yuddhe śanair yāhi yato cyutaḥa arjunaṃ bhīmasenaṃ vā samare prāpya sārathec kṣemam adya bhaved yantar iti me naiṣṭhikī matiḥa tataḥ prāyān mahārāja sārathis tvarayan hayānc yato bhīmo maheṣvāso yuyudhe tava sainikaiḥa pradrutaṃ tu rathaṃ dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭadyumnasya māriṣac kirañ śaraśatāny eva gautamo nuyayau tadāa śaṅkhaṃ ca pūrayām āsa muhur muhur ariṃdamaḥc pārṣataṃ prādravad yantaṃ mahendra iva śambarama śikhaṇḍinaṃ tu samare bhīṣmamṛtyuṃ durāsadamc hārdikyo vārayām āsa smayann iva muhur muhuḥa śikhaṇḍī ca samāsādya hṛdikānāṃ mahārathamc pañcabhir niśitair bhallair jatrudeśe samārdayata kṛtavarmā tu saṃkruddho bhittvā ṣaṣṭibhir āśugaiḥc dhanur ekena ciccheda hasan rājan mahārathaḥa athānyad dhanur ādāya drupadasyātmajo balīc tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti saṃkruddho hārdikyaṃ pratyabhāṣataa tato sya navatiṃ bāṇān rukmapuṅkhān sutejanānc preṣayām āsa rājendra te syābhraśyanta varmaṇaḥa vitathāṃs tān samālakṣya patitāṃś ca mahītalec kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena kārmukaṃ cicchide balīa athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ bhagnaśṛṅgam ivarṣabhamc aśītyā mārgaṇaiḥ kruddho bāhvor urasi cārdayata kṛtavarmā tu saṃkruddho mārgaṇaiḥ kṛtavikṣataḥb vavāma rudhiraṃ gātraiḥ kumbhavaktrād ivodakamb rudhireṇa pariklinnaḥ kṛtavarmā tv arājatab varṣeṇa kledito rājan yathā gairikaparvataḥc dhanur anyat samādāya samārgaṇagaṇaṃ prabhoe śikhaṇḍinaṃ bāṇavaraiḥ skandhadeśe bhyatāḍayata skandhadeśe sthitair bāṇaiḥ śikhaṇḍī ca rarāja hac śākhāpratānair vimalaiḥ sumahān sa yathā drumaḥa tāv anyonyaṃ bhṛśaṃ viddhvā rudhireṇa samukṣitaub poplūyamānau hi yathā mahāntau śoṇitahradeb tadvad virejatur vīrau śoṇitena pariplutaub yathā ca kiṃśukau phullau puṣyamāse bhyupāgataub rudhirokṣitasarvāṅgau raktacandanarūṣitaub bhujagāv iva saṃkruddhau rejatus tau narottamaub tāv ubhau śaranunnāṅgau parasparaśarakṣatauc anyonyaśṛṅgābhihatau rejatur vṛṣabhāv ivaa anyonyasya vadhe yatnaṃ kurvāṇau tau mahārathauc rathābhyāṃ ceratus tatra maṇḍalāni sahasraśaḥa kṛtavarmā mahārāja pārṣataṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc raṇe vivyādha saptatyā svarṇapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaiḥa tato sya samare bāṇaṃ bhojaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥc jīvitāntakaraṃ ghoraṃ vyasṛjat tvarayānvitaḥa sa tenābhihato rājan mūrchām āśu samāviśatc dhvajayaṣṭiṃ ca sahasā śiśriye kaśmalāvṛtaḥa apovāha raṇāt taṃ tu sārathī rathināṃ varamc hārdikyaśarasaṃtaptaṃ niḥśvasantaṃ punaḥ punaḥa parājite tataḥ śūre drupadasya sute prabhoc prādravat pāṇḍavī senā vadhyamānā samantataḥ saṃjaya uvācaa śvetāśvo pi mahārāja vyadhamat tāvakaṃ balamc yathā vāyuḥ samāsādya tūlarāśiṃ samantataḥa pratyudyayus trigartās taṃ śibayaḥ kauravaiḥ sahac śālvāḥ saṃśaptakāś caiva nārāyaṇabalaṃ ca yata satyasenaḥ satyakīrtir mitradevaḥ śrutaṃjayaḥc sauśrutiś citrasenaś ca mitravarmā ca bhāratad suśarmā ca sudharmā ca suvarmā caiva bhārataa trigartarājaḥ samare bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥc putraiś caiva maheṣvāsair nānāśastradharair yudhia te sṛjantaḥ śaravrātān kiranto rjunam āhavec abhyadravanta samare vāryoghā iva sāgarama te tv arjunaṃ samāsādya yodhāḥ śatasahasraśaḥc agacchan vilayaṃ sarve tārkṣyaṃ dṛṣṭveva pannagāḥa te vadhyamānāḥ samare nājahuḥ pāṇḍavaṃ tadāc dahyamānā yathā rājañ śalabhā iva pāvakama satyasenas tribhir bāṇair vivyādha yudhi pāṇḍavamc mitradevas triṣaṣṭyā ca candradevaś ca saptabhiḥa mitravarmā trisaptatyā sauśrutiś cāpi pañcabhiḥc śatruṃjayaś ca viṃśatyā suśarmā navabhiḥ śaraiḥd sa viddho bahubhiḥ saṃkhye prativivyādha tān nṛpānd sauśrutiṃ saptabhir viddhvā satyasenaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥd sauśrutiṃ pañcaviṃśatyā candradevaṃ tathāṣṭabhiḥd śatruṃjayaṃ ca viṃśatyā candradevaṃ tathāṣṭabhiḥd mitradevaṃ śatenaiva śrutasenaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥd navabhir mitravarmāṇaṃ suśarmāṇaṃ tathāṣṭabhiḥd suvarmāṇaṃ śatenājau suśarmāṇaṃ ca paṃcabhiḥd bhūyaś caiva suśarmāṇaṃ suvarmāṇaṃ tathāṣṭabhiḥa śatruṃjayaṃ ca rājānaṃ hatvā tatra śilāśitaiḥc sauśruteḥ saśirastrāṇaṃ śiraḥ kāyād apāharate tvaritaś candradevaṃ ca śarair ninye yamakṣayama athetarān mahārāja yatamānān mahārathānc pañcabhiḥ pañcabhir bāṇair ekaikaṃ pratyavārayata satyasenas tu saṃkruddhas tomaraṃ vyasṛjan mahatc samuddiśya raṇe kṛṣṇaṃ siṃhanādaṃ nanāda caa sa nirbhidya bhujaṃ savyaṃ mādhavasya mahātmanaḥc ayasmayo mahācaṇḍo jagāma dharaṇīṃ tadāa mādhavasya tu viddhasya tomareṇa mahāraṇec pratodaḥ prāpatad dhastād raśmayaś ca viśāṃ pated vāsudevaṃ vibhinnāṅgaṃ dṛṣṭvā pārtho dhanaṃjayaḥd krodham āhārayat tīvraṃ kṛṣṇaṃ cedam uvāca had prāpayāśvān mahābāho satyasenaṃ prati prabhod yāvad enaṃ śarais tīkṣṇair nayāmi yamasādanamd tataḥ saṃcodayām āsa satyasenarathaṃ pratid atha divyāstravic chūro jātamanyur dhanaṃjayaḥa sa pratodaṃ punar gṛhya raśmīṃś caiva mahāyaśāḥc vāhayām āsa tān aśvān satyasenarathaṃ pratia viṣvaksenaṃ tu nirbhinnaṃ prekṣya pārtho dhanaṃjayaḥc satyasenaṃ śarais tīkṣṇair dārayitvā mahābalaḥa tataḥ suniśitair bāṇai rājñas tasya mahac chiraḥc kuṇḍalopacitaṃ kāyāc cakarta pṛtanāntarea taṃ nihatya śitair bāṇair mitravarmāṇam ākṣipatc vatsadantena tīkṣṇena sārathiṃ cāsya māriṣaa tataḥ śaraśatair bhūyaḥ saṃśaptakagaṇān vaśīc pātayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa tato rajatapuṅkhena rājñaḥ śīrṣaṃ mahātmanaḥc mitradevasya ciccheda kṣurapreṇa mahāyaśāḥe suśarmāṇaṃ ca saṃkruddho jatrudeśe samārdayatf nārācena sutīkṣṇena sumuktena mahāyaśāḥa tataḥ saṃśaptakāḥ sarve parivārya dhanaṃjayamc śastraughair mamṛduḥ kruddhā nādayanto diśo daśaa abhyarditas tu tair jiṣṇuḥ śakratulyaparākramaḥc aindram astram ameyātmā prāduścakre mahārathaḥe tataḥ śarasahasrāṇi prādurāsan viśāṃ patef kārmukāt pāṇḍuputrasya pārthasyāmitatejasaḥa dhvajānāṃ chidyamānānāṃ kārmukāṇāṃ ca saṃyugec rathānāṃ sapatākānāṃ tūṇīrāṇāṃ śaraiḥ sahaa akṣāṇām atha yoktrāṇāṃ cakrāṇāṃ raśmibhiḥ sahac kūbarāṇāṃ varūthānāṃ pṛṣatkānāṃ ca saṃyugea aśmanāṃ patatāṃ caiva prāsānām ṛṣṭibhiḥ sahac gadānāṃ parighāṇāṃ ca śaktīnāṃ tomaraiḥ sahaa śataghnīnāṃ sacakrāṇāṃ bhujānām ūrubhiḥ sahac kaṇṭhasūtrāṅgadānāṃ ca keyūrāṇāṃ ca māriṣaa hārāṇām atha niṣkāṇāṃ tanutrāṇāṃ ca bhāratac chatrāṇāṃ vyajanānāṃ ca śirasāṃ mukuṭaiḥ sahae aśrūyata mahāñ śabdas tatra tatra viśāṃ patea sakuṇḍalāni svakṣīṇi pūrṇacandranibhāni cac śirāṃsy urvyām adṛśyanta tārāgaṇa ivāmbarea susragvīṇi suvāsāṃsi candanenokṣitāni cac śarīrāṇi vyadṛśyanta hatānāṃ ca mahītalee gandharvanagarākāraṃ ghoram āyodhanaṃ tadāa nihatai rājaputraiś ca kṣatriyaiś ca mahābalaiḥb arjunena mahārāja tatra tatra mahāraṇec hastibhiḥ patitaiś caiva turagaiś cābhavan mahīe agamyamārgā samare viśīrṇair iva parvataiḥa nāsīc cakrapathaś caiva pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥc nighnataḥ śātravān bhallair hastyaśvaṃ cāmitaṃ mahata ā tumbād avasīdanti rathacakrāṇi māriṣab āsāditas tato rājan rathacakraṃ viśāṃ patec raṇe vicaratas tasya tasmiṃl lohitakardamea sīdamānāni cakrāṇi samūhus turagā bhṛśamc śrameṇa mahatā yuktā manomārutaraṃhasaḥa vadhyamānaṃ tu tat sainyaṃ pāṇḍuputreṇa dhanvināc prāyaśo vimukhaṃ sarvaṃ nāvatiṣṭhata saṃyugea tāñ jitvā samare jiṣṇuḥ saṃśaptakagaṇān bahūnc rarāja sa mahārāja vidhūmo gnir iva jvalana yudhiṣṭhiraṃ mahārāja visṛjantaṃ śarān bahūnc svayaṃ duryodhano rājā pratyagṛhṇād abhītavata tam āpatantaṃ sahasā tava putraṃ mahābalamc dharmarājo drutaṃ viddhvā tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīta sā ca taṃ prativivyādha navabhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc sārathiṃ cāsya bhallena bhṛśaṃ kruddho bhyatāḍayata tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā hemapuṅkhāñ śilīmukhāna   pratyagṛhṇād abhītavata tvarayā parayā yuktoc duryodhanāya cikṣepa trayodaśa śilāśitāna caturbhiś caturo vāhāṃs tasya hatvā mahārathaḥc pañcamena śiraḥ kāyāt sārathes tu samākṣipata ṣaṣṭhena ca dhvajaṃ rājñaḥ saptamena ca kārmukamc aṣṭamena tathā khaḍgaṃ pātayām āsa bhūtalee pañcabhir nṛpatiṃ cāpi dharmarājo rdayad bhṛśama hatāśvāt tu rathāt tasmād avaplutya sutas tavac uttamaṃ vyasanaṃ prāpto bhūmāv eva vyatiṣṭhataa taṃ tu kṛcchragataṃ dṛṣṭvā karṇadrauṇikṛpādayaḥc abhyavartanta sahitāḥ parīpsanto narādhipama atha pāṇḍusutāḥ sarve parivārya yudhiṣṭhiramc abhyayuḥ samare rājaṃs tato yuddham avartataa atha tūryasahasrāṇi prāvādyanta mahāmṛdhec kṣveḍāḥ kilakilāśabdāḥ prādurāsan mahīpatee yad abhyagacchan samare pāñcālāḥ kauravaiḥ sahaf te śūrāḥ samare sarve prākṣīyanta tatas tataḥa narā naraiḥ samājagmur vāraṇā varavāraṇaiḥc rathāś ca rathibhiḥ sārdhaṃ hayāś ca hayasādibhiḥa dvaṃdvāny āsan mahārāja prekṣaṇīyāni saṃyugeb tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca citrāṇi ca gurūṇi cac vismāpanāny acintyāni śastravanty uttamāni cad te śūrāḥ samare sarve citraṃ laghu ca suṣṭhu caa ayudhyanta mahāvegāḥ parasparavadhaiṣiṇaḥc anyonyaṃ samare jaghnur yodhavratam anuṣṭhitāḥe na hi te samaraṃ cakruḥ pṛṣṭhato vai kathaṃ canaa muhūrtam eva tad yuddham āsīn madhuradarśanamc tata unmattavad rājan nirmaryādam avartataa rathī nāgaṃ samāsādya vicaran raṇamūrdhanic preṣayām āsa kālāya śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥa nāgā hayān samāsādya vikṣipanto bahūn athac drāvayām āsur atyugrās tatra tatra tadā tadād hayārohāś ca bahavaḥ parivārya gajottamānd talaśabdaravāṃś cakruḥ saṃpatantas tatas tataḥd dhāvamānāṃs tatas tāṃs tu dravamāṇān mahāgajānd pārśvataḥ pṛṣṭhataś caiva nijaghnur hayasādinaḥa vidrāvya ca bahūn aśvān nāgā rājan balotkaṭāḥc viṣāṇaiś cāpare jaghnur mamṛduś cāpare bhṛśama sāśvārohāṃś ca turagān viṣāṇair bibhidū raṇec aparāṃś cikṣipur vegāt pragṛhyātibalās tathāa pādātair āhatā nāgā vivareṣu samantataḥc cakrur ārtasvaraṃ ghoraṃ vyadravanta diśo daśaa padātīnāṃ tu sahasā pradrutānāṃ mahāmṛdhec utsṛjyābharaṇaṃ tūrṇam avaplutya raṇājirea nimittaṃ manyamānās tu pariṇamya mahāgajāḥc jagṛhur bibhiduś caiva citrāṇy ābharaṇāni cad tāṃs tu tatra prasaktān vai parivārya padātayaḥd hastyārohān nijaghnus te mahāvegā balotkaṭāḥd apare hastibhir hastaiḥ khaṃ vikṣiptā mahāmṛdhed nipatanto viṣāṇāgrair bhṛśaṃ viddhāḥ suśikṣitaiḥd apare sahasā gṛhya viṣāṇair eva sūditāḥd senāntaraṃ samāsādya ke cit tatra mahāgajaiḥd kṣuṇṇagātrā mahārāja vikṣipya ca punaḥ punaḥd apare vyajanānīva vibhrāmya nihatā mṛdhed puraḥsarāś ca nāgānām apareṣāṃ viśāṃ pated śarīrāṇy atividdhāni tatra tatra raṇājirea pratimāneṣu kumbheṣu dantaveṣṭeṣu cāparec nigṛhītā bhṛśaṃ nāgāḥ prāsatomaraśaktibhiḥa nigṛhya ca gadāḥ ke cit pārśvasthair bhṛśadāruṇaiḥb nāgāś ca śataśo rājan nirbhinnā bhūmim āviśanc rathāśvasādibhis tatra saṃbhinnā nyapatan bhuvia sarathaṃ sādinaṃ tatra apare tu mahāgajāḥc bhūmāv amṛdnan vegena savarmāṇaṃ patākinamd tathā sāvaraṇān kāṃś cit tatra tatra viśāṃ patea rathaṃ nāgāḥ samāsādya dhuri gṛhya ca māriṣac vyākṣipan sahasā tatra ghorarūpe mahāmṛdhea nārācair nihataś cāpi nipapāta mahāgajaḥc parvatasyeva śikharaṃ vajrabhagnaṃ mahītalea yodhā yodhān samāsādya muṣṭibhir vyahanan yudhic keśeṣv anyonyam ākṣipya cicchidur bibhiduḥ sahaa udyamya ca bhujāv anyo nikṣipya ca mahītalec padā coraḥ samākramya sphurato vyahanac chiraḥa mṛtam anyo mahārāja padbhyāṃ tāḍitavāṃs tadāb patataś cāparo rājan vijahārāsinā śiraḥc jīvataś ca tathaivānyaḥ śastraṃ kāye nyamajjayata muṣṭiyuddhaṃ mahac cāsīd yodhānāṃ tatra bhāratac tathā keśagrahaś cogro bāhuyuddhaṃ ca kevalama samāsaktasya cānyena avijñātas tathāparaḥc jahāra samare prāṇān nānāśastrair anekadhāa saṃsakteṣu ca yodheṣu vartamāne ca saṃkulec kabandhāny utthitāni sma śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa lohitaiḥ sicyamānāni śastrāṇi kavacāni cac mahāraṅgānuraktāni vastrāṇīva cakāśirea mahārāja parāṃś caiva samāgatānc ubhayoḥ senayor vīrair vyākulaṃ samapadyataa rathair bhagnair mahārāja vāraṇaiś ca nipātitaiḥc hayaiś ca patitais tatra naraiś ca vinipātitaiḥa agamyarūpā pṛthivī prāyujyanta nareśvarāḥa tataḥ kṛte vahāre ca prahṛṣṭāḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥc niśāyāṃ śibiraṃ gatvā nyaviśanta nareśvarāḥd raṇe pravṛttāny ahani kathayantaḥ sukhaṃ tathāa yakṣarakṣaḥpiśācāś ca śvāpadāni ca bhadrām ekaś cāgnim atarpayatc ekaś cemāṃ mahīṃ jitvā cakre balibhṛto nṛpāna eko nivātakavacān avadhīd divyakārmukaḥb nivātakavacānāṃ ca tisraḥ koṭīr jaghāna hac ekaḥ kirātarūpeṇa sthitaṃ śarvam ayodhayata eko bhyarakṣad bharatān eko bhavam atoṣayatc tenaikena jitāḥ sarve madīyā ugratejasaḥe te na nindyāḥ praśasyāś ca yat te cakrur bravīhi tatf tato duryodhanaḥ sūta paścāt kim akarot tadā saṃjaya uvācaa hataprahatavidhvastā vivarmāyudhavāhanāḥc dīnasvarā dūyamānā māninaḥ śatrubhir jitāḥa śibirasthāḥ punar mantraṃ mantrayanti sma kauravāḥc bhagnadaṃṣṭrā hataviṣāḥ padākrāntā ivoragāḥa tān abravīt tataḥ karṇaḥ kruddhaḥ sarpa iva śvasanc karaṃ kareṇābhipīḍya prekṣamāṇas tavātmajama yatto dṛḍhaś ca dakṣaś ca dhṛtimān arjunaḥ sadāc sa bodhayati cāpy enaṃ prāptakālam adhokṣajaḥa sahasāstravisargeṇa vayaṃ tenādya vañcitāḥc śvas tv ahaṃ tasya saṃkalpaṃ sarvaṃ hantā mahīpatea evam uktas tathety uktvā so nujajñe nṛpottamānb te nujñātā nṛpāḥ sarve svāni veśmāni bhejirec sukhoṣitās te rajanīṃ hṛṣṭā yuddhāya niryayuḥa te paśyan vihitaṃ vyūhaṃ dharmarājena durjayamc prayatnāt kurumukhyena bṛhaspatyuśanomatāta atha pratīpakartāraṃ satataṃ vijitātmanāmc sasmāra vṛṣabhaskandhaṃ karṇaṃ duryodhanas tadāa puraṃdarasamaṃ yuddhe marudgaṇasamaṃ balec kārtavīryasamaṃ vīrye karṇaṃ rājño gaman manaḥd sarveṣāṃ caiva sainyānāṃ karṇam evāgaman manaḥe sūtaputraṃ maheṣvāsaṃ bandhum ātyayikeṣv iva dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa yad vo gaman mano mandāḥ karṇaṃ vaikartanaṃ tadāc apy adrākṣata taṃ yūyaṃ śītārtā iva bhāskarama kṛte vahāre sainyānāṃ pravṛtte ca raṇe punaḥc kathaṃ vaikartanaḥ karṇas tatrāyudhyata saṃjayae kathaṃ ca pāṇḍavāḥ sarve yuyudhus tatra sūtajama karṇo hy eko mahābāhur hanyāt pārthān sasomakānc karṇasya bhujayor vīryaṃ śakraviṣṇusamaṃ matame tathāstrāṇi sughorāṇi vikramaś ca mahātmanaḥf mama caiva sadā mandaḥ śaṃsate nityam agrataḥf karṇaś ca tān maheṣvāsān pāṇḍuputrān mahārathāna duryodhanaṃ tadā dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavena bhṛśārditamc parākrāntān pāṇḍusutān dṛṣṭvā cāpi mahāhavea karṇam āśritya saṃgrāme darpo duryodhane punaḥc jetum utsahate pārthān saputrān sahakeśavāna aho bata mahad duḥkhaṃ yatra pāṇḍusutān raṇec nātarad rabhasaḥ karṇo daivaṃ nūnaṃ parāyaṇame aho dyūtasya niṣṭheyaṃ ghorā saṃprati vartatea aho duḥkhāni tīvrāṇi duryodhanakṛtāny ahamc sahiṣyāmi sughorāṇi śalyabhūtāni saṃjayaa saubalaṃ ca tathā tāta nītimān iti manyateb karṇaś ca rabhaso nityaṃ rājānaṃ cāpy anuvrataḥb karṇaṃ cāpratimaṃ yuddhe devair api durutsahamb manyate bhyadhikaṃ pārthād daivaṃ cāsya hṛdi sthitama yuddheṣu nāma divyeṣu vartamāneṣu saṃjayac aśrauṣaṃ nihatān putrān nityam eva ca nirjitāna na pāṇḍavānāṃ samare kaś cid asti nivārakaḥc strīmadhyam iva gāhanti daivaṃ hi balavattaram saṃjaya uvāca rājan pūrvanimittāni dharmiṣṭhāni vicintayaa atikrāntaṃ hi yat kāryaṃ paścāc cintayatīti cac tac cāsya na bhavet kāryaṃ cintayā ca vinaśyatia tad idaṃ tava kāryaṃ tu dūraprāptaṃ vijānatāc na kṛtaṃ yat tvayā pūrvaṃ prāptāprāptavicāraṇea ukto si bahudhā rājan mā yudhyasveti pāṇḍavaiḥc gṛhṇīṣe na ca tan mohāt pāṇḍaveṣu viśāṃ patea tvayā pāpāni ghorāṇi samācīrṇāni pāṇḍuṣuc tvatkṛte vartate ghoraḥ pārthivānāṃ janakṣayaḥa tat tv idānīm atikramya mā śuco bharatarṣabhac śṛṇu sarvaṃ yathāvṛttaṃ ghoraṃ vaiśasam acyutaa prabhātāyāṃ rajanyāṃ tu karṇo rājānam abhyayātc sametya ca mahābāhur duryodhanam abhāṣataa adya rājan sameṣyāmi pāṇḍavena yaśasvināc haniṣyāmi ca taṃ vīraṃ sa vā māṃ nihaniṣyatia bahutvān mama kāryāṇāṃ tathā pārthasya pārthivac nābhūt samāgamo rājan mama caivārjunasya caa idaṃ tu me yathāprajñaṃ śṛṇu vākyaṃ viśāṃ patec anihatya raṇe pārthaṃ nāham eṣyāmi bhārataa hatapravīre sainye smin mayi caiva sthite yudhic abhiyāsyati māṃ pārthaḥ śakraśaktyā vinākṛtama tataḥ śreyaskaraṃ yat te tan nibodha janeśvarac āyudhānāṃ ca yad vīryaṃ dravyāṇām arjunasya caa kāyasya mahato bhede lāghave dūrapātanec sauṣṭhave cāstrayoge ca savyasācī na matsamaḥd prāṇe śaurye ca vijñāne vikrame cāpi bhāratad nimittajñānayoge ca savyasācī na matsamaḥa sarvāyudhamahāmātraṃ vijayaṃ nāma tad dhanuḥc indrārtham abhikāmena nirmitaṃ viśvakarmaṇāa yena daityagaṇān rājañ jitavān vai śatakratuḥc yasya ghoṣeṇa daityānāṃ vimuhyanti diśo daśae tad bhārgavāya prāyacchac chakraḥ paramasaṃmatama tad divyaṃ bhārgavo mahyam adadād dhanur uttamamc yena yotsye mahābāhum arjunaṃ jayatāṃ varame yathendraḥ samare sarvān daiteyān vai samāgatānf nijaghāna tathā sarvāñ jeṣyāmi yudhi pāṇḍavāna dhanur ghoraṃ rāmadattaṃ gāṇḍīvāt tad viśiṣyatec triḥsaptakṛtvaḥ pṛthivī dhanuṣā tena nirjitāa dhanuṣo yasya karmāṇi divyāni prāha bhārgavaḥc tad rāmo hy adadān mahyaṃ yena yotsyāmi pāṇḍavama adya duryodhanāhaṃ tvāṃ nandayiṣye sabāndhavamc nihatya samare vīram arjunaṃ jayatāṃ varama saparvatavanadvīpā hatadviḍ bhūḥ sasāgarāc putrapautrapratiṣṭhā te bhaviṣyaty adya pārthivaa nāsādhyaṃ vidyate me dya tvatpriyārthaṃ viśeṣataḥc samyag dharmānuraktasya siddhir ātmavato yathāa na hi māṃ samare soḍhuṃ sa śakto gniṃ tarur yathāc avaśyaṃ tu mayā vācyaṃ yena hīno smi phalgunāta jyā tasya dhanuṣo divyā tathākṣayyau maheṣudhīb sārathis tasya govindo mama tādṛṅ na vidyatec tasya divyaṃ dhanuḥ śreṣṭhaṃ gāṇḍīvam ajaraṃ yudhia vijayaṃ ca mahad divyaṃ mamāpi dhanur uttamamc tatrāham adhikaḥ pārthād dhanuṣā tena pārthivaa mayā cābhyadhiko vīraḥ pāṇḍavas tan nibodha mec raśmigrāhaś ca dāśārhaḥ sarvalokanamaskṛtaḥa agnidattaś ca vai divyo rathaḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇaḥc acchedyaḥ sarvato vīra vājinaś ca manojavāḥe dhvajaś ca divyo dyutimān vānaro vismayaṃkaraḥa kṛṣṇaś ca sraṣṭā jagato rathaṃ tam abhirakṣatic ebhir dravyair ahaṃ hīno yoddhum icchāmi pāṇḍavama ayaṃ tu sadṛśo vīraḥ śalyaḥ samitiśobhanaḥc sārathyaṃ yadi me kuryād dhruvas te vijayo bhaveta tasya me sārathiḥ śalyo bhavatv asukaraḥ paraiḥc nārācān gārdhrapatrāṃś ca śakaṭāni vahantu mea rathāś ca mukhyā rājendra yuktā vājibhir uttamaiḥc āyāntu paścāt satataṃ mām eva bharatarṣabhaa evam abhyadhikaḥ pārthād bhaviṣyāmi guṇair ahamc śalyo hy abhyadhikaḥ kṛṣṇād arjunād adhiko hy ahama yathāśvahṛdayaṃ veda dāśārhaḥ paravīrahāc tathā śalyo pi jānīte hayānāṃ vai mahārathaḥa bāhuvīrye samo nāsti madrarājasya kaś canac tathāstrair matsamo nāsti kaś cid eva dhanurdharaḥa tathā śalyasamo nāsti hayayāne ha kaś canab vīryataḥ sārataś caiva yogataḥ karmato rthataḥc so yam abhyadhikaḥ pārthād bhaviṣyati ratho mamad samudyātuṃ na śakṣyanti devā api savāsavāḥd evaṃ kṛte rathastho haṃ guṇair abhyadhiko rjunātd bhave yudhi jayeyaṃ ca phālgunaṃ kurusattamad vijayeyam ahaṃ saṃkhye phalgunaṃ kurunandanaa etat kṛtaṃ mahārāja tvayecchāmi paraṃtapab kriyatām eṣa kāmo me mā vaḥ kālo tyagād ayamc evaṃ kṛte kṛtaṃ mahyaṃ sarvakāmair bhaviṣyatia tato draṣṭāsi samare yat kariṣyāmi bhāratac sarvathā pāṇḍavān sarvāñ jeṣyāmy adya samāgatānd na hi me samare śaktāḥ samudyātuṃ surāsurāḥd saṃjaya uvācad kim u pāṇḍusutā rājan raṇe mānuṣayonayaḥd evam uktas tava sutaḥ karṇenāhavaśobhinād saṃpūjya saṃprahṛṣṭātmā tato rādheyam abravīt duryodhana uvācaa sarvam etat kariṣyāmi yathā tvaṃ karṇa manyasec sopāsaṅgā rathāḥ sāśvā anuyāsyanti sūtajaa nārācān gārdhrapakṣāṃś ca śakaṭāni vahantu tec anuyāsyāma karṇa tvāṃ vayaṃ sarve ca pārthivāḥ saṃjaya uvācaa evam uktvā mahārāja tava putrāḥ pratāpavānc abhigamyābravīd rājā madrarājam idaṃ vacaḥ saṃjaya uvācaa putras tava mahārāja madrarājam idaṃ vacaḥb evam ukto mahārāja tava putraḥ pratāpavānb madreśvaraṃ prati raṇe parasainyabhayaṃkaramb sarvaṃ tathākarot tūrṇaṃ rādheyas tad yad abravītb madrarājaṃ ca samare praṇamya ca mahārathamc vinayenopasaṃgamya praṇayād vākyam abravīta satyavrata mahābhāga dviṣatām aghavardhanac madreśvara raṇe śūra parasainyabhayaṃkaraa śrutavān asi karṇasya bruvato vadatāṃ varac yathā nṛpatisiṃhānāṃ madhye tvāṃ varayaty ayamd tat tvām aprativīryādya śatrupakṣakṣayāvahad madreśvara prayāce haṃ śirasā vinayena cad tvaṃ pāhi sarvataḥ karṇaṃ bhavaṃ brahmeva suvrataa tasmāt pārthavināśārthaṃ hitārthaṃ mama caiva hic sārathyaṃ rathināṃ śreṣṭha sumanāḥ kartum arhasid tvayi yantari rādheyo vidviṣo me vijeṣyated abhīṣūṇāṃ hi karṇasya grahītānyo na vidyatea asyābhīśugraho loke nānyo sti bhavatā samaḥb ṛte hi tvāṃ mahābhāga vāsudevasamaṃ yudhic sa pātu sarvataḥ karṇaṃ bhavān brahmeva śaṃkarama pārthasya sacivaḥ kṛṣṇo yathābhīśugraho varaḥc tathā tvam api rādheyaṃ sarvataḥ paripālayad yathā ca sarvathāpatsu vārṣṇeyaḥ pāti pāṇḍavamd tathā madreśvarādya tvaṃ rādheyaṃ pratipālayaa bhīṣmo droṇaḥ kṛpaḥ karṇo bhavān bhojaś ca vīryavānc śakuniḥ saubalo drauṇir aham eva ca no balame eṣām eva kṛto bhāgo navadhā pṛtanāpatea naiva bhāgo tra bhīṣmasya droṇasya ca mahātmanaḥc tābhyām atītya tau bhāgau nihatā mama śatravaḥa vṛddhau hi tau naravyāghrau chalena nihatau ca tauc kṛtvā nasukaraṃ karma gatau svargam ito naghaa tathānye puruṣavyāghrāḥ parair vinihatā yudhic asmadīyāś ca bahavaḥ svargāyopagatā raṇee tyaktvā prāṇān yathāśakti ceṣṭāḥ kṛtvā ca puṣkalāḥf tad idaṃ hatabhūyiṣṭhaṃ balaṃ mama narādhipaf pūrvam apy alpakaiḥ pārthair hataṃ kim uta sāṃpratamf balavanto mahātmānaḥ kaunteyāḥ satyavikramāḥf balaṃ śeṣaṃ na hanyur me yathā tat kuru pārthivaf hatavīram idaṃ sainyaṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ samare vibhoa karṇo hy eko mahābāhur asmatpriyahite rataḥc bhavāṃś ca puruṣavyāghra sarvalokamahārathaḥd śalya karṇo rjunenādya yoddhum icchati saṃyugee tasmiñ jayāśā vipulā mama madrajanādhipaf tasyābhīṣugrahavaro nānyo sti bhuvi kaś canaf tasmāj jayāya me vīra sārathyaṃ kartum arhasia pārthasya samare kṛṣṇo yathābhīśuvaragrahaḥb tathā karṇarathe rājaṃs tvam abhīṣugraho bhavac tena yukto raṇe pārtho rakṣyamāṇaś ca pārthivae yāni karmāṇi kurute pratyakṣāṇi tathaiva tea pūrvaṃ na samare hy evam avadhīd arjuno ripūnb idānīṃ vikramo hy asya kṛṣṇena sahitasya cab kṛṣṇena sahitaḥ pārtho dhārtarāṣṭrīṃ mahācamūmc ahany ahani madreśa drāvayan dṛśyate yudhia bhāgo vaśiṣṭaḥ karṇasya tava caiva mahādyutec taṃ bhāgaṃ saha karṇena yugapan nāśayāhaved aruṇena yathā sārdhaṃ tamaḥ sūryo vyapohatid tathā karṇena sahito jahi pārthaṃ mahāhaved udyantau ca yathā sūryau bālasūryasamaprabhaud karṇaśalyau raṇe dṛṣṭvā vidravantu mahārathāḥa sūryāruṇau yathā dṛṣṭvā tamo naśyati māriṣac tathā naśyantu kaunteyāḥ sapāñcālāḥ sasṛñjayāḥa rathānāṃ pravaraḥ karṇo yantṝṇāṃ pravaro bhavānb saṃyogo yuvayor loke nābhūn na ca bhaviṣyatic saṃnipātaḥ samo loke bhavator nāsti kaś canaa yathā sarvāsv avasthāsu vārṣṇeyaḥ pāti pāṇḍavamc tathā bhavān paritrātu karṇaṃ vaikartanaṃ raṇed sārathyaṃ kriyatāṃ tasya yudhyamānasya saṃyuged yathā ca samare kṛṣṇo rakṣate sarvato rjunamd tathā tvam api rādheyaṃ rakṣasva ca mahāraṇea tvayā sārathinā hy eṣa apradhṛṣyo bhaviṣyatic devatānām api raṇe saśakrāṇāṃ mahīpatee kiṃ punaḥ pāṇḍaveyānāṃ mātiśaṅkīr vaco mamaa duryodhanavacaḥ śrutvā śalyaḥ krodhasamanvitaḥb dhārtarāṣṭram athovāca sṛkkiṇī parilelihanb evam uktas tu sa krodhāt padā spṛṣṭa ivoragaḥc triśikhāṃ bhrukuṭīṃ kṛtvā dhunvan hastau punaḥ punaḥa krodharakte mahānetre parivartya mahābhujaḥc kulaiśvaryaśrutibalair dṛptaḥ śalyo bravīd idama avamanyase māṃ gāndhāre dhruvaṃ māṃ pariśaṅkasec yan māṃ bravīṣi visrabdhaṃ sārathyaṃ kriyatām itia asmatto bhyadhikaṃ karṇaṃ manyamānaḥ praśaṃsasic na cāhaṃ yudhi rādheyaṃ gaṇaye tulyam ātmanāa ādiśyatām abhyadhiko mamāṃśaḥ pṛthivīpatec tam ahaṃ samare hatvā gamiṣyāmi yathāgatama atha vāpy eka evāhaṃ yotsyāmi kurunandanac paśya vīryaṃ mamādya tvaṃ saṃgrāme dahato ripūna na cābhikāmān kauravya vidhāya hṛdaye pumānc asmadvidhaḥ pravarteta mā mā tvam atiśaṅkithāḥa yudhi cāpy avamāno me na kartavyaḥ kathaṃ canac paśya hīmau mama bhujau vajrasaṃhananopamaua dhanuḥ paśya ca me citraṃ śarāṃś cāśīviṣopamānc rathaṃ paśya ca me kḷptaṃ sadaśvair vātavegitaiḥe gadāṃ ca paśya gāndhāre hemapaṭṭavibhūṣitāma dārayeyaṃ mahīṃ kruddho vikireyaṃ ca parvatānc śoṣayeyaṃ samudrāṃś ca tejasā svena pārthivaa tan mām evaṃvidhaṃ jānan samartham arinigrahec kasmād yunakṣi sārathye nyūnasyādhirather nṛpad na cāpi mama rādheyaḥ kalām arhati ṣoḍaśīmd sakarṇā ye trayo lokāḥ sārjunāḥ sajanārdanāḥd nibaddhāṃs tān raṇe rājan na mucyeyaṃ kathaṃ canad tathāpi śaktaṃ kauravya vihāya hṛdayena māmd na cāhaṃ prākṛtaḥ kaś cin na cāpy adhigataḥ svayamd ayaṃ cāpy avamāno me na kartavyaḥ kathaṃ canaa na nāma dhuri rājendra prayoktuṃ tvam ihārhasic na hi pāpīyasaḥ śreyān bhūtvā preṣyatvam utsahea yo hy abhyupagataṃ prītyā garīyāṃsaṃ vaśe sthitamc vaśe pāpīyaso dhatte tat pāpam adharottarama brāhmaṇā brahmaṇā sṛṣṭā mukhāt kṣatram athorasaḥc ūrubhyām asṛjad vaiśyāñ śūdrān padbhyām iti śrutiḥe tebhyo varṇaviśeṣāś ca pratilomānulomajāḥa athānyonyasya saṃyogāc cāturvarṇyasya bhāratac goptāraḥ saṃgrahītāro dātāraḥ kṣatriyāḥ smṛtāḥa yājanādhyāpanair viprā viśuddhaiś ca pratigrahaiḥc lokasyānugrahārthāya sthāpitā brahmaṇā bhuvid prajānāṃ rakṣaṇaṃ dānaṃ yuddhaṃ kṣatrasya nirmitama kṛṣiś ca pāśupālyaṃ ca viśāṃ dānaṃ ca sarvaśaḥc brahmakṣatraviśāṃ śūdrā vihitāḥ paricārakāḥa brahmakṣatrasya vihitāḥ sūtā vai paricārakāḥc na viṭśūdrasya tatraiva śṛṇu vākyaṃ mamānaghaa so haṃ mūrdhāvasiktaḥ san rājarṣikulasaṃbhavaḥc mahārathaḥ samākhyātaḥ sevyaḥ stavyaś ca bandināma so ham etādṛśo bhūtvā nehārikulamardanac sūtaputrasya saṃgrāme sārathyaṃ kartum utsahea avamānam ahaṃ prāpya na yotsyāmi kathaṃ canac āpṛcchya tvādya gāndhāre gamiṣyāmi yathāgatamd na cāhaṃ sūtaputrasya sārathyam upajagmivāna evam uktvā naravyāghraḥ śalyaḥ samitiśobhanaḥc utthāya prayayau tūrṇaṃ rājamadhyād amarṣitaḥa praṇayād bahumānāc ca taṃ nigṛhya sutas tavac abravīn madhuraṃ vākyaṃ sāma sarvārthasādhakama yathā śalya tvam ātthedam evam etad asaṃśayamc abhiprāyas tu me kaś cit taṃ nibodha janeśvaraa na karṇo bhyadhikas tvattaḥ śaṅke naiva kathaṃ canac na hi madreśvaro rājā kuryād yad anṛtaṃ bhaveta ṛtam eva hi pūrvās te vahanti puruṣottamāḥb jñātam eva hi pūrvaṃ te vartma rājarṣisattamac tasmād ārtāyaniḥ prokto bhavān iti matir mamaa śalyabhūtaś ca śatrūṇāṃ yasmāt tvaṃ bhuvi mānadac tasmāc chalyeti te nāma kathyate pṛthivīpatea yad eva vyāhṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ bhavatā bhūridakṣiṇac tad eva kuru dharmajña madarthaṃ yad yad ucyasea na ca tvatto hi rādheyo na cāham api vīryavānc vṛṇīmas tvāṃ hayāgryāṇāṃ yantāram iti saṃyugea yathā hy abhyadhikaṃ karṇaṃ guṇais tāta dhanaṃjayātc vāsudevād api tvāṃ ca loko yam iti manyatea karṇo hy abhyadhikaḥ pārthād astrair eva nararṣabhac bhavān apy adhikaḥ kṛṣṇād aśvayāne bale tathāa yathāśvahṛdayaṃ veda vāsudevo mahāmanāḥc dviguṇaṃ tvaṃ tathā vettha madrarāja na saṃśayaḥ śalya uvācaa yan mā bravīṣi gāndhāre madhye sainyasya kauravac viśiṣṭaṃ devakīputrāt prītimān asmy ahaṃ tvayia eṣa sārathyam ātiṣṭhe rādheyasya yaśasvinaḥc yudhyataḥ pāṇḍavāgryeṇa yathā tvaṃ vīra manyasea samayaś ca hi me vīra kaś cid vaikartanaṃ pratic utsṛjeyaṃ yathāśraddham ahaṃ vāco sya saṃnidhau saṃjaya uvācaa tatheti rājan putras te saha karṇena bhāratac abravīn madrarājasya sutaṃ bharatasattama duryodhana uvācaa bhūya eva tu madreśa yat te vakṣyāmi tac chṛṇuc yathā purā vṛttam idaṃ yuddhe devāsure vibhoa yad uktavān pitur mahyaṃ mārkaṇḍeyo mahān ṛṣiḥc tad aśeṣeṇa bruvato mama rājarṣisattamae tvaṃ nibodha na cāpy atra kartavyā te vicāraṇāf samutpannā hi rājānaḥ pramoha iti niścayaḥf kṛtvā caiva vyavasyanti sarve dharmārthaniścayāna devānām asurāṇāṃ ca mahān āsīt samāgamaḥb saiṃhikeyās tadodvṛttā vibudhān avasūdayanb te nirastāḥ kṛtā devair dānavā balagarvitāḥc babhūva prathamo rājan saṃgrāmas tārakāmayaḥe nirjitāś ca tadā daityā daivatair iti naḥ śrutamf bhagnadarpā nirutsāhāḥ pātālaṃ viviśus tadāa nirjiteṣu ca daityeṣu tārakasya sutās trayaḥc tārākṣaḥ kamalākṣaś ca vidyunmālī ca pārthivad kaś cit prajāpatir ghoras tena sārdhaṃ mahātmanād yuddham āsīn mahāghoraṃ daivatair na iti śrutiḥd parābabhūvur asurā dānavaiḥ saha saṃyuged devair nirastā hy asurā niḥśvasyāmarṣitās tataḥa tapa ugraṃ samāsthāya niyame parame sthitāḥc tapasā karśayām āsur dehān svāñ śatrutāpanaa damena tapasā caiva niyamena ca pārthivac teṣāṃ pitāmahaḥ prīto varadaḥ pradadau varāna avadhyatvaṃ ca te rājan sarvabhūteṣu sarvadāc sahitā varayām āsuḥ sarvalokapitāmahama tān abravīt tadā devo lokānāṃ prabhur īśvaraḥc nāsti sarvāmaratvaṃ hi nivartadhvam ato surāḥe varam anyaṃ vṛṇīdhvaṃ vai yādṛśaṃ saṃprarocatea tatas te sahitā rājan saṃpradhāryāsakṛd bahuc sarvalokeśvaraṃ vākyaṃ praṇamyainam athābruvand vayam icchāma nagaraṃ kartuṃ kāmagamaṃ śubhamd sarvakāmasamṛddhārtham avadhyaṃ devadānavaiḥd yakṣarakṣoragagaṇair nānājātibhir eva cad na kṛtyābhir na śastraiś ca na śāpair brahmavādināmd vadhyeta tripuraṃ devaṃ prasanne tvayi sādarama asmākaṃ tvaṃ varaṃ deva prayacchemaṃ pitāmahac vayaṃ purāṇi trīṇy eva samāsthāya mahīm imāme vicariṣyāma loke smiṃs tvatprasādapuraskṛtāḥa tato varṣasahasre tu sameṣyāmaḥ parasparamb brahmovācab vilayaḥ samayasyānte maraṇaṃ jīvitasya cab iti cintya vadhopāyaṃ kaṃ cid eva niśāmayac ekībhāvaṃ gamiṣyanti purāṇy etāni cānaghaa samāgatāni caitāni yo hanyād bhagavaṃs tadāc ekeṣuṇā devavaraḥ sa no mṛtyur bhaviṣyatid teṣāṃ tad vacanaṃ śrutvā dānavānāṃ mahāyaśāḥe evam astv iti tān devaḥ pratyuktvā prāviśad divama te tu labdhavarāḥ prītāḥ saṃpradhārya parasparamc puratrayavisṛṣṭyarthaṃ mayaṃ vavrur mahāsurame viśvakarmāṇam ajaraṃ daityadānavapūjitama tato mayaḥ svatapasā cakre dhīmān purāṇi hac trīṇi kāñcanam ekaṃ tu raupyaṃ kārṣṇāyasaṃ tathāa kāñcanaṃ divi tatrāsīd antarikṣe ca rājatamc āyasaṃ cābhavad bhūmau cakrasthaṃ pṛthivīpatea ekaikaṃ yojanaśataṃ vistārāyāmasaṃmitamc gṛhāṭṭāṭṭālakayutaṃ bṛhatprākāratoraṇama guṇaprasavasaṃbādham asaṃbādham anāmayamc prāsādair vividhaiś caiva dvāraiś cāpy upaśobhitama pureṣu cābhavan rājan rājāno vai pṛthak pṛthakb divyamālyāmbaradharā daiteyā rājasattamac kāñcanaṃ tārakākṣasya citram āsīn mahātmanaḥe rājataṃ kamalākṣasya vidyunmālina āyasama trayas te daityarājānas trīṃl lokān āśu tejasāc ākramya tasthur varṣāṇāṃ pūgān nāma prajāpatiḥa teṣāṃ dānavamukhyānāṃ prayutāny arbudāni cac koṭyaś cāprativīrāṇāṃ samājagmus tatas tataḥd māṃsāśanāḥ sudṛptāś ca surair vinikṛtās tathāe mahad aiśvaryam icchantas tripuraṃ durgam āśritāḥa sarveṣāṃ ca punas teṣāṃ sarvayogavaho mayaḥc tam āśritya hi te sarve avartantākutobhayāḥa yo hi yaṃ manasā kāmaṃ dadhyau tripurasaṃśrayaḥc tasmai kāmaṃ mayas taṃ taṃ vidadhe māyayā tadāa tārakākṣasutaś cāsīd dharir nāma mahābalaḥc tapas tepe paramakaṃ yenātuṣyat pitāmahaḥa sa tuṣṭam avṛṇod devaṃ vāpī bhavatu naḥ purec śastrair vinihatā yatra kṣiptāḥ syur balavattarāḥa sa tu labdhvā varaṃ vīras tārakākṣasuto hariḥc sasṛje tatra vāpīṃ tāṃ mṛtānāṃ jīvanīṃ prabhod pūrṇāṃ divyasya toyasya pīyūṣapratimasya vaia yena rūpeṇa daityas tu yena veṣeṇa caiva hac mṛtas tasyāṃ parikṣiptas tādṛśenaiva jajñivānd saṃpūrṇabalavīryas tu rājañ śauryasamanvitaḥd evaṃ vīryeṇa saṃyuktāḥ kṛtās tena mahātmanāa tāṃ prāpya traipurasthās tu sarvāṃl lokān babādhireb varaloke vasat so pi hariḥ paramatejasāb vidhāya sarvalokānāṃ hitaṃ pathyaṃ vidhāya cab tataḥ paramanirvigno hitakārī tāvakātmasuc mahatā tapasā siddhāḥ surāṇāṃ bhayavardhanāḥd ekasmin nihate daitye sṛjanti sma daśāsurāne na teṣām abhavad rājan kṣayo yuddhe kathaṃ canaa tatas te lobhamohābhyām abhibhūtā vicetasaḥc nirhrīkāḥ saṃsthitiṃ sarve sthāpitāṃ samalūlupana vidrāvya sagaṇān devāṃs tatra tatra tadā tadāc viceruḥ svena kāmena varadānena darpitāḥa devāraṇyāni sarvāṇi priyāṇi ca divaukasāmc ṛṣīṇām āśramān puṇyān yūpāñ janapadāṃs tathāe ahaṃ manye ye vai yuṣmān apīḍayana ahaṃ hi tulyaḥ sarveṣāṃ bhūtānāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥc adhārmikās tu hantavyā ity ahaṃ prabravīmi vaḥd ekeṣuṇā vibhedyāni tāni durgāṇi nānyathād na ca sthāṇumṛte śakto sthitāḥb divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ vai tapas taptvā surarṣabhāḥb śubhātmāno mahātmāno jagmur vai vṛṣabhadhvajamc brahmāṇam agrataḥ kṛtvā vṛṣāṅkaṃ śaraṇaṃ yayuḥa tapaḥ paraṃ samātasthur gṛṇanto brahma rodasīd tam ārurukṣuṃ deveśaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ paramarṣayaḥd gandharvā devasaṃghāś ca tathaivāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥd maharṣibhiḥ stūyamāno vandyamānaś ca bandibhiḥd upanṛttaś cāpsarasāṃ gaṇair nṛttaviśāradaiḥa sa śobhamāno varadaḥ khaḍgī bāṇī śarāsanīc hasann ivābravīd devo sārathiḥ ko bhaviṣyatia tam abruvan devagaṇā yaṃ bhavān saṃniyokṣyatec sa bhaviṣyati deveśa sārathis te na saṃśayaḥa tān abravīt punar devo mattaḥ śreṣṭhataro hi yaḥc taṃ sārathiṃ kurudhvaṃ me svayaṃ saṃcintya mācirama etac chrutvā tato devā vākyam uktaṃ mahātmanāc gatvā pitāmahaṃ devaṃ prasādyaivaṃ vaco bruvana deva tvayedaṃ kathitaṃ tridaśārinibarhaṇamc tathā ca kṛtam asmābhiḥ prasanno vṛṣabhadhvajaḥa rathaś ca vihito smābhir vicitrāyudhasaṃvṛtaḥc sārathiṃ tu na jānīmaḥ kaḥ syāt tasmin rathottamea tasmād vidhīyatāṃ kaś cit sārathir devasattamac saphalāṃ tāṃ giraṃ deva kartum arhasi no vibhoa evam asmāsu hi purā bhagavann uktavān asic hitaṃ kartāsmi bhavatām iti tat kartum arhasia sa deva yukto rathasattamo nodurāvaro drāvaṇaḥ śātravāṇāmc pinākapāṇir vihito tra yoddhāvibhīṣayan dānavān udyato saua tathaiva vedāś caturo hayāgryādharā saśailā ca ratho mahātmanc nakṣatravaṃśo nugato varūtheyasmin yoddhā sārathinābhirakṣyaḥa tatra sārathir eṣṭavyaḥ sarvair etair viśeṣavānc tatpratiṣṭho ratho deva hayā yoddhā tathaiva cae kavacāni ca śastrāṇi kārmukaṃ ca pitāmahaa tvām ṛte sārathiṃ tatra nānyaṃ paśyāmahe vayamc tvaṃ hi sarvair guṇair yukto devatābhyo dhikaḥ prabhod tvaṃ deva śakto loke smin niyantuṃ pradrutān imānd vedāśvān sopaniṣadaḥ sārathir bhava naḥ svayamd yoddhuṃ balena sattvena vayasā vinayena cad adhikaḥ sārathiḥ kāryo nāsti cānyo dhiko bhavānd sa bhavāṃs tārayatv asmān kuru sārathyam avyayad bhavān abhyadhikas tvatto nānyo sti bhavitā tv ihad tvaṃ hi deveśa sarvais tu viśiṣṭo vadatāṃ varad taṃ rathaṃ tvaṃ samāruhya saṃyaccha paramān hayānd tava prasādād vadhyeyur deva daivatakaṇṭakāḥd sa no rakṣa mahābāho daityebhyo mahato bhayātd tvaṃ hi no gatir avyagra tvaṃ no goptā mahāvratad tvatprasādāt surāḥ sarve pūjyante tridive prabhoe sārathye tūrṇam āroha saṃyaccha paramān hayānf jayāya tridiveśānāṃ vadhāya tridaśadviṣāma iti te śirasā natvā trilokeśaṃ pitāmahamc devāḥ prasādayām āsuḥ sārathyāyeti naḥ śrutam brahmovāca evam etat surās tathyaṃ nānyas tv abhyadhiko bhavān sārathitvaṃ kariṣyāmi śaṃkarasya mahātmanaḥ sarvathā rathinaḥ śreyān kartavyo rathasārathiḥ tasmād etad yathātattvaṃ jñātvā yuṣmāṃś ca saṃgatān saṃgacchāmi hayān eṣa vibudhāḥ kālamardinea nātra kiṃ cin mṛṣā vākyaṃ yad uktaṃ vo divaukasaḥc saṃyacchāmi hayān eṣa yudhyato vai kapardinaḥd duryodhanaḥd evam uktvā jaṭābhāraṃ saṃyamya prapitāmahaḥd paridhāyājinaṃ gāḍhaṃ saṃnyasya ca kamaṇḍalumd pratodapāṇir bhagavān āruroha rathaṃ tadāa tataḥ sa bhagavān devo lokasraṣṭā pitāmahaḥc sārathye kalpito devair īśānasya mahātmanaḥa tasminn ārohati kṣipraṃ syandanaṃ lokapūjitec śirobhir agamaṃs tūrṇaṃ te hayā vātaraṃhasaḥd āruhya bhagavān devo dīpyamānaḥ svatejasād abhīṣūn hi pratodaṃ ca saṃjagrāha pitāmahaḥa maheśvare tv āruhati jānubhyām agaman mahīmb ubhābhyāṃ lokanāthābhyām āsthitaṃ rathasattamamb voḍhuṃ na śaktā vedāśvā jānubhyām apatan mahīma abhīśūn hi trilokeśaḥ saṃgṛhya prapitāmahaḥc tān aśvāṃś codayām āsa manomārutaraṃhasaḥd abhīśubhis tu bhagavān udyamya ca hayān vibhuḥd astu vīryaṃ ca śauryaṃ ca vedāśvānām iti prabhuḥd rathaṃ saṃcodayām āsa devānāṃ prabhur avyayaḥd tata utthāpya bhagavāṃs tān hayān anilopamānd babhāṣe ca tadā sthāṇum āroheti surottamaḥd tatas tam iṣum ādāya viṣṇusomāgnisaṃbhavamd āruroha tadā sthāṇur dhanuṣā kampayan parānd tam ārūḍhaṃ tu deveśaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ paramarṣayaḥd gandharvā devasaṃghāś ca tathaivāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥd sa śobhamāno varadaḥ khaḍgī bāṇī śarāsanīd pradīpayan rathe tasthau trīṃl lokān svena tejasād tato bhūyo bravīd devo devān indrapurogamānd na hanyād iti kartavyo na śoko vaḥ kathaṃ canad hatān ity eva jānīta bāṇenānena cāsurānd te devāḥ satyam ity āhur nihatā iti cābruvand na ca tad vacanaṃ mithyā yad āha bhagavān prabhuḥd iti saṃcintya vai devāḥ parāṃ tuṣṭim avāpnuvand tataḥ prayāto deveśaḥ sarvair devagaṇair vṛtaḥd rathena mahatā rājann upamā nāsti yasya had svaiś ca pāriṣadair devaḥ pūjyamāno mahāyaśāḥd nṛtyadbhir aparaiś caiva māṃsabhakṣair durāsadaiḥd dhāvamānaiḥ samantāc ca tarjamānaiḥ parasparamd ṛṣayaś ca mahābhāgās tapoyuktā mahāguṇāḥd āśaṃsur vai jayaṃ devā mahādevasya sarvaśaḥd evaṃ prayāte deveśe lokānām abhayaṃkared tuṣṭam āsīj jagat sarvaṃ devatāś ca narottamad ṛṣayas tatra deveśaṃ stuvanto bahubhiḥ stavaiḥd tejaś cāsmai vardhayanto rājann āsan punaḥ punaḥd gandharvāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi prayutāny arbudāni cad vādayanti prayāṇe sya vādyāni vividhāni caa tato dhirūḍhe varade prayāte cāsurān pratic sādhu sādhv iti viśveśaḥ smayamāno bhyabhāṣataa yāhi deva yato daityāś codayāśvān atandritaḥc paśya bāhvor balaṃ me dya nighnataḥ śātravān raṇea tatas tāṃś codayām āsa vāyuvegasamāñ javeb purāṇy uddiśya khasthāni dānavānāṃ tarasvināmc yena tat tripuraṃ rājan daityadānavarakṣitamd tatas te sahasotpatya vedākhyā rathavājinaḥd kṣaṇena tāni daityānāṃ purāṇi prāpayan prabhumd pibadbhir iva cākāśaṃ tair hayair lokapūjitaiḥd jagāma bhagavān kṣipraṃ jayāya tridivaukasāmd prayāte ratham āsthāya tripurābhimukhe bhaved nanāda sumahānādaṃ vṛṣabhaḥ pūrayan diśaḥd vṛṣabhasyāsya ninadaṃ śrutvā bhayaṃkaraṃ mahatd vināśam agamaṃs tatra tārakāḥ suraśatravaḥd apare vasthitās tatra yuddhāyābhimukhās tadād tataḥ sthāṇur mahārāja śūladhṛk krodhamūrchitaḥd trastāni sarvabhūtāni trailokyaṃ bhūḥ prakampated nimittāni ca ghorāṇi tatra saṃdadhataḥ śaramd tasmin somāgniviṣṇūnāṃ kṣobheṇa brahmarudrayoḥd sa ratho dhanuṣaḥ kṣobhād atīva hy avasīdatid tato nārāyaṇas tasmāc charabhāgād viniḥsṛtaḥd vṛṣarūpaṃ samāsthāya ujjahāra mahārathamd sīdamāne rathe caiva nardamāneṣu śatruṣud sa saṃbhramāt tu bhagavān nādaṃ cakre mahābalaḥd vṛṣabhasya sthito mūrdhni hayapṛṣṭhe ca mānadad tadā sa bhagavān rudro niraikṣad dānavaṃ puramd vṛṣabhasyāsthito rudro hayasya ca narottamad stanāṃs tadāśātayata khurāṃś caiva dvidhākarotd tataḥ prabhṛti bhadraṃ te gavāṃ dvaidhīkṛtāḥ khurāḥd hayānāṃ ca stanā rājaṃs tadā prabhṛti nābhavand pīḍitānāṃ balavatā rudreṇādbhutakarmaṇāa athādhijyaṃ dhanuḥ kṛtvā śarvaḥ saṃdhāya taṃ śaramc yuktvā pāśupatāstreṇa tripuraṃ samacintayata tasmin sthite tadā rājan kruddhe vidhṛtakārmukec purāṇi tāni kālena jagmur ekatvatāṃ tadāa ekībhāvaṃ gate caiva tripure samupāgatec babhūva tumulo harṣo daivatānāṃ mahātmanāma tato devagaṇāḥ sarve siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥc jayeti vāco mumucuḥ saṃstuvanto mudānvitāḥa tato grataḥ prādurabhūt tripuraṃ jaghnuṣo surānc anirdeśyogravapuṣo devasyāsahyatejasaḥd trīṇi dṛṣṭvaikasaṃsthāni purāṇy atha pinākadhṛka sa tad vikṛṣya bhagavān divyaṃ lokeśvaro dhanuḥc trailokyasāraṃ tam iṣuṃ mumoca tripuraṃ pratid utsṛṣṭe vai mahābhāga tasminn iṣuvare tadād mahān ārtasvaro hy āsīt purāṇāṃ patatāṃ bhuvid ekabāṇena tad devas tripuraṃ parameśvaraḥd nijaghne sāsuragaṇaṃ devadevo maheśvaraḥd bāṇatejognidagdhe tat praviśīrṇaṃ cātmakrodhajo vahnir hāhety uktvā nivāritaḥb trailokyam avaśeṣeṇa punar dagdhuṃ pracakrameb kālāgnim iva nirdagdhum utthitaṃ taṃ punaḥ punaḥc mā kārṣīr bhasmasāl lokān iti tryakṣo bravīc ca tama tataḥ narā bhuvid śalyena sahitaṃ dṛṣṭvā karṇam āhavaśobhiname nirjitān pāṇḍavāṃś caiva menire tava kauravāḥa tato rathasthaḥ paravīrahantābhīṣmadroṇāv āttavīryau nirīkṣyac samajvalad bhārata pāvakābhovaikartano sau rathakuñjaro vṛṣaḥa sa śalyam ābhāṣya jagāda vākyaṃpārthasya karmāpratimaṃ ca dṛṣṭvāc mānena darpeṇa ca dahyamānaḥkrodhena dīpyann iva niḥśvasitvāa nāhaṃ mahendrād api vajrapāṇeḥkruddhād bibhemy āttadhanū rathasthaḥc dṛṣṭvā tu bhīṣmapramukhāñ śayānānna tv eva māṃ sthiratā saṃjahātia mahendraviṣṇupratimāv aninditaurathāśvanāgapravarapramāthinauc avadhyakalpau nihatau yadā paraistato mamādyāpi raṇe sti sādhvasama samīkṣya saṃkhye tibalān narādhipairnarāśvamātaṅgarathāñ śarair hatānc kathaṃ na sarvān ahitān raṇe vadhīnmahāstravid brāhmaṇapuṃgavo guruḥa sa saṃsmaran droṇahavaṃ mahāhavebravīmi satyaṃ kuravo nibodhatac na vo mad anyaḥ prasahed raṇe rjunaṃkramāgataṃ mṛtyum ivograrūpiṇama śikṣā prasādaś ca balaṃ dhṛtiś cadroṇe mahāstrāṇi ca saṃnatiś cac sa ced agān mṛtyuvaśaṃ mahātmāsarvān anyān āturān adya manyea neha dhruvaṃ kiṃ cid api pracintyaṃvidur loke karmaṇo nityayogātc sūryodaye ko hi vimuktasaṃśayogarvaṃ kurvītādya gurau nipātitea na nūnam astrāṇi balaṃ parākramaḥkriyā sunītaṃ paramāyudhāni vāc alaṃ manuṣyasya sukhāya vartituṃtathā hi yuddhe nihataḥ parair guruḥa hutāśanādityasamānatejasaṃparākrame viṣṇupuraṃdaropamamc naye bṛhaspatyuśanaḥsamaṃ sadāna cainam astraṃ tad apāt suduḥsahama saṃprakruṣṭe ruditastrīkumāreparābhūte pauruṣe dhārtarāṣṭrec mayā kṛtyam iti jānāmi śalyaprayāhi tasmād dviṣatām anīkama yatra rājā pāṇḍavaḥ satyasaṃdhovyavasthito bhīmasenārjunau cac vāsudevaḥ sṛñjayāḥ sātyakiś cayamau ca kas tau viṣahen mad anyaḥa tasmāt kṣipraṃ madrapate prayāhiraṇe pāñcālān pāṇḍavān sṛñjayāṃś cac tān vā haniṣyāmi sametya saṃkhyeyāsyāmi vā droṇamukhāya manyea na tv evāhaṃ na gamiṣyāmi madhyaṃteṣāṃ śūrāṇām iti mā śalya viddhic mitradroho marṣaṇīyo na me yaṃtyaktvā prāṇān anuyāsyāmi droṇama prājñasya mūḍhasya ca jīvitānteprāṇapramokṣo ntakavaktragasyac ato vidvann abhiyāsyāmi pārthaṃdiṣṭaṃ na śakyaṃ vyativartituṃ vaia kalyāṇavṛttaḥ satataṃ hi rājanvaicitravīryasya suto mamāsītc tasyārthasiddhyartham ahaṃ tyajāmipriyān bhogān dustyajaṃ jīvitaṃ caa vaiyāghracarmāṇam akūjanākṣaṃhaimatrikośaṃ rajatatriveṇumc rathaprabarhaṃ turagaprabarhairyuktaṃ prādān mahyam idaṃ hi rāmaḥa dhanūṃṣi citrāṇi nirīkṣya śalyadhvajaṃ gadāṃ sāyakāṃś cograrūpānc asiṃ ca dīptaṃ paramāyudhaṃ caśaṅkhaṃ ca śubhraṃ svanavantam ugramd astrāṇi divyāny adadān mahātmāa patākinaṃ vajranipātanisvanaṃsitāśvayuktaṃ śubhatūṇaśobhitamb  rathaprabarhaṃ puruṣaprabarhaḥc imaṃ samāsthāya rathaṃ ratharṣabhaṃraṇe haniṣyāmy aham arjunaṃ balāta taṃ cen mṛtyuḥ sarvaharo bhirakṣatesadāpramattaḥ samare pāṇḍuputramc taṃ vā haniṣyāmi sametya yuddheyāsyāmi vā bhīṣmamukho yamāyaa yamavaruṇakuberavāsavā vāyadi yugapat sagaṇā mahāhavec jugupiṣava ihaitya pāṇḍavaṃkim u bahunā saha tair jayāmi tama iti raṇarabhasasya katthatastad upaniśamya vacaḥ sa madrarāṭc avahasad avamanya vīryavānpratiṣiṣidhe ca jagāda cottarama virama virama karṇa katthanādatirabhaso syati cāpy ayuktavākc kva ca hi naravaro dhanaṃjayaḥkva punar iha tvam upāramābudhaa yadusadanam upendrapālitaṃtridivam ivāmararājarakṣitamc prasabham iha vilokya ko haretpuruṣavarāvarajām ṛte rjunāta tribhuvanasṛjam īśvareśvaraṃka iha pumān bhavam āhvayed yudhic mṛgavadhakalahe ṛte rjunātsurapativīryasamaprabhāvataḥa asurasuramahoragān narāngaruḍapiśācasayakṣarākṣasānc iṣubhir ajayad agnigauravātsvabhilaṣitaṃ ca havir dadau jayaḥa smarasi nanu yadā parair hṛtaḥsa ca dhṛtarāṣṭrasuto vimokṣitaḥc dinakaraja narottamair yadāmaruṣu bahūn vinihatya tān arīna prathamam api palāyite tvayipriyakalahā dhṛtarāṣṭrasūnavaḥc smarasi nanu yadā pramocitāḥkhacaragaṇān avajitya pāṇḍavaiḥa samuditabalavāhanāḥ punaḥpuruṣavareṇa jitāḥ stha gograhec sagurugurusutāḥ sabhīṣmakāḥkim u na jitaḥ sa tadā tvayārjunaḥa idam aparam upasthitaṃ punastava nidhanāya suyuddham adya vaic yadi na ripubhayāt palāyasesamaragato dya hato si sūtaja saṃjaya uvācaa iti bahuparuṣaṃ prabhāṣatipramanasi madrapatau ripustavamc bhṛśam atiruṣitaḥ paraṃ vṛṣaḥkurupṛtanāpatir āha madrapama bhavatu bhavatu kiṃ vikatthasenanu mama tasya ca yuddham udyatamc yadi sa jayati māṃ mahāhavetata idam astu sukatthitaṃ tavaa evam astv iti madreśa uktvā nottaram uktavānc yāhi madreśa cāpy enaṃ karṇaḥ prāha yuyutsayāa sa rathaḥ prayayau śatrūñ śvetāśvaḥ śalyasārathiḥc nighnann amitrān samare tamo ghnan savitā yathāa tataḥ prāyāt prītimān vai rathenavaiyāghreṇa śvetayujātha karṇaḥc sa cālokya dhvajinīṃ pāṇḍavānāṃdhanaṃjayaṃ tvarayā paryapṛcchat saṃjaya uvācaa prayān eva tadā karṇo harṣayan vāhinīṃ tavac ekaikaṃ samare dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavaṃ paryapṛcchataa yo mamādya mahātmānaṃ darśayec chvetavāhanamc tasmai dadyām abhipretaṃ varaṃ yaṃ manasecchatia sa cet tad abhimanyeta tasmai dadyām ahaṃ punaḥc śakaṭaṃ ratnasaṃpūrṇaṃ yo me brūyād dhanaṃjayamd atha vā śakaṭaṃ pūrṇaṃ ratnānāṃ ṣaḍgavāyutamd dhuri kṣamair bṛhadbhiś ca gobhir yuktam akālikama sa cet tad abhimanyeta puruṣo rjunadarśivānb śataṃ dadyāṃ gavāṃ tasmai naityakaṃ kāṃsyadohanamb śataṃ grāmavarāṃś caiva dadyām arjunadarśineb tathā tasmai punar dadyāṃ śvetam aśvatarīrathamb yuktam añjanakeśībhir yo me brūyād dhanaṃjayamb atha vāsmai punar dadyāṃ varam anyad yathepsitamb yuktaṃ hayavarair jaitraṃ kāmbojair abhiniṣṭhitamb sa cet tad abhimanyeta puruṣo rjunadarśivānc anyaṃ tasmai punar dadyāṃ sauvarṇaṃ hastiṣaḍgavama tathā tasmai punar dadyāṃ strīṇāṃ śatam alaṃkṛtamc śyāmānāṃ niṣkakaṇṭhīnāṃ gītavādyavipaścitāmd sa cet tad abhimanyeta puruṣo rjunadarśivānd tasmai dadyāṃ śataṃ nāgāñ śataṃ grāmāñ śataṃ rathānd suvarṇasya ca mukhyasya hayāgryāṇāṃ śataṃ śatānd ṛddhyā guṇaiḥ sudāntāṃś ca dhuryavāhān suśikṣitānd tathā suvarṇaśṛṅgīṇāṃ godhenūnāṃ catuḥśatamd dadyāṃ tasmai savatsānāṃ yo me brūyād dhanaṃjayama sa cet tad abhimanyeta puruṣo rjunadarśivānc anyaṃ tasmai varaṃ dadyāṃ śvetān pañcaśatān hayāna hemabhāṇḍaparicchannān sumṛṣṭamaṇikuṇḍalānc sudāntān api caivāhaṃ dadyām aṣṭaśatān parānd atha vāsmai vicitrāṅgān vicitramaṇimaṇḍitānd rathāñ jātyair hayair yuktān dadyām aṣṭādaśaiva tānd anyam asmai varaṃ dadyāṃ dhuryān dāntāś catuḥśatamd rohiṇī rūpasaṃpannā hemaśṛṅgīś catuḥśatamd dadyām asmai payasvinyo yo me brūyād dhanaṃjayama rathaṃ ca śubhraṃ sauvarṇaṃ dadyāṃ tasmai svalaṃkṛtamc yuktaṃ paramakāmbojair yo me brūyād dhanaṃjayamd sa cet tad abhimanyeta puruṣo rjunadarśivāna anyaṃ tasmai varaṃ dadyāṃ kuñjarāṇāṃ śatāni ṣaṭc kāñcanair vividhair bhāṇḍair ācchannān hemamālinaḥe utpannān aparānteṣu vinītān hastiśikṣakaiḥa sa cet tad abhimanyeta puruṣo rjunadarśivānb dadyāṃ varṇasya varṇasya hayāgryāṇāṃ śataṃ śatamb dhuryāṇāṃ sādhudāntānāṃ śikṣitānāṃ narottamaiḥb sa cet tad abhimanyeta puruṣo rjunadarśivānb tasmai dadyāṃ grāmaśataṃ śataṃ hastīñ śataṃ hayānb sa cet tad abhimanyeta puruṣo rjunadarśivānb anyaṃ tasmai varaṃ dadyāṃ vaiśyagrāmāṃś caturdaśab susphītān dhanasaṃyuktān pratyāsannavanodakānb akutobhayān susaṃpannān rājabhojyāṃś caturdaśab dāsīnāṃ niṣkakaṇṭhīnāṃ māgadhīnāṃ śataṃ tathāb pratyagravayasāṃ dadyāṃ yo me brūyād dhanaṃjayamb sa cet tad abhimanyeta puruṣo rjunadarśivānc anyaṃ tasmai varaṃ dadyāṃ yam asau kāmayet svayama putradārān vihārāṃś ca yad anyad vittam asti mec tac ca tasmai punar dadyāṃ yad yat sa manasecchatia hatvā ca sahitau kṛṣṇau tayor vittāni sarvaśaḥc tasmai dadyām ahaṃ yo me prabrūyāt keśavārjunaua etā vācaḥ subahuśaḥ karṇa uccārayan yudhic dadhmau sāgarasaṃbhūtaṃ susvanaṃ śaṅkham uttamama tā vācaḥ sūtaputrasya tathā yuktā niśamya tuc duryodhano mahārāja prahṛṣṭaḥ sānugo bhavata tato dundubhinirghoṣo mṛdaṅgānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥc siṃhanādaḥ savāditraḥ kuñjarāṇāṃ ca nisvanaḥa prādurāsīt tadā rājaṃs tvatsainye bharatarṣabhac yodhānāṃ saṃprahṛṣṭānāṃ tathā samabhavat svanaḥa tathā prahṛṣṭe sainye tu plavamānaṃ mahārathamc vikatthamānaṃ samare rādheyam arikarśaname madrarājaḥ prahasyedaṃ vacanaṃ pratyabhāṣataa mā sūtaputra mānena sauvarṇaṃ hastiṣaḍgavamc prayaccha puruṣāyādya drakṣyasi tvaṃ dhanaṃjayama bālyād iva tvaṃ tyajasi vasu vaiśravaṇo yathāc ayatnenaiva rādheya draṣṭāsy adya dhanaṃjayama parāsṛjasi mithyā kiṃ kiṃ ca tvaṃ bahu mūḍhavatc apātradāne ye doṣās tān mohān nāvabudhyasea yat pravedayase vittaṃ bahutvena khalu tvayāc śakyaṃ bahuvidhair yajñair yaṣṭuṃ sūta yajasva taiḥa yac ca prārthayase hantuṃ kṛṣṇau mohān mṛṣaiva tatc na hi śuśruma saṃmarde kroṣṭrā siṃhau nipātitaua aprārthitaṃ prārthayase suhṛdo na hi santi tec ye tvāṃ na vārayanty āśu prapatantaṃ hutāśanea kālakāryaṃ na jānīṣe kālapakvo sy asaṃśayamc bahvabaddham akarṇīyaṃ ko hi brūyāj jijīviṣuḥa samudrataraṇaṃ dorbhyāṃ kaṇṭhe baddhvā yathā śilāmc giryagrād vā nipatanaṃ tādṛk tava cikīrṣitama sahitaḥ sarvayodhais tvaṃ vyūḍhānīkaiḥ surakṣitaḥc dhanaṃjayena yudhyasva śreyaś cet prāptum icchasia hitārthaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya bravīmi tvā na hiṃsayāc śraddhatsvaitan mayā proktaṃ yadi te sti jijīviṣā karṇa uvācaa svavīrye haṃ parāśvasya prārthayāmy arjunaṃ raṇec tvaṃ tu mitramukhaḥ śatrur māṃ bhīṣayitum icchasia na mām asmād abhiprāyāt kaś cid adya nivartayetc apīndro vajram udyamya kiṃ nu martyaḥ kariṣyati saṃjaya uvācaa iti karṇasya vākyānte śalyaḥ prāhottaraṃ vacaḥc cukopayiṣur atyarthaṃ karṇaṃ madreśvaraḥ punaḥa yadā vai tvāṃ phalgunaveganunnājyācoditā hastavatā visṛṣṭāḥc anvetāraḥ kaṅkapatrāḥ śitāgrāstadā tapsyasy arjunasyābhiyogāta yadā divyaṃ dhanur ādāya pārthaḥprabhāsayan pṛtanāṃ savyasācīc tvām ardayeta niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkaistadā paścāt tapsyase sūtaputraa bālaś candraṃ mātur aṅke śayānoyathā kaś cit prārthayate pahartumc tadvan mohād yatamāno rathasthastvaṃ prārthayasy arjunam adya jetumd khanyād asiṃ tīkṣṇadhāraṃ yathājñaḥd sutejanaṃ nihitaṃ vai pṛthivyāmd tathā khanasy adya śitān pṛṣatkānd yaḥ prārthayasy arjuneneha yuddhama triśūlam āśliṣya sutīkṣṇadhāraṃsarvāṇi gātrāṇi nigharṣasi tvamc sutīkṣṇadhāropamakarmaṇā tvaṃyuyutsase yo rjunenādya karṇaa siddhaṃ siṃhaṃ kesariṇaṃ bṛhantaṃbālo mūḍhaḥ kṣudramṛgas tarasvīc samāhvayet tadvad etat tavādyasamāhvānaṃ sūtaputrārjunasyaa mā sūtaputrāhvaya rājaputraṃmahāvīryaṃ kesariṇaṃ yathaivac vane sṛgālaḥ piśitasya tṛptomā pārtham āsādya vinaṅkṣyasi tvama īṣādantaṃ mahānāgaṃ prabhinnakaraṭāmukhamc śaśakāhvayase yuddhe karṇa pārthaṃ dhanaṃjayama bilasthaṃ kṛṣṇasarpaṃ tvaṃ bālyāt kāṣṭhena vidhyasic mahāviṣaṃ pūrṇakośaṃ yat pārthaṃ yoddhum icchasia siṃhaṃ kesariṇaṃ kruddham atikramyābhinardasic sṛgāla iva mūḍhatvān nṛsiṃhaṃ karṇa pāṇḍavama suparṇaṃ patagaśreṣṭhaṃ vainateyaṃ tarasvinamc laṭvevāhvayase pāte karṇa pārthaṃ dhanaṃjayama sarvāmbhonilayaṃ bhīmam ūrmimantaṃ jhaṣāyutamc candrodaye vivartantam aplavaḥ saṃtitīrṣasia ṛṣabhaṃ dundubhigrīvaṃ tīkṣṇaśṛṅgaṃ prahāriṇamc vatsa āhvayase yuddhe karṇa pārthaṃ dhanaṃjayamd yathā vatsataro bhūtvā jātaskandhena śuṣmiṇād yuddham icched gopatinā tathecchasi kirīṭināa mahāghoṣaṃ mahāmeghaṃ darduraḥ pratinardasic kāmatoyapradaṃ loke naraparjanyam arjunama yathā ca svagṛhasthaḥ śvā vyāghraṃ vanagataṃ bhaṣetc tathā tvaṃ bhaṣase karṇa naravyāghraṃ dhanaṃjayama sṛgālo pi vane karṇa śaśaiḥ parivṛto vasanc manyate siṃham ātmānaṃ yāvat siṃhaṃ na paśyatia tathā tvam api rādheya siṃham ātmānam icchasic apaśyañ śatrudamanaṃ naravyāghraṃ dhanaṃjayama vyāghraṃ tvaṃ manyase tmānaṃ yāvat kṛṣṇau na paśyasic samāsthitāv ekarathe sūryācandramasāv ivaa yāvad gāṇḍīvanirghoṣaṃ na śṛṇoṣi mahāhavec tāvad eva tvayā karṇa śakyaṃ vaktuṃ yathecchasia rathaśabdadhanuḥśabdair nādayantaṃ diśo daśac nardantam iva śārdūlaṃ dṛṣṭvā kroṣṭā bhaviṣyasia nityam eva sṛgālas tvaṃ nityaṃ siṃho dhanaṃjayaḥc vīrapradveṣaṇān mūḍha nityaṃ kroṣṭeva lakṣyasea yathākhuḥ syād biḍālaś ca śvā vyāghraś ca balābalec yathā sṛgālaḥ siṃhaś ca yathā ca śaśakuñjaraua yathānṛtaṃ ca satyaṃ ca yathā cāpi viṣāmṛtec tathā tvam api pārthaś ca prakhyātāv ātmakarmabhiḥ saṃjaya uvācaa adhikṣiptas tu rādheyaḥ śalyenāmitatejasāc śalyam āha susaṃkruddho vākśalyam avadhārayana guṇān guṇavataḥ śalya guṇavān vetti nāguṇaḥc tvaṃ tu nityaṃ guṇair hīnaḥ kiṃ jñāsyasy aguṇo guṇāna arjunasya mahāstrāṇi krodhaṃ vīryaṃ dhanuḥ śarānc ahaṃ śalyābhijānāmi na tvaṃ jānāsi tat tathāc   vikramaṃ ca mahātmanaḥc tathā kṛṣṇasya māhātmyam ṛṣabhasya mahīkṣitāmc yathāhaṃ śalya jānāmia evam evātmano vīryam ahaṃ vīryaṃ ca pāṇḍavec jānann evāhvaye yuddhe śalya nāgniṃ pataṃgavata asti cāyam iṣuḥ śalya supuṅkho raktabhojanaḥc ekatūṇīśayaḥ patrī sudhautaḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥa śete candanapūrṇena pūjito bahulāḥ samāḥc āheyo viṣavān ugro narāśvadvipasaṃghahāa ekavīro mahāraudras tanutrāsthividāraṇaḥc nirbhindyāṃ yena ruṣṭo ham api meruṃ mahāgirima tam ahaṃ jātu nāsyeyam anyasmin phalgunād ṛtec kṛṣṇād vā devakīputrāt satyaṃ cātra śṛṇuṣva mea tenāham iṣuṇā śalya vāsudevadhanaṃjayauc yotsye paramasaṃkruddhas tat karma sadṛśaṃ mamaa sarveṣāṃ vāsudevānāṃ kṛṣṇe lakṣmīḥ pratiṣṭhitāc sarveṣāṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ jayaḥ pārthe pratiṣṭhitaḥe ubhayaṃ tat samāsādya ko tivartitum arhatia tāv etau puruṣavyāghrau sametau syandane sthitauc mām ekam abhisaṃyātau sujātaṃ śalya paśya mea pitṛṣvasāmātulajau bhrātarāv aparājitauc maṇī sūtra iva protau draṣṭāsi nihatau mayāa arjune gāṇḍivaṃ kṛṣṇe cakraṃ tārkṣyakapidhvajauc bhīrūṇāṃ trāsajananau śalya harṣakarau mamaa tvaṃ tu duṣprakṛtir mūḍho mahāyuddheṣv akovidaḥc bhayāvatīrṇaḥ saṃtrāsād abaddhaṃ bahu bhāṣasea saṃstauṣi tvaṃ tu kenāpi hetunā tau kudeśajac tau hatvā samare hantā tvām addhā sahabāndhavama pāpadeśaja durbuddhe kṣudra kṣatriyapāṃsanac suhṛd bhūtvā ripuḥ kiṃ māṃ kṛṣṇābhyāṃ bhīṣayann asia tau vā mamādya hantārau hantāsmi samare sthitauc nāhaṃ bibhemi kṛṣṇābhyāṃ vijānann ātmano balama vāsudevasahasraṃ vā phalgunānāṃ śatāni cac aham eko haniṣyāmi joṣam āssva kudeśajaa striyo bālāś ca vṛddhāś ca prāyaḥ vaktavyeṣu kuvartmasua madrakāḥ sindhusauvīrā dharmaṃ vidyuḥ kathaṃ tv ihac pāpadeśodbhavā mlecchā dharmāṇām avicakṣaṇāḥa eṣa mukhyatamo dharmaḥ kṣatriyasyeti naḥ śrutamc yad ājau nihataḥ śete sadbhiḥ samabhipūjitaḥa āyudhānāṃ saṃparāye yan mucyeyam ahaṃ tataḥc na me sa prathamaḥ kalpo nidhane svargam icchataḥa so haṃ priyaḥ sakhā cāsmi dhārtarāṣṭrasya dhīmataḥc tadarthe hi mama prāṇā yac ca me teṣāṃ dharmaḥ kathaṃ bhaveta iti śalya vijānīhi hanta bhūyo bravīmi tec yad anyo py uktavān asmān brāhmaṇaḥ kurusaṃsadia pañca nadyo vahanty etā yatra pīluvanāny apic śatadruś ca vipāśā ca tathāb śrāddhatarpaṇakarmeṣu te viprā yatra saṃsthitāḥb tat sarvaṃ viphalībhūtam iti satyavatī śrutiḥc teṣāṃ pranaṣṭadharmāṇāṃ bāhlīkānām iti śrutiḥa brāhmaṇena tathā proktaṃ viduṣā sādhusaṃsadic kāṣṭhakuṇḍeṣu bāhlīkā mṛṇmayeṣu ca bhuñjatee saktuvāṭyāvalipteṣu śvādilīḍheṣu nirghṛṇāḥa āvikaṃ cauṣṭrikaṃ caiva kṣīraṃ gārdabham eva cac tadvikārāṃś ca bāhlīkāḥ khādanti ca pibanti caa putrasaṃkariṇo acyutasthalec tadvad bhūtilaye snātvā kathaṃ svargaṃ gamiṣyatia pañca nadyo vahanty etā yatra niḥsṛtya parvatātc āraṭṭā nāma bāhlīkā na teṣv āryo dvyahaṃ vaseta bahiś ca nāma hlīkaś ca vipāśāyāṃ piśācakauc tayor apatyaṃ bāhlīkā naiṣā sṛṣṭiḥ prajāpateḥd te kathaṃ vividhān dharmāñ jñāsyante hīnayonayaḥa kāraskarān mahiṣakān kaliṅgān kīkaṭāṭavīnc karkoṭakān vīrakāṃś ca durdharmāṃś ca vivarjayeta iti tīrthānusartāraṃ rākṣasī kā cid abravītc ekarātrā śamīgehe maholūkhalamekhalāa āraṭṭā nāma te deśā bāhlīkā nāma te janāḥb brāhmaṇāpasadā yatra tulyakālāḥ prajāpateḥb vedā na teṣāṃ vedyaṃ ca yajñā yajanam eva cab vrātyānāṃ dāśamīyānām annaṃ devā na bhuñjateb prasthalā madragāndhārā āraṭṭā nāmataḥ khaśāḥc vasātisindhusauvīrā iti prāyo vikutsitāḥa uta śalya vijānīhi hanta bhūyo bravīmi tec ucyamānaṃ mayā samyak tad ekāgramanāḥ śṛṇua brāhmaṇaḥ śilpino geham abhyagacchat purātithiḥc ācāraṃ tatra saṃprekṣya prītaḥ śilpinam abravīta mayā himavataḥ śṛṅgam ekenādhyuṣitaṃ ciramc dṛṣṭāś ca bahavo deśā nānādharmasamākulāḥa na ca kena ca dharmeṇa virudhyante prajā imāḥc sarve hi te bruvan dharmaṃ yathoktaṃ vedapāragaiḥa aṭatā tu sadā deśān nānādharmasamākulānc āgacchatā mahārāja bāhlīkeṣu niśāmitama tatraiva brāhmaṇo bhūtvā tato bhavati kṣatriyaḥc vaiśyaḥ śūdraś ca bāhlīkas tato bhavati nāpitaḥa nāpitaś ca tato bhūtvā punar bhavati brāhmaṇaḥc dvijo bhūtvā ca tatraiva punar dāso pi śalya vijānīhi hanta bhūyo bravīmi tec yad apy anyo bravīd vākyaṃ bāhlīkānāṃ vikutsitama satī purā hṛtā kā cid āraṭṭā kila dasyubhiḥc adharmataś copayātā sā tān abhyaśapat tataḥa bālāṃ bandhumatīṃ yan mām adharmeṇopagacchathac tasmān nāryo bhaviṣyanti bandhakyo vai kuleṣu vaḥe na caivāsmāt pramokṣyadhvaṃ ghorāt pāpān narādhamāḥf tasmāt teṣāṃ bhāgaharā bhāgineyā na sūnavaḥa kuravaḥ sahapāñcālāḥ śālvā matsyāḥ sanaimiṣāḥc kosalāḥ kāśayo ṅgāś ca kaliṅgā magadhās tathāa cedayaś ca mahābhāgā dharmaṃ jānanti śāśvatamc nānādeśeṣu santaś ca prāyo bāhyā layād ṛtea ā matsyebhyaḥ kurupāñcāladeśyāā naimiṣāc cedayo ye viśiṣṭāḥc dharmaṃ purāṇam upajīvanti santomadrān ṛte pañcanadāṃś ca jihmāna evaṃ vidvan dharmakathāṃś ca rājaṃstūṣṇīṃbhūto jaḍavac chalya bhūyāḥc tvaṃ tasya goptā ca janasya rājāṣaḍbhāgahartā śubhaduṣkṛtasyaa atha vā duṣkṛtasya tvaṃ hartā teṣām arakṣitāc rakṣitā puṇyabhāg rājā prajānāṃ tvaṃ tv apuṇyabhāka pūjyamāne purā dharme sarvadeśeṣu śāśvatec dharmaṃ pāñcanadaṃ dṛṣṭvā dhig ity āha pitāmahaḥa vrātyānāṃ dāśamīyānāṃ kṛte py aśubhakarmaṇāmb brahmaṇā nindite dharme sa tvaṃ loke kim abravīḥc iti pāñcanadaṃ dharmam avamene pitāmahaḥe svadharmastheṣu varṇeṣu so py etaṃ nābhipūjayeta uta śalya vijānīhi hanta bhūyo bravīmi tec kalmāṣapādaḥ sarasi nimajjan rākṣaso bravīta kṣatriyasya malaṃ bhaikṣaṃ brāhmaṇasyānṛtaṃ malamc malaṃ pṛthivyā bāhlīkāḥ strīṇāṃ madrastriyo malama nimajjamānam uddhṛtya kaś cid rājā niśācaramc apṛcchat tena cākhyātaṃ proktavān yan nibodha tata mānuṣāṇāṃ malaṃ mlecchā mlecchānāṃ mauṣṭikā malamc mauṣṭikānāṃ malaṃ śaṇḍāḥ śaṇḍānāṃ rājayājakāḥa rājayājakayājyānāṃ madrakāṇāṃ ca yan malamc tad bhaved vai tava malaṃ yady asmān na vimuñcasia iti rakṣopasṛṣṭeṣu viṣavīryahateṣu cac rākṣasaṃ bheṣajaṃ proktaṃ saṃsiddhaṃ vacanottarama brāhmaṃ pāñcālāḥ kauraveyāḥ svadharmaḥsatyaṃ matsyāḥ śūrasenāś ca yajñaḥc prācyā dāsā vṛṣalā dākṣiṇātyāḥstenā bāhlīkāḥ saṃkarā vai surāṣṭrāḥa kṛtaghnatā paravittāpahāraḥsurāpānaṃ gurudārāvamarśaḥb dharmamc kaliṅgakāś cāṅgakā māgadhāś caśiṣṭān dharmān upajīvanti vṛddhāḥa prācīṃ diśaṃ śritā devā jātavedaḥpurogamāḥc dakṣiṇāṃ pitaro guptāṃ yamena śubhakarmaṇāa pratīcīṃ varuṇaḥ pāti pālayann asurān balīc udīcīṃ bhagavān somo brahmaṇyo brāhmaṇaiḥ sahaa rakṣaḥpiśācān himavān guhyakān gandhamādanaḥb tathā rakṣaḥ piśācāś ca himavantaṃ nagottamamb guhyakāś ca mahārāja parvataṃ gandhamādanamc dhruvaḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni viṣṇur lokāñ janārdanaḥd naiva pāñcanadān pāpān samadān pāti kaś canaa iṅgitajñāś ca magadhāḥ prekṣitajñāś ca kosalāḥc ardhoktāḥ kurupāñcālāḥ śālvāḥ kṛtsnānuśāsanāḥe pārvatīyāś ca viṣamā yathaiva girayas tathāa sarvajñā yavanā rājañ śūrāś caiva viśeṣataḥc mlecchāḥ svasaṃjñāniyatā nānukta itaro janaḥa pratirabdhās tu bāhlīkā na ca ke cana madrakāḥc sa tvam etādṛśaḥ śalya nottaraṃ vaktum arhasid pṛthivyāṃ sarvadeśānāṃ madrako malam ucyated tathā strīṇāṃ ca sarvāsāṃ madrikā mala ucyated sīdhoḥ pānaṃ gurutalpāvamardod bhrūṇahatyā paravittāpahāraḥa etaj jñātvā joṣam āssva pratīpaṃ mā sma vai kṛthāḥc sa tvāṃ pūrvam ahaṃ hatvā haniṣye keśavārjunaud evaṃ jñātvā joṣam āssva pratīpaṃd mā sma krudhyaḥ pāpabhṛtāṃ variṣṭhaḥd pūrvaṃ hatvā tvāṃ saputraṃ balaiś cad paścād dhaṃsye vāsudevārjunau ca śalya uvācaa āturāṇāṃ parityāgaḥ svadārasutavikrayaḥc aṅgeṣu vartate karṇa yeṣām adhipatir bhavāna rathātirathasaṃkhyāyāṃ yat tvā bhīṣmas tadābravītc tān viditvātmano doṣān nirmanyur bhava mā krudhaḥa sarvatra brāhmaṇāḥ santi santi sarvatra kṣatriyāḥc vaiśyāḥ śūdrās tathā karṇa striyaḥ sādhvyaś ca suvratāḥa ramante copahāsena puruṣāḥ puruṣaiḥ sahac anyonyam avatakṣanto deśe deśe samaithunāḥa paravācyeṣu nipuṇaḥ sarvo bhavati sarvadāc ātmavācyaṃ na jānīte jānann api vimuhyatid sarvatra santi rājānaḥ svaṃ svaṃ dharmam anuvratāḥd durmanuṣyān nigṛhṇanti santi sarvatra dhārmikāḥd na karṇa deśasāmānyāt sarvaḥ pāpaṃ niṣevated saṃjaya uvācad yādṛśāḥ svasvabhāvena devā api na tādṛśāḥd tato duryodhano rājā karṇaśalyāv avārayatd sakhibhāvena rādheyaṃ śalyaṃ svāñjalyakena cad tato nivāritaḥ karṇo dhārtarāṣṭreṇa māriṣa saṃjaya uvācaa karṇo pi nottaraṃ prāha śalyo py abhimukhaḥ parānc punaḥ prahasya rādheyaḥ punar yāhīty acodayatd idaṃ tava mayākhyātaṃ kṣiptena na tv asauhṛdātd tataḥ prayāntaṃ rādheyaṃ madrarājaḥ smayann ivad avasphūrjya idaṃ vākyam abravīt kurusaṃnidhaud camūṃ tavemāṃ vipulāṃ samṛddhāmd asaṃkhyeyām aśvanarākulāṃ cad tathā praveṣṭā samare dhanaṃjayaḥd kakṣaṃ dahan dīpta ivāśrayāśīḥd rathe sthitau vīra raṇe vareṇyaud siṃhaskandhau lohitapadmanetraud draṣṭā bhavān adya vinā prayatnātd tathā hi me śakunā vedayanti saṃjaya uvācaa tataḥ parānīkabhidaṃ vyūham apratimaṃ paraiḥc samīkṣya karṇaḥ pārthānāṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnābhirakṣitama prayayau rathaghoṣeṇa siṃhanādaraveṇa cac vāditrāṇāṃ ca ninadaiḥ kampayann iva medinīma vepamāna iva krodhād yuddhaśauṇḍaḥ paraṃtapaḥc pativyūhya mahātejā yathāvad bharatarṣabhaa vyadhamat pāṇḍavīṃ senām āsurīṃ maghavān ivac yudhiṣṭhiraṃ cābhibhavann asapavyaṃ cakāra had karṇasya rathaghoṣeṇa maurvīniṣpeṣaṇena cad saṃgraheṇa ca raśmīnāṃ samakampanta sṛñjayāḥd tāni sarvāṇi sainyāni karṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā viśāṃ pated babhūvuḥ saṃprahṛṣṭāni tāvakāni yuyutsayād aśrūyanta tato vācas tāvakānāṃ viśāṃ pated karṇārjunamahāyuddham etad adya bhaviṣyatid adya duryodhano rājā hatāmitro bhaviṣyatid adya karṇaṃ raṇe dṛṣṭvā phalguno vidraviṣyatid adya tāvad rathaṃ yuddhe karṇasyaivānugāminaḥd karṇabāṇamayaṃ yuddhaṃ bhīmaṃ drakṣyāma saṃyuged cirakālodyatam idam adyedānīṃ bhaviṣyatid adya drakṣyāma saṃgrāmaṃ ghoraṃ devāsuropamamd adyedānīṃ mahad yuddhaṃ bhaviṣyati bhayānakamd adyedānīṃ jayo nityam ekasyaikasya vā raṇed arjunaṃ kila rādheyo vadhiṣyati mahāraṇed atha vā kaṃ naraṃ loke na spṛśanti manorathāḥd ity uktvā vividhā vācaḥ kuravaḥ kurunandanad ājaghnuḥ paṭahāṃś caiva tūryāṃś caiva
