dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa kathaṃ saṃjaya rādheyaḥ pratyavyūhata pāṇḍavānc dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhān vīrān bhīmasenābhirakṣitānd sarvān eva maheṣvāsān ajayyān amarair apia ke ca prapakṣau pakṣau vā mama sainyasya saṃjayac pravibhajya yathānyāyaṃ kathaṃ vā samavasthitāḥa kathaṃ pāṇḍusutāś cāpi pratyavyūhanta māmakānc kathaṃ caitan mahāyuddhaṃ prāvartata sudāruṇama kva ca bībhatsur abhavad yat karṇo yād yudhiṣṭhiramc ko hy arjunasya sāṃnidhye śakto bhyetuṃ yudhiṣṭhirama sarvabhūtāni yo hy ekaḥ khāṇḍave jitavān purāc kas tam anyatra rādheyāt pratiyudhyej jijīviṣuḥ saṃjaya uvācaa śṛṇu vyūhasya racanām arjunaś ca yathā gataḥc paridāya nṛpaṃ tebhyaḥ saṃgrāmaś cābhavad yathāa kṛpaḥ śāradvato rājan māgadhaś ca tarasvinaḥc sātvataḥ kṛtavarmā ca dakṣiṇaṃ pakṣam āśritāḥa teṣāṃ prapakṣe śakunir ulūkaś ca mahārathaḥc sādibhir vimalaprāsais tavānīkam arakṣatāma gāndhāribhir asaṃbhrāntaiḥ pārvatīyaiś ca durjayaiḥc śalabhānām iva vrātaiḥ piśācair iva durdṛśaiḥa catustriṃśat sahasrāṇi rathānām anivartināmc saṃśaptakā yuddhaśauṇḍā vāmaṃ pārśvam apālayana samuccitās tava sutaiḥ kṛṣṇārjunajighāṃsavaḥc teṣāṃ prapakṣaḥ kāmbojāḥ śakāś ca yavanaiḥ sahaa nideśāt sūtaputrasya sarathāḥ sāśvapattayaḥc āhvayanto rjunaṃ tasthuḥ keśavaṃ ca mahābalama madhyesenāmukhaṃ karṇo vyavātiṣṭhata daṃśitaḥc citravarmāṅgadaḥ sragvī pālayan dhvajinīmukhama rakṣyamāṇaḥ susaṃrabdhaiḥ putraiḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥc vāhinīpramukhaṃ vīraḥ saṃprakarṣann aśobhataa ayoratnir mahābāhuḥ sūryavaiśvānaradyutiḥc mahādvipaskandhagataḥ piṅgalaḥ priyadarśanaḥe duḥśāsano vṛtaḥ sainyaiḥ sthito vyūhasya pṛṣṭhataḥa tam anvayān mahārāja svayaṃ duryodhano nṛpaḥc citrāśvaiś citrasaṃnāhaiḥ sodaryair abhirakṣitaḥa rakṣyamāṇo mahāvīryaiḥ sahitair madrakekayaiḥc aśobhata mahārāja devair iva śatakratuḥa aśvatthāmā kurūṇāṃ ca ye pravīrā mahārathāḥc nityamattāś ca mātaṅgāḥ śūrair mlecchair adhiṣṭhitāḥd ārohaṇair mahāmātrais tomarāṅkuśapāṇibhiḥe anvayus tad rathānīkaṃ kṣaranta iva toyadāḥa te dhvajair vaijayantībhir jvaladbhiḥ paramāyudhaiḥc sādibhiś cāsthitā rejur drumavanta ivācalāḥa teṣāṃ padātināgānāṃ pādarakṣāḥ sahasraśaḥc paṭṭiśāsidharāḥ śūrā babhūvur anivartinaḥd bhiṇḍipāladharāś caiva śūlahastāḥ sucakriṇaḥd teṣāṃ samāgamo ghoro devāsuraraṇopamaḥa sādibhiḥ syandanair nāgair adhikaṃ samalaṃkṛtaiḥc sa vyūharājo vibabhau devāsuracamūpamaḥa bārhaspatyaḥ suvihito nāyakena vipaścitāc nṛtyatīva mahāvyūhaḥ pareṣām ādadhad bhayama tasya pakṣaprapakṣebhyo niṣpatanti yuyutsavaḥc pattyaśvarathamātaṅgāḥ prāvṛṣīva balāhakāḥa tataḥ senāmukhe karṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥc dhanaṃjayam amitraghnam ekavīram uvāca haa paśyārjuna mahāvyūhaṃ karṇena vihitaṃ raṇec yuktaṃ pakṣaiḥ prapakṣaiś ca senānīkaṃ prakāśatea tad etad vai samālokya pratyamitraṃ mahad balamc yathā nābhibhavaty asmāṃs tathā nītir vidhīyatāma evam ukto rjuno rājñā prāñjalir nṛpam abravītc yathā bhavān āha tathā tat sarvaṃ na tad anyathāa yas tv asya vihito ghātas taṃ kariṣyāmi bhāratac pradhānavadha evāsya vināśas taṃ karomy aham yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa tasmāt tvam eva rādheyaṃ bhīmasenaḥ suyodhanamc vṛṣasenaṃ ca nakulaḥ sahadevo pi saubalama duḥśāsanaṃ śatānīko hārdikyaṃ śinipuṃgavaḥc dhṛṣṭadyumnas tathā drauṇiṃ svayaṃ yāsyāmy ahaṃ kṛpama draupadeyā dhārtarāṣṭrāñ śiṣṭān saha śikhaṇḍināc te te ca tāṃs tān ahitān asmākaṃ ghnantu māmakāḥ saṃjaya uvācaa ity ukto dharmarājena tathety uktvā dhanaṃjayaḥc vyādideśa svasainyāni svayaṃ cāgāc camūmukhamd arkavaiśvānaraprakhyaṃ samucchritapatākinamd agnir vaiśvānaraḥ pūrvo brahmenduḥ saptitāṃ gataḥd tasmād yaḥ prathamaṃ jātas taṃ devā brāhmaṇā viduḥd tam ādyaṃ prathamaṃ sṛṣṭaṃ brahmaṇā lokakartṛṇād brahmeśānendravaruṇān kramaśo yo vahat purād tam ādyaṃ ratham āsthāya prayātau keśavārjunaud dhanaṃjayo mahārāja dakṣiṇaṃ pakṣam āsthitaḥd bhīmaseno mahābāhur vāmaṃ pakṣam upāśritaḥd sātyakir draupadeyāś ca svayaṃ rājā ca pāṇḍavaḥd vyūhasya pramukhe tasthuḥ svenānīkena saṃvṛtāḥd svabalenārisainyaṃ tat pratyavasthāpya pāṇḍavaḥd pratyavyūhat puraskṛtya dhṛṣṭadyumnaśikhaṇḍinaud tat sādināgakalilaṃ padātirathasaṃkulamd dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhaṃ vyūham aśobhata mahābalama atha taṃ ratham āyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvātyadbhutadarśanamc uvācādhirathiṃ śalyaḥ punas taṃ yuddhadurmadamd avasthitam idaṃ vākyaṃ madrarājaḥ smayann ivaa ayaṃ sa ratha āyāti śvetāśvaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥb durvāraḥ sarvasainyānāṃ vipākaḥ karmaṇām ivac nighnann amitrān kaunteyo yaṃ yaṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasia śrūyate tumulaḥ śabdo rathanemisvano mahānb dhruvam etau mahātmānau vāsudevadhanaṃjayauc eṣa reṇuḥ samudbhūto divam āvṛtya tiṣṭhatia cakranemipraṇunnā ca kampate karṇa medinīb camūṃ tavemāṃ vipulāṃ samṛddhāmb asaṃkhyeyām aśrukulākulāṃ cab dhruvaṃ pravekṣaty ajito dhanaṃjayaḥb kathaṃ dahan dīpta ivāśrayāśaḥb amī hayāś candramarīcivarṇāḥb kṛṣṇapratodena pratudyamānāḥb vahanti bībhatsum udārasattvāḥb sitaprabhāḥ svabhram ivābhrasaṃghāḥc pravāty eṣa mahāvāyur abhitas tava vāhinīme kravyādā vyāharanty ete mṛgāḥ kurvanti bhairavama paśya karṇa mahāghoraṃ bhayadaṃ lomaharṣaṇamc kabandhaṃ meghasaṃkāśaṃ bhānum āvṛtya saṃsthitama paśya yūthair bahuvidhair mṛgāṇāṃ sarvatodiśamc balibhir dṛptaśārdūlair ādityo bhinirīkṣyated rarāsa dīptalāṅgūlam ādityam abhitaḥ sthitama paśya kaṅkāṃś ca gṛdhrāṃś ca samavetān sahasraśaḥb ādityam abhivīkṣante hy aśivāḥ karṇa satvarāḥc sthitān abhimukhān ghorān anyonyam abhibhāṣataḥa sitāś cāśvāḥ samāyuktās tava karṇa mahārathec pradarāḥ prajvalanty ete dhvajaś caiva prakampatea udīryato hayān paśya mahākāyān mahājavānc plavamānān darśanīyān ākāśe garuḍān ivaa dhruvam eṣu nimitteṣu bhūmim āvṛtya pārthivāḥc svapsyanti nihatāḥ karṇa śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa śaṅkhānāṃ tumulaḥ śabdaḥ śrūyate lomaharṣaṇaḥc ānakānāṃ ca rādheya mṛdaṅgānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥa bāṇaśabdān bahuvidhān narāśvarathanisvanānc jyātalatreṣuśabdāṃś ca śṛṇu karṇa mahātmanāma hemarūpyapramṛṣṭānāṃ vāsasāṃ śilpinirmitāḥc nānāvarṇā rathe bhānti śvasanena prakampitāḥa sahemacandratārārkāḥ patākāḥ kiṅkiṇīyutāḥc paśya karṇārjunasyaitāḥ saudāminya ivāmbudea dhvajāḥ kaṇakaṇāyante vātenābhisamīritāḥb vibhrājanti raṇe karṇa vimāne devatā yathāc sapatākā rathāś cāpi pāñcālānāṃ mahātmanāmd paśya kuntīsutaṃ vīraṃ bībhatsum aparājitamd pradharṣayitum āyāntaṃ kapipravaraketanamd eṣa dhvajāgre pārthasya prekṣamāṇaḥ samantataḥd dṛśyate vānaro bhīmo dviṣatām aghavardhanaḥd etac cakraṃ gadā śārṅgaṃ śaṅkhaḥ kṛṣṇasya dhīmataḥd atyarthaṃ bhrājate kṛṣṇe kaustubhas tu maṇis tataḥd eṣa śārṅgagadāpāṇir vāsudevo tivīryavānd vāhayann eti turagān pāṇḍurān vātaraṃhasaḥd etat kūjati gāṇḍīvaṃ vikṛṣṭaṃ savyasācinād ete hastavatā muktā ghnanty amitrāñ śitāḥ śarāḥd viśālāyatatāmrākṣaiḥ pūrṇacandranibhānanaiḥd eṣā bhūḥ kīryate rājñāṃ śirobhir apalāyināmd ete suparighākārāḥ puṇyagandhānulepanāḥd udyatāyudhaśauṇḍānāṃ pātyante sāyudhā bhujāḥd nirastanetrajihvāntā vājinaḥ saha sādibhiḥd patitāḥ pātyamānāś ca kṣitau kṣīṇāś ca śerated ete parvataśṛṅgāṇāṃ tulyarūpā hatā dvipāḥd saṃchinnabhinnāḥ pārthena prapanty adrayo yathād gandharvanagarākārā rathā hatanareśvarāḥd vimānānīva puṇyāni svargiṇāṃ nipatanty amīd vyākulīkṛtam atyarthaṃ paśya sainyaṃ kirīṭinād nānāmṛgasahasrāṇāṃ yūthaṃ kesariṇā yathād ghnanty ete pārthivān vīrāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ samabhidrutāḥa nāgāśvarathapattyaughāṃs tāvakān samabhighnataḥc dhvajāgraṃ dṛśyate tv asya jyāśabdaś cāpi śrūyatea adya draṣṭāsi taṃ vīraṃ śvetāśvaṃ kṛṣṇasārathimc nighnantaṃ śātravān saṃkhye yaṃ karṇa paripṛcchasia adya tau puruṣavyāghrau lohitākṣau paraṃtapauc vāsudevārjunau karṇa draṣṭāsy ekarathasthitaud yatra kṛṣṇo jagannātho yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥd yatra gāṇḍīvadhṛk pārtho kathaṃ tvaṃ haṃsi tad balama sārathir yasya vārṣṇeyo gāṇḍīvaṃ yasya kārmukamc taṃ ced dhantāsi rādheya tvaṃ no rājā bhaviṣyasid rathanemisvanaḥ saṃkhye meghasyevābhigarjitaḥd śrūyate vai yathā vyaktam etau kṛṣṇadhanaṃjayaua eṣa saṃśaptakāhūtas tān evābhimukho gataḥc karoti kadanaṃ caiṣāṃ saṃgrāme dviṣatāṃ balīe iti bruvāṇaṃ madreśaṃ karṇaḥ prāhātimanyumāna paśya saṃśaptakaiḥ kruddhaiḥ sarvataḥ samabhidrutaḥc eṣa sūrya ivāmbhodaiś channaḥ pārtho na dṛśyatee etad anto rjunaḥ śalya nimagnaḥ śokasāgare śalya uvācaa varuṇaṃ ko mbhasā hanyād indhanena ca pāvakamc ko vānilaṃ nigṛhṇīyāt pibed vā ko mahārṇavama īdṛg rūpam ahaṃ manye pārthasya yudhi nigrahamc na hi śakyo rjuno jetuṃ sendraiḥ sarvaiḥ surāsuraiḥa athaivaṃ paritoṣas te vācoktvā sumanā bhavac na sa śakyo yudhā jetum anyaṃ kuru manorathama bāhubhyām uddhared bhūmiṃ dahet kruddha imāḥ prajāḥc pātayet tridivād devān yo rjunaṃ samare jayeta paśya kuntīsutaṃ vīraṃ bhīmam akliṣṭakāriṇamc prabhāsantaṃ mahābāhuṃ sthitaṃ merum ivācalama amarṣī nityasaṃrabdhaś ciraṃ vairam anusmaranc eṣa bhīmo jayaprepsur yudhi tiṣṭhati vīryavāna eṣa dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭho dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥc tiṣṭhaty asukaraḥ saṃkhye paraiḥ parapuraṃjayaḥa etau ca puruṣavyāghrāv aśvināv iva sodarauc nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca tiṣṭhato yudhi durjayaua dṛśyanta ete kārṣṇeyāḥ pañca pañcācalā ivac vyavasthitā yotsyamānāḥ sarve rjunasamā yudhia ete drupadaputrāś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamāḥc hīnāḥ satyajitā vīrās tiṣṭhanti paramaujasaḥd asāv indra ivāsahyaḥ sātyakiḥ sātvatāṃ varaḥd yuyutsur upayāty asmān kruddhāntakasamaḥ puraḥd yatra kṛṣṇārjunau vīrau yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥd tatra dharmaś ca satyaṃ ca yato dharmas tato jayaḥa iti saṃvadator eva tayoḥ puruṣasiṃhayoḥc te sene samasajjetāṃ gaṅgāyamunavad bhṛśamd tadāsthitam anājñāya pratyamitramahadbalamd avyūhatārjuno vyūhaṃ putrasya tava durjayam dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa tathā vyūḍheṣv anīkeṣu saṃsakteṣu ca saṃjayac saṃśaptakān kathaṃ pārtho gataḥ karṇaś ca pāṇḍavāna etad vistarato yuddhaṃ prabrūhi kuśalo hy asic na hi tṛpyāmi vīrāṇāṃ śṛṇvāno vikramān raṇe saṃjaya uvācaa tat sthāne samavasthāpya pratyamitraṃ mahābalamc avyūhatārjuno vyūhaṃ putrasya tava durnayea tat sādināgakalilaṃ padātirathasaṃkulamc dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhair vyūḍham aśobhata mahad balama pārāvatasavarṇāśvaś candrādityasamadyutiḥc pārṣataḥ prababhau dhanvī kālo vigrahavān ivaa pārṣataṃ tv abhi saṃtasthur draupadeyā yuyutsavaḥb divyavarmāyudhabhṛtaḥ śārdūlasamavikramāḥc sānugā bhīmavapuṣaś candraṃ tārāgaṇā ivaa atha vyūḍheṣv anīkeṣu prekṣya saṃśaptakān raṇec kruddho rjuno bhidudrāva vyākṣipan gāṇḍivaṃ dhanuḥa atha saṃśaptakāḥ pārtham abhyadhāvan vadhaiṣiṇaḥc vijaye kṛtasaṃkalpā mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanama tad aśvasaṃghabahulaṃ mattanāgarathākulamb udīryamāṇaṃ saṃrabdhaṃ dhanaṃjayam abhidravatb tad udyataṃ mahat sainyaṃ sāgaraughasamaṃ javeb pārthavelāṃ samāsādya viṣṭhitaṃ samadṛśyatac pattimac chūravīraughair drutam arjunam ādravata sa saṃprahāras tumulas teṣām āsīt kirīṭināc tasyaiva naḥ śruto yādṛṅ nivātakavacaiḥ sahaa rathān aśvān dhvajān nāgān pattīn rathapatīn apic iṣūn dhanūṃṣi khaḍgāṃś ca cakrāṇi ca paraśvadhāna sāyudhān udyatān bāhūn udyatāny āyudhāni cac ciccheda dviṣatāṃ pārthaḥ śirāṃsi ca sahasraśaḥa tasmin sainye mahāvarte pātālāvartasaṃnibhec nimagnaṃ taṃ rathaṃ matvā neduḥ saṃśaptakā mudāa sa purastād arīn hatvā paścārdhenottareṇa cac dakṣiṇena ca bībhatsuḥ kruddho rudraḥ paśūn ivaa atha pāñcālacedīnāṃ sṛñjayānāṃ ca māriṣac tvadīyaiḥ saha saṃgrāma āsīt paramadāruṇaḥa kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥc hṛṣṭasenāḥ susaṃrabdhā rathānīkaiḥ prahāriṇaḥa kosalaiḥ kāśimatsyaiś ca kārūṣaiḥ kekayair apic śūrasenaiḥ śūravīrair yuyudhur yuddhadurmadāḥa teṣām antakaraṃ yuddhaṃ dehapāpmapraṇāśanamc śūdraviṭkṣatravīrāṇāṃ dharmyaṃ svargyaṃ yaśaskarama duryodhano pi sahito bhrātṛbhir bharatarṣabhac guptaḥ kurupravīraiś ca madrāṇāṃ ca mahārathaiḥa pāṇḍavaiḥ sahapāñcālaiś cedibhiḥ sātyakena cac yudhyamānaṃ raṇe karṇaṃ kuruvīro bhyapālayata karṇo pi niśitair bāṇair vinihatya mahācamūmc pramṛdya ca rathaśreṣṭhān yudhiṣṭhiram apīḍayata vipatrāyudhadehāsūn kṛtvā śatrūn sahasraśaḥc yuktvā svargayaśobhyāṃ ca svebhyo mudam udāvahatd evaṃ māriṣa saṃgrāmo naravājigajakṣayaḥd kurūṇāṃ sṛñjayānāṃ ca devāsurasamo bhavatd tad vigāhya rathānīkaṃ sūtaputro mahārathaḥd nadīṃ pravartayām āsa śoṇitaughataraṅgiṇīmd śoṇitodāṃ kṣudramatsyāṃ nāganakrāṃ duratyayāmd māṃsamajjākardaminīṃ cakrakūrmāṃ rathoḍupāmd patitair meghasaṃkāśais tatra tatra mahādvipaiḥd aśanībhir iva dhvastā mahī rājan virājated tāṃ śarormimahāvartāṃ chattrahaṃsasamākulāmd tanutroṣṇīṣasaṃghāṭāṃ hastipāṣāṇasaṃkulāmd apārām anapārāṃ tāṃ śaṅkhadundubhighoṣiṇīmd raudrāṃ nadīṃ mahārāja rajasā sarvato vṛtāmd atitīkṣṇāṃ nadākīrṇāṃ nadīm antakagāminīmd samaṃ ca viṣamaṃ caiva samāyāntīṃ mahābhayāmd ā gulphāc cātra sīdantīṃ narāñ śoṇitakardamed narair abhiparikṣiptā yathā rājan mahādrumāḥd tatas te tatra tatraiva prataranto mahānadīmd viceruḥ sarvato yodhā nauvāraṇamahāsanaiḥd śoṇitena samaṃ rājan kṛtam āsīt samantataḥd nadīvegair yathā bhūmis tadvad āsīd viśāṃ pate dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa yat tat praviśya pārthānāṃ senāṃ kurvañ janakṣayamc karṇo rājānam abhyarcchat tan mamācakṣva saṃjayaa ke ca pravīrāḥ pārthānāṃ yudhi karṇam avārayanc kāṃś ca pramathyādhirathir yudhiṣṭhiram apīḍayat saṃjaya uvācaa dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhān pārthān dṛṣṭvā karṇo vyavasthitānc samabhyadhāvat tvaritaḥ pāñcālāñ śatrukarśanaḥa taṃ tūrṇam abhidhāvantaṃ pāñcālā jitakāśinaḥc pratyudyayur mahārāja haṃsā iva mahārṇavama tataḥ śaṅkhasahasrāṇāṃ nisvano hṛdayaṃgamaḥc prādurāsīd ubhayato bherīśabdaś ca dāruṇaḥa nānāvāditranādaś ca dvipāśvarathanisvanaḥc siṃhanādaś ca vīrāṇām abhavad dāruṇas tadāa sādridrumārṇavā bhūmiḥ savātāmbudam ambaramc sārkendugrahanakṣatrā dyauś ca vyaktaṃ vyaghūrṇataa ati bhūtāni taṃ śabdaṃ menire ti ca vivyathuḥc yāni cāplavasattvāni prāyas tāni mṛtāni caa atha karṇo bhṛśaṃ kruddhaḥ śīghram astram udīrayanc jaghāna pāṇḍavīṃ senām āsurīṃ maghavān ivaa sa pāṇḍavarathāṃs tūrṇaṃ praviśya visṛjañ śarānc prabhadrakāṇāṃ pravarān ahanat saptasaptatima tataḥ supuṅkhair niśitai rathaśreṣṭho ratheṣubhiḥc avadhīt pañcaviṃśatyā pāñcālān pañcaviṃśatima suvarṇapuṅkhair nārācaiḥ parakāyavidāraṇaiḥc cedikān avadhīd vīraḥ śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa taṃ tathā samare karma kurvāṇam atimānuṣamc parivavrur mahārāja pāñcālānāṃ rathavrajāḥa tataḥ saṃdhāya viśikhān pañca bhārata duḥsahānc pāñcālān avadhīt pañca karṇo vaikartano vṛṣaḥa bhānudevaṃ citrasenaṃ senābinduṃ ca bhāratac tapanaṃ śūrasenaṃ ca pāñcālān avadhīd raṇea pāñcāleṣu ca śūreṣu vadhyamāneṣu sāyakaiḥc hāhākāro mahān āsīt pāñcālānāṃ mahāhaved parivavrur mahārāja pāñcālānāṃ rathā daśaa teṣāṃ saṃkīryamāṇānāṃ hāhākārakṛtā diśaḥc punar eva ca tān karṇo jaghānāśu patatribhiḥa cakrarakṣau tu karṇasya putrau māriṣa durjayauc suṣeṇaḥ satyasenaś ca tyaktvā prāṇān ayudhyatāma pṛṣṭhagopas tu karṇasya jyeṣṭhaḥ putro mahārathaḥc vṛṣasenaḥ svayaṃ karṇaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ paryapālayata dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ sātyakiś ca draupadeyā vṛkodaraḥb nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥc janamejayaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca pravīrāś ca prabhadrakāḥa cedikekayapāñcālā yamau matsyāś ca daṃśitāḥc samabhyadhāvan rādheyaṃ jighāṃsantaḥ prahāriṇaḥa ta enaṃ vividhaiḥ śastraiḥ śaradhārābhir eva cac abhyavarṣan vimṛdnantaḥ prāvṛṣīvāmbudā girima pitaraṃ tu parīpsantaḥ karṇaputrāḥ prahāriṇaḥc tvadīyāś cāpare rājan vīrā vīrān avārayana suṣeṇo bhīmasenasya chittvā bhallena kārmukamc nārācaiḥ saptabhir viddhvā hṛdi bhīmaṃ nanāda haa athānyad dhanur ādāya sudṛḍhaṃ bhīmavikramaḥc sajyaṃ vṛkodaraḥ kṛtvā suṣeṇasyācchinad dhanuḥa vivyādha cainaṃ navabhiḥ kruddho nṛtyann iveṣubhiḥc karṇaṃ ca tūrṇaṃ vivyādha trisaptatyā śitaiḥ śaraiḥa satyasenaṃ ca daśabhiḥ sāśvasūtadhvajāyudhamc paśyatāṃ suhṛdāṃ madhye karṇaputram apātayata kṣurapraṇunnaṃ tat tasya śiraś candranibhānanamc śubhadarśanam evāsīn nālabhraṣṭam ivāmbujama hatvā karṇasutaṃ bhīmas tāvakān punar ārdayatc kṛpahārdikyayoś chittvā cāpe tāv apy athārdayata duḥśāsanaṃ tribhir viddhvā śakuniṃ ṣaḍbhir āyasaiḥc ulūkaṃ ca patatriṃ ca cakāra virathāv ubhaua he suṣeṇa hato sīti bruvann ādatta sāyakamc tam asya karṇaś ciccheda tribhiś cainam atāḍayata athānyam api jagrāha suparvāṇaṃ sutejanamc suṣeṇāyāsṛjad bhīmas tam apy asyācchinad vṛṣaḥa punaḥ karṇas trisaptatyā bhīmasenaṃ ratheṣubhiḥc putraṃ parīpsan vivyādha krūraṃ krūrair jighāṃsayāa suṣeṇas tu dhanur gṛhya bhārasādhanam uttamamc nakulaṃ pañcabhir bāṇair bāhvor urasi cārdayata nakulas taṃ tu viṃśatyā viddhvā bhārasahair dṛḍhaiḥc nanāda balavan nādaṃ karṇasya bhayam ādadhata taṃ suṣeṇo mahārāja viddhvā daśabhir āśugaiḥc ciccheda ca dhanuḥ śīghraṃ kṣurapreṇa mahārathaḥa athānyad dhanur ādāya nakulaḥ krodhamūrcchitaḥc suṣeṇaṃ bahubhir bāṇair vārayām āsa saṃyugea sa tu bāṇair diśo rājann ācchādya paravīrahāc ājaghne sārathiṃ cāsya suṣeṇaṃ ca tatas tribhiḥe ciccheda cāsya sudṛḍhaṃ dhanur bhallais tribhis tridhāa athānyad dhanur ādāya suṣeṇaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥc avidhyan nakulaṃ ṣaṣṭyā sahadevaṃ ca saptabhiḥa tad yuddhaṃ sumahad ghoram āsīd devāsuropamamc nighnatāṃ sāyakais tūrṇam anyonyasya vadhaṃ pratid sātyakir vṛṣasenaṃ tu viddhvā saptabhir āśugaiḥd punar vivyādha saptatyā sārathiṃ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥd vṛṣasenas tu śaineyaṃ śareṇa nataparvaṇād ājaghāna mahārāja śaṅkhadeśe mahārathamd śaineyo vṛṣasenena patriṇā paripīḍitaḥd krodhaṃ cakre mahārāja kruddho vegaṃ ca dāruṇamd jagrāheṣuvarān vīraḥ śīghraṃ sa daśa pañca caa sātyakir vṛṣasenasya hatvā sūtaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥc dhanuś ciccheda bhallena jaghānāśvāṃś ca saptabhiḥe dhvajam ekeṣuṇonmathya tribhis taṃ hṛdy atāḍayata athāvasannaḥ svarathe muhūrtāt punar utthitaḥb sa raṇe yuyudhānena visūtāśvarathadhvajaḥc atho jighāṃsuḥ śaineyaṃ khaḍgacarmabhṛd abhyayāta tasya cāplavataḥ śīghraṃ vṛṣasenasya sātyakiḥc varāhakarṇair daśabhir avidhyad asicarmaṇīa catuḥṣaṣṭyā sahadevaś ca pañcabhiḥc nakulas triṃśatā bāṇaiḥ śatānīkaś ca saptabhiḥe śikhaṇḍī daśabhir vīro dharmarājaḥ śatena tua ete cānye ca rājendra pravīrā jayagṛddhinaḥc abhyardayan maheṣvāsaṃ sūtaputraṃ mahāmṛdhea tān sūtaputro viśikhair daśabhir daśabhiḥ śitaiḥc rathe cāru caran vīraḥ pratyavidhyad ariṃdamaḥd sātyakiṃ bhīmasenaṃ ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ śikhaṇḍinamd draupadeyāṃś ca saṃrabdhān śikharāṇi dvipottamāḥb pralutvā vīra śailānāṃ śikharāṇi dvipopamāḥc sārohā nihatāḥ petur vajrabhinnā ivādrayaḥa chinnabhinnaviparyastair varmālaṃkāravigrahaiḥc sārohās turagāḥ petur hatavīrāḥ sahasraśaḥa vipraviddhāyudhāṅgāś ca dviradāśvarathair hatāḥc prativīraiś ca saṃmarde pattisaṃghāḥ sahasraśaḥa viśālāyatatāmrākṣaiḥ padmendusadṛśānanaiḥc śirobhir yuddhaśauṇḍānāṃ sarvataḥ saṃstṛtā mahīa tathā tu vitate vyomni nisvanaṃ śuśruvur janāḥc vimānair apsaraḥsaṃghair gītavāditranisvanaiḥa hatān kṛttān abhimukhān vīrān vīraiḥ sahasraśaḥc āropyāropya gacchanti vimāneṣv apsarogaṇāḥd tavāyaṃ na tavaivāyaṃ mamāyam iti vallabhaḥd pariṣvakto vijānāti nārībhir uparisthitaḥd iti bāhulatāpāśapāśino divyarūpiṇaḥd samādhāyāpsaraḥsaṃghā nānāyānair divaṃ yayuḥa tad dṛṣṭvā mahad āścaryaṃ pratyakṣaṃ svargalipsayāc prahṛṣṭamanasaḥ śūrāḥ kṣipraṃ jagmuḥ parasparama rathino rathibhiḥ sārdhaṃ citraṃ yuyudhur āhavec pattayaḥ pattibhir nāgā nāgaiḥ saha hayair hayāḥa evaṃ pravṛtte saṃgrāme gajavājijanakṣayec sainye ca rajasā vyāpte sve svāñ jaghnuḥ pare parāna kacākaci babhau yuddhaṃ dantādanti nakhānakhic muṣṭiyuddhaṃ niyuddhaṃ ca dehapāpmavināśanama tathā vartati saṃgrāme gajavājijanakṣayec narāśvagajadehebhyaḥ prasṛtā lohitāpagāe narāśvagajadehān sā vyuvāha patitān bahūna narāśvagajasaṃbādhe narāśvagajasādināmc lohitodā mahāghorā nadī lohitakardamāe narāśvagajadehān sā vahantī bhīrubhīṣaṇīa tasyāḥ paramapāraṃ ca vrajanti vijayaiṣiṇaḥc gādhena ca plavantaś ca nimajjyonmajjya cāparea te tu lohitadigdhāṅgā raktavarmāyudhāmbarāḥc sasnus tasyāṃ papuś cāsṛṅ mamluś ca bharatarṣabhaa rathān aśvān narān nāgān āyudhābharaṇāni cac vasanāny atha varmāṇi hanyamānān hatān apie bhūmiṃ khaṃ dyāṃ diśaś caiva prāyaḥ paśyāma lohitama lohitasya tu gandhena sparśena ca rasena cac rūpeṇa cātiriktena śabdena ca visarpatāe viṣādaḥ sumahān āsīt prāyaḥ sainyasya bhārataa tat tu viprahataṃ sainyaṃ bhīmasenamukhais tavac bhūyaḥ samādravan vīrāḥ sātyakipramukhā rathāḥa teṣām āpatatāṃ vegam aviṣahya mahātmanāmc putrāṇāṃ te mahat sainyam āsīd rājan parāṅmukhama tat prakīrṇarathāśvebhaṃ naravājisamākulamc vidhvastacarmakavacaṃ praviddhāyudhakārmukama vyadravat tāvakaṃ sainyaṃ loḍyamānaṃ samantataḥc siṃhārditaṃ mahāraṇye yathā gajakulaṃ tathā saṃjaya uvācaa tān abhidravato dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavāṃs tāvakaṃ balamb duryodhano mahārāja vārayām āsa sarvaśaḥb yodhāṃś ca svabalaṃ caiva samantād bharatarṣabhac krośatas tava putrasya na sma rājan nyavartataa tataḥ pakṣāt prapakṣāc ca prapakṣaiś cāpi dakṣiṇātc udastaśastrāḥ kuravo bhīmam abhyadravan raṇea karṇo pi dṛṣṭvā dravato dhārtarāṣṭrān parāṅmukhānb madrarājam uvācedaṃ yāhi bhīmarathaṃ pratib evam uktaś ca karṇena śalyo madrādhipas tadāc haṃsavarṇān hayāgryāṃs tān praiṣīd yatra vṛkodarama te preṣitā mahārāja śalyenāhavaśobhināc bhīmasenarathaṃ prāpya samasajjanta vājinaḥa dṛṣṭvā karṇaṃ samāyāntaṃ bhīmaḥ krodhasamanvitaḥc matiṃ dadhre vināśāya karṇasya bharatarṣabhaa so bravīt sātyakiṃ vīraṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca pārṣatamc enaṃ rakṣata rājānaṃ dharmātmānaṃ yudhiṣṭhirame saṃśayān mahato muktaṃ kathaṃ cit prekṣato mamaa agrato me kṛto rājā chinnasarvaparicchadaḥc duryodhanasya prītyarthaṃ rādheyena durātmanāa antam adya kariṣyāmi tasya duḥkhasya pārṣatac hantā vāsmi raṇe karṇaṃ sa vā māṃ nihaniṣyatie saṃgrāmeṇa sughoreṇa satyam etad bravīmi vaḥa rājānam adya bhavatāṃ nyāsabhūtaṃ dadāmi vaic asya saṃrakṣaṇe sarve yatadhvaṃ vigatajvarāḥa evam uktvā mahābāhuḥ prāyād ādhirathiṃ pratic siṃhanādena mahatā sarvāḥ saṃnādayan diśaḥa dṛṣṭvā tvaritam āyāntaṃ bhīmaṃ yuddhābhinandinamc sūtaputram athovāca madrāṇām īśvaro vibhuḥa paśya karṇa mahābāhuṃ kruddhaṃ pāṇḍavanandanamc dīrghakālārjitaṃ krodhaṃ moktukāmaṃ tvayi dhruvama īdṛśaṃ nāsya rūpaṃ me dṛṣṭapūrvaṃ kadā canac abhimanyau hate karṇa rākṣase vā ghaṭotkacea trailokyasya samastasya śaktaḥ kruddho nivāraṇec bibharti yādṛśaṃ rūpaṃ kālāgnisadṛśaṃ śubhama iti bruvati rādheyaṃ madrāṇām īśvare nṛpac abhyavartata vai karṇaṃ krodhadīpto vṛkodaraḥa tathāgataṃ tu saṃprekṣya bhīmaṃ yuddhābhinandinamc abravīd vacanaṃ śalyaṃ rādheyaḥ prahasann ivaa yad uktaṃ vacanaṃ me dya tvayā madrajaneśvarac bhīmasenaṃ prati vibho tat satyaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥa eṣa śūraś ca vīraś ca krodhanaś ca vṛkodaraḥc nirapekṣaḥ śarīre ca prāṇataś ca balādhikaḥa ajñātavāsaṃ vasatā virāṭanagare tadāc draupadyāḥ priyakāmena kevalaṃ bāhusaṃśrayāte gūḍhabhāvaṃ samāśritya kīcakaḥ sagaṇo hataḥa so dya saṃgrāmaśirasi saṃnaddhaḥ krodhamūrcchitaḥc kiṃkarodyatadaṇḍena mṛtyunāpi vrajed raṇama cirakālābhilaṣito mamāyaṃ tu manorathaḥc arjunaṃ samare hanyāṃ māṃ vā hanyād dhanaṃjayaḥe sa me kadā cid adyaiva bhaved bhīmasamāgamātf saṃśayaḥ sumahāñ śalya prāpya bhīmam ariṃdamama nihate bhīmasene tu yadi vā virathīkṛtec abhiyāsyati māṃ pārthas tan me sādhu bhaviṣyatie atra yan manyase prāptaṃ tac chīghraṃ saṃpradhārayaf bhīmasenaṃ samāsādya mayā śakyaṃ nivartitumf mūrtimantam ahaṃ manye mārutiṃ marutāṃ patimf yudhiṣṭhiraṃ bhīmam ihātha śaknuyāṃf yamau tathā daṇḍadharaṃ yamaprabhamf tair eva naḥ sukhakaram āhavo stuf vrajāmi bībhatsum ahaṃ gadādharama etac chrutvā tu vacanaṃ rādheyasya mahātmanaḥc uvāca vacanaṃ śalyaḥ sūtaputraṃ tathāgatama abhiyāsi mahābāho bhīmasenaṃ mahābalamc nirasya bhīmasenaṃ tu tataḥ prāpsyasi phalgunamd nirapekṣaś ca yudhyasva śaktiṃ svāṃ saṃpradarśayana yas te kāmo bhilaṣitaś cirāt prabhṛti hṛdgataḥc sa vai saṃpatsyate karṇa satyam etad bravīmi tea evam ukte tataḥ karṇaḥ śalyaṃ punar abhāṣatac hantāham arjunaṃ saṃkhye māṃ vā hantā dhanaṃjayaḥd evam uktvā tato rājan rādheyo rathināṃ varaḥe yuddhe manaḥ samādhāya yāhi yāhīty acodayata tataḥ prāyād rathenāśu śalyas tatra viśāṃ patec yatra bhīmo maheṣvāso vyadrāvayata vāhinīma tatas tūryaninādaś ca bherīṇāṃ ca mahāsvanaḥc udatiṣṭhata rājendra karṇabhīmasamāgamea bhīmaseno tha saṃkruddhas tava sainyaṃ durāsadamc nārācair vimalais tīkṣṇair diśaḥ prādrāvayad balīa sa saṃnipātas tumulo bhīmarūpo viśāṃ patec āsīd raudro mahārāja karṇapāṇḍavayor mṛdhee tato muhūrtād rājendra pāṇḍavaḥ karṇam ādravate   nātikṛcchrād dhasann ivae bhīmaseno mahābāhuḥa tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya karṇo vaikartano vṛṣaḥc ājaghānorasi kruddho nārācena stanāntaree punaś cainam ameyātmā śaravarṣair avākirata sa viddhaḥ sūtaputreṇa chādayām āsa patribhiḥc vivyādha niśitaiḥ karṇa navabhir nataparvabhiḥa tasya karṇo dhanurmadhye dvidhā ciccheda patriṇāc atha taṃ chinnadhanvānam abhyavidhyat stanāntaree nārācena sutīkṣṇena sarvāvaraṇabhedināa so nyat kārmukam ādāya sūtaputraṃ vṛkodaraḥc rājan marmasu marmajño viddhvā suniśitaiḥ śaraiḥe nanāda balavan nādaṃ kampayann iva rodasīa taṃ karṇaḥ pañcaviṃśatyā nārācānāṃ samārdayatc madotkaṭaṃ vane dṛptam ulkābhir iva kuñjarama tataḥ sāyakabhinnāṅgaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ krodhamūrcchitaḥc saṃrambhāmarṣatāmrākṣaḥ sūtaputravadhecchayāa sa kārmuke mahāvegaṃ bhārasādhanam uttamamc girīṇām api bhettāraṃ sāyakaṃ samayojayata vikṛṣya balavac cāpam ā karṇād atimārutiḥc taṃ mumoca maheṣvāsaḥ kruddhaḥ karṇajighāṃsayāa sa visṛṣṭo balavatā bāṇo vajrāśanisvanaḥc adārayad raṇe karṇaṃ vajravega ivācalama sa bhīmasenābhihato sūtaputraḥ kurūdvahac niṣasāda rathopasthe visaṃjñaḥ pṛtanāpatiḥd rudhireṇāvasiktāṅgo gatāsuvad ariṃdamaḥd etasminn antare dṛṣṭvā madrarājo vṛkodaramd jihvāṃ chettuṃ samāyāntaṃ sāntvayann idam abravītd bhīmasena mahābāho yat tvā vakṣyāmi tac chṛṇud vacanaṃ hetusaṃpannaṃ śrutvā caitat tathā kurud arjunena pratijñāto vadhaḥ karṇasya śuṣmiṇaḥd bhīma uvācad tāṃ tathā kuru bhadraṃ te pratijñāṃ savyasācinaḥd dṛḍhavratatvaṃ pārthasya jānāmi nṛpasattamad rājñas tu dharṣaṇaṃ pāpaḥ kṛtavān mama saṃnidhaud tataḥ krodhābhibhūtena śeṣaṃ na gaṇitaṃ mayād patite cāpi rādheye na me manyuḥ śamaṃ gataḥd jihvoddharaṇam evāsya prāptakālaṃ mataṃ mamad anena tu nṛśaṃsena samaveteṣu rājasud asmākaṃ śṛṇvatāṃ kṛṣṇā yāni vākyāni mātulad asahyāni ca nīcena bahūni śrāvitāni bhoḥd nūnaṃ te tat parijñātaṃ dūrasthasyāpi pārthivad chedanaṃ cāsya jihvāyās tad evākāṅkṣitaṃ mayād rājñas tu priyakāmena kālo yaṃ paripālitaḥd bhavatā tu yad ukto smi vākyaṃ hetvarthasaṃhitamd tad gṛhītaṃ mahārāja kaṭukastham ivauṣadhamd hīnapratijño bībhatsur na hi jīveta karhi citd asmin vinaṣṭe naṣṭāḥ smaḥ sarva eva sakeśavāḥd adya caiva nṛśaṃsātmā pāpaḥ pāpakṛtāṃ varaḥd gamiṣyati parābhāvaṃ dṛṣṭamātraḥ kirīṭinād yudhiṣṭhirasya kopena pūrvaṃ dagdho nṛśaṃsakṛtd tvayā saṃrakṣitas tv adya matsamīpād upāyataḥa tato madrādhipo dṛṣṭvā visaṃjñaṃ sūtanandanamc apovāha rathenājau karṇam āhavaśobhinama tataḥ parājite karṇe dhārtarāṣṭrīṃ mahācamūmc vyadrāvayad bhīmaseno yathendro dānavīṃ camūm dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa suduṣkaram idaṃ karma kṛtaṃ bhīmena saṃjayac yena karṇo mahābāhū rathopasthe nipātitaḥa karṇo hy eko raṇe hantā sṛñjayān pāṇḍavaiḥ sahac iti duryodhanaḥ sūta prābravīn māṃ muhur muhuḥa parājitaṃ tu rādheyaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmena saṃyugec tataḥ paraṃ kim akarot putro duryodhano mama saṃjaya uvācaa vibhrāntaṃ prekṣya rādheyaṃ sūtaputraṃ mahāhavec mahatyā senayā rājan sodaryān samabhāṣataa śīghraṃ gacchata bhadraṃ vo rādheyaṃ parirakṣatac bhīmasenabhayāgādhe majjantaṃ vyasanārṇavea te tu rājñā samādiṣṭā bhīmasenajighāṃsavaḥc abhyavartanta saṃkruddhāḥ pataṃgā iva pāvakama śrutāyur durdharaḥ krātho vivitsur vikaṭaḥ samaḥc niṣaṅgī kavacī pāśī tathā nandopanandakaua duṣpradharṣaḥ subāhuś ca vātavegasuvarcasauc dhanurgrāho durmadaś ca tathā sattvasamaḥ sahaḥa ete rathaiḥ parivṛtā vīryavanto mahābalāḥc bhīmasenaṃ samāsādya samantāt paryavārayane te vyamuñcañ śaravrātān nānāliṅgān samantataḥa sa tair abhyardyamānas tu bhīmaseno mahābalaḥc teṣām āpatatāṃ kṣipraṃ sutānāṃ te narādhipae rathaiḥ pañcāśatā sārdhaṃ pañcāśan nyahanad rathāna vivitsos tu tataḥ kruddho bhallenāpāharac chiraḥc sakuṇḍalaśirastrāṇaṃ pūrṇacandropamaṃ tadād aśobhata mahārāja pūrṇacandra ivāmbaree bhīmena ca mahārāja sa papāta hato bhuvia taṃ dṛṣṭvā nihataṃ śūraṃ bhrātaraḥ sarvataḥ prabhoc abhyadravanta samare bhīmaṃ bhīmaparākramama tato parābhyāṃ bhallābhyāṃ putrayos te mahāhavec jahāra samare prāṇān bhīmo bhīmaparākramaḥa tau dharām anvapadyetāṃ vātarugṇāv iva drumauc vikaṭaś ca samaś cobhau devagarbhasamau nṛpaa tatas tu tvarito bhīmaḥ krāthaṃ ninye yamakṣayamc nārācena sutīkṣṇena sa hato nyapatad bhuvia hāhākāras tatas tīvraḥ saṃbabhūva janeśvarac vadhyamāneṣu te rājaṃs tadā putreṣu dhanviṣua teṣāṃ saṃlulite sainye bhīmaseno mahābalaḥc nandopanandau samare prāpayad yamasādanama tatas te prādravan bhītāḥ putrās te vihvalīkṛtāḥc bhīmasenaṃ raṇe dṛṣṭvā kālāntakayamopamama putrāṃs te nihatān dṛṣṭvā sūtaputro mahāmanāḥc haṃsavarṇān hayān bhūyaḥ prāhiṇod yatra pāṇḍavaḥa te preṣitā mahārāja madrarājena vājinaḥc bhīmasenarathaṃ prāpya samasajjanta vegitāḥa sa saṃnipātas tumulo ghorarūpo viśāṃ patec āsīd raudro mahārāja karṇapāṇḍavayor mṛdhea dṛṣṭvā mama mahārāja tau sametau mahārathauc āsīd buddhiḥ kathaṃ nūnam etad adya bhaviṣyatid ājaghne bahubhir bāṇair dhvajam ekeṣuṇāhanatd sārathiṃ cāsya bhallena preṣayām āsa mṛtyaved chittvā ca kārmukaṃ tūrṇaṃ pāṇḍavasyāśu patriṇād tato bhīmo raṇaślāghī chādayām āsa patribhiḥd karṇaṃ raṇe mahārāja putrāṇāṃ tava paśyatāmd tataḥ karṇo bhṛśaṃ kruddho bhīmaṃ navabhir āyasaiḥd vivyādha paramāstrajño bhallaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥd āhataḥ sa mahābāhur bhīmo bhīmaparākramaḥd ākarṇapūrṇair viśikhaiḥ karṇaṃ vivyādha saptabhiḥd tataḥ karṇo mahārāja āśīviṣa iva śvasand śaravarṣeṇa mahatā chādayām āsa pāṇḍavamd bhīmo pi taṃ śaravrātaiś chādayitvā mahārathamd paśyatāṃ kauraveyāṇāṃ vinanarda mahābalaḥd tataḥ karṇo bhṛśaṃ kruddho dṛḍham ādāya kārmukamd bhīmaṃ vivyādha daśabhiḥ kaṅkapatraiḥ śilāśitaiḥd kārmukaṃ cāsya ciccheda bhallena niśitena cad tato bhīmo mahābāhur hemapaṭṭavibhūṣitamd parighaṃ ghoram ādāya mṛtyudaṇḍam ivāparamd karṇasya nidhanākāṅkṣī cikṣepātibalo nadand tam āpatantaṃ parighaṃ vajrāśanisamasvanamd ciccheda bahudhā karṇaḥ śarair āśīviṣopamaiḥd tataḥ kārmukam ādāya bhīmo dṛḍhataraṃ tadād chādayām āsa viśikhaiḥ karṇaṃ parabalārdanamd tato yuddham abhūd ghoraṃ karṇapāṇḍavayor mṛdhed harīndrayor iva muhuḥ parasparavadhaiṣiṇoḥd tataḥ karṇo mahārāja bhīmasenaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥd ākarṇamūlaṃ vivyādha dṛḍham āyamya kārmukamd so tividdho maheṣvāsaḥ karṇena balināṃ varaḥd ghoram ādatta viśikhaṃ karṇakāyāvadāraṇamd tasya bhittvā tanutrāṇaṃ bhittvā kāyaṃ ca sāyakaḥd prāviśad dharaṇīṃ rājan valmīkam iva pannagaḥd sa tenātiprahāreṇa vyathito vihvalann ivad saṃcacāla rathe karṇaḥ kṣitikampe yathācalaḥd tataḥ karṇo mahārāja roṣāmarṣasamanvitaḥd pāṇḍavaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā nārācānāṃ samārpayata tato muhūrtād rājendra nātikṛcchrād dhasann ivac virathaṃ bhīmakarmāṇaṃ bhīmaṃ karṇaś cakāra haa viratho bharataśreṣṭhaḥ prahasann anilopamaḥb tato marṣī mahātejā viratho rathināṃ varaḥc gadāhasto mahābāhur apatat syandanottamātd avaplutya ca vegena tava sainyaṃ viśāṃ pated vyadhamad gadayā bhīmaḥ śaran meghān ivānilaḥd gadayā ca mahārāja karṇasya rathakūbaramd pothayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ samare śatrutāpanaḥd sa krodhavaśam āpannaḥ pāṇḍuputraḥ pratāpavānd vidrāvya gadayā vīras tava putrān mahāhaved karṇaṃ śalyaṃ ca yugapad gadayā prahasann ivad apātayad rathopasthe nihatya vinanāda haa nāgān saptaśatān rājann īṣādantān prahāriṇaḥc vyadhamat sahasā bhīmaḥ kruddharūpaḥ paraṃtapaḥa dantaveṣṭeṣu netreṣu kambheṣu sa kaṭeṣu cac marmasv api ca marmajño ninadan vyadhamad bhṛśamd te bhyarditā mārutinā vinadanto bhṛśāturāḥa tatas te prādravan bhītāḥ pratīpaṃ prahitāḥ punaḥc mahāmātrais tam āvavrur meghā iva divākarama tān sa saptaśatān nāgān sārohāyudhaketanānc bhūmiṣṭho gadayā jaghne śaranmeghān ivānilaḥa tataḥ subalaputrasya nāgān atibalān punaḥc pothayām āsa kaunteyo dvāpañcāśatam āhavea tathā rathaśataṃ sāgraṃ pattīṃś ca śataśo parānc nyahanat pāṇḍavo yuddhe tāpayaṃs tava vāhinīma pratāpyamānaṃ sūryeṇa bhīmena ca mahātmanāc tava sainyaṃ saṃcukoca carma vahnigataṃ yathāa te bhīmabhayasaṃtrastās tāvakā bharatarṣabhac vihāya samare bhīmaṃ dudruvur vai diśo daśaa rathāḥ pañcaśatāś cānye hrādinaś carmavarmiṇaḥc bhīmam abhyadravaṃs tūrṇaṃ śarapūgaiḥ samantataḥa tān sasūtarathān sarvān sapatākādhvajāyudhānc pothayām āsa gadayā bhīmo viṣṇur ivāsurāna tataḥ śakuninirdiṣṭāḥ sādinaḥ śūrasaṃmatāḥc trisāhasrā yayur bhīmaṃ śaktyṛṣṭiprāsapāṇayaḥa tān pratyudgamya yavanān aśvārohān varārihāc vicaran vividhān mārgān ghātayām āsa pothayana teṣām āsīn mahāñ śabdas tāḍitānāṃ ca sārvaśaḥc asibhiś chidyamānānāṃ naḍānām iva bhārataa evaṃ subalaputrasya trisāhasrān hayottamānc hatvānyaṃ ratham āsthāya kruddho rādheyam abhyayāta karṇo pi samare rājan dharmaputram ariṃdamamc śaraiḥ pracchādayām āsa sārathiṃ cāpy apātayata tataḥ saṃpradrutaṃ saṃkhye rathaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahārathaḥc anvadhāvat kiran bāṇaiḥ kaṅkapatrair ajihmagaiḥa rājānam abhi dhāvantaṃ śarair āvṛtya rodasīc kruddhaḥ pracchādayām āsa śarajālena mārutiḥa saṃnivṛttas tatas tūrṇaṃ rādheyaḥ śatrukarśanaḥc bhīmaṃ pracchādayām āsa samantān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa bhīmasenarathavyagraṃ karṇaṃ bhārata sātyakiḥc abhyardayad ameyātmā pārṣṇigrahaṇakāraṇāte abhyavartata karṇas tam ardito pi śarair bhṛśama tāv anyonyaṃ samāsādya vṛṣabhau sarvadhanvināmc visṛjantau śarāṃś citrān vibhrājetāṃ manasvinaua tābhyāṃ viyati rājendra vitataṃ bhīmadarśanamc krauñcapṛṣṭhāruṇaṃ raudraṃ bāṇajālaṃ vyadṛśyataa naiva sūryaprabhāṃ khaṃ vā na diśaḥ pradiśaḥ kutaḥc prājñāsiṣma vayaṃ tābhyāṃ śarair muktaiḥ sahasraśaḥa madhyāhne tapato rājan bhāskarasya mahāprabhāḥc hṛtāḥ sarvāḥ śaraughais taiḥ karṇamādhavayos tadāa saubalaṃ kṛtavarmāṇaṃ drauṇim ādhirathiṃ kṛpamc saṃsaktān pāṇḍavair dṛṣṭvā nivṛttāḥ kuravaḥ punaḥa teṣām āpatatāṃ śabdas tīvra āsīd viśāṃ patec uddhūtānāṃ yathā vṛṣṭyā sāgarāṇāṃ bhayāvahaḥa te sene bhṛśasaṃvigne dṛṣṭvānyonyaṃ mahāraṇec harṣeṇa mahatā yukte parigṛhya parasparama tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ madhyaṃ prāpte divākarec yādṛśaṃ na kadā cid dhi dṛṣṭapūrvaṃ na ca śrutama balaughas tu samāsādya balaughaṃ sahasā raṇec upāsarpata vegena jalaugha iva sāgarama āsīn ninādaḥ sumahān balaughānāṃ parasparamc garjatāṃ sāgaraughāṇāṃ yathā syān nisvano mahāna te tu sene samāsādya vegavatyau parasparamb upāsarpata vegena anyonyena narādhipac ekībhāvam anuprāpte nadyāv iva samāgamea tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ viśāṃ pateb harṣeṇa mahatā yuktaiḥ kurupāṇḍavasainikaiḥc kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca lipsatāṃ sumahad yaśaḥa kurūṇāṃ garjatāṃ tatra avicchedakṛtā giraḥc śrūyante vividhā rājan nāmāny uddiśya bhārataa yasya yad dhi raṇe nyaṅgaṃ pitṛto mātṛto pi vāc karmataḥ śīlato vāpi sa tac chrāvayate yudhia tān dṛṣṭvā samare śūrāṃs tarjayānān parasparamc abhavan me matī rājan naiṣām astīti jīvitama teṣāṃ dṛṣṭvā tu kruddhānāṃ vapūṃṣy amitatejasāmc abhavan me bhayaṃ tīvraṃ katham etad bhaviṣyatia tatas te pāṇḍavā rājan kauravāś ca tatra vasāṃ pītvā ca bhāratac medomajjāvasātṛptās tṛptā māṃsasya caiva hie dhāvamānāś ca dṛśyante kākagṛdhrabalās tathāa śūrās tu samare rājan bhayaṃ tyaktvā sudustyajamc yodhavratasamākhyātāś cakruḥ śrāvayanto hi bahavas tatra yodhā viśāṃ patec anyonyam avamṛdnantaḥ śaktitomarapaṭṭiśaiḥa vartamāne tadā yuddhe ghorarūpe sudāruṇec vyaṣīdat kauravī senā bhinnā naur iva sāgare saṃjaya uvācaa kaṅkapatraiḥ śilāśitaiḥc āsasāda raṇe pārthaḥ suśarmāṇaṃ mahārathama sa tasya śaravarṣāṇi vavarṣa rathināṃ varaḥc tathā saṃśaptakāś caiva pārthasya samare sthitāḥa suśarmā tu tataḥ pārthaṃ viddhvā navabhir āśugaiḥc janārdanaṃ tribhir bāṇair abhyahan dakṣiṇe bhujee tato pareṇa bhallena ketuṃ vivyādha māriṣaf vivyādha samare rājan suśarmā krodhamūrcchitaḥa sa vānaravaro rājan viśvakarmakṛto mahānc nanāda sumahan nādaṃ bhīṣayan vai nanarda caa kapes tu ninadaṃ śrutvā saṃtrastā tava vāhinīc bhayaṃ vipulam ādāya niśceṣṭā samapadyataa tataḥ sā śuśubhe senā niśceṣṭāvasthitā nṛpac nānāpuṣpasamākīrṇaṃ yathā caitrarathaṃ vanama pratilabhya tataḥ saṃjñāṃ yodhās te kurusattamac arjunaṃ siṣicur bāṇaiḥ parvataṃ jaladā ivae parivavrus tadā sarve pāṇḍavasya mahārathamf nigṛhya taṃ pracukruśur vadhyamānāḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥf nigrahītum upākrāman krodhāviṣṭāḥ samantataḥf nigṛhya taṃ rathaṃ tasya yodhās te tu sahasraśaḥf rathabandhaṃ pracakrur hi pāṇḍavasyāmitaujasaḥf ratham āruruhuḥ ke cit pārthakṛṣṇau jighṛkṣavaḥf saṃśaptakānāṃ yodhās te siṃhanādāṃś ca nediref sa rathas tair gṛhītas tu pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥf syandamāno nāśakat tu tad adbhutam ivābhavatf tataḥ pārtho mahābāhuḥ saṃvṛtas tair mahārathaiḥf nigṛhītaṃ rathaṃ dṛṣṭvā tāṃś cābhidravato bahūnf rathavadhaṃ pracukṣus te sarve tatra mahāhavea te hayān rathacakre ca ratheṣāś cāpi bhāratac nigṛhya balavat tūrṇaṃ hastinaḥa tataḥ kruddho raṇe pārthaḥ saṃvṛtas tair mahārathaiḥc nigṛhītaṃ rathaṃ dṛṣṭvā keśavaṃ cāpy abhidrutame rathārūḍhāṃś ca subahūn padātīṃś cāpy apātayata āsannāṃś ca tato yodhāñ śarair āsannayodhibhiḥb tāṃs tāpayitvā samare pārthaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥc cyāvayām āsa samare keśavaṃ cedam abravīta paśya kṛṣṇa mahābāho saṃśaptakagaṇān mayāc kurvāṇān dāruṇaṃ karma vadhyamānān sahasraśaḥa rathabandham imaṃ ghoraṃ pṛthivyāṃ nāsti kaś canac yaḥ saheta pumāṃl loke mad anyo yadupuṃgavad paśya tān adya samare matprayuktaiḥ sutejanaiḥd patyamānān raṇe kṛṣṇa śarair āśīviṣopamaiḥa ity evam uktvā bībhatsur devadattam athādhamatb vyanādayad ameyātmā devadattaṃ mahāmṛdheb devadattasvanaṃ śrutvā keśavo pi mahāyaśāḥc pāñcajanyaṃ ca kṛṣṇo pi pūrayann iva rodasīa taṃ tu śaṅkhasvanaṃ śrutvā saṃśaptakavarūthinīc saṃcacāla mahārāja vitrastā cābhavad bhṛśama padabandhaṃ tataś cakre pāṇḍavaḥ paravīrahāc nāgam astraṃ mahārāja saṃprodīrya muhur muhuḥd nāgam astraṃ tataḥ pārthaḥ prāduś cakre hasann ivad pādabandhaṃ sa teṣāṃ vai cakre tena mahāstravita yān uddiśya raṇe pārthaḥ padabandhaṃ cakāra hac te baddhāḥ padabandhena pāṇḍavena mahātmanāe niśceṣṭā abhavan rājann aśmasāramayā ivaa niśceṣṭāṃs tu tato yodhān avadhīt pāṇḍunandanaḥc yathendraḥ samare daityāṃs tārakasya vadhe purāa te vadhyamānāḥ samare mumucus taṃ rathottamamc āyudhāni ca sarvāṇi visraṣṭum upacakramuḥd te baddhāḥ pādabandhena na śekuś ceṣṭituṃ nṛpad tatas tān avadhīt pārthaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥd sarvayodhā hi samare bhujagair veṣṭitābhavana tataḥ suśarmā rājendra gṛhītāṃ vīkṣya vāhinīmc sauparṇam astraṃ tvaritaḥ prāduścakre mahārathaḥa tataḥ suparṇāḥ saṃpetur bhakṣayanto bhujaṃgamānc te vai vidudruvur nāgā dṛṣṭvā tān khacarān nṛpaa babhau balaṃ tad vimuktaṃ padabandhād viśāṃ patec meghavṛndād yathā mukto bhāskaras tāpayan prajāḥa vipramuktās tu te yodhāḥ phalgunasya rathaṃ pratic sasṛjur bāṇasaṃghāṃś ca śastrasaṃghāṃś ca māriṣad vividhāni ca śastrāṇi pratyavidhyanta sarvaśaḥa tāṃ mahāstramayīṃ vṛṣṭiṃ saṃchidya śaravṛṣṭibhiḥc vyavātiṣṭhat tato yodhān vāsaviḥ paravīrahāa suśarmā tu tato rājan bāṇenānataparvaṇāc arjunaṃ hṛdaye viddhvā vivyādhānyais tribhiḥ śaraiḥd so tividdho maheṣvāsaḥ śarair āśīviṣopamaiḥd suśarmāṇaṃ mahārāja krodhāviṣṭo mahārathaḥd tataḥ śaraśataiḥ pārthaḥ saṃchādyainaṃ kṣaṇād raṇed diśa āvārayām āsa bāṇais tatra mahāstravitd vimukhīkṛtya samare suśarmāṇaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥe sa gāḍhaviddho vyathito rathopastha upāviśatf tata uccukruśuḥ sarve hataḥ pārtha iti sma haf tataḥ śaṅkhaninādāś ca bherīśabdāś ca puṣkalāḥf nānāvāditraninadāḥ siṃhanādāś ca jajñirea pratilabhya tataḥ saṃjñāṃ śvetāśvaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥc aindram astram ameyātmā prāduścakre tvarānvitaḥe tato bāṇasahasrāṇi samutpannāni māriṣaa sarvadikṣu vyadṛśyanta sūdayanto nṛpa dvipānc hayān rathāṃś ca samare śastraiḥ śatasahasraśaḥd rarāja samare rājañ śakro nighnann ivāsurāna vadhyamāne tataḥ sainye vipulā bhīḥ samāviśatc saṃśaptakagaṇānāṃ ca gopālānāṃ ca bhāratae na hi kaś cit pumāṃs tatra yo rjunaṃ caturdaśa sahasrāṇi yāni śiṣṭāni bhāratac rathānām ayutaṃ caiva trisāhasrāś ca dantinaḥa tataḥ saṃśaptakā bhūyaḥ parivavrur dhanaṃjayamc martavyam iti niścitya jayaṃ vāpi nivartanama tatra yuddhaṃ mahad dhy āsīt tāvakānāṃ viśāṃ patec śūreṇa balinā sārdhaṃ pāṇḍavena kirīṭinād jitvā tān nyahanat pārthaḥ śatrūñ śakra ivāsurān saṃjaya uvācaa kṛtavarmā kṛpo drauṇiḥ sūtaputraś ca māriṣac ulūkaḥ saubalaś caiva rājā ca saha sodaraiḥa sīdamānāṃ camūṃ dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍuputrabhayārditāmc samujjihīrṣur vegena bhinnāṃ nāvam ivārṇavea tato yuddham atīvāsīn muhūrtam iva bhāratac bhīrūṇāṃ trāsajananaṃ śūrāṇāṃ harṣavardhanamd bhīmasenaṃ sapāñcālaṃ cedikaikeyasaṃvṛtamd vaikartanaḥ svayaṃ yuddhvā vārayām āsa kārmukaiḥd tataś cedikarūṣāṃś ca sṛñjayāṃś ca mahārathānd karṇo jaghāna saṃkruddho bhīmasenasya paśyataḥa kṛpeṇa śaravarṣāṇi vipramuktāni saṃyugec sṛñjayāḥ śātayām āsuḥ śalabhānāṃ vrajā ivaa śikhaṇḍī tu tataḥ kruddho gautamaṃ tvarito yayauc vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi samantād eva brāhmaṇed mahad āsīt tadā yuddhaṃ muhūrtād iva dāruṇamd kruddhayoḥ samare rājan rāmarāvaṇayor ivaa kṛpas tu śaravarṣaṃ tad vinihatya mahāstravitc śikhaṇḍinaṃ raṇe kruddho vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥa tataḥ śikhaṇḍī kupītaḥ śaraiḥ saptabhir āhavec kṛpaṃ vivyādha subhṛśaṃ kaṅkapatrair ajihmagaiḥa tataḥ kṛpaḥ śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ so tividdho mahārathaḥb tatas tu niśitais tīkṣṇaiḥ kṣuraprair hemabhūṣaṇaiḥc vyaśvasūtarathaṃ cakre pārṣataṃ tu dvijottamaḥa hatāśvāt tu tato yānād avaplutya mahārathaḥc carmakhaḍge ca saṃgṛhya satvaraṃ brāhmaṇaṃ yayaua tam āpatantaṃ sahasā śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc chādayām āsa samare tad adbhutam ivābhavata tatrādbhutam apaśyāma śilānāṃ plavanaṃ yathāc niśceṣṭo yad raṇe rājañ śikhaṇḍī samatiṣṭhataa kṛpeṇa chāditaṃ dṛṣṭvā nṛpottama śikhaṇḍinamc pratyudyayau kṛpaṃ tūrṇaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārathaḥa dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ tato yāntaṃ śāradvatarathaṃ pratic pratijagrāha vegena kṛtavarmā mahārathaḥa yudhiṣṭhiram athāyāntaṃ śāradvatarathaṃ pratic saputraṃ sahasenaṃ ca droṇaputro nyavārayata nakulaṃ sahadevaṃ ca tvaramāṇau mahārathauc pratijagrāha te putraḥ śaravarṣeṇa vārayana bhīmasenaṃ karūṣāṃś ca kekayān sahasṛñjayānc karṇo vaikartano yuddhe vārayām āsa bhārataa śikhaṇḍinas tato bāṇān kṛpaḥ śāradvato yudhic prāhiṇot tvarayā yukto didhakṣur iva māriṣaa tāñ śarān preṣitāṃs tena samantād dhemabhūṣaṇānc ciccheda khaḍgam āvidhya bhrāmayaṃś ca punaḥ punaḥa śatacandraṃ tataś carma gautamaḥ pārṣatasya hac vyadhamat sāyakais tūrṇaṃ tata uccukruśur janāḥa sa vicarmā mahārāja khaḍgapāṇir upādravatc kṛpasya vaśam āpanno mṛtyor āsyam ivāturaḥa śāradvataśarair grastaṃ kliśyamānaṃ mahābalamc citraketusuto rājan suketus tvarito yayaua vikiran brāhmaṇaṃ yuddhe bahubhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc abhyāpatad ameyātmā gautamasya rathaṃ pratia dṛṣṭvāviṣahyaṃ taṃ yuddhe brāhmaṇaṃ caritavratamc apayātas tatas tūrṇaṃ śikhaṇḍī rājasattamaa suketus tu tato rājan gautamaṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥc viddhvā vivyādha saptatyā punaś cainaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥa athāsya saśaraṃ cāpaṃ punaś ciccheda māriṣac sārathiṃ ca śareṇāsya bhṛśaṃ marmaṇy atāḍayata gautamas tu tataḥ kruddho dhanur gṛhya navaṃ dṛḍhamc suketuṃ triṃśatā bāṇaiḥ sarvamarmasv atāḍayata sa vihvalitasarvāṅgaḥ pracacāla rathottamec bhūmicāle yathā vṛkṣaś calaty ākampito bhṛśama calatas tasya kāyāt tu śiro jvalitakuṇḍalamc soṣṇīṣaṃ saśirastrāṇaṃ kṣurapreṇānvapātayata tac chiraḥ prāpatad bhūmau śyenāhṛtam ivāmiṣamc tato sya kāyo vasudhāṃ paścāt prāpa tadā cyutaḥa tasmin hate mahārāja trastās tasya padānugāḥc gautamaṃ samare tyaktvā dudruvus te diśo daśaa dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ tu samare saṃnivārya mahābalaḥc kṛtavarmābravīd dhṛṣṭas tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti pārṣatama tad abhūt tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ vṛṣṇipārṣatayo raṇec āmiṣārthe yathā yuddhaṃ śyenayor gṛddhayor nṛpaa dhṛṣṭadyumnas tu samare hārdikyaṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥc ājaghānorasi kruddhaḥ pīḍayan hṛdikātmajama kṛtavarmā tu samare pārṣatena dṛḍhāhataḥc pārṣataṃ sarathaṃ sāśvaṃ chādayām āsa sāyakaiḥa sarathaś chādito rājan dhṛṣṭadyumno na dṛśyatec meghair iva paricchanno bhāskaro jaladāgamea vidhūya taṃ bāṇagaṇaṃ śaraiḥ kanakabhūṣaṇaiḥc vyarocata raṇe rājan dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ kṛtavraṇaḥa tatas tu pārṣataḥ kruddhaḥ śastravṛṣṭiṃ sudāruṇāmc kṛtavarmāṇam āsādya vyasṛjat pṛtanāpatiḥa tām āpatantīṃ sahasā śastravṛṣṭiṃ nirantarāmc śarair anekasāhasrair hārdikyo vyadhamad yudhid yathā rukmarathenājau vāhān vāhair amiśrayatd tathaiva sātvato rājan vāhān vāhair amiśrayatd gṛhītvā carma khaḍgaṃ ca rathaṃ tasyāvapupluved miśriteṣv atha vāheṣu pratyāsanne ca pārṣated dṛṣṭvāpadānaṃ tasyāśu gadāṃ jagrāha sātvataḥd gadāpāṇis tato rājan rathāt tūrṇam avaplutaḥd tam adṛṣṭvā rathopasthe sārathiṃ samatāḍayatd khaḍgena śitadhāreṇa sa hataḥ prāpatad rathātd kṛtavarmā tato hṛṣṭas talaśabdaṃ cakāra had pārṣataṃ cābravīd rājann ehy ehīti punaḥ punaḥd sa taṃ na mamṛṣe yuddhe talaśabdaṃ samīritamd yathā nāgaḥ sadā mattas talaśabdaṃ samīritamd avaplutya rathāt tasmāt svarathaṃ punar āsthitaḥd abhyayāt sa tu taṃ tūrṇaṃ tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravītd kṛtavarmā susaṃkruddho didhakṣur iva pāvakaḥd dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhān sarvān pāṇḍavān paryavārayatd tato rājan maheṣvāsaḥ kṛtavarmāṇam āśu vaid gadāṃ gṛhya punar vegāt kṛtavarmāṇam āhanatd so tividdho balavatā nyapatan mūrchayā hataḥd tato rājan maheṣvāsaṃ kṛtavarmāṇam āśu vaid śrutavān ratham āropya apovāha raṇājirāta dṛṣṭvā tu dāritāṃ yuddhe śastravṛṣṭiṃ duruttarāmc kṛtavarmāṇam abhyetya vārayām āsa pārṣataḥd hārdikyaṃ chādayām āsa pārṣato niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa sārathiṃ cāsya tarasā prāhiṇod yamasādanamc bhallena śitadhāreṇa sa hataḥ prāpatad rathāta dhṛṣṭadyumnas tu balavāñ jitvā śatruṃ mahārathamc kauravān samare tūrṇaṃ vārayām āsa sāyakaiḥa tatas te tāvakā yodhā dhṛṣṭadyumnam upādravanc siṃhanādaravaṃ kṛtvā tato yuddham avartata saṃjaya uvācaa drauṇir yudhiṣṭhiraṃ dṛṣṭvā śaineyenābhirakṣitamc draupadeyais tathā śūrair abhyavartata hṛṣṭavata kirann iṣugaṇān ghorān svarṇapuṅkhāñ śilāśitānc darśayan vividhān mārgāñ śikṣārthaṃ laghuhastavata tataḥ khaṃ pūrayām āsa śarair divyāstramantritaiḥc yudhiṣṭhiraṃ ca samare paryavārayad astravita drauṇāyaniśaracchannaṃ na prājñāyata kiṃ canac bāṇabhūtam abhūt sarvam āyodhanaśiro hi tata bāṇajālaṃ diviṣṭhaṃ tat svarṇajālavibhūṣitamc śuśubhe bharataśreṣṭha vitānam iva viṣṭhitama tena channe raṇe rājan bāṇajālena bhāsvatāc abhracchāyeva saṃjajñe bāṇaruddhe nabhastalea tatrāścaryam apaśyāma bāṇabhūte tathāvidhec na sma saṃpatate bhūmau dṛṣṭvā drauṇeḥ parākramama lāghavaṃ droṇaputrasya dṛṣṭvā tatra mahārathāḥc vyasmayanta mahārāja na cainaṃ prativīkṣitume śekus te sarvarājānas tapantam iva bhāskarama sātyakir yatamānas tu dharmarājaś ca pāṇḍavaḥc tathetarāṇi sainyāni na sma cakruḥ parākramama vadhyamāne tataḥ sainye draupadeyā mahārathāḥc sātyakir dharmarājaś ca pāñcālāś cāpi saṃgatāḥe tyaktvā mṛtyubhayaṃ ghoraṃ drauṇāyanim upādravana sātyakiḥ pañcaviṃśatyā drauṇiṃ viddhvā śilāmukhaiḥc punar vivyādha nārācaiḥ saptabhiḥ svarṇabhūṣitaiḥa yudhiṣṭhiras trisaptatyā prativindhyaś ca saptabhiḥc śrutakarmā tribhir bāṇaiḥ śrutakīrtis tu saptabhiḥa sutasomaś ca navabhiḥ śatānīkaś ca saptabhiḥc anye ca bahavaḥ śūrā vivyadhus taṃ samantataḥa so tikruddhas tato rājann āśīviṣa iva śvasanc sātyakiṃ pañcaviṃśatyā prāvidhyata śilāśitaiḥa śrutakīrtiṃ ca navabhiḥ sutasomaṃ ca pañcabhiḥc aṣṭabhiḥ śrutakarmāṇaṃ prativindhyaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥe śatānīkaṃ ca navabhir dharmaputraṃ ca saptabhiḥa athetarāṃs tataḥ śūrān dvābhyāṃ dvābhyām atāḍayatc śrutakīrtes tathā cāpaṃ ciccheda niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa athānyad dhanur ādāya śrutakīrtir mahārathaḥc drauṇāyaniṃ tribhir viddhvā vivyādhānyaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥa tato drauṇir mahārāja śaravarṣeṇa bhāratac chādayām āsa tat sainyaṃ samantāc ca śarair nṛpāna tataḥ punar ameyātmā dharmarājasya kārmukamc drauṇiś ciccheda vihasan vivyādha ca śarais tribhiḥa tato dharmasuto rājan pragṛhyānyan mahad dhanuḥc drauṇiṃ vivyādha saptatyā bāhvor urasi cārdayata sātyakis tu tataḥ kruddho drauṇeḥ praharato raṇec ardhacandreṇa tīkṣṇena dhanuś chittvānadad bhṛśama chinnadhanvā tato drauṇiḥ śaktyā śaktimatāṃ varaḥc sārathiṃ pātayām āsa śaineyasya rathād drutama athānyad dhanur ādāya droṇaputraḥ pratāpavānc śaineyaṃ śaravarṣeṇa chādayām āsa bhārataa tasyāśvāḥ pradrutāḥ saṃkhye patite rathasārathauc tatra tatraiva dhāvantaḥ samadṛśyanta bhārataa yudhiṣṭhirapurogās te drauṇiṃ śastrabhṛtāṃ varamc abhyavarṣanta vegena visṛjantaḥ śitāñ śarāna āgacchamānāṃs tān dṛṣṭvā raudrarūpān paraṃtapaḥc prahasan pratijagrāha droṇaputro mahāraṇea tataḥ śaraśatajvālaḥ senākakṣaṃ mahārathaḥc drauṇir dadāha samare kakṣam agnir yathā vanea tad balaṃ pāṇḍuputrasya droṇaputrapratāpitamc cukṣubhe bharataśreṣṭha timineva nadīmukhamc   tasminn eva camūmukhec tad balaṃ pāṇḍaveyasya droṇaputraśarārciṣāc tāpayan bharataśreṣṭha gabhastibhir ivāṃśumānc tat tāpyamānaṃ tīkṣṇāgrair brāhmaṇasya ca sāyakaiḥc kṣubhyate pāṇḍavaṃ sainyaṃc tad bhajyamānaṃ marṣeṇa brāhmaṇasya śarāhatama dṛṣṭvā te ca mahārāja droṇaputraparākramamc nihatān menire sarvān pāṇḍūn droṇasutena vaia yudhiṣṭhiras tu tvarito drauṇiṃ śliṣya mahārathamc abravīd droṇaputraṃ tu roṣāmarṣasamanvitaḥd jānāmi tvāṃ yudhi śreṣṭhaṃ vīryavantaṃ balānvitamd kṛtāstraṃ kṛtinaṃ caiva tathā laghuparākramamd balam etad bhavān sarvaṃ pārṣate yadi darśayetd tatas tvāṃ balavantaṃ ca kṛtavīryaṃ ca vidmahed sa hi vai pārṣataṃ dṛṣṭvā samare śatrusūdanamd bhavet tava balaṃ kiṃ cid bravīmi tvāṃ na tu dvijaa naiva nāma tava prītir naiva nāma kṛtajñatāc yatas tvaṃ puruṣavyāghra mām evādya jighāṃsasia brāhmaṇena tapaḥ kāryaṃ dānam adhyayanaṃ tathāc kṣatriyeṇa dhanur nāmyaṃ sa bhavān brāhmaṇabruvaḥa miṣatas te mahābāho jeṣyāmi yudhi kauravānc kuruṣva samare karma brahmabandhur asi dhruvama evam ukto mahārāja droṇaputraḥ smayann ivac yuktatvaṃ tac ca saṃcintya nottaraṃ kiṃ cid abravīta anuktvā ca tataḥ kiṃ cic charavarṣeṇa pāṇḍavamc chādayām āsa samare kruddho ntaka iva prajāḥa saṃchādyamānas tu tadā droṇaputreṇa māriṣac pārtho payātaḥ śīghraṃ vai vihāya mahatīṃ camūma apayāte tatas tasmin dharmaputre yudhiṣṭhirec droṇaputraḥ sthito rājan pratyādeśān mahātmanaḥa tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā tyaktvā drauṇiṃ mahāhavec prayayau tāvakaṃ sainyaṃ yuktaḥ krūrāya karmaṇe saṃjaya uvācaa bhīmasenaṃ sapāñcālyaṃ cedikekayasaṃvṛtamc vaikartanaḥ svayaṃ ruddhvā vārayām āsa sāyakaiḥa tatas tu cedikārūṣān sṛñjayāṃś ca mahārathānc karṇo jaghāna saṃkruddho bhīmasenasya paśyataḥa bhīmasenas tataḥ karṇaṃ vihāya rathasattamamc prayayau kauravaṃ sainyaṃ kakṣam agnir iva jvalana sūtaputro pi samare pāñcālān kekayāṃs tathāc sṛñjayāṃś ca maheṣvāsān nijaghāna sahasraśaḥa saṃśaptakeṣu pārthaś ca kauraveṣu vṛkodaraḥc pāñcāleṣu tathā karṇaḥ kṣayaṃ cakrūr mahārathāḥa te kṣatriyā dahyamānās tribhis taiḥ pāvakopamaiḥc jagmur vināśaṃ samare rājan durmantrite tavaa tato duryodhanaḥ kruddho nakulaṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥc vivyādha bharataśreṣṭha caturaś cāsya vājinaḥa tataḥ punar ameyātmā tava putro janādhipaḥc kṣureṇa sahadevasya dhvajaṃ ciccheda kāñcanama nakulas tu tataḥ kruddhas tava putraṃ trisaptabhiḥc jaghāna samare rājan sahadevaś ca pañcabhiḥa tāv ubhau bharataśreṣṭhau śreṣṭhau sarvadhanuṣmatāmc vivyādhorasi saṃkruddhaḥ pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥa tato parābhyāṃ bhallābhyāṃ dhanuṣī samakṛntatac yamayoḥ prahasan rājan vivyādhaiva ca saptabhiḥa tāv anye dhanuṣī śreṣṭhe śakracāpanibhe śubhec pragṛhya rejatuḥ śūrau devaputrasamau yudhia tatas tau rabhasau yuddhe bhrātarau bhrātaraṃ nṛpac śarair vavarṣatur ghorair mahāmeghau yathācalama tataḥ kruddho mahārāja tava putro mahārathaḥc pāṇḍuputrau maheṣvāsau vārayām āsa patribhiḥa dhanurmaṇḍalam evāsya dṛśyate yudhi bhāratac sāyakāś caiva dṛśyante niścarantaḥ samantataḥa tasya sāyakasaṃchannau cakāśetāṃ ca pāṇḍavauc meghacchannau yathā vyomni candrasūryau hataprabhaua te tu bāṇā mahārāja hemapuṅkhāḥ śilāśitāḥc ācchādayan diśaḥ sarvāḥ sūryasyevāṃśavas tadāa bāṇabhūte tatas tasmin saṃchanne ca nabhastaleb nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca krodhaṃ tīvraṃ samāsthitaub tāṃ bāṇavṛṣṭiṃ rājñas tu śaraiḥ śatasahasrabhiḥ sicb chādayām āsatur ubhau bāṇaughais tanayaṃ tavab tatas tayor mahārāja sṛjator aniśaṃ śarānc yamābhyāṃ dadṛśe rūpaṃ kālāntakayamopamama parākramaṃ tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā tava sūnor mahārathāḥb krodham āsthāya paramaṃ niḥśvasaṃś ca yathoragaḥb bāṇāndhakāraṃ sasṛje tava putras tayos tadāc mṛtyor upāntikaṃ prāptau mādrīputrau sma menirea tataḥ senāpatī rājan pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥc pārṣataḥ prayayau tatra yatra rājā suyodhanaḥa mādrīputrau tataḥ śūrau vyatikramya mahārathauc dhṛṣṭadyumnas tava sutaṃ tāḍayām āsa sāyakaiḥa tam avidhyad ameyātmā tava putro tyamarṣaṇaḥc pāñcālyaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā prahasya puruṣarṣabhaa tataḥ punar ameyātmā putras te pṛthivīpatec viddhvā nanāda pāñcālyaṃ ṣaṣṭyā pañcabhir eva caa athāsya saśaraṃ cāpaṃ hastāvāpaṃ ca māriṣac kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena rājā ciccheda saṃyugea tad apāsya dhanuś chinnaṃ pāñcālyaḥ śatrukarśanaḥc anyad ādatta vegena dhanur bhārasahaṃ navama prajvalann iva vegena saṃrambhād rudhirekṣaṇaḥc aśobhata maheṣvāso dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ kṛtavraṇaḥa sa pañcadaśa nārācāñ śvasataḥ pannagān ivac jighāṃsur bharataśreṣṭhaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumno vyavāsṛjata te varma hemavikṛtaṃ bhittvā rājñaḥ śilāśitāḥc viviśur vasudhāṃ vegāt kaṅkabarhiṇavāsasaḥa so tividdho mahārāja putras te tivyarājatac vasante puṣpaśabalaḥ sapuṣpa iva kiṃśukaḥa sa chinnavarmā nārācaiḥ prahārair jarjaracchaviḥc dhṛṣṭadyumnasya bhallena kruddhaś ciccheda kārmukama athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ tvaramāṇo mahīpatiḥc sāyakair daśabhī rājan bhruvor madhye samārdayatd vivyādha vividhair bāṇaiḥ kālāntakayamopamaiḥa tasya te śobhayan vaktraṃ karmāraparimārjitāḥc praphullaṃ campakaṃ yadvad bhramarā madhulipsavaḥa tad apāsya dhanuś chinnaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumno mahāmanāḥc anyad ādatta vegena dhanur bhallāṃś ca ṣoḍaśaa tato duryodhanasyāśvān hatvā sūtaṃ ca pañcabhiḥc dhanuś ciccheda bhallena jātarūpapariṣkṛtama rathaṃ sopaskaraṃ chatraṃ śaktiṃ khaḍgaṃ gadāṃ dhvajamc bhallaiś ciccheda navabhiḥ putrasya tava pārṣataḥa tapanīyāṅgadaṃ citraṃ nāgaṃ maṇimayaṃ śubhamc dhvajaṃ kurupateś chinnaṃ dadṛśuḥ sarvapārthivāḥa duryodhanaṃ tu virathaṃ chinnasarvāyudhaṃ raṇec bhrātaraḥ paryarakṣanta sodaryā bharatarṣabhaa tam āropya rathe rājan daṇḍadhāro janādhipamc apovāha ca saṃbhrānto dhṛṣṭadyumnasya paśyataḥa karṇas tu sātyakiṃ jitvā rājagṛddhī mahābalaḥc droṇahantāram ugreṣuṃ sasārābhimukhaṃ raṇea taṃ pṛṣṭhato bhyayāt tūrṇaṃ śaineyo vitudañ śaraiḥc vāraṇaṃ jaghanopānte viṣāṇābhyām iva dvipaḥa sa bhārata mahān āsīd yodhānāṃ sumahātmanāmc karṇapārṣatayor madhye tvadīyānāṃ mahāraṇaḥa na pāṇḍavānāṃ nāsmākaṃ yodhaḥ kaś cit parāṅmukhaḥc pratyadṛśyata yat karṇaḥ pāñcālāṃs tvarito yayaua tasmin kṣaṇe naraśreṣṭha gajavājinarakṣayaḥc prādurāsīd ubhayato rājan madhyaṃgate hania pāñcālās tu mahārāja tvaritā vijigīṣavaḥc sarvato bhyadravan karṇaṃ patatriṇa iva drumama teṣām ādhirathiḥ kruddho yatamānān manasvinaḥc vicinvann eva bāṇāgraiḥ samāsādayad agrataḥa vyāghraketuṃ suśarmāṇaṃ śaṅkuṃ cograṃ dhanaṃjayamc śuklaṃ ca rocamānaṃ ca siṃhasenaṃ ca durjayama te vīrā rathavegena parivavrur narottamamc sṛjantaṃ sāyakān kruddhaṃ karṇam āhavaśobhinama yudhyamānāṃs tu tāñ śūrān manujendraḥ pratāpavānc aṣṭābhir aṣṭau rādheyo nyahanan niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa athāparān mahārāja sūtaputraḥ pratāpavānc jaghāna bahusāhasrān yodhān yuddhaviśāradaḥa viṣṇuṃ ca viṣṇukarmāṇaṃ devāpiṃ bhadram eva cac daṇḍaṃ ca samare rājaṃś citraṃ citrāyudhaṃ harima siṃhaketuṃ rocamānaṃ śalabhaṃ ca mahārathamc nijaghāna susaṃkruddhaś cedīnāṃ ca mahārathāna teṣām ādadataḥ prāṇān āsīd ādhirather vapuḥc śoṇitābhyukṣitāṅgasya rudrasyevorjitaṃ mahata tatra bhārata karṇena mātaṅgās tāḍitāḥ śaraiḥc sarvato bhyadravan bhītāḥ kurvanto mahad ākulama nipetur urvyāṃ samare karṇasāyakapīḍitāḥc kurvanto vividhān nādān vajranunnā ivācalāḥa gajavājimanuṣyaiś ca nipatadbhiḥ samantataḥc rathaiś cāvagatair mārge paryastīryata medinīa naiva bhīṣmo na ca droṇo nāpy anye yudhi tāvakāḥc cakruḥ sma tādṛśaṃ karma yādṛśaṃ vai kṛtaṃ raṇea sūtaputreṇa nāgeṣu ratheṣu ca hayeṣu cac nareṣu ca naravyāghra kṛtaṃ sma kadanaṃ mahata mṛgamadhye yathā siṃho dṛśyate nirbhayaś caranc pāñcālānāṃ tathā madhye karṇo carad abhītavata yathā mṛgagaṇāṃs trastān siṃho drāvayate diśaḥc pāñcālānāṃ rathavrātān karṇo drāvayate tathāa siṃhāsyaṃ ca yathā prāpya na jīvanti mṛgāḥ kva citc tathā karṇam anuprāpya na jīvanti mahārathāḥa vaiśvānaraṃ yathā dīptaṃ dahyante prāpya vai janāḥc karṇāgninā raṇe tadvad dagdhā bhārata sṛñjayāḥa karṇena cediṣv ekena pāñcāleṣu ca bhāratac viśrāvya nāma nihatā bahavaḥ śūrasaṃmatāḥa mama cāsīn manuṣyendra dṛṣṭvā karṇasya vikramamc naiko py ādhirather jīvan pāñcālyo mokṣyate yudhia pāñcālān vidhaman saṃkhye sūtaputraḥ pratāpavānb pāñcālān atha nighnantaṃ karṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahāraṇec abhyadhāvata saṃkruddho dharmaputraṃ yudhiṣṭhirama dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca rājānaṃ draupadeyāś ca māriṣac parivavrur amitraghnaṃ śataśaś cāpare janāḥa śikhaṇḍī sahadevaś ca nakulo nākulis tathāc janamejayaḥ śiner naptā bahavaś ca prabhadrakāḥa ete purogamā bhūtvā dhṛṣṭadyumnasya saṃyugec karṇam asyantam iṣvastrair vicerur amitaujasaḥa tāṃs tatrādhirathiḥ saṃkhye cedipāñcālapāṇḍavānb sātyakiṃ ca mahārāja nātyavartata saṃyugec eko bahūn abhyapatad garutman pannagān ivad taiḥ karṇasyābhavad yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ viśāṃ pated tādṛg yādṛk purā vṛttaṃ devānāṃ dānavaiḥ sahad tān sametān maheṣvāsāñ śaravarṣaughavarṣiṇaḥd eko bhyabhavad avyagras tamāṃsīva divākaraḥa bhīmasenas tu saṃkruddhaḥ kurūn madrān sakekayānb sarvato bhyahanat kruddho yamadaṇḍanibhaiḥ śaraiḥb bāhlīkān kekayān matsyān vāsātyān madrasaindhavānc ekaḥ saṃkhye maheṣvāso yodhayan bahv aśobhataa tatra marmasu bhīmena nārācais tāḍitā gajāḥc prapatanto hatārohāḥ kampayanti sma medinīma vājinaś ca hatārohāḥ pattayaś ca gatāsavaḥc śerate yudhi nirbhinnā vamanto rudhiraṃ bahud tāḍitāḥ sahasā nāgā bhīmasenena māriṣad nipatanti sma vegena vajrarugṇā ivācalāḥd nihatais tair mahārāja vegavadbhir mahāgajaiḥd śuśubhe vasudhā rājan vikīrṇair iva parvataiḥa sahasraśaś ca rathinaḥ patitāḥ patitāyudhāḥc akṣatāḥ samadṛśyanta bhīmād bhītā gatāsavaḥa rathibhir vājibhiḥ sūtaiḥ pattibhiś ca tathā gajaiḥc bhīmasenaśaracchinnair āstīrṇā vasudhābhavata tat stambhitam ivātiṣṭhad bhīmasenabalārditamc duryodhanabalaṃ rājan nirutsāhaṃ kṛtavraṇama niśceṣṭaṃ tumule dīnaṃ babhau tasmin mahāraṇec prasannasalilaḥ kāle yathā syāt sāgaro nṛpad tadvat tava balaṃ tad vai niścalaṃ samavasthitama manyuvīryabalopetaṃ balāt paryavaropitamc abhavat tava putrasya tat sainyam iṣubhis tadād tad balaṃ bharataśreṣṭha vadhyamānaṃ parasparame rudhiraughapariklinnaṃ rudhirārdraṃ babhūva haf jagāma bharataśreṣṭha vadhyamānaṃ parasparama sūtaputro raṇe kruddhaḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīmc bhīmasenaḥ kurūṃś cāpi drāvayan bahv aśobhataa vartamāne tathā raudre saṃgrāme dbhutadarśanec nihatya pṛtanāmadhye saṃśaptakagaṇān bahūna arjuno jayatāṃ śreṣṭho vāsudevam athābravītc prabhagnaṃ balam etad dhi yotsyamānaṃ janārdanaa ete dhāvanti sagaṇāḥ saṃśaptakamahārathāḥb durjayā hy eva samare devair api savāsavaiḥc apārayanto madbāṇān siṃhaśabdān mṛgā ivad kuravaś cāpi dhāvanti bhīmasenabhayārditāḥa dīryate ca mahat sainyaṃ sṛñjayānāṃ mahāraṇec hastikakṣyo hy asau kṛṣṇa ketuḥ karṇasya dhīmataḥe dṛśyate rājasainyasya madhye vicarato muhuḥa na ca karṇaṃ raṇe śaktā jetum anye mahārathāḥb durjayā hy eṣa samare devadānavarākṣasaiḥc jānīte hi bhavān karṇaṃ vīryavantaṃ parākramea tatra yāhi yataḥ karṇo drāvayaty eṣa no balama varjayitvā raṇe yāhi sūtaputraṃ mahārathamc śramo mā bādhate kṛṣṇa yathā vā tava rocatea etac chrutvā mahārāja govindaḥ prahasann ivac abravīd arjunaṃ tūrṇaṃ kauravāñ jahi pāṇḍavaa tatas tava mahat sainyaṃ govindapreritā hayāḥc haṃsavarṇāḥ praviviśur vahantaḥ kṛṣṇapāṇḍavaua keśavaprahitair aśvaiḥ śvetaiḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇaiḥc praviśadbhis tava balaṃ caturdiśam abhidyatad meghastanitanirhrādaḥ sa ratho vānaradhvajaḥd calatpatākas tāṃ senāṃ vimānaṃ dyām ivāviśataa tau vidārya mahāsenāṃ praviṣṭau keśavārjunauc kruddhau saṃrambharaktākṣau vyabhrājetāṃ mahādyutīa yuddhaśauṇḍau samāhūtāv aribhis tau raṇādhvaramc yajvabhir vidhināhūtau makhe devāv ivāśvinaud krodhatāmrekṣaṇau śūrau śuśubhāte mahābalaud madotkaṭau yathā nāgau dṛṣṭisaṃcāracāriṇaua kruddhau tau tu naravyāghrau vegavantau babhūvatuḥc talaśabdena ruṣitau yathā nāgau mahāhavea vigāhan sa rathānīkam aśvasaṃghāṃś ca phalgunaḥc vyacarat pṛtanāmadhye pāśahasta ivāntakaḥa taṃ dṛṣṭvā yudhi vikrāntaṃ senāyāṃ tava bhāratac saṃśaptakagaṇān bhūyaḥ putras te samacodayata tato rathasahasreṇa dviradānāṃ tribhiḥ śataiḥc caturdaśasahasraiś ca turagāṇāṃ mahāhavea dvābhyāṃ śatasahasrābhyāṃ padātīnāṃ ca dhanvināmc śūrāṇāṃ nāmalabdhānāṃ viditānāṃ samantataḥd duryodhanena te sārdhaṃ jātavegāḥ samantataḥe abhyavartanta tau vīrau chādayanto mahārathāḥf śaravarṣair mahārāja sarvataḥ pāṇḍunandanama sa chādyamānaḥ samare śaraiḥ parabalārdanaḥc darśayan raudram ātmānaṃ pāśahasta ivāntakaḥe nighnan saṃśaptakān pārthaḥ prekṣaṇīyataro bhavata tato vidyutprabhair bāṇaiḥ kārtasvaravibhūṣitaiḥc nirantaram ivākāśam āsīn nunnaiḥ kirīṭināa kirīṭibhujanirmuktaiḥ saṃpatadbhir mahāśaraiḥc samācchannaṃ babhau sarvaṃ kādraveyair iva prabhoa rukmapuṅkhān prasannāgrāñ śarān saṃnataparvaṇaḥc adarśayad ameyātmā dikṣu sarvāsu pāṇḍavaḥd mahī viyad diśaḥ sarvāḥ samudrā girayo pi vād sphuṭantīti janā jajñuḥ pārthasya talanisvanāta hatvā daśa sahasrāṇi pārthivānāṃ mahārathaḥc saṃśaptakānāṃ kaunteyaḥ prapakṣaṃ tvarito bhyayāta prapakṣaṃ sa samāsādya pārthaḥ kāmbojarakṣitamc pramamātha balād bāṇair dānavān iva vāsavaḥa pracicchedāśu bhallaiś ca dviṣatām ātatāyināmc śastrapāṇīṃs tathā bāhūṃs tathāpi ca śirāṃsy utaa aṅgāṅgāvayavaiś chinnair vyāyudhās te patan kṣitauc viṣvagvātābhisaṃbhagnā bahuśākhā iva drumāḥd kāmbojas tu tataḥ kruddho dṛṣṭvā pārthaṃ mahārathama hastyaśvarathapattīnāṃ vrātān nighnantam arjunamb acodayata yantāram arjunāyaiva māṃ vahab tatas taṃ rathināṃ śreṣṭhaṃ bahudakṣiṇam āhaveb arjunasya rathaṃ kṣipraṃ prāpayām āsa sārathiḥb tato rjunaṃ tribhir bāṇair viddhvā bhārasahair yudhib keśavaṃ navabhī rājan bāhvor urasi cāparyatb tataḥ kruddho mahārāja pāṇḍavaḥ paravīrahāc sudakṣiṇād avarajaḥ śaravṛṣṭyābhyavīvṛṣata asyāsyato rdhacandrābhyāṃ sa bāhū parighopamauc pūrṇacandrābhavaktraṃ ca kṣureṇābhyahanac chiraḥa sa papāta tato vāhāt svalohitaparisravaḥc manaḥśilāgireḥ śṛṅgaṃ vajreṇevāvadāritama sudakṣiṇād avarajaṃ kāmbojaṃ dadṛśur hatamc prāṃśuṃ kamalapatrākṣam atyarthaṃ priyadarśaname kāñcanastambhasaṃkāśaṃ bhinnaṃ hemagiriṃ yathāa tato bhavat punar yuddhaṃ ghoram adbhutadarśanamc nānāvasthāś ca yodhānāṃ babhūvus tatra yudhyatāma eteṣv āvarjitair aśvaiḥ kāmbojair yavanaiḥ śakaiḥc śoṇitāktais tadā raktaṃ sarvam āsīd viśāṃ patea rathai rathāśvasūtaiś ca hatārohaiś ca vājibhiḥc dviradaiś ca hatārohair mahāmātrair hatadvipaiḥe anyonyena mahārāja kṛto ghoro janakṣayaḥa tasmin prapakṣe pakṣe ca vadhyamāne mahātmanāc arjunaṃ jayatāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tvarito drauṇir āyayaua vidhunvāno mahac cāpaṃ kārtasvaravibhūṣitamc ādadānaḥ śarān ghorān svaraśmīn iva bhāskaraḥd krodhāmarṣavivṛttāsyo lohitākṣo babhau balīd antakāle yathā kruddho mṛtyuḥ kiṃkaradaṇḍabhṛtd tataḥ prāsṛjad ugrāṇi śaravarṣāṇi saṃghaśaḥd tair visṛṣṭair mahārāja vyadravat pāṇḍavī camūḥd sa dṛṣṭvaiva tu dāśārhaṃ syandanasthaṃ viśāṃ pated punaḥ prāsṛjad ugrāṇi śaravarṣāṇi māriṣad tayor āsīn mahad yuddhaṃ dharmabhrātror anaiṣṭhikamd visiṣmāpayiṣor lokaṃ yaśaś cottamam icchatoḥd saṃśaptakāṃs tu kaunteyaḥ kurūṃś cāpi vṛkodaraḥd sūtaputras tu pāñcālān bhūyo ghnaṃs tvaritāḥ śaraiḥd evam eṣa mahārāja vināśaḥ pṛthivīkṣitāmd āsīt kruddhe rjune karṇe bhīmasene ca dāruṇed yuddhaṃ ghoraṃ tathā tv āsīt tridhābhūte camūmukhea taiḥ patadbhir mahārāja drauṇimuktaiḥ samantataḥc saṃchāditau rathasthau tāv ubhau kṛṣṇadhanaṃjayaua tataḥ śaraśatais tīkṣṇair bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavānc niśceṣṭau tāv ubhau cakre yuddhe mādhavapāṇḍavaua hāhākṛtam abhūt sarvaṃ jaṅgamaṃ sthāvaraṃ tathāc carācarasya goptārau dṛṣṭvā saṃchāditau śaraiḥa siddhacāraṇasaṃghāś ca saṃpetur vai samantataḥc cintayanto bhaved adya lokānāṃ svasty apīty ahaa na mayā tādṛśo rājan dṛṣṭapūrvaḥ parākramaḥc saṃjajñe yādṛśo drauṇeḥ kṛṣṇau saṃchādayiṣyataḥa drauṇes tu dhanuṣaḥ śabdam ahitatrāsanaṃ raṇec aśrauṣaṃ bahuśo rājan siṃhasya nadato yathāa jyā cāsya carato yuddhe savyadakṣiṇam asyataḥc vidyud ambudamadhyasthā bhrājamāneva sābhavata sa tathā kṣiprakārī ca dṛḍhahastaś ca pāṇḍavaḥc saṃmohaṃ paramaṃ gatvā praikṣata droṇajaṃ tataḥa sa vikramaṃ hṛtaṃ mene ātmanaḥ sumahātmanāc tathāsya samare rājan vapur āsīt sudurdṛśama drauṇipāṇḍavayor evaṃ vartamāne mahāraṇec vardhamāne ca rājendra droṇaputre mahābalee hīyamāne ca kaunteye kṛṣṇaṃ roṣaḥ samabhyayāta sa roṣān niḥśvasan rājan nirdahann iva cakṣuṣāc drauṇiṃ hy apaśyat saṃgrāme phalgunaṃ ca muhur muhuḥa tataḥ kruddho bravīt kṛṣṇaḥ pārthaṃ sapraṇayaṃ tadāc atyadbhutam idaṃ pārtha tava paśyāmi saṃyugee atiśete hi yatra tvā droṇaputro dya bhārataf kaccid vīryaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ bhujayor vā balaṃ tavaa kaccit te gāṇḍivaṃ haste rathe tiṣṭhasi cārjunac kaccit kuśalinau bāhū kaccid vīryaṃ tad eva ted udīryamāṇaṃ hi raṇe paśyāmi drauṇim āhaved guruputra iti hy enaṃ mānayan bharatarṣabhad upekṣāṃ kuru mā pārtha nāyaṃ kāla upekṣituma evam uktas tu kṛṣṇena kṣiptvā bhallāṃś caturdaśac tvaramāṇas tvarākāle drauṇer dhanur athācchinate dhvajaṃ chatraṃ patākāṃ ca rathaṃ śaktiṃ gadāṃ tathāa jatrudeśe ca subhṛśaṃ vatsadantair atāḍayatc sa mūrcchāṃ paramāṃ gatvā dhvajayaṣṭiṃ samāśritaḥa taṃ visaṃjñaṃ mahārāja kirīṭibhayapīḍitamc apovāha raṇāt sūto rakṣamāṇo dhanaṃjayāta etasminn eva kāle tu vijayaḥ śatrutāpanaḥc nyavadhīt tāvakaṃ sainyaṃ śataśo tha sahasraśaḥe paśyatas tava putrasya tasya vīrasya bhārataa evam eṣa kṣayo vṛttas tāvakānāṃ paraiḥ sahac krūro viśasano ghoro rājan durmantrite tavaa saṃśaptakāṃś ca kaunteyaḥ kurūṃś cāpi vṛkodaraḥc vasuṣeṇaṃ ca pāñcālaḥ kṛtsnena vyadhamad raṇed vartamāne tathā raudre rājan vīravarakṣayed utthitāny agaṇeyāni kabandhāni samantataḥd yudhiṣṭhiro pi saṃgrāme prahārair gāḍhavedanaḥd krośamātram apakramya tasthau bharatasattamad saṃjayaḥd duryodhanas tataḥ karṇam upetya bharatarṣabhad abravīn madrarājaṃ ca tathaivānyān mahārathānd yadṛcchayopasaṃprāptaṃ svargadvāram apāvṛtamd sukhinaḥ kṣatriyāḥ karṇa labhante yuddham īdṛśamd sadṛśaiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ śūraiḥ śūrāṇāṃ yudhyatāṃ yudhid iṣṭaṃ bhavati rādheya tad idaṃ samupasthitamd hatvā vā pāṇḍavān yuddhe sphītām urvīm avāpsyathad nihatā vā parair yuddhe vīralokam avāpsyathad duryodhanasya tac chrutvā vacanaṃ kṣatriyarṣabhāḥd hṛṣṭā nādān udakrośan vāditrāṇi ca sarvaśaḥd tataḥ pramudite tasmin duryodhanabale tadād harṣayaṃs tāvakān yodhān drauṇir vacanam abravītd pratyakṣaṃ sarvasainyānāṃ bhavatāṃ cāpi paśyatāmd nyastaśastro mama pitā dhṛṣṭadyumnena pātitaḥd sa tenāham amarṣeṇa mitrārthe cāpi pārthivāḥd satyaṃ vaḥ pratijānāmi tad vākyaṃ me nibodhatad dhṛṣṭadyumnam ahatvāhaṃ na vimokṣyāmi daṃśanamd anṛtāyāṃ pratijñāyāṃ nāhaṃ svargam avāpnuyāmd arjuno bhīmasenaś ca yaś ca māṃ pratyudeṣyatid sarvāṃs tān pramathiṣye ham iti me nāsti saṃśayaḥd evam ukte tataḥ sarvā sahitā bhāratī camūḥd abhyadravata kaunteyāṃs tathā te cāpi pāṇḍavāḥd sa saṃnipāto rathayūthapānāṃd mahātmanāṃ bhārata mohanīyaḥd janakṣayaḥ kālayugāntakalpaḥd prāvartatāgre kurusṛñjayānāmd tataḥ pravṛtte yudhi saṃprahāred bhūtāni sarvāṇi sadaivatānid āsan sametāni sahāpsarobhird didṛkṣamāṇāni narapravīrānd divyaiś ca mālyair vividhaiś ca gandhaird divyaiś ca ratnair vividhair narāgryānd raṇe svakarmodvahataḥ pravīrānd avākirann apsarasaḥ prahṛṣṭāḥd samīraṇas tāṃś ca niṣevya gandhānd siṣeva sarvān api yodhamukhyānd niṣevyamāṇās tv anilena yodhāḥd parasparaghnā dharaṇīṃ nipetuḥd sā divyapuṣpair avakīryamāṇād suvarṇapuṅkhaiś ca śarair vicitraiḥd nakṣatrasaṃghair iva citritā dyauḥd kṣitair babhau yodhavarair vicitrād tato ntarikṣād api sādhuvādaird vāditraghoṣaiḥ samudīryamāṇaḥd jyāghoṣanemisvananādacitraḥd samākulaḥ so bhavat saṃprahāraḥd tathā tu tasmiṃs tumule pravṛtted duryodhanaḥ krodham amṛṣyamāṇaḥd abhyetya bhīmaṃ balinaṃ baliṣṭhaḥd samarpayat kṣudrakāṇāṃ śatenad duḥśāsanaś citrasenaś ca vīrasd tathā caivaṃ kitavaḥ saubalaś cad gajānīkaiḥ sarvato bhīmasenaṃd tathā viṣaktaṃ sahasaivābhyagacchand tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya gajānīkaṃ vṛkodaraḥd duryodhanaṃ mahābāhuḥ śaravarṣair avākiratd duryodhanaṃ tathā bhīmaḥ sāyakaiḥ śataśaḥ śitaiḥd pāṇḍavo vimukhīkṛtya gajān abhyadravad balīd tataḥ pāvakasaṃkāśair bhīmo bāṇair avakragaiḥd śalabhair iva nāgāṃs tān ardayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥd tataḥ kuñjarayūthāni bhīmaseno mahābalaḥd vyadhaman niśitair bāṇair mahābhrāṇīva mārutaḥd anvayus tad rathānīkaṃ maṇijālaiś ca kuñjarāḥd rūpyajāmbūnadābhāsāḥ kṣuramālyābhyalaṃkṛtāḥd vadhyamānāḥ śarai rājan bhīmasenena te gajāḥd vibhinnahṛdayāḥ ke cit tatraivābhyapatan bhuvid nipatadbhir mahāvegair hemabhāṇḍavibhūṣitaiḥd aśobhata mahārāja dhātucitrair ivācalaiḥd dīptābharaṇavadbhiś ca gajapṛṣṭhān nipātitaiḥd sa raṇaḥ śuśubhe rājan kṣīṇapuṇyair ivāmaraiḥd mahāparighasaṃkāśau candanāgarurūṣitaud apaśyan bhīmasenasya dhanur vikṣipato bhujaud tasya jyātalanirghoṣam asyataḥ savyadakṣiṇamd śrutvā hy abhyadravan nāgā bhīmasenaṃ bhayārditāḥd tasya bhīmasya tat karma rājann ekasya dhīmataḥd apaśyāma mahārāja tad adbhutam ivābhavatd saṃjaya uvācad evam eṣa mahān āsīt saṃgrāmaḥ pṛthivīkṣitāmd kruddhe rjune tathā karṇe bhīmasene ca pāṇḍaved droṇaputraṃ parājitya jitvā cānyān mahārathānd abravīd arjuno rājan vāsudevam idaṃ vacaḥd paśya kṛṣṇa mahābāho dravantīṃ pāṇḍavīṃ camūmd karṇaṃ paśya ca saṃgrāme kālayantaṃ mahārathānd na ca paśyāmi dāśārha dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiramd nāpi ketur yudhāṃ śreṣṭha dharmarājasya dṛśyated tribhāgaś cāvaśiṣṭo yaṃ divasasya janārdanad na ca māṃ dhārtarāṣṭreṣu kaś cid yudhyati saṃyuged tasmāt tvaṃ matpriyaṃ kurvan yāhi yatra yudhiṣṭhiraḥd dṛṣṭvā kuśalinaṃ yuddhe dharmaputraṃ sahānujamd punar yoddhāsmi vārṣṇeya śatrubhiḥ saha saṃyuged tataḥ prāyād rathenāśu bībhatsor vacanād dhariḥd yato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā sṛñjayāś ca mahārathāḥd ayudhyaṃs tāvakaiḥ sārdhaṃ mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanam saṃjaya uvācaa tvaramāṇaḥ punaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ pārtham abhyavadac chanaiḥc paśya kauravya rājānam apayātāṃś ca pāṇḍavāna karṇaṃ paśya mahāraṅge jvalantam iva pāvakamc asau bhīmo maheṣvāsaḥ saṃnivṛtto raṇaṃ pratia tam ete nu nivartante dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamāḥc pāñcālānāṃ sṛñjayānāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca yan mukhame nivṛttaiś ca tathā pārthair bhagnaṃ śatrubalaṃ mahata kauravān dravato hy eṣa karṇo dhārayate rjunac antakapratimo vege śakratulyaparākramaḥa asau gacchati kauravya drauṇir astrabhṛtāṃ varaḥc tam eṣa pradrutaḥ saṃkhye dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārathaḥd anuprayāti saṃgrāme hatān paśya ca sṛñjayāna sarvaṃ vyācaṣṭa durdharṣo vāsudevaḥ kirīṭinec tato rājan prādurāsīn mahāghoro mahāraṇaḥa siṃhanādaravāś cātra prādurāsan samāgamec ubhayoḥ senayo rājan mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanamd evam eṣa kṣayo vṛttaḥ pṛthivyāṃ pṛthivīpated tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca rājan durmantrite tava saṃjaya uvācaa tataḥ punaḥ samājagmur abhītāḥ kurusṛñjayāḥc yudhiṣṭhiramukhāḥ pārthā vaikartanamukhā vayama tataḥ pravavṛte bhīmaḥ saṃgrāmo lomaharṣaṇaḥc karṇasya pāṇḍavānāṃ ca yamarāṣṭravivardhanaḥa tasmin pravṛtte saṃgrāme tumule śoṇitodakec saṃśaptakeṣu śūreṣu kiṃcicchiṣṭeṣu bhārataa dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārāja sahitaḥ sarvarājabhiḥc karṇam evābhidudrāva pāṇḍavāś ca mahārathāḥa āgacchamānāṃs tān saṃkhye prahṛṣṭān vijayaiṣiṇaḥc dadhāraiko raṇe karṇo jalaughān iva parvataḥa tam āsādya tu te karṇaṃ vyaśīryanta mahārathāḥc yathācalaṃ samāsādya jalaughāḥ sarvatodiśame tayor āsīn mahārāja saṃgrāmo lomaharṣaṇaḥf prayudhyator mahāraṅge balinor vijigīṣatoḥa dhṛṣṭadyumnas tu rādheyaṃ śareṇa nataparvaṇāc tāḍayām āsa saṃkruddhas tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīta vijayaṃ tu dhanuḥśreṣṭhaṃ vidhunvāno mahārathaḥb vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi toyavarṣān ivāmbudaḥc pārṣatasya dhanuś chittvā śarān āśīviṣopamāne tāḍayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ pārṣataṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥa te varma hemavikṛtaṃ bhittvā tasya mahātmanaḥc śoṇitāktā vyarājanta śakragopā ivānaghaa tad apāsya dhanuś chinnaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārathaḥc anyad dhanur upādāya śarāṃś cāśīviṣopamāne karṇaṃ vivyādha saptatyā śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥa tathaiva rājan karṇo pi pārṣataṃ śatrutāpanamb chādayām āsa samare śarair āśīviṣopamaiḥc droṇaśatruṃ maheṣvāso vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa tasya karṇo mahārāja śaraṃ kanakabhūṣaṇamc preṣayām āsa saṃkruddho mṛtyudaṇḍam ivāparama tam āpatantaṃ sahasā ghorarūpaṃ viśāṃ patec ciccheda saptadhā rājañ śaineyaḥ kṛtahastavata dṛṣṭvā vinihitaṃ bāṇaṃ śaraiḥ karṇo viśāṃ patec sātyakiṃ śaravarṣeṇa samantāt paryavārayata vivyādha cainaṃ samare nārācais tatra saptabhiḥc taṃ pratyavidhyac chaineyaḥ śarair hemavibhūṣitaiḥa tato yuddham atīvāsīc cakṣuḥśrotrabhayāvahamc rājan ghoraṃ ca citraṃ ca prekṣaṇīyaṃ samantataḥa sarveṣāṃ tatra bhūtānāṃ lomaharṣo vyajāyatac tad dṛṣṭvā samare karma karṇaśaineyayor nṛpaa etasminn antare drauṇir abhyayāt sumahābalamc pārṣataṃ śatrudamanaṃ śatruvīryāsunāśanamd sa dṛṣṭvā samare karṇaṃ pārṣataṃ ca mahārathama abhyabhāṣata saṃkruddho drauṇir dūre dhanaṃjayeb rathaṃ rathena saṃpīḍya śatruvīryapraṇāśanaḥc tiṣṭha tiṣṭhādya brahmaghna na me jīvan vimokṣyasea ity uktvā subhṛśaṃ vīraḥ śīghrakṛn niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc pārṣataṃ chādayām āsa ghorarūpaiḥ sutejanaiḥe yatamānaṃ paraṃ śaktyā yatamāno mahārathaḥf chādayām āsa samare yatamāno mahārathaḥf yatnataḥ parayā śaktyā dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ mahāraṇef yodhayām āsa samare kruddharūpo viśāṃ patea yathā hi samare drauṇiḥ pārṣataṃ vīkṣya māriṣac tathā drauṇiṃ raṇe dṛṣṭvā pārṣataḥ paravīrahāe nātihṛṣṭamanā bhūtvā manyate mṛtyum ātmanaḥf sa jñātvā samare tmānaṃ śastreṇāvadhyam eva tuf javenābhiyayau drauṇiṃ kālaḥ kālam iva kṣayea drauṇis tu dṛṣṭvā rājendra dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ raṇe sthitamc krodhena niḥśvasan vīraḥ pārṣataṃ samupādravate tāv anyonyaṃ tu dṛṣṭvaiva saṃrambhaṃ jagmatuḥ paramf tato roṣaparītātmā dhṛṣṭadyumno py amarṣaṇaḥf provāca cainaṃ saṃrabdho droṇaputraṃ paraṃtapaḥf pragṛhya mahatī cāpe śarāsanavirājitea athābravīn mahārāja droṇaputraḥ pratāpavānc dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ samīpasthaṃ tvaramāṇo viśāṃ patee pāñcālāpasadādya tvāṃ preṣayiṣyāmi mṛtyavea pāpaṃ hi yat tvayā karma ghnatā droṇaṃ purā kṛtamc adya tvā patsyate tad vai yathā hy akuśalaṃ tathād pataṅgadarśanenādya darśanena vyapohyated śaśismaraṇatanmātrān vaṃśān kṛtam apohyated mayā mārayitavyas tvaṃ paśumāreṇa pārṣatad adya śvo vā paraśvo vā satyam etad bhaviṣyatia arakṣyamāṇaḥ pārthena yadi tiṣṭhasi saṃyugec nāpakramasi vā mūḍha satyam etad bravīmi tea evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ pratāpavānc prativākyaṃ sa evāsir māmako dāsyate tavae yenaiva te pitur dattaṃ yatamānasya saṃyugef eṣa te prativākyaṃ vai asir dāsyati māmakaḥf yena kṛttaṃ tava pitur yatamānasya tac chiraḥa yadi tāvan mayā droṇo nihato brāhmaṇabruvaḥc tvām idānīṃ kathaṃ yuddhe na haniṣyāmi vikramāta evam uktvā mahārāja senāpatir amarṣaṇaḥc niśitenātha bāṇena drauṇiṃ vivyādha pārṣataḥa tato drauṇiḥ susaṃkruddhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc prācchādayad diśo rājan dhṛṣṭadyumnasya saṃyugea naivāntarikṣaṃ na diśo naiva yodhāḥ samantataḥc dṛśyante vai mahārāja śaraiś channāḥ sahasraśaḥa tathaiva pārṣato rājan drauṇim āhavaśobhinamc śaraiḥ saṃchādayām āsa sūtaputrasya paśyataḥa rādheyo pi mahārāja pāñcālān saha pāṇḍavaiḥc draupadeyān yudhāmanyuṃ sātyakiṃ ca mahārathame ekaḥ sa vārayām āsa prekṣaṇīyaḥ samantataḥf sātyakiṃ ca mahārāja yodhāṃś cānyān sahasraśaḥa dhṛṣṭadyumno pi samare drauṇeś ciccheda kārmukamb kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena paśyatāṃ sarvayodhināmc tad apāsya dhanuś chinnam anyad ādatta kārmukame vegavat samare ghoraṃ śarāṃś cāśīviṣopamāna sa pārṣatasya rājendra dhanuḥ śaktiṃ gadāṃ dhvajamb sa śaktiṃ prāhiṇot tasmai tāṃ drauṇir vyadhamac charaiḥb tāṃ nikṛttāṃ raṇe dṛṣṭvā drauṇinā pārṣato balīb parighaṃ ghoram ādāya kārtasvaravibhūṣitamb cikṣepa bhujavīryeṇa pārṣato vai purā nadanb tam āpatantaṃ parighaṃ droṇaputrasya lāghavātb ciccheda bahudhā rājañ śarair atiratho raṇec hayān sūtaṃ rathaṃ caiva nimeṣād vyadhamac charaiḥd pārṣatasya tataḥ kruddho droṇaputraḥ paraṃtapaḥa sa chinnadhanvā viratho hatāśvo hatasārathiḥc khaḍgam ādatta vipulaṃ śatacandraṃ ca bhānumata drauṇis tad api rājendra bhallaiḥ kṣipraṃ mahārathaḥc ciccheda samare vīraḥ kṣiprahasto dṛḍhāyudhaḥe rathād anavarūḍhasya tad adbhutam ivābhavate   dhanvino bāhuśālinaḥe paśyatāṃ sarvasainyānāṃa dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ tu virathaṃ hatāśvaṃ chinnakārmukamc śaraiś ca bahudhā viddham astraiś ca śakalīkṛtame nātarad bharataśreṣṭha yatamāno mahārathaḥa tasyāntam iṣubhī rājan yadā drauṇir na jagmivānc atha tyaktvā dhanur vīraḥ pārṣataṃ tvarito nvagātd pragṛhya vipulaṃ khaḍgaṃ jātarūpapariṣkṛtama āsīd ādravato rājan vegas tasya mahātmanaḥc garuḍasyeva patato jighṛkṣoḥ pannagottamama etasminn eva kāle tu mādhavo rjunam abravītc paśya pārtha yathā drauṇiḥ pārṣatasya vadhaṃ pratid etasminn eva kāle tu keśavaḥ paravīrahād abravīd bharataśreṣṭham arjunaṃ jayatāṃ varamd paśya drauṇiṃ pārṣatasya yatamānaṃ vadhaṃ pratie yatnaṃ karoti vipulaṃ hanyāc cainam asaṃśayama taṃ mocaya mahābāho pārṣataṃ śatrutāpanamc drauṇer āsyam anuprāptaṃ mṛtyor āsyagataṃ yathāa evam uktvā mahārāja vāsudevaḥ pratāpavānc praiṣayat tatra turagān yatra drauṇir vyavasthitaḥa te hayāś candrasaṃkāśāḥ keśavena pracoditāḥc pibanta iva tad vyoma jagmur drauṇirathaṃ pratia dṛṣṭvāyāntau mahāvīryāv ubhau kṛṣṇadhanaṃjayauc dhṛṣṭadyumnavadhe rājaṃś cakre yatnaṃ mahābalaḥa vikṛṣyamāṇaṃ dṛṣṭvaiva dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ janeśvarac śarāṃś cikṣepa vai pārtho drauṇiṃ prati mahābalaḥa te śarā hemavikṛtā gāṇḍīvapreṣitā bhṛśamc drauṇim āsādya viviśur valmīkam iva pannagāḥa sa vidhvastaiḥ śarair ghorair droṇaputraḥ pratāpavānb utsṛjya samare rājan pāñcālyam amitaujasamc ratham āruruhe vīro dhanaṃjayaśarārditaḥe pragṛhya ca dhanuḥ śreṣṭhaṃ pārthaṃ vivyādha sāyakaiḥa etasminn antare vīraḥ sahadevo janādhipac apovāha rathenājau pārṣataṃ śatrutāpanama arjuno pi mahārāja drauṇiṃ vivyādha patribhiḥc taṃ droṇaputraḥ saṃkruddho bāhvor urasi cārdayata krodhitas tu raṇe pārtho nārācaṃ kālasaṃmitamc droṇaputrāya cikṣepa kāladaṇḍam ivāparame sa brāhmaṇasyāṃsadeśe nipapāta mahādyutiḥa sa vihvalo mahārāja śaravegena saṃyugec niṣasāda rathopasthe vaiklavyaṃ ca paraṃ yayaua tataḥ karṇo mahārāja vyākṣipad vijayaṃ dhanuḥc arjunaṃ samare kruddhaḥ prekṣamāṇo muhur muhuḥe dvairathaṃ cāpi pārthena kāmayāno mahāraṇea taṃ tu hitvā hataṃ vīraṃ sārathiḥ śatrukarśanamc apovāha rathenājau tvaramāṇo raṇājirāta athotkruṣṭaṃ mahārāja pāñcālair jitakāśibhiḥc mokṣitaṃ pārṣataṃ dṛṣṭvā droṇaputraṃ ca pīḍitama vāditrāṇi ca divyāni prāvādyanta sahasraśaḥc siṃhanādaś ca saṃjajñe dṛṣṭvā ghoraṃ mahādbhutama evaṃ kṛtvābravīt pārtho vāsudevaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥc yāhi saṃśaptakān kṛṣṇa kāryam etat paraṃ mamaa tataḥ prayāto dāśārhaḥ śrutvā pāṇḍavabhāṣitamc rathenātipatākena manomārutaraṃhasā saṃjaya uvāca teṣāṃ pravṛtte saṃgrāme vipule śoṇitodake rarāja lohitenorvī saṃraktā bahudhā bhṛśam tato rajasi saṃśānte rudhireṇa samantataḥ tadā vilokya pārthaṃ ca kṛṣṇo vacanam abravīta etasminn antare kṛṣṇaḥ pārthaṃ vacanam abravītc darśayann iva kaunteyaṃ dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhirama eṣa pāṇḍava te bhrātā dhārtarāṣṭrair mahābalaiḥc jighāṃsubhir maheṣvāsair drutaṃ pārthānusaryatea tathānuyānti saṃrabdhāḥ pāñcālā yuddhadurmadāḥc yudhiṣṭhiraṃ mahātmānaṃ parīpsanto mahājavāḥa eṣa duryodhanaḥ pārtha rathānīkena daṃśitaḥc rājā sarvasya lokasya rājānam anudhāvatia jighāṃsuḥ puruṣavyāghraṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito balīc āśīviṣasamasparśaiḥ sarvayuddhaviśāradaiḥa ete jighṛkṣavo yānti dvipāśvarathapattayaḥc yudhiṣṭhiraṃ dhārtarāṣṭrā ratnottamam ivārthinaḥa paśya sātvatabhīmābhyāṃ niruddhādhiṣṭhitaḥ prabhuḥc jihīrṣavo mṛtaṃ daityāḥ śakrāgnibhyām ivāvaśāḥa ete bahutvāt tvaritāḥ punar gacchanti pāṇḍavamc samudram iva vāryoghāḥ prāvṛṭkāle mahārathāḥa nadantaḥ siṃhanādāṃś ca dhamantaś cāpi vārijānc balavanto maheṣvāsā vidhunvanto dhanūṃṣi caa mṛtyor mukhagataṃ manye kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiramc hutam agnau ca bhadraṃ te duryodhanavaśaṃ gatama yathāyuktam anīkaṃ hi dhārtarāṣṭrasya pāṇḍavac nāsya śakro pi mucyeta saṃprāpto bāṇagocarama duryodhanasya śūrasya drauṇeḥ śāradvatasya cac karṇasya ceṣuvego vai parvatān api dārayeta duryodhanasya śūrasya śaraughāñ śīghram asyataḥc saṃkruddhasyāntakasyeva ko vegaṃ saṃsahed raṇea karṇena ca kṛto rājā vimukhaḥ śatrutāpanaḥc balavāṃl laghuhastaś ca kṛtī yuddhaviśāradaḥa rādheyaḥ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭhaṃ śaktaḥ pīḍayituṃ raṇec sahito dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putraiḥ śūro mahātmabhiḥa tasyaivaṃ yudhyamānasya saṃgrāme saṃyatātmanaḥc anyair api ca pārthasya hṛtaṃ varma mahārathaiḥa upavāsakṛśo rājā bhṛśaṃ bharatasattamac brāhme bale sthito hy eṣa na kṣatre tibale vibhod karme sute kṛtaṃ rāṣṭraṃ jīvitaṃ śatrutāpanaḥd nityānaśanasaṃgrāme samāptavrataniścayaḥd yo vatsodayikaṃ śrāddhe viśeṣeṇa mahībhujād karṇena cābhiyukto yaṃ bhūpatiḥ śatrutāpanaḥd saṃśayaṃ samanuprāptaḥ pāṇḍavo vai yudhiṣṭhiraḥa na jīvati mahārājo manye pārtha yudhiṣṭhiraḥc yad bhīmasenaḥ sahate siṃhanādam amarṣaṇaḥa nardatāṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ punaḥ punar ariṃdamac dhamatāṃ ca mahāśaṅkhān saṃgrāme jitakāśināma yudhiṣṭhiraṃ pāṇḍaveyaṃ hateti bharatarṣabhac saṃcodayaty asau karṇo dhārtarāṣṭrān mahābalānd astrair nānāvidhaiś citraiḥ kauravāḥ pārtha saṃyugea sthūṇākarṇendrajālena pārtha pāśupatena cac pracchādayanto rājānam anuyānti mahārathāḥe āturo me mato rājā saṃniṣevyaś ca bhārataa yathainam anuvartante pāñcālāḥ saha pāṇḍavaiḥc tvaramāṇās tvarākāle sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varāḥe majjantam iva pātāle balino py ujjihīrṣavaḥa na ketur dṛśyate rājñaḥ karṇena nihataḥ śaraiḥc paśyator yamayoḥ pārtha sātyakeś ca śikhaṇḍinaḥa dhṛṣṭadyumnasya bhīmasya śatānīkasya vā vibhoc pāñcālānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ cedīnāṃ caiva bhārataa eṣa karṇo raṇe pārtha pāṇḍavānām anīkinīmc śarair vidhvaṃsayati vai nalinīm iva kuñjaraḥa ete dravanti rathinas tvadīyāḥ pāṇḍunandanab drāvyamāṇā raṇe pārtha karṇenāmitatejasāc paśya paśya yathā pārtha gacchanty ete mahārathāḥa ete bhārata mātaṅgāḥ karṇenābhihatā raṇec ārtanādān vikurvāṇā vidravanti diśo daśaa rathānāṃ dravatāṃ vṛndaṃ paśya pārtha samantataḥc drāvyamāṇaṃ raṇe caiva karṇenāmitrakarśināa hastikakṣyāṃ raṇe paśya carantīṃ tatra tatra hac rathasthaṃ sūtaputrasya ketuṃ ketumatāṃ varaa asau dhāvati rādheyo bhīmasenarathaṃ pratic kirañ śaraśatānīva vinighnaṃs tava
