vāhinīma etān paśya ca pāñcālān drāvyamāṇān mahātmanāc śakreṇeva yathā daityān hanyamānān mahāhavea eṣa karṇo raṇe jitvā pāñcālān pāṇḍusṛñjayānc diśo viprekṣate sarvās tvadartham iti me matiḥa paśya pārtha dhanuḥ śreṣṭhaṃ vikarṣan sādhu śobhatec śatrūñ jitvā yathā śakro devasaṃghaiḥ samāvṛtaḥa ete nadanti kauravyā dṛṣṭvā karṇasya vikramamc trāsayanto raṇe pārthān sṛñjayāṃś ca sahasraśaḥa eṣa sarvātmanā pāṇḍūṃs trāsayitvā mahāraṇeb trāsayitvā raṇe pārtha rādheyo rathināṃ varaḥc abhibhāṣati rādheyaḥ sarvasainyāni mānadaḥa abhidravata gacchadhvaṃ drutaṃ dravata kauravāḥc yathā jīvan na vaḥ kaś cin mucyate yudhi sṛñjayaḥa tathā kuruta saṃyattā vayaṃ yāsyāma pṛṣṭhataḥc evam uktvā yayāv eṣa pṛṣṭhato vikirañ śaraiḥd rādheyaḥ kauravīṃ senāṃ rakṣamāṇaḥ samantataḥa paśya karṇaṃ raṇe pārtha śvetacchavivirājitamc udayaṃ parvataṃ yadvac chobhayan vai divākaraḥa pūrṇacandranikāśena mūrdhni chatreṇa bhāratac dhriyamāṇena samare tathā śataśalākināa eṣa tvāṃ prekṣate karṇaḥ sakaṭākṣo viśāṃ patec uttamaṃ yatnam āsthāya dhruvam eṣyati saṃyugea paśya hy enaṃ mahābāho vidhunvānaṃ mahad dhanuḥc śarāṃś cāśīviṣākārān visṛjantaṃ mahābalama asau nivṛtto rādheyo dṛśyate vānaradhvajab prārthayan samaraṃ pārtha tvayā saha paraṃtapac vadhāya cātmano bhyeti dīpasya śalabho yathād eṣa hy amarṣī śūraś ca dhārtarāṣṭrahite rataḥd tvāṃ na marṣayate pārtha nityam eva sumandadhīḥd ekākinaṃ ca dṛṣṭvainaṃ dhārtarāṣṭro raṇājired tvāṃ ca pārthābhisaṃrabdhaṃ karṇaṃ prati mahārathama karṇam ekākinaṃ dṛṣṭvā rathānīkena bhāratab asau duryodhanaḥ kruddho rathānīkena daṃśitaḥc rirakṣiṣuḥ susaṃyatto dhārtarāṣṭro bhivartatea sārvaiḥ sahaibhir duṣṭātmā vadhya eṣa prayatnataḥb adīnayor viśrutayor yuvayor yotsyamānayoḥb devāsure pārtha mṛdhe devadānavayor ivab paśyantu kauravāḥ sarve tava pārtha parākramamb tvāṃ ca dṛṣṭvātisaṃrabdhaṃ karṇaṃ ca bharatarṣabhab asau duryodhanaḥ kruddho nottaraṃ pratipadyatec tvayā yaśaś ca rājyaṃ ca sukhaṃ cottamam icchatāa ātmānaṃ ca kṛtātmānaṃ samīkṣya bharatarṣabhac kṛtāgasaṃ ca rādheyaṃ dharmātmani yudhiṣṭhired sahitaḥ sa tu duṣṭātmā dhārtarāṣṭro bhyavartated eṣa eva nihantavyo mūlaṃ vairasya bhāratad mūle chinne yathā nāśaḥ śākhānāṃ jāyate dhruvamd tathā duryodhane pārtha hate syur akhilā hatāḥd dhārtarāṣṭrā mahābāho sabhṛtyāmātyabāndhavāḥd paśya sarve yathā yodhā yānti bhīmarathaṃ pratid bhīmo pi śeroṣatāmrākṣo hanti śatrūn aśeṣataḥd eṣa dharmasuto rājā yamābhyāṃ paripālitaḥd duryodhano pi karṇena rakṣyate sasutena cad kṛtavarmā kṛpo drauṇī rakṣanto nyonyam uttamāḥd kulūkaḥ śakuniś caiva kṛtvā rakṣāṃ sthitāv ubhaua pratipadyasva rādheyaṃ prāptakālam anantaramc āryāṃ yuddhe matiṃ kṛtvā pratyehi rathayūthapama pañca hy etāni mukhyānāṃ rathānāṃ rathasattamac śatāny āyānti vegena balināṃ bhīmatejasāma pañca nāgasahasrāṇi dviguṇā vājinas tathāc abhisaṃhatya kaunteya padātiprayutāni cae anyonyarakṣitaṃ vīra balaṃ tvām abhivartatef droṇaputraṃ puraskṛtya tataḥ śīghraṃ ca sūdayaf nikṛtyaitad rathānīkaṃ balinaṃ lokaviśrutama sūtaputre maheṣvāse darśayātmānam ātmanāc uttamaṃ yatnam āsthāya pratyehi bharatarṣabhad bhūtāni caiva sarvāṇi kurupāñcālasṛñjayāḥa asau karṇaḥ susaṃrabdhaḥ pāñcālān abhidhāvatic ketum asya hi paśyāmi dhṛṣṭadyumnarathaṃ pratie samucchetsyati pāñcālān iti manye paraṃtapaa ācakṣe te priyaṃ pārtha tad evaṃ bharatarṣabhac rājā jīvati kauravyo dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥa asau bhimo mahābāhuḥ saṃnivṛttaś camūmukhec vṛtaḥ sṛñjayasainyena sātyakena ca bhārataa vadhyanta ete samare kauravā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc bhīmasenena kaunteya pāñcālaiś ca mahātmabhiḥa senā hi dhārtarāṣṭrasya vimukhā cābhavad raṇātc vipradhāvati vegena bhīmasya nihatā śaraiḥa vipannasasyeva mahī rudhireṇa samukṣitāc bhāratī bharataśreṣṭha senā kṛpaṇadarśanāa nivṛttaṃ paśya kaunteya bhīmasenaṃ yudhāṃ patimc āśīviṣam iva kruddhaṃ tasmād dravati vāhinīa pītaraktāsitasitās tārācandrārkamaṇḍitāḥc patākā viprakīryante chatrāṇy etāni cārjunaa sauvarṇā rājatāś caiva taijasāś ca pṛthagvidhāḥc ketavo vinipātyante hastyaśvaṃ viprakīryatea rathebhyaḥ prapatanty ete rathino vigatāsavaḥc nānāvarṇair hatā bāṇaiḥ pāñcālair apalāyibhiḥa nirmanuṣyān gajān aśvān rathāṃś caiva dhanaṃjayac samādravanti pāñcālā dhārtarāṣṭrāṃs tarasvinaḥa mṛdnanti ca naravyāghrā bhīmasenavyapāśrayātc balaṃ pareṣāṃ durdharṣaṃ tyaktvā prāṇān ariṃdamaa ete nadanti pāñcālā dhamanty api ca vārijānc abhidravanti ca raṇe nighnantaḥ sāyakaiḥ parāna paśya svargasya māhātmyaṃ pāñcālā hi paraṃtapac dhārtarāṣṭrān vinighnanti kruddhāḥ siṃhā iva dvipānd śastram ācchidya śatrūṇāṃ sāyudhānāṃ nirāyudhāḥd tenaivaitān amoghāstrā nighnanti ca nadanti cad śirāṃsy etāni pātyante śatrūṇāṃ bāhavo pi cad rathanāgahayā vīrā yaśasyāḥ sarva eva caa sarvataś cābhipannaiṣā dhārtarāṣṭrī mahācamūḥb pāñcālair māgadhaiś caiva yodhā nītā yamakṣayamb tyaktvā prāṇān maheṣvāsaiḥ pāñcālaiḥ paripātyatec pāñcālair mānasād etya haṃsair gaṅgeva vegitaiḥa subhṛśaṃ ca parākrāntāḥ pāñcālānāṃ nivāraṇec kṛpakarṇādayo vīrā ṛṣabhāṇām ivarṣabhāḥd suhṛdaś ca parākrāntāḥ kṛpakarṇādayo vibhod nivāraṇe maheṣvāsāḥ pāñcālānāṃ paraṃtapaa sunimagnāṃś ca bhīmāstrair dhārtarāṣṭrān mahārathānc dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhā vīrā ghnanti śatrūn sahasraśaḥd pāñcāleṣv abhibhūteṣu dviṣadbhir apabhīr nadand śatrupakṣam avaskandya śarān asyati mārutiḥd rathāś ca vimukhāḥ sarve nivṛtte bharatarṣabhee viṣaṇṇabhūyiṣṭharathā dhārtarāṣṭrī mahācamūḥf rathāś caite suvitrastā bhīmasenabhayārditāḥa paśya bhīmena nārācaiś chinnā nāgāḥ patanty amīb nānā nāgā hatā bāṇair bhīmena prapatanty amīc vajrivajrāhatānīva śikharāṇi mahībhṛtāmd bhīmasenena mātaṅgāḥ prāpitā yamasādanamd girīṇāṃ śikharāṇīva nipatanti nararṣabhaa bhīmasenasya nirviddhā bāṇaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc svāny anīkāni mṛdnanto dravanty ete mahāgajāḥd ete dravanti kuravo bhīmasenabhayārditāḥd tyaktvā rathān gajāṃś caiva hayāṃś caiva sahasraśaḥd hastyaśvarathapattīnaṃ dravatāṃ nisvanaṃ śṛṇud bhīmasenasya ninadaṃ drāvayāṇasya kauravāna nābhijānāsi bhīmasya siṃhanādaṃ durutsahamc nadato rjuna saṃgrāme vīrasya jitakāśinaḥa eṣa naiṣādir abhyeti dvipamukhyena pāṇḍavamc jighāṃsus tomaraiḥ kruddho daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥa satomarāv asya bhujau chinnau bhīmena garjataḥc tīkṣṇair agniśikhāprakhyair nārācair daśabhir hataḥa hatvainaṃ punar āyāti nāgān anyān prahāriṇaḥc paśya nīlāmbudanibhān mahāmātrair adhiṣṭhitāne śaktitomarasaṃkāśair vinighnantaṃ vṛkodarama sapta sapta ca nāgāṃs tān vaijayantīś ca sadhvajāḥc nihatya niśitair bāṇaiś chinnāḥ pārthāgrajena tee daśabhir daśabhiś caiko nārācair nihato gajaḥa na cāsau dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ śrūyate ninadas tathāc puraṃdarasame kruddhe nivṛtte bharatarṣabhea akṣauhiṇyas tathā tisro dhārtarāṣṭrasya saṃhatāḥc kruddhena narasiṃhena bhīmasenena vāritāḥd na śaknuvanti vai pārthaṃ pārthivāḥ samudīkṣitumd madhyaṃdinagataṃ sūryaṃ yathā durbalacakṣuṣaḥd ete bhīmasya saṃtrastāḥ siṃhasyevetare mṛgāḥd śaraiḥ saṃtrāsitāḥ saṃkhye na labhante sukhaṃ kva citd rājānaṃ ca mahābāhuṃ pīḍayanty āttamanyavaḥd rādheyo bahubhiḥ sārdham asau gacchati vegitaḥd varjayitvā tu bhīruṃ taṃ pārśvato hy ānayad dhanuḥd taṃ pālayan mahārājaṃ dhārtarāṣṭro balānvitaḥ saṃjaya uvāca etac chrutvā mahābāhur vāsudevād dhanaṃjayaḥa bhīmasenena tat karma kṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā suduṣkaramc arjuno vyadhamac chiṣṭān ahitān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa te vadhyamānāḥ samare saṃśaptakagaṇāḥ prabhob prabhagnāḥ samare bhītāḥ diśo daśa mahābalāḥc śakrasyātithitāṃ gatvā viśokā hy abhavan mudād śakrasyātithitāṃ prāptāḥ samapadyanta vijvarāḥd viśokāḥ samapadyanta śakrasyāntikatāṃ gatāḥd nārāyaṇāṃs tu gopālān vyadhamat pāṇḍunandanaḥd uttamaṃ vegam āsthāya caṇḍavāyur ghanān ivad anvakīryanta bhītās te tatra tatraiva bhāratad lulitāṃś ca tataḥ śūrān ahanat puruṣottamaḥa pārthaś ca puruṣavyāghraḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc jaghāna dhārtarāṣṭrasya caturvidhabalāṃ camūm dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa nivṛtte bhīmasene ca pāṇḍave ca yudhiṣṭhirec vadhyamāne bale cāpi māmake pāṇḍusṛñjayaiḥa dravamāṇe balaughe ca nirākrande muhur muhuḥb avaśeṣaṃ na paśyāmi mama sainyeṣu saṃjayab aho bata daśāṃ prāpto na hi śakṣyāmi jīvitumb jayakāṅkṣī kathaṃ sūta putrāṇām anivartināmb kathaṃ jīvāmi nihatāñ śrutvā ca mama sainikānb bahunādya kim uktena daivaṃ teṣāṃ parāyaṇamc kim akurvanta kuravas tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya saṃjaya uvāca kṣayas teṣāṃ mahāñ jāto rājan durmantrite tavaa dṛṣṭvā bhīmaṃ mahābāhuṃ sūtaputraḥ pratāpavānc krodharaktekṣaṇo rājan bhīmasenam upādravatd tiṣṭha tiṣṭha pṛthāputra paśya me dya parākramamd adya tvāṃ preṣayiṣyāmi yamasya sadanaṃ pratid ity uktvā prayayau tūrṇaṃ yatra bhīmo vyavasthitaḥa tāvakaṃ ca balaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenāt parāṅmukhamc yatnena mahatā rājan paryavasthāpayad balīa vyavasthāpya mahābāhus tava putrasya vāhinīmc pratyudyayau tadā karṇaḥ pāṇḍavān yuddhadurmadāna pratyudyayus tu rādheyaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥc dhunvānāḥ kārmukāṇy ājau vikṣipantaś ca sāyakāna bhīmasenaḥ śiner naptā śikhaṇḍī janamejayaḥc dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca balavān sarve cāpi prabhadrakāḥa pāñcālāś ca naravyāghrāḥ samantāt tava vāhinīmc abhyadravanta saṃkruddhāḥ samare jitakāśinaḥa tathaiva tāvakā rājan pāṇḍavānām anīkinīmc abhyadravanta tvaritā jighāṃsanto mahārathāḥa rathanāgāśvakalilaṃ pattidhvajasamākulamc babhūva puruṣavyāghra sainyam adbhutadarśanama śikhaṇḍī ca yayau karṇaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ sutaṃ tavac duḥśāsanaṃ mahārāja mahatyā senayā vṛtama nakulo vṛṣasenaṃ ca citrasenaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥc ulūkaṃ samare rājan sahadevaḥ samabhyayāta sātyakiḥ śakuniṃ cāpi bhīmasenaś ca kauravānc arjunaṃ ca raṇe yattaṃ droṇaputro mahārathaḥa yudhāmanyuṃ maheṣvāsaṃ gautamo bhyapatad raṇec kṛtavarmā ca balavān uttamaujasam ādravatd yudhāmanyuṃ kṛpo rājann uttamaujasam āhaved kṛtavarmā maheṣvāsaḥ paryavārayad āhavea bhīmasenaḥ kurūn sarvān putrāṃś ca tava māriṣac sahānīkān mahābāhur eka evābhyavārayata śikhaṇḍī ca tataḥ karṇaṃ vicarantam abhītavatc bhīṣmahantā mahārāja vārayām āsa patribhiḥa pratirabdhas tataḥ karṇo roṣāt prasphuritādharaḥc śikhaṇḍinaṃ tribhir bāṇair bhruvor madhye vyatāḍayata dhārayaṃs tu sa tān bāṇāñ śikhaṇḍī bahv aśobhatac rājataḥ parvato yadvat tribhiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ samanvitaḥa so tividdho maheṣvāsaḥ sūtaputreṇa saṃyugec karṇaṃ vivyādha samare navatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa tasya karṇo hayān hatvā sārathiṃ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥc unmamātha dhvajaṃ cāsya kṣurapreṇa mahārathaḥa hatāśvāt tu tato yānād avaplutya mahārathaḥb saṃchinnakārmuko rājan sūtaputreṇa saṃyugec śaktiṃ cikṣepa karṇāya saṃkruddhaḥ śatrutāpanaḥa tāṃ chittvā samare karṇas tribhir bhārata sāyakaiḥc śikhaṇḍinam athāvidhyan navabhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa karṇacāpacyutān bāṇān varjayaṃs tu narottamaḥc apayātas tatas tūrṇaṃ śikhaṇḍī jayatāṃ varaḥa tataḥ karṇo mahārāja pāṇḍusainyāny aśātayatc tūlarāśiṃ samāsādya yathā vāyur mahājavaḥa dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārāja tava putreṇa pīḍitaḥc duḥśāsanaṃ tribhir bāṇair abhyavidhyat stanāntarea tasya duḥśāsano bāhuṃ savyaṃ vivyādha māriṣac śitena rukmapuṅkhena bhallena nataparvaṇāa dhṛṣṭadyumnas tu nirviddhaḥ śaraṃ ghoram amarṣaṇaḥc duḥśāsanāya saṃkruddhaḥ preṣayām āsa bhāratad āśīviṣasamaṃ bāṇam āśu mārutaraṃhasama āpatantaṃ mahāvegaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnasamīritamc śaraiś ciccheda putras te tribhir eva viśāṃ patea athāparaiḥ saptadaśair bhallaiḥ kanakabhūṣaṇaiḥc dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ samāsādya bāhvor urasi cārdayata tataḥ sa pārṣataḥ kruddho dhanuś ciccheda māriṣac kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena tata uccukruśur janāḥa athānyad dhanur ādāya putras te bharatarṣabhac dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ śaravrātaiḥ samantāt paryavārayata tava putrasya te dṛṣṭvā vikramaṃ taṃ mahātmanaḥc vyahasanta raṇe yodhāḥ siddhāś cāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥd dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ na paśyāma ghaṭamānaṃ mahābalamd duḥśāsanena saṃruddhaṃ siṃheneva mahāgajamd tataḥ sarathanāgāśvāḥ pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍupūrvajad senāpatiṃ parīpsanto rurudhus tanayaṃ tavaa tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tāvakānāṃ paraiḥ sahac ghoraṃ prāṇabhṛtāṃ kāle ghorarūpaṃ paraṃtapaa nakulaṃ vṛṣasenas tu viddhvā pañcabhir āyasaiḥc pituḥ samīpe tiṣṭhantaṃ tribhir anyair avidhyataa nakulas tu tataḥ kruddho vṛṣasenaṃ smayann ivac nārācena sutīkṣṇena vivyādha hṛdaye dṛḍhama so tividdho balavatā śatruṇā śatrukarśanaḥc śatruṃ vivyādha viṃśatyā sa ca taṃ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥa tataḥ śarasahasreṇa tāv ubhau puruṣarṣabhauc anyonyam ācchādayatām athābhajyata vāhinīa dṛṣṭvā tu pradrutāṃ senāṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya sūtajaḥc nivārayām āsa balād anupatya viśāṃ pated etasminn antare kaṣṭaṃ yuddham āsīd viśāṃ patee nivṛtte tu tataḥ karṇe nakulaḥ kauravān yayauf vṛṣasenas tu pāñcālān pitrā sārdhaṃ viśāṃ patea karṇaputras tu samare hitvā nakulam eva tuc jugopa cakraṃ tvaritaṃ rādheyasyaiva māriṣaa ulūkas tu raṇe kruddhaḥ sahadevena vāritaḥb nivāritaḥ śaraśataiḥ kruddhena raṇamūrdhanic tasyāśvāṃś caturo hatvā sahadevaḥ pratāpavāne sārathiṃ preṣayām āsa yamasya sadanaṃ pratia ulūkas tu tato yānād avaplutya viśāṃ pateb apayātas tatas tūrṇam ulūko raṇamūrdhanic trigartānāṃ balaṃ pūrṇaṃ jagāma pitṛnandanaḥd ratham anyaṃ samāsthāya jagāma pitur antikama sātyakiḥ śakuniṃ viddhvā viṃśatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc dhvajaṃ ciccheda bhallena saubalasya hasann ivaa saubalas tasya samare kruddho rājan pratāpavānb sārathiṃ preṣayām āsa yamasya sadanaṃ pratic vidārya kavacaṃ bhūyo dhvajaṃ ciccheda kāñcanama athainaṃ niśitair bāṇaiḥ sātyakiḥ pratyavidhyatac sārathiṃ ca mahārāja tribhir eva samārdayate athāsya vāhāṃs tvaritaḥ śarair ninye yamakṣayama tato vaplutya sahasā śakunir bharatarṣabhac āruroha rathaṃ tūrṇam ulūkasya mahārathaḥe apovāhātha śīghraṃ sa śaineyād yuddhaśālinaḥf apovāha rathasthaṃ taṃ sātyakasyājisāgarāta sātyakis tu raṇe rājaṃs tāvakānām anīkinīmc abhidudrāva vegena tato nīkam abhidyataa śaineyaśaranunnaṃ tu tataḥ sainyaṃ viśāṃ patec bheje daśa diśas tūrṇaṃ nyapatac ca gatāsuvata bhīmasenaṃ tava suto vārayām āsa saṃyugec taṃ tu bhīmo muhūrtena vyaśvasūtarathadhvajame cakre lokeśvaraṃ tatra tenātuṣyanta cāraṇāḥf śatruṇā vijitaṃ jñātvā bhayāt supuruṣarṣabhaa tato pāyān nṛpas tatra bhīmasenasya gocarātc kurusainyaṃ tataḥ sarvaṃ bhīmasenam upādravate tatra rāvo mahān āsīd bhīmam ekaṃ jighāṃsatāma yudhāmanyuḥ kṛpaṃ viddhvā dhanur asyāśu cicchidec athānyad dhanur ādāya kṛpaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥa yudhāmanyor dhvajaṃ sūtaṃ chatraṃ cāpātayat kṣitauc tato pāyād rathenaiva yudhāmanyur mahārathaḥa uttamaujās tu hārdikyaṃ śarair bhīmaparākramamc chādayām āsa sahasā megho vṛṣṭyā yathācalama tad yuddhaṃ sumahac cāsīd ghorarūpaṃ paraṃtapac yādṛśaṃ na mayā yuddhaṃ dṛṣṭapūrvaṃ viśāṃ patea kṛtavarmā tato rājann uttamaujasam āhavec hṛdi vivyādha sa tadā rathopastha upāviśata sārathis tam apovāha rathena rathināṃ varamc tatas tu satvaraṃ rājan pāṇḍusainyam upādravatd kurusainyaṃ tataḥ sarvaṃ bhīmasenam upādravatd yudhiṣṭhiraś citrasenaṃ śaravarṣair avākiratd citraseno pi kaunteyaṃ saṃkruddhaḥ samavārayatd muhūrtād vimukhīkṛtya citrasenaṃ sa dharmarāṭd tāvakaṃ sainyam abhyaghnat samantān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥd tasmin pravṛtte tumule naravīrajanakṣayed duryodhanaḥ krodham upetya tīvraṃd krodhāgnināsau paridahyamānaḥd anyaṃ rathaṃ samupetyāśu caivad bhīmaṃ pravivyādha sucitrapuṅkhaiḥd duḥśāsano dyāpi ca citrasenod durdyūtasevī kitavaḥ saubalaś cad gajānīkaiḥ sarvato bhīmasenaṃd tathābhyarditaṃ sahasābhyadhāvatd tāvakāś ca mahābāho duryodhanapurogamāḥd yudhiṣṭhiraṃ jighṛkṣantaḥ sarvasainyam avākṣipand duḥśāsanaḥ saubalaś ca gajānīkena pāṇḍavamd mahatā parivāryaiva kṣudrakair abhyatāḍayatd tato bhīmaḥ śaraśatair duryodhanam amarṣaṇamd vimukhīkṛtya tarasā gajānīkam upādravatd tam āpatantaṃ sahasā gajānīkaṃ vṛkodaraḥd dṛṣṭvaiva subhṛśaṃ kruddho divyam astram udairayatd gajair gajān abhyahanad vajreṇendra ivāsurānd tato ntarikṣaṃ bāṇaughaiḥ śalabhair iva pādapamd chādayām āsa samare gajān nighnan vṛkodaraḥd tataḥ kuñjarayūthāni sametāni sahasraśaḥd vyadhamat tarasā bhīmo meghasaṃghān ivānilaḥd suvarṇajālāpihitā maṇijālaiś ca kuñjarāḥd rejur abhyadhikaṃ saṃkhye vidyutvanta ivāmbudāḥd te vadhyamānā bhīmena gajā rājan vidudruvuḥd ke cid vibhinnahṛdayāḥ kuñjarā nyapatan bhuvid patitair nipatadbhiś ca gajair hemavibhūṣitaiḥd aśobhata mahī tatra viśīrṇair iva parvataiḥd dīptābhai ratnavadbhiś ca patitair gajayodhibhiḥd rarāja bhūmiḥ patitaiḥ kṣīṇapuṇyair iva grahaiḥd tato bhinnakaṭā nāgā bhinnakumbhakarās tathād dudruvuḥ śataśaḥ saṃkhye bhīmasenaśarāhatāḥd ke cid vamanto rudhiraṃ bhayārtāḥ parvatopamāḥd vyadravañ śaraviddhāṅgā dhātucitrā ivācalāḥd mahābhujagasaṃkāśau candanāgarurūṣitaud apaśyaṃ bhīmasenasya dhanur vikṣipato bhujaud tasya jyātalanirghoṣaṃ śrutvāśanisamasvanamd vimuñcantaḥ śakṛnmūtraṃ gajāḥ prādudruvur bhṛśamd bhīmasenasya tat karma rājann ekasya dhīmataḥd nighnataḥ sarvabhūtāni rudrasyeva ca nirbabhaud saṃjaya uvācad tataḥ śvetāśvasaṃyukte nārāyaṇasamāhited tiṣṭhan rathavare śrīmān arjunaḥ samapadyatad tad balaṃ nṛpatiśreṣṭha tāvakaṃ vijayo raṇed vyakṣobhayad udīrṇāśvaṃ mahodadhim ivānalaḥd duryodhanas tava sutaḥ pramatte śvetavāhaned abhyetya sahasā kruddhaḥ sainyārdhenābhisaṃvṛtaḥd paryavārayad āyāntaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram amarṣaṇamd kṣuraprāṇāṃ trisaptatyā tato vidhyata pāṇḍavamd akrudhyata bhṛśaṃ tatra kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥd sa bhallāṃs triṃśatas tūrṇaṃ tava putre nyaveśayatd tato dhāvanta kauravyā jighṛkṣanto yudhiṣṭhiramd duṣṭabhāvān parāñ jñātvā samavetā mahārathāḥd ājagmus taṃ parīpsaṃtaḥ kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiramd nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥd akṣauhiṇyā parivṛtās te bhyadhāvan yudhiṣṭhiramd bhīmasenaś ca samare mṛdnaṃs tava mahārathānd abhyadhāvad abhiprepsū rājānaṃ śatrubhir vṛtamd tāṃs tu sarvān maheṣvāsān karṇo vaikartano nṛpad śaravarṣeṇa mahatā pratyavārayad āgatānd śaraughān visṛjantas te prerayantaś ca tomarānd na śekur yatnavanto pi rādheyaṃ prativīkṣitumd tāṃś ca sarvān maheṣvāsān sarvaśastrāstrapāragaḥd mahatā śaravarṣeṇa rādheyaḥ pratyavārayatd duryodhanaṃ tu viṃśatyā śīghram astram udīrayand avidhyat tūrṇam abhyetya sahadevo mahāmanāḥd sa viddhaḥ sahadevena rarājācalasaṃnibhaḥd prabhinna iva mātaṅgo rudhireṇa pariplutaḥd dṛṣṭvā tava sutaṃ tatra gāḍhaviddhaṃ sutejanaiḥd abhyadhāvad dṛḍhaṃ kruddho rādheyo rathināṃ varaḥd duryodhanaṃ tathā dṛṣṭvā śīghram astram udīrya saḥd tena yaudhiṣṭhiraṃ sainyam avadhīt pārṣataṃ tathād tato yaudhiṣṭhiraṃ sainyaṃ vadhyamānaṃ mahātmanād sahasā prādravad rājan sūtaputraśarārditamd vividhā viśikhās tatra saṃpatantaḥ parasparamd phalaiḥ puṅkhān samājaghnuḥ sūtaputradhanuścyutāḥd antarikṣe śaraughāṇāṃ patatāṃ ca parasparamd saṃgharṣeṇa mahārāja pāvakaḥ samajāyatad tato daśa diśaḥ karṇaḥ śalabhair iva yāyibhiḥd abhyaghnaṃs tarasā rājañ śaraiḥ paraśarīragaiḥd raktacandanasaṃdigdhau maṇihemavibhūṣitaud bāhū vyatyakṣipat karṇaḥ paramāstraṃ vidarśayand tataḥ sarvā diśo rājan sāyakair vipramohayand apīḍayad bhṛśaṃ karṇo dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiramd tataḥ kruddho mahārāja dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥd niśitair iṣubhiḥ karṇaṃ pañcāśadbhiḥ samārpayatd bāṇāndhakāram abhavat tad yuddhaṃ ghoradarśanamd hāhākāro mahān āsīt tāvakānāṃ viśāṃ pated vadhyamāne tadā sainye dharmaputreṇa māriṣad sāyakair vividhais tīkṣṇaiḥ kaṅkapatraiḥ śilāśitaiḥd bhallair anekair vividhaiḥ śaktyṛṣṭimusalair apid yatra yatra sa dharmātmā duṣṭāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ vyasarjayatd tatra tatra vyaśīryanta tāvakā bharatarṣabhad karṇo pi bhṛśasaṃkruddho dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiramd nārācair ardhacandraiś ca vatsadantaiś ca saṃyuged amarṣī krodhanaś caiva roṣaprasphuritānanaḥd sāyakair aprameyātmā yudhiṣṭhiram abhidravatd yudhiṣṭhiraś cāpi śataṃ svarṇapuṅkhaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥd prahasann iva taṃ karṇaḥ kaṅkapatraiḥ śilāśitaiḥd urasy avidhyad rājānaṃ tribhir bhallaiś ca pāṇḍavamd sa pīḍito bhṛśaṃ tena dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥd upaviśya rathopasthe sūtaṃ yāhīty acodayatd prākrośanta tataḥ sarve dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ sarājakāḥd gṛhīdhvam iti rājānam abhyadhāvanta sarvaśaḥd tataḥ śatāḥ saptadaśa kekayānāṃ prahāriṇāmd pāñcālaiḥ sahitā rājan dhārtarāṣṭrān nyavārayand tasmin sutumule yuddhe vartamāne janakṣayed duryodhanaś ca bhīmaś ca sameyātāṃ mahābalaud karṇo tha śarajālena kekayānāṃ mahārathānd vyadhamat parameṣvāsān agrataḥ paryavasthitānd teṣāṃ prayatamānānāṃ rādheyasya nivāraṇed rathān pañcaśatān karṇaḥ prāhiṇod yamasādanamd aviṣahyaṃ tato dṛṣṭvā rādheyaṃ yudhi yodhinaḥd bhīmasenam upāgacchan karṇabāṇaprapīḍitāḥd rathānīkaṃ vidāryaiva śarajālair anekadhād karṇa ekarathenaiva yudhiṣṭhiram upādravatd senāniveśam ārchantaṃ mārgaṇaiḥ kṣatavikṣatamd yamayor madhyagaṃ vīraṃ śanair yāntaṃ vicetasamd samāsādya tu rājānaṃ duryodhanahitepsayād sūtaputras tribhis tīkṣṇair vivyādha parameṣubhiḥd tathaiva rājā rādheyaṃ pratyavidhyat stanāntared śarais tribhiś ca yantāraṃ caturbhiś caturo hayānd cakrarakṣau tu pārthasya mādrīputrau paraṃtapaud tāv apy adhāvatāṃ karṇaṃ rājānaṃ mā vadhīr itid tau pṛthak śaravarṣābhyāṃ rādheyam abhyavarṣatāmd nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca paramaṃ yatnam āsthitaud tathaiva tau pratyavidhyat sūtaputraḥ pratāpavānd bhallābhyāṃ śitadhārābhyāṃ mahātmānāv ariṃdamaud dantavarṇāṃs tu rādheyo nijaghāna manojavānd yudhiṣṭhirasya saṃgrāme kālavālān hayottamānd tato pareṇa bhallena śirastrāṇam apātayatd kaunteyasya maheṣvāsaḥ prahasann iva sūtajaḥd tathaiva nakulasyāpi hayān hatvā pratāpavānd īṣāṃ dhanuś ca ciccheda mādrīputrasya dhīmataḥd tau hatāśvau hatarathau pāṇḍavau bhṛśavikṣataud bhrātarāv āruruhatuḥ sahadevarathaṃ tadād tau dṛṣṭvā mātulas tatra virathau paravīrahād abhyabhāṣata rādheyaṃ madrarājo nukampayād yoddhavyam adya pārthena phalgunena tvayā sahad kimarthaṃ dharmarājena yudhayse bhṛśaroṣitaḥd kṣīṇaśastrāstrakavacaḥ kṣīṇabāṇo vibāṇadhiḥd śrāntasārathivāhaś ca channo strair aribhis tathād pārtham āsādya rādheya upahāsyo bhaviṣyasid evam ukto pi karṇas tu madrarājena saṃyuged tathaiva karṇaḥ saṃrabdho yudhiṣṭhiram atāḍayatd śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ parāvidhya mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavaud prahasya samare karṇaś cakāra vimukhaṃ śaraiḥd tataḥ śalyaḥ prahasyedaṃ karṇaṃ punar uvāca had rathastham atisaṃrabdhaṃ yudhiṣṭhiravadhe dhṛtamd yadarthaṃ dhārtarāṣṭreṇa satataṃ mānito bhavānd taṃ pārthaṃ jahi rādheya kiṃ te hatvā yudhiṣṭhiramd śaṅkhayor dhmāyatoḥ śabdaḥ sumahān eṣa kṛṣṇayoḥd śrūyate cāpaghoṣo yaṃ prāvṛṣīvāmbudasya had asau nighnan rathodārān arjunaḥ śaravṛṣṭibhiḥd sarvāṃ grasati naḥ senāṃ karṇa paśyainam āhaved pṛṣṭharakṣau ca śūrasya yudhāmanyūttamaujasaud uttaraṃ cāsya vai śūraś cakraṃ rakṣati sātyakiḥd dhṛṣṭadyumnas tathā cāsya cakraṃ rakṣati dakṣiṇamd bhīmasenaś ca vai rājñā dhārtarāṣṭreṇa yudhyated yathā na hanyāt taṃ bhīmaḥ sarveṣāṃ no dya paśyatāmd tathā rādheya kriyatāṃ rājā mucyeta no yathād paśyainaṃ bhīmasenena grastam āhavaśobhinamd yadi tv āsādya mucyeta vismayaḥ sumahān bhavetd paritrāhy enam abhyetya saṃśayaṃ paramaṃ gatamd kiṃ nu mādrīsutau hatvā rājānaṃ ca yudhiṣṭhiramd iti śalyavacaḥ śrutvā rādheyaḥ pṛthivīpated dṛṣṭvā duryodhanaṃ caiva bhīmagrastaṃ mahāhaved rājagṛddhī bhṛśaṃ caiva śalyavākyapracoditaḥd ajātaśatrum utsṛjya mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavaud tava putraṃ paritrātum abhyadhāvata vīryavānd madrarājapraṇuditair aśvair ākāśagair ivad gate karṇe tu kaunteyaḥ pāṇḍuputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥd apāyāj javanair aśvaiḥ sahadevasya māriṣad tābhyāṃ sa sahitas tūrṇaṃ vrīḍann iva nareśvaraḥd prāpya senāniveśaṃ ca mārgaṇaiḥ kṣatavikṣataḥd avatīrṇo rathāt tūrṇam āviśac chayanaṃ śubhamd apanītaśalyaḥ subhṛśaṃ hṛcchalyābhinipīḍitaḥd so bravīd bhrātarau rājā mādrīputrau mahārathaud anīkaṃ bhīmasenasya pāṇḍavāv āśu gacchatāmd jīmūta iva nardaṃs tu yudhyate sa vṛkodaraḥd tato nyaṃ ratham āsthāya nakulo rathapuṃgavaḥd sahadevaś ca tejasvī bhrātarau śatrukarśanaud turagair agryaraṃhobhir yātvā bhīmasya śuṣmiṇaud anīkaṃ sahitau tatra bhrātarau paryavasthitau saṃjaya uvācaa drauṇis tu rathavaṃśena mahatā parivāritaḥc āpatat sahasā rājan yatra rājā vyavasthitaḥa tam āpatantaṃ sahasā śūraḥ śaurisahāyavānc dadhāra sahasā pārtho veleva makarālayama tataḥ kruddho mahārāja droṇaputraḥ pratāpavānc arjunaṃ vāsudevaṃ ca chādayām āsa patribhiḥa avacchannau tataḥ kṛṣṇau dṛṣṭvā tatra mahārathāḥc vismayaṃ paramaṃ gatvā praikṣanta kuravas tadāa arjunas tu tato divyam astraṃ cakre hasann ivac tad astraṃ brāhmaṇo yuddhe vārayām āsa bhārataa yad yad dhi vyākṣipad yuddhe pāṇḍavo straṃ jighāṃsayāc tat tad astraṃ maheṣvāso droṇaputro vyaśātayata astrayuddhe tato rājan vartamāne bhayāvahec apaśyāma raṇe drauṇiṃ vyāttānanam ivāntakama sa diśo vidiśaś caiva chādayitvā vijihmagaiḥc vāsudevaṃ tribhir bāṇair avidhyad dakṣiṇe bhujea tato rjuno hayān hatvā sarvāṃs tasya mahātmanaḥc cakāra samare bhūmiṃ śoṇitaughataraṅgiṇīmd sarvalokavahāṃ raudrāṃ paralokavahāṃ nadīmd sarathān rathinaḥ sarvān pārthacāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥd drauṇer apahatān saṃkhye dadṛśuḥ sa ca tāṃ tathād prāvartayan mahāghorāṃ nadīṃ paravahāṃ tathād tayos tu vyākule yuddhe drauṇeḥ pārthasya dāruṇed amaryādaṃ yodhayantaḥ paryadhāvann itas tataḥd rathair hatāśvasūtaiś ca hatārohaiś ca vājibhiḥd dviradaiś ca hatārohair mahāmātrair hatadvipaiḥd pārthena samare rājan kṛto ghoro janakṣayaḥa nihatā rathinaḥ petuḥ pārthacāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥc hayāś ca paryadhāvanta muktayoktrās tatas tataḥa tad dṛṣṭvā karma pārthasya drauṇir āhavaśobhinaḥb arjunaṃ jayatāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tvarito bhyetya vīryavānb vidhunvāno mahac cāpaṃ kārtasvaravibhūṣitamc avākirad raṇe kṛṣṇaṃ samantān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa tato rjunaṃ mahārāja drauṇir āyamya patriṇāc vakṣodeśe samāsādya tāḍayām āsa saṃyugea so tividdho raṇe tena droṇaputreṇa bhāratab gāṇḍīvadhanvā prasabhaṃ śaravarṣair udāradhīḥb saṃchādya samare drauṇiṃ cicchedāsya ca cārmukamb sa chinnadhanvā parighaṃ vajrasparśasamaṃ yudhic ādatta parighaṃ ghoraṃ drauṇeś cainam avākṣipatd ādāya cikṣepa tadā droṇaputraḥ kirīṭinea tam āpatantaṃ parighaṃ kārtasvaravibhūṣitama   jāmbūnadapariṣkṛtama ciccheda sahasā rājan prahasann iva pāṇḍavaḥc drauṇiś ciccheda sahasā tata uccukruśur janāḥa so nekadhāpatad bhūmau bhāradvājasya sāyakaiḥc viśīrṇaḥ parvato rājan yathā syān mātariśvanād tataḥ kruddho mahārāja droṇaputro mahārathaḥd aindreṇa cāstravegena bībhatsuṃ samavākiratd tasyendrajālāvatataṃ samīkṣyad pārtho rājan gāṇḍivam ādade saḥd aindraṃ jālaṃ pratyahanat tarasvīd varāstram ādāya mahendrasṛṣṭamd vidārya taj jālam athendramuktaṃd pārthas tato drauṇirathaṃ kṣaṇenad pracchādayām āsa tathābhyupetyad drauṇis tadā pārthaśarābhibhūtaḥd vigāhya tāṃ pāṇḍavabāṇavṛṣṭiṃd śaraiḥ paraṃ nāma tataḥ prakāśyad śatena kṛṣṇaṃ sahasābhyavidhyatd tribhiḥ śatair arjunaṃ kṣudrakāṇāmd tato rjunaḥ sāyakānāṃ śatenad guroḥ sutaṃ marmasu nirbibhedad aśvāṃś ca sūtaṃ ca tathā dhanur jyāmd avākirat paśyatāṃ tāvakānāma tato rjuno raṇe drauṇiṃ vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥb sa viddhvā marmasu drauṇiṃ pāṇḍavaḥ paravīrahāc sārathiṃ cāsya bhallena rathanīḍād apāharata sa saṃgṛhya svayaṃ vāhān kṛṣṇau prācchādayac charaiḥc tatrādbhutam apaśyāma drauṇer āśu parākramama ayacchat turagān yac ca phalgunaṃ cāpy ayodhayatc tad asya samare rājan sarve yodhā apūjayand tenāsya samare rājaṃs tuṣṭuvuḥ sarvasainikāḥd tataḥ prahasya bībhatsur droṇaputrasya saṃyugea yadā tv agrasyata raṇe droṇaputreṇa phalgunaḥc tato raśmīn rathāśvānāṃ kṣurapraiś cicchide jayaḥa prādravaṃs turagās te tu śaravegaprabādhitāḥc tato bhūn ninado bhūyas tava sainyasya bhārataa pāṇḍavās tu jayaṃ labdhvā tava sainyam upādravanc samantān niśitān bāṇān vimuñcanto jayaiṣiṇaḥa pāṇḍavais tu mahārāja dhārtarāṣṭrī mahācamūḥc punaḥ punar atho vīrair abhajyata jayoddhataiḥa paśyatāṃ te mahārāja putrāṇāṃ citrayodhināmc śakuneḥ saubaleyasya karṇasya ca mahātmanaḥa vāryamāṇā mahāsenā putrais tava janeśvarac nāvatiṣṭhata saṃgrāme tāḍyamānā samantataḥa tato yodhair mahārāja palāyadbhis tatas tataḥc abhavad vyākulaṃ bhītaiḥ putrāṇāṃ te mahad balama tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti satataṃ sūtaputrasya jalpataḥc nāvatiṣṭhata sā senā vadhyamānā mahātmabhiḥa athotkruṣṭaṃ mahārāja pāṇḍavair jitakāśibhiḥc dhārtarāṣṭrabalaṃ dṛṣṭvā dravamāṇaṃ samantataḥa tato duryodhanaḥ karṇam abravīt praṇayād ivac paśya karṇa yathā senā pāṇḍavair arditā bhṛśama tvayi tiṣṭhati saṃtrāsāt palāyati samantataḥc etaj jñātvā mahābāho kuru prāptam ariṃdamaa sahasrāṇi ca yodhānāṃ tvām eva puruṣarṣabhac krośanti samare vīra drāvyamāṇāni pāṇḍavaiḥa etac chrutvā tu rādheyo duryodhanavaco mahatc madrarājam idaṃ vākyam abravīt sūtanandanaḥa paśya me bhujayor vīryam astrāṇāṃ ca janeśvarac adya hanmi raṇe sarvān pāñcālān pāṇḍubhiḥ sahae vāhayāśvān naravyāghra bhadreṇaiva janeśvaraa evam uktvā mahārāja sūtaputraḥ pratāpavānc pragṛhya vijayaṃ vīro dhanuḥśreṣṭhaṃ purātaname sajyaṃ kṛtvā mahārāja saṃmṛjya ca punaḥ punaḥa saṃnivārya ca yodhān svān satyena śapathena cac prāyojayad ameyātmā bhārgavāstraṃ mahābalaḥa tato rājan sahasrāṇi prayutāny arbudāni cac koṭiśaś ca śarās tīkṣṇā niragacchan mahāmṛdhea jvalitais tair mahāghoraiḥ kaṅkabarhiṇavājitaiḥc saṃchannā pāṇḍavī senā na prājñāyata kiṃ canaa hāhākāro mahān āsīt pāñcālānāṃ viśāṃ patec pīḍitānāṃ balavatā bhārgavāstreṇa saṃyugea nipatadbhir gajai rājan naraiś cāpi sahasraśaḥc rathaiś cāpi naravyāghra hayaiś cāpi samantataḥa prākampata mahī rājan nihatais tais tatas tataḥc vyākulaṃ sarvam abhavat pāṇḍavānāṃ mahad balama karṇas tv eko yudhāṃ śreṣṭho vidhūma iva pāvakaḥc dahañ śatrūn naravyāghra śuśubhe sa paraṃtapaḥa te vadhyamānāḥ karṇena pāñcālāś cedibhiḥ sahac tatra tatra vyamuhyanta vanadāhe yathā dvipāḥe cukruśus te naravyāghra yathāprāg vā narottamāḥa teṣāṃ tu krośatāṃ śrutvā bhītānāṃ raṇamūrdhanic dhāvatāṃ ca diśo rājan vitrastānāṃ samantataḥe ārtanādo mahāṃs tatra pretānām iva saṃplavea vadhyamānāṃs tu tān dṛṣṭvā sūtaputreṇa māriṣac vitresuḥ sarvabhūtāni tiryagyonigatāny apia te vadhyamānāḥ samare sūtaputreṇa sṛñjayāḥc arjunaṃ vāsudevaṃ ca vyākrośanta muhur muhuḥd śrutvā tu ninadaṃ teṣāṃ vadhyatāṃ karṇasāyakaiḥe pretarājapure yadvat pretarājaṃ vicetasaḥf athārjuno mahābāhuḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥf duḥsaho vajriṇāpy ājau parājitya guroḥ sutama athābravīd vāsudevaṃ kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥc bhārgavāstraṃ mahāghoraṃ dṛṣṭvā tatra sabhīritama paśya kṛṣṇa mahābāho bhārgavāstrasya vikramamc naitad astraṃ hi samare śakyaṃ hantuṃ kathaṃ canaa sūtaputraṃ ca saṃrabdhaṃ paśya kṛṣṇa mahāraṇec antakapratimaṃ vīraṃ kurvāṇaṃ karma dāruṇama sutīkṣṇaṃ codayann aśvān prekṣate māṃ muhur muhuḥc na ca paśyāmi samare karṇasya prapalāyitama jīvan prāpnoti puruṣaḥ saṃkhye jayaparājayauc jitasya tu hṛṣīkeśa vadha eva kuto jayaḥd evam uktas tu pārthena kṛṣṇo matimatāṃ varamd dhanaṃjayam uvācedaṃ prāptakālam ariṃdamamd karṇena hi dṛḍhaṃ rājā kuntīputraḥ parikṣataḥd taṃ dṛṣṭvāśvāsya ca punaḥ karṇaṃ pārtha vadhiṣyasid pratipadyasva kaunteya prāptakālam anantaramd karṇam ekākinaṃ hatvā rathānīkena bhāratad eṣa karṇo raṇe bhāti madhyāhna iva bhāskaraḥd nivartaya rathaṃ kṛṣṇa jīvan bhadrāṇi paśyatia tato janārdanaḥ prāyād draṣṭum icchan yudhiṣṭhiramb saṃjaya uvācab tato janārdanaḥ śrutvā tasya vākyaṃ viśāṃ pateb rathenāpayayau kṣipraṃ saṃgrāmād iti bhāratab pratyanīkam avasthāpya bhīmaṃ bhīmaparākramamb alaṃ viṣahituṃ hy eṣa kurūṇāṃ saṃprapadyatāmc śrameṇa grāhayiṣyaṃś ca karṇaṃ yuddhena māriṣad karṇaṃ ca samare rājan grāhayiṣyañ śramaṃ pratid viśramārthaṃ ca kauravya pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥd apayāto raṇād vīro rājānaṃ draṣṭum eva caa arjunaṃ cābravīt kṛṣṇo bhṛśaṃ rājā parikṣataḥc tam āśvāsya kuruśreṣṭha tataḥ karṇaṃ haniṣyasia tato dhanaṃjayo draṣṭuṃ rājānaṃ bāṇapīḍitamb yāhi yāhīti bahuśo vāsudevam acodayatb rājānaṃ prati vārṣṇeya dūyate me dṛḍhaṃ manaḥb sa codyamānaḥ pārthena keśighno vṛṣṇinandanaḥc rathena prayayau kṣipraṃ saṃgrāme keśavājñayāa gacchann eva tu kaunteyo dharmarājadidṛkṣayāc sainyam ālokayām āsa nāpaśyat tatra cāgrajama yuddhaṃ kṛtvā tu kaunteyo droṇaputreṇa bhāratac duḥsahaṃ vajriṇā saṃkhye parājigye bhṛgoḥ sutama drauṇiṃ parājitya tatogradhanvākṛtvā mahad duṣkaram āryakarmac ālokayām āsa tataḥ svasainyaṃdhanaṃjayaḥ śatrubhir apradhṛṣyaḥa sa yudhyamānaḥ pṛtanāmukhasthāñśūrāñ śūro harṣayan savyasācīc pūrvāpadānaiḥ prathitaiḥ praśaṃsansthirāṃś cakārātmarathān anīkea apaśyamānas tu kirīṭamālīyudhi jyeṣṭhaṃ bhrātaram ājamīḍhamc uvāca bhīmaṃ tarasābhyupetyarājñaḥ pravṛttis tv iha keti rājan bhīma uvācaa apayāta ito rājā dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥc karṇabāṇavibhugnāṅgo yadi jīvet kathaṃ cana arjuna uvācaa tasmād bhavāñ śīghram itaḥ prayāturājñaḥ pravṛttyai kurusattamasyac nūnaṃ hi viddho tibhṛśaṃ pṛṣatkaiḥkarṇena rājā śibiraṃ gato saua yaḥ saṃprahāre niśi saṃpravṛttedroṇena viddho tibhṛśaṃ tarasvīc tasthau ca tatrāpi jayapratīkṣodroṇena yāvan na hataḥ kilāsīta sa saṃśayaṃ gamitaḥ pāṇḍavāgryaḥsaṃkhye dya karṇena mahānubhāvaḥc jñātuṃ prayāhy āśu tam adya bhīmasthāsyāmy ahaṃ śatrugaṇān nirudhya bhīma uvācaa tvam eva jānīhi mahānubhāvarājñaḥ pravṛttiṃ bharatarṣabhasyac ahaṃ hi yady arjuna yāmi tatravakṣyanti māṃ bhīta iti pravīrāḥa tato bravīd arjuno bhīmasenaṃsaṃśaptakāḥ pratyanīkaṃ sthitā mec etān ahatvā na mayā tu śakyamito payātuṃ ripusaṃghagoṣṭhāta athābravīd arjunaṃ bhīmasenaḥsvavīryam āśritya kurupravīrac saṃśaptakān pratiyotsyāmi saṃkhyesarvān ahaṃ yāhi dhanaṃjayetia tad bhīmasenasya vaco niśamyasudurvacaṃ bhrātur amitramadhyeb saṃśaptakānīkam asahyam ekaḥb suduṣkaraṃ dhārayāmīti pārthaḥb uvāca nārāyaṇam aprameyaṃb kapidhvajaḥ satyaparākramasyab śrutvā vaco bhrātur adīnasattvasb tadāhave satyavaco mahātmāc draṣṭuṃ kuruśreṣṭham abhiprayātuṃprovāca vṛṣṇipravaraṃ tadānīmd rājānaṃ prati vārṣṇeya dūyate me dṛḍhaṃ manaḥa codayāśvān hṛṣīkeśa vigāhyaitaṃ rathārṇavamc ajātaśatruṃ rājānaṃ draṣṭum icchāmi keśavad taṃ rathaṃ codayām āsa bībhatsor vacanād dhariḥa tato hayān sarvadāśārhamukhyaḥprācodayad bhīmam uvāca cedamc naitac citraṃ tava karmādya vīrayāsyāmahe jahi bhīmārisaṃghāna tato yayau hṛṣīkeśo yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥc śīghrāc chīghrataraṃ rājan vājibhir garuḍopamaiḥa pratyanīke vyavasthāpya bhīmasenam ariṃdamamc saṃdiśya caiva rājendra yuddhaṃ prati vṛkodaramd kṣaṇenaiva tu rājānam āsedatur ariṃdamaua tatas tu gatvā puruṣapravīraurājānam āsādya śayānam ekamc rathād ubhau pratyavaruhya tasmādvavandatur dharmarājasya pādaud javena gatvā tu dāśārhamukhyaḥd śayānam ekaṃ kururājaṃ dadarśad praharṣavegeritamānasāv ubhaud rājānam āsādya parisravad vraṇamd ity evam abhisaṃgṛhya ubhau tu prāñjalī sthitaud śastrakṣatau mahārāja rudhireṇa samukṣitaud nihatya vāhinīṃ tubhyam apayātau raṇājirāta tau dṛṣṭvā puruṣavyāghrau kṣemiṇau puruṣarṣabhac mudābhyupagatau kṛṣṇāv aśvināv iva vāsavama tāv abhyanandad rājā hi vivasvān aśvināv ivac hate mahāsure jambhe śakraviṣṇū yathā guruḥa manyamāno hataṃ karṇaṃ dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥa   prītaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥa sa bhūtvā puruṣavyāghrauc harṣagadgadayā vācā prītaḥ prāha paraṃtapau saṃjaya uvāca athopayātau pṛthulohitākṣau śarācitāṅgau rudhirapradigdhau yudhiṣṭhirasya prativedayantau priyaṃ tadānīṃ puruṣapravīrau tāv āgatau prekṣya mahendrakalpau yudhiṣṭhiro duḥkhaparītacetāḥ kṛcchreṇa rājā pratilabhya saṃjñāṃ tataḥ punaḥ prītamanā babhūva samīkṣya senāgranarapravīrau yudhiṣṭhiro vākyam idaṃ babhāṣea mahāsattvau tu tau dṛṣṭvā sahitau keśavārjunauc hatam ādhirathiṃ mene saṃkhye gāṇḍīvadhanvanāa tāv abhyanandat kaunteyaḥ sāmnā paramavalgunāc smitapūrvam amitraghnaḥ pūjayan bharatarṣabha yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa svāgataṃ devakīputra svāgataṃ te dhanaṃjayac priyaṃ me darśanaṃ bāḍhaṃ yuvayor acyutārjunaua akṣatābhyām ariṣṭābhyāṃ kathaṃ yudhya mahārathamc āśīviṣasamaṃ yuddhe sarvaśastraviśāradama agragaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ śarma varma cac rakṣitaṃ vṛṣasenena suṣeṇena ca dhanvināa anujñātaṃ mahāvīryaṃ rameṇāstreṣu durjayamb rāmeṇa jāmadagnyena anujñātaṃ yaśasvināb mukhyaṃ sarvasya lokasya rathinaṃ lokaviśrutamc trātāraṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ gantāraṃ vāhinīmukhea hantāram arisainyānām amitragaṇamardanamc duryodhanahite yuktam asmadyuddhāya codyatama apradhṛṣyaṃ mahāyuddhe devair api savāsavaiḥc analānilayos tulyaṃ tejasā ca balena caa pātālam iva gambhīraṃ suhṛdānandavardhanamc antakābham amitrāṇāṃ karṇaṃ hatvā mahāhavee diṣṭyā yuvām anuprāptau jitvāsuram ivāmaraua tena yuddham adīnena mayā hy adyācyutārjunaub kṛtaṃ ghoraṃ mahābāho dhṛṣṭadyumnasya paśyataḥc kupitenāntakeneva prajāḥ sarvā jighāṃsatāa tena ketuś ca me chinno hatau ca pārṣṇisārathīc hatavāhaḥ kṛtaś cāsmi yuyudhānasya paśyataḥa dhṛṣṭadyumnasya yamayor vīrasya ca śikhaṇḍinaḥc paśyatāṃ draupadeyānāṃ pāñcālānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥa etāñ jitvā mahāvīryān karṇaḥ śatrugaṇān bahūnc jitavān māṃ mahābāho yatamānaṃ mahāraṇea anusṛtya ca māṃ yuddhe paruṣāṇy uktavān bahuc tatra tatra yudhāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ paribhūya na saṃśayaḥa bhīmasenaprabhāvāt tu yaj jīvāmi dhanaṃjayac bahunātra kim uktena nāhaṃ tat soḍhum utsahea trayodaśāhaṃ varṣāṇi yasmād bhīto dhanaṃjayac na sma nidrāṃ labhe rātrau na cāhani sukhaṃ kva cita tasya dveṣeṇa saṃyuktaḥ paridahye dhanaṃjayac ātmano maraṇaṃ jānan vādhrīṇasa iva dvipaḥd kṛṣṇagrīvo raktaśirāḥ śvetapakṣo vihaṃgamaḥd sa vai vādhrīṇasaḥ prokto yājñikaiḥ pitṛkarmasua yasyāyam agamat kālaś cintayānasya me vibhoc kathaṃ śakyo mayā karṇo yuddhe kṣapayituṃ bhaveta jāgrat svapaṃś ca kaunteya karṇam eva sadā hy ahamc paśyāmi tatra tatraiva karṇabhūtam idaṃ jagata yatra yatra hi gacchāmi karṇād bhīto dhanaṃjayac tatra tatra hi paśyāmi karṇam evāgrataḥ sthitama so haṃ tenaiva vīreṇa samareṣv apalāyināc sahayaḥ sarathaḥ pārtha jitvā jīvan visarjitaḥa ko nu me jīvitenārtho rājyenārtho tha vā punaḥc mamaivaṃ dhikkṛtasyeha karṇenāhavaśobhināa na prāptapūrvaṃ yad bhīṣmāt kṛpād droṇāc ca saṃyugec tat prāptam adya me yuddhe sūtaputrān mahārathāta tat tvā pṛcchāmi kaunteya yathā hy akuśalas tathāc tan mamācakṣva kārtsnyena yathā karṇas tvayā hataḥa śakravīryasamo yuddhe yamatulyaparākramaḥc rāmatulyas tathāstre yaḥ sa kathaṃ vai niṣūditaḥa mahārathaḥ samākhyātaḥ sarvayuddhaviśāradaḥc dhanurdharāṇāṃ pravaraḥ sarveṣām ekapūruṣaḥa pūjito dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa saputreṇa viśāṃ patec sadā tvadarthaṃ rādheyaḥ sa kathaṃ nihatas tvayāa dhṛtarāṣṭro hi yodheṣu sarveṣv eva sadārjunac tava mṛtyuṃ raṇe karṇaṃ manyate puruṣarṣabhaḥa sa tvayā puruṣavyāghra kathaṃ yuddhe niṣūditaḥc taṃ mamācakṣva bībhatso yathā karṇo hatas tvayāa sotsedham asya ca śiraḥ paśyatāṃ suhṛdāṃ hṛtamc tvayā puruṣaśārdūla śārdūlena yathā ruroḥa yaḥ paryupāsīt pradiśo diśaś catvāṃ sūtaputraḥ samare parīpsanc ditsuḥ karṇaḥ samare hastipūgaṃsa hīdānīṃ kaṅkapatraiḥ sutīkṣṇaiḥd ditsan nṛṇāṃ śakaṭaṃ ratnapūrṇaṃd kathaṃ tvayāsau nihato dya karṇaḥa tvayā raṇe nihataḥ sūtaputraḥkaccic chete bhūmitale durātmāc kaccit priyaṃ me paramaṃ tvayādyakṛtaṃ raṇe sūtaputraṃ nihatyaa yaḥ sarvataḥ paryapatat tvadarthemadānvito garvitaḥ sūtaputraḥc sa śūramānī samare sametyakaccit tvayā nihataḥ saṃyuge dyaa raukmaṃ rathaṃ hastivaraiś ca yuktaṃrathaṃ ditsur yaḥ parebhyas tvadarthec sadā raṇe spardhate yaḥ sa pāpaḥkaccit tvayā nihatas tāta yuddhea yo sau nityaṃ śūramadena mattovikatthate saṃsadi kauravāṇāmc priyo tyarthaṃ tasya suyodhanasyakaccit sa pāpo nihatas tvayādyaa kaccit samāgamya dhanuḥpramuktaistvatpreṣitair lohitārthair vihaṃgaiḥc śete dya pāpaḥ sa vibhinnagātraḥkaccid bhagno dhārtarāṣṭrasya bāhuḥa yo sau sadā ślāghate rājamadhyeduryodhanaṃ harṣayan darpapūrṇaḥc ahaṃ hantā phalgunasyeti mohātkaccid dhatas tasya na vai tathā rathaḥd kaccid vaco sya vitathaṃ tvayā kṛtaṃd yat tat priyām avadat tāta karṇaḥd sabhāmadhye rūkṣam anekarūpaṃd dhik pāṇḍavān apatis tvaṃ hi kṛṣṇed kaccid dhruvaṃ śatrur ayaṃ mahātmād hy adhārayad dvādaśa yaḥ samāstud karṇo vrataṃ ghoram amitrasāhod duryodhanasyārthaniviṣṭabuddhiḥa nāhaṃ pādau dhāvayiṣye kadā cidyāvat sthitaḥ pārtha ity alpabuddhiḥc vrataṃ tasyaitat sarvadā śakrasūnokaccit tvayā nihataḥ so dya karṇaḥd pādau na dhāve yāvad ahaṃ na hanmid dhanaṃjayaṃ samareṣūgravegamd kaccid raṇe phalguna taṃ nihatyad kaccid vrataṃ tasya bhagnaṃ tvayādyaa yo sau kṛṣṇām abravīd duṣṭabuddhiḥkarṇaḥ sabhāyāṃ kuruvīramadhyec kiṃ pāṇḍavāṃs tvaṃ na jahāsi kṛṣṇesudurbalān patitān hīnasattvāna yat tat karṇaḥ pratyajānāt tvadarthenāhatvāhaṃ saha kṛṣṇena pārthama mahābalaḥ saṃyuge śatruhantāc ihopayāteti sa pāpabuddhiḥkaccic chete śarasaṃbhinnagātraḥa kaccit saṃgrāme vidito vā tadāyaṃsamāgamaḥ sṛñjayakauravāṇāmc yatrāvasthām īdṛśīṃ prāpito haṃkaccit tvayā so dya hataḥ sametyaa kaccit tvayā tasya sumandabuddhergāṇḍīvamuktair viśikhair jvaladbhiḥc sakuṇḍalaṃ bhānumad uttamāṅgaṃkāyāt prakṛttaṃ yudhi savyasācina yat tan mayā bāṇasamarpitenadhyāto si karṇasya vadhāya vīrac tan me tvayā kaccid amogham adyadhyātaṃ kṛtaṃ karṇanipātanenaa yad darpapūrṇaḥ sa suyodhano smānavekṣate karṇasamāśrayeṇac kaccit tvayā so dya samāśrayo syabhagnaḥ parākramya suyodhanasyaa yo naḥ purā ṣaṇḍhatilān avocatsabhāmadhye pārthivānāṃ samakṣamc sa durmatiḥ kaccid upetya saṃkhyetvayā hataḥ sūtaputro tyamarṣīa yaḥ sūtaputraḥ prahasan durātmāpurābravīn nirjitāṃ saubalenac svayaṃ prasahyānaya yājñasenīmapīha kaccit sa hatas tvayādyad yaḥ prāhiṇot sūtaputro durātmād kṛṣṇāṃ jitāṃ saubalenānayetid sa mandabuddhir nihataḥ prasahyad vaikartanas tv adya kaccin mahātmand anavāpyāṃ prāptum icchann acintyaṃd śiśur yathā candramasaṃ grahītumd sa pāpātmā sa tu no vidviṣāṇaḥd kaccit karṇo nihato vā tvayā dhikd asmin saṃgrāme bhīmarūpe tvayādyad vrataṃ tu bhagnaṃ sūtaputrasya pārthad kaccit pāpaṃ vacanaṃ dyūtakāled yac cāpy asau samitau vāsudevamd tadoktavān paruṣaṃ so tikāmamd hitaṃ caran yaḥ satataṃ kurūṇāmd kaccit sa karṇo nihato dya saṃkhed yo dhārtarāṣṭraṃ paripālayan raṇed ekaḥ sadā śoṣayan māmakaṃ balaṃd sa pāñcālān kekayāṃś caiva sarvānd śriyaṃ diditsan dhārtarāṣṭrīṃ sa karṇaḥd kaccin mahyaṃ pratyavadhīs tvam adyad atho bhāsāś ca sṛgālāś ca gṛdhrād hatasya māṃsāny uddharanti sma kāyāta yaḥ śastrabhṛc chreṣṭhatamaṃ pṛthivyāṃpitāmahaṃ vyākṣipad alpacetāḥc saṃkhyāyamāno rdharathaḥ sa kaccittvayā hato dyādhirathir durātmād yat tat tvayā saṃśrutaṃ me kirīṭind sabhāmadhye dvairatheneha bhūyaḥd ahaṃ karṇaṃ sūdayiṣye saputraṃd tat karma kṛtvā hy anṛṇo si kaccita amarṣaṇaṃ nikṛtisamīraṇeritaṃhṛdi śritaṃ jvalanam imaṃ sadā mamac hato mayā so dya sametya pāpadhīriti bruvan praśamaya me dya phalgunad bravīhi me durlabham etad adyad kathaṃ tvayā nihataḥ sūtaputraḥd anudhyāye tvāṃ satataṃ pravīrad vṛtre hate sau bhagavān ivendraḥ saṃjaya uvācaa tad dharmaśīlasya vaco niśamyarājñaḥ kruddhasyādhirathau mahātmāc uvāca durdharṣam adīnasattvaṃyudhiṣṭhiraṃ jiṣṇur anantavīryaḥd droṇaṃ hataṃ pārtha karṇo viditvād bhinnāṃ nāvam ivātyagādhe kurūṇāmd saṃmuhyamānān dhārtarāṣṭrān viditvād nirutsāhāṃś ca vijaye pareṣāmd sodaryavat tvarito mitaujād uttārayiṣyan dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putrānd raṇe rathenādhirathir mahātmād tato hi māṃ tvaritaḥ so bhyadhāvata saṃśaptakair yudhyamānasya me dyasenāgrayāyī kurusainyasya rājanc āśīviṣābhān khagamān pramuñcandrauṇiḥ purastāt sahasā vyatiṣṭhata dṛṣṭvā rathaṃ meghanibhaṃ mamemamambaṣṭhasenā maraṇe vyatiṣṭhatc teṣām ahaṃ pañca śatāni hatvātato drauṇim agamaṃ pārthivāgryad sa me dṛṣṭvā śūratamo dhvajāgraṃd samādiśad rathasaṃghān anekānd teṣām ahaṃ pañcaśatān nihatyad āsādayaṃ droṇaputraṃ nadantamd sa droṇaputraḥ sadṛśaṃ mahātmād mām apy arautsīt tadanīkamadhyed kirañ śaraughān bahurūpān vicitrāṃśd citrāṃ gataḥ śukra ivātivarṣand sa me śarān sarvataḥ kaṅkapatrānd avāsṛjad vai pṛthivīprakāśānd nivārya tūrṇaṃ paramājimadhyed tato hi māṃ bāṇagaṇaiḥ samarpayatd ākarṣaṇaṃ vāpi vikṛṣya muktaṃd na dṛśyate tasya mahārathasyad sa māṃ samāsādya narendra yattaḥd samabhyayāt siṃha iva dvipendraḥd akārṣīc ca rathinām ujjihīrṣāṃd mahārāja vadhyatāṃ kauravāṇāmd tato raṇe bhārata duṣprakampyad ācāryaputraḥ pravaraḥ kurūṇāmd mām ardayām āsa śitaiḥ pṛṣatkaird janārdanaṃ caiva viṣāgnikalpaiḥd aṣṭau gavām aṣṭaśatāni bāṇānd mayā prayuddhasya vahanti tasyad tāṃs tena muktān aham asya bāṇaird vyanāśayaṃ vāyur ivābhrajālama tato parān bāṇasaṃghān anekānākarṇapūrṇāyatavipramuktānc sasarja śikṣāstrabalaprayatnaistathā yathā prāvṛṣi kālameghaḥa naivādadānaṃ na ca saṃdadhānaṃjānīmahe katareṇāsyatītic vāmena vā yadi vā dakṣiṇenasa droṇaputraḥ samare paryavartatd na saṃdadhānaḥ kuta ādadhānod na vyākṣipann āvikarṣan vimuñcand savyena vā yadi vā dakṣiṇenad na jñāyate katareṇāsyatītid ācāryavat samare paryavartand mahac citraṃ dṛśyate sarvataḥ smad dṛṣṭir viṣaṃ cāsukaraṃ pareṣāṃd sarvā diśaḥ pūrayānaṃ śaraughaiḥd alātacakrapratimaṃ mahātmanaḥd sadā nataṃ kārmukaṃ brahmabandhoḥd tasyātataṃ maṇḍalam eva sajyaṃd pradṛśyate kārmukaṃ droṇasūnoḥa avidhyan māṃ pañcabhir droṇaputraḥśitaiḥ śaraiḥ pañcabhir vāsudevamc ahaṃ tu taṃ triṃśatā vajrakalpaiḥsamārdayaṃ nimiṣasyāntareṇad abhyaghnaṃ bāṇais tam ahaṃ sudhāraird nimeṣamātreṇa suvarṇapuṅkhaiḥd kṣaṇāc chvāvitsamarūpo babhūvad samārdito madvisṛṣṭaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥa sa vikṣaran rudhiraṃ sarvagātrairathānīkaṃ sūtasūnor viveśac mayābhibhūtaḥ sainikānāṃ prabarhānasāv apaśyan rudhireṇa pradigdhānd sa nirviddho vikṣaran droṇaputrod rathānīkaṃ cātirather viveśad mayābhibhūtān svarathaprabarhānd astraṃ ca paśyan rudhirapradigdhama tato bhibhūtaṃ yudhi vīkṣya sainyaṃvidhvastayodhaṃ drutavājināgamc pañcāśatā rathamukhyaiḥ sametaḥkarṇas tvaran mām upāyāt pramāthīa tān sūdayitvāham apāsya karṇaṃdraṣṭuṃ bhavantaṃ tvarayābhiyātaḥc sarve pāñcālā hy udvijante sma karṇādgandhād gāvaḥ kesariṇo yathaivaa mahājhaṣasyeva mukhaṃ prapannāḥprabhadrakāḥ karṇam abhi dravantic mṛtyor āsyaṃ vyāttam ivānvapadyanprabhadrakāḥ karṇam āsādya rājand yāsyāmi tāṃs tārayiṣyan balaughānd diṣṭyā bhavān svastimān pārtha dṛṣṭaḥd rathāṃs tu tān saptaśatān nimagnāṃsd tadā karṇaḥ prāhiṇon mṛtyusadmad na cāpy abhūt klāntamanāḥ sa rājand yāvan nāsmān dṛṣṭavān sūtaputraḥd śrutvā tu tvāṃ tena dṛṣṭaṃ sametamd aśvatthāmnā pūrvataraṃ kṣataṃ cad manye kālam apayānasya rājand krūrāt karṇāt te ham acintyakarmand na me karṇasyāstram idaṃ purastādd yuddhe dṛṣṭaṃ pāṇḍava citrarūpamd na hy anyayoddhā vidyate sṛñjayānāṃd mahārathaṃ yo dya saheta karṇamd śaineyo me sātyakiś cakrarakṣaud dhṛṣṭadyumnaś cāpi tathaiva rājand yudhāmanyuś cottamaujāś ca śūraud pṛṣṭhato māṃ rakṣatāṃ rājaputraud rathapravīreṇa mahānubhāvad dviṣatsainye vartatā dustareṇaa āyāhi paśyādya yuyutsamānaṃmāṃ sūtaputraṃ ca vṛtau jayāyac ṣaṭsāhasrā bhārata rājaputrāḥsvargāya lokāya rathā nimagnāḥd tān adya yāsyāmi raṇād vimoktuṃd sarvātmanā sūtaputraṃ ca hantumd rathapravīreṇa mahānubhāvad dviṣat sainyaṃ nirdahan vistareṇaa sametyāhaṃ sūtaputreṇa saṃkhyevṛtreṇa vajrīva narendramukhyab evaṃ gate kiṃ ca mayādya śakyaṃb kāryaṃ kartuṃ nigrahe sūtajasyab tathaiva rājñaś ca suyodhanasyab ye cāpi māṃ yoddhukāmāḥ sametāḥc yotsye bhṛśaṃ bhārata sūtaputramasmin saṃgrāme yadi vai dṛśyate dyaa karṇaṃ na ced adya nihanmi rājansabāndhavaṃ yudhyamānaṃ prasahyac pratiśrutyākurvatāṃ vai gatir yākaṣṭāṃ gaccheyaṃ tām ahaṃ rājasiṃhaa āmantraye tvāṃ brūhi jayaṃ raṇe mepurā bhīmaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrā grasantec sautiṃ haniṣyāmi narendrasiṃhasainyaṃ tathā śatrugaṇāṃś ca sarvān saṃjaya uvācaa śrutvā karṇaṃ kalyam udāravīryaṃkruddhaḥ pārthaḥ phalgunasyāmitaujāḥc dhanaṃjayaṃ vākyam uvāca cedaṃyudhiṣṭhiraḥ karṇaśarābhitaptaḥd vipradrutā tāta camūs tvadīyād tiraskṛtā cādya yathā na sādhud bhīto bhīmaṃ tyajya cāyās tathā tvaṃd yan nāśakaḥ karṇam atho nihantumd steyaṃ tvayā pārtha kṛtaṃ pṛthāyād garbhaṃ samāviśya yathā na sādhud raudraṃ raṇe duṣprativāryavīryaḥd sautis tvayā nādya śakyo nihantumd tyaktvā raṇe yad apāyāḥ sa bhīmaṃd yan nāśakaḥ sūtaputraṃ nihantumd yat tad vākyaṃ dvaitavane tvayoktaṃd hantā karṇam ekarathena satyamd tyaktvā taṃ vai katham adyāpayātaḥd karṇād bhīto bhīmasenaṃ vihāyad imāṃ ca vasatiṃ prāpto bhayāt karṇena bādhitaḥd ahaṃ tvaṃ bhīmasenaś ca mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavaud vāsudevena sahitā vayaṃ karṇena nirjitāḥd punar eva vanaṃ prāpya tapaścaryāṃ carāmahed atha vā dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ paricaryāṃ carāmahed ity evam uktvā bībhatsuṃ roṣāt saṃraktalocanaḥd abravīt punar evātra dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥa idaṃ yadi dvaitavane hy avakṣyaḥkarṇaṃ yoddhuṃ na prasahe nṛpetic vayaṃ tadā prāptakālāni sarvevṛttāny upaiṣyāma tadaiva pārthaa mayi pratiśrutya vadhaṃ hi tasyabalasya cāptasya tathaiva vīrac ānīya naḥ śatrumadhyaṃ sa kasmātsamutkṣipya sthaṇḍile pratyapiṃṣṭhāḥa anvāśiṣma vayam arjuna tvayiyiyāsavo bahu kalyāṇam iṣṭamc tan naḥ sarvaṃ viphalaṃ rājaputraphalārthināṃ nicula ivātipuṣpaḥd anvāsya satyena yad āttha pārthad satyaṃ śapan vāsudevena sārdhamd taṃ naḥ satyam aphalam akārṣīs tvaṃd phalakāle puṣpavṛkṣaṃ nikṛntaḥa pracchāditaṃ baḍiśam ivāmiṣeṇapracchādito gavaya ivāpavācāc anarthakaṃ me darśitavān asi tvaṃrājyārthino rājyarūpaṃ vināśamd pracchāditas tvaṃ bāliśa duryaśenād narthavākyo syarjuna naiva sādhuḥd tyaktvā bhīmaṃ sarvabhīmeṣu bhīmaṃd saṃyojitas tvaṃ sūtaputraṃ nihantumd trayodaśemā hi samāḥ sadā vayaṃd tvām anvajīviṣma dhanaṃjayāśayād kāle varṣaṃ devam ivoptabījaṃd tan naḥ sarvān narake tvaṃ nyamajjayaḥa yat tat pṛthāṃ vāg uvācāntarikṣesaptāhajāte tvayi mandabuddhauc jātaḥ putro vāsavavikramo yaṃsarvāñ śūrāñ śātravāñ jeṣyatītid apāpīyān vāsavāt kuntijātod bahūn saṃgrāmān ayam eva jetāa ayaṃ jetā khāṇḍave devasaṃghānsarvāṇi bhūtāny api cottamaujāḥc ayaṃ jetā madrakaliṅgakekayānayaṃ kurūn hanti ca rājamadhyec daityāṃś ca rakṣāṃsi samāgatānic bhūmiṃ ca sarvān nikhilena jetāa asmāt paro na bhavitā dhanurdharona vai bhūtaḥ kaś cana jātu jetāc icchann āryaḥ sarvabhūtāni kuryādvaśe vaśī sarvasamāptavidyaḥa kāntyā śaśāṅkasya javena vāyoḥsthairyeṇa meroḥ kṣamayā pṛthivyāḥc sūryasya bhāsā dhanadasya lakṣmyāśauryeṇa śakrasya balena viṣṇoḥa tulyo mahātmā tava kunti putrojāto diter viṣṇur ivārihantāc sveṣāṃ jayāya dviṣatāṃ vadhāyakhyāto mitaujāḥ kulatantukartāa ity antarikṣe śataśṛṅgamūrdhnitapasvināṃ śṛṇvatāṃ vāg uvācac evaṃvidhaṃ tvāṃ tac ca nābhūt tavādyadevā hi nūnam anṛtaṃ vadantia tathāpareṣām ṛṣisattamānāṃśrutvā giraṃ pūjayatāṃ sadaivac na saṃnatiṃ praimi suyodhanasyana tvā jānāmy ādhirather bhayārtama tvaṣṭrā kṛtaṃ vāham akūjanākṣaṃśubhaṃ samāsthāya kapidhvajaṃ tvamc khaḍgaṃ gṛhītvā hemacitraṃ samiddhaṃdhanuś cedaṃ gāṇḍivaṃ tālamātrame sa keśavenohyamānaḥ kathaṃ nukarṇād bhīto vyapayāto si pārthaf pūrvaṃ yad uktaṃ hi suyodhanenaf na phalgunaḥ pramukhe sthāsyatītif karṇasya yuddhe hi mahābalasyaf maurkhyāt tu tan nāvabuddhaṃ mayāsītf tenādya tapsye bhṛśam aprameyaṃf yan mitravargo narakaṃ praviṣṭaḥf tadaiva vācyo smi nanu tvayāhaṃf na yotsye haṃ sūtaputraṃ kathaṃ citf tato nāhaṃ sṛñjayān kekayāṃś caf samānayeyaṃ suhṛdo raṇāyaf evaṃ gate kiṃ ca mayādya śakyaṃf kāryaṃ kartuṃ nigrahe sūtajasyaf tathaiva rājñaś ca suyodhanasyaf ye cāpi māṃ yoddhukāmāḥ sametāḥf dhig astu majjīvitam adya kṛṣṇaf yo haṃ vaśaṃ sūtaputrasya yātaḥf madhye kurūṇāṃ sasuyodhanānāṃf ye cāpy anye yoddhukāmāḥ sametāḥf ekas tu me bhīmaseno dya nāthof yenābhipanno smi raṇe mahābhayef vimocya māṃ cāpi ruṣānvitas tataḥf śareṇa tīkṣṇena bibheda karṇamf tyaktvā prāṇān samare bhīmasenaśf cakre yuddhaṃ kurumukhyaiḥ sametaiḥf gadāgrahasto rudhirokṣitāṅgaśf caran raṇe kāla ivāntakālef asau hi bhīmasya mahān ninādof muhur muhuḥ śrūyate dhārtarāṣṭraiḥf yadi sma jīvet samare nihantāf mahārathānāṃ pravaro narottamaḥf tavābhimanyus tanayo dya pārthaf na cāsmi gantā samare parābhavamf athāpi jīvet samare ghaṭotkacasf tathāpi nāhaṃ samare parāṅmukhaḥf bhīmasya putraḥ samarāgrayāyīf mahāstravic cāpi tavānurūpaḥf yatnaṃ samāsādya ripor balaṃ nof nimīlitākṣaṃ bhayaviplutaṃ bhavetf cakāra yo sau niśi yuddham ekasf tyaktvā raṇaṃ yasya bhayād dravantef sa cet samāsādya mahānubhāvaḥf karṇaṃ raṇe bāṇagaṇaiḥ pramohyaf dhairye sthitenāpi ca sūtajenaf śaktyā hato vāsavadattayā tayāf mamaiva bhāgyāni purā kṛtānif pāpāni nūnaṃ phalavanti yuddhef tṛṇaṃ ca kṛtvā samare bhavantaṃf tato ham evaṃ nikṛto durātmanāf vaikartaneneha tathā kṛto haṃf yathā hy aśaktaḥ kriyate hy abāndhavaḥf āpadgataṃ yaś ca naraṃ vimokṣayetf sa bāndhavaḥ snehayutaḥ suhṛd vaif evaṃ purāṇā ṛṣayo vadantif dharmaḥ sadā sadbhir anuṣṭhitaś caa dhanuś caitat keśavāya pradāyayantābhaviṣyas tvaṃ raṇe ced durātmanc tato haniṣyat keśavaḥ karṇam ugraṃmarutpatir vṛtram ivāttavajraḥd rādheyam evaṃ yadi cāpy aśaktaśd carantam ugraṃ pratibodhanāyad yacchānyasmai gāṇḍivam etad adyad tvatto yo strair abhyadhiko narendraḥd tasmān naivaṃ putradārair vihīnānd sukhād bhraṣṭān rājyanāśāc ca bhūyaḥd draṣṭā lokaḥ patitān apy agādhed pāpair juṣṭe narake pāṇḍaveyad rathe sthitaḥ phālguna keśavas ted raśmī samādāya raṇe prayātud jahi tvam adyaiva sametya karṇaṃd caidyaṃ yathā keśavo rājamadhyea māse patiṣyaḥ pañcame tvaṃ prakṛcchrena vā garbho py abhaviṣyaḥ pṛthāyāḥc tat te śramo rājaputrābhaviṣyanna saṃgrāmād apayātuṃ durātmand dhig gāṇḍivaṃ dhik ca te bāhuvīryamd asaṃkhyeyān bāṇagaṇāṃś ca dhik ted dhik te ketuḥ kesariṇaḥ sutasyad kṛśānudattaṃ ca rathaṃ ca te dhik saṃjaya uvācaa yudhiṣṭhireṇaivam uktaḥ kaunteyaḥ śvetavāhanaḥc asiṃ jagrāha saṃkruddho jighāṃsur bharatarṣabhama tasya kopaṃ samudvīkṣya cittajñaḥ keśavas tadāc uvāca kim idaṃ pārtha gṛhītaḥ khaḍga ity utaa neha paśyāmi yoddhavyaṃ tava kiṃ cid dhanaṃjayac te dhvastā dhārtarāṣṭrā hi sarve bhīmena dhīmatāa apayāto si kaunteya rājā draṣṭavya ity apic sa rājā bhavatā dṛṣṭaḥ kuśalī ca yudhiṣṭhiraḥa taṃ dṛṣṭvā nṛpaśārdūlaṃ śārdūlasamavikramamc harṣakāle tu saṃprāpte kasmāt tvā manyur āviśata na taṃ paśyāmi kaunteya yas te vadhyo bhaved ihab prahartum icchase kasmāt kiṃ vā te cittavibhramaḥc kasmād bhavān mahākhaḍgaṃ parigṛhṇāti satvarama tat tvā pṛcchāmi kaunteya kim idaṃ te cikīrṣitamc parāmṛśasi yat kruddhaḥ khaḍgam adbhutavikramaa evam uktas tu kṛṣṇena prekṣamāṇo yudhiṣṭhiramc arjunaḥ prāha govindaṃ kruddhaḥ sarpa iva śvasana dada gāṇḍīvam anyasmā iti māṃ yo bhicodayetc chindyām ahaṃ śiras tasya ity upāṃśuvrataṃ mamad yudhiṣṭhireṇa tenāham uktaś cāsmi janārdanaa tad ukto ham adīnātman rājñāmitaparākramac samakṣaṃ tava govinda na tat kṣantum ihotsahea tasmād enaṃ vadhiṣyāmi rājānaṃ dharmabhīrukamc pratijñāṃ pālayiṣyāmi hatvemaṃ narasattamame etadarthaṃ mayā khaḍgo gṛhīto yadunandanaa so haṃ yudhiṣṭhiraṃ hatvā satye py ānṛṇyatāṃ gataḥc viśoko vijvaraś cāpi bhaviṣyāmi janārdanaa kiṃ vā tvaṃ manyase prāptam asmin kāle samutthitec tvam asya jagatas tāta vettha sarvaṃ gatāgatamd jātas tvatto hi dharmaś cādharmaś ceti parā śrutiḥe tat tathā prakariṣyāmi yathā māṃ vakṣyate bhavānf saṃjaya uvācaf dhig dhig ity eva govindaḥ pārtham uktvābravīt punaḥ kṛṣṇa uvācaa idānīṃ pārtha jānāmi na vṛddhāḥ sevitās tvayāc akāle puruṣavyāghra saṃrambhakriyayānayāe na hi dharmavibhāgajñaḥ kuryād evaṃ dhanaṃjayaf yathā tvaṃ pāṇḍavādyeha dharmabhīrur apaṇḍitaḥa akāryāṇāṃ ca kāryāṇāṃ saṃyogaṃ yaḥ karoti vaic kāryāṇām akriyāṇāṃ ca sa pārtha puruṣādhamaḥa anusṛtya tu ye dharmaṃ kavayaḥ samupasthitāḥc samāsavistaravidāṃ na teṣāṃ vettha niścayama aniścayajño hi naraḥ kāryākāryaviniścayec avaśo muhyate pārtha yathā tvaṃ mūḍha eva tua na hi kāryam akāryaṃ vā sukhaṃ jñātuṃ kathaṃ canac śrutena jñāyate sarvaṃ tac ca tvaṃ nāvabudhyasea avijñānād bhavān yac ca dharmaṃ rakṣati dharmavitc prāṇināṃ hi vadhaṃ pārtha dhārmiko nāvabudhyatea prāṇinām avadhas tāta sarvajyāyān mato mamac anṛtaṃ tu bhaved vācyaṃ na ca hiṃsyāt kathaṃ canaa sa kathaṃ bhrātaraṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ rājānaṃ dharmakovidamc hanyād bhavān naraśreṣṭha prākṛto nyaḥ pumān ivaa ayudhyamānasya vadhas tathāśastrasya bhāratac parāṅmukhasya dravataḥ śaraṇaṃ vābhigacchataḥe kṛtāñjaleḥ prapannasya na vadhaḥ pūjyate budhaiḥe   pramattasya tathaiva cae na vadhaḥ pūjyate sadbhis tac ca sarvaṃ gurau tavaa tvayā caiva vrataṃ pārtha bālenaiva kṛtaṃ purāc tasmād adharmasaṃyuktaṃ mauḍhyāt karma vyavasyasia sa guruṃ pārtha kasmāt tvaṃ hanyā dharmam anusmaranc asaṃpradhārya dharmāṇāṃ gatiṃ sūkṣmāṃ duranvayāma idaṃ dharmarahasyaṃ ca vakṣyāmi bharatarṣabhac yad brūyāt tava bhīṣmo vā dharmajño vā yudhiṣṭhiraḥa viduro vā tathā kṣattā kuntī vāpi yaśasvinīb kuntī vā bharataśreṣṭha draupadī vā yaśasvinīc tat te vakṣyāmi tattvena tan nibodha dhanaṃjayaa satyasya vacanaṃ sādhu na satyād vidyate paramc tattvenaitat sudurjñeyaṃ yasya satyam anuṣṭhitama bhavet satyam avaktavyaṃ vaktavyam anṛtaṃ bhavetc sarvasvasyāpahāre tu vaktavyam anṛtaṃ bhaveta prāṇātyaye vivāhe ca vaktavyam anṛtaṃ bhavetc yatrānṛtaṃ bhavet satyaṃ satyaṃ cāpy anṛtaṃ bhavetd vivāhakāle ratisaṃprayoged prāṇātyaye sarvadhanāpahāred viprasya cārthe hy anṛtaṃ vadetad pañcānṛtāny āhur apātakānia tādṛśaṃ paśyate bālo yasya satyam anuṣṭhitamb bhavet satyam avaktavyaṃ na vaktavyam anuṣṭhitamc satyānṛte viniścitya tato bhavati dharmavita kim āścaryaṃ kṛtaprajñaḥ puruṣo pi sudāruṇaḥc sumahat prāpnuyāt puṇyaṃ balāko ndhavadhād ivaa kim āścaryaṃ punar mūḍho dharmakāmo py apaṇḍitaḥc sumahat prāpnuyāt pāpam āpagām iva kauśikaḥ arjuna uvācaa ācakṣva bhagavann etad yathā vidyām ahaṃ tathāc balākāndhābhisaṃbaddhaṃ nadīnāṃ kauśikasya ca kṛṣṇa uvācaa mṛgavyādho bhavat kaś cid balāko nāma bhāratac yātrārthaṃ putradārasya mṛgān hanti na kāmataḥa so ndhau ca mātāpitarau bibharty anyāṃś ca saṃśritānc svadharmanirato nityaṃ satyavāg anasūyakaḥa sa kadā cin mṛgāṃl lipsur nānvavindat prayatnavānc athāpaśyat sa pītodaṃ śvāpadaṃ ghrāṇacakṣuṣama adṛṣṭapūrvam api tat sattvaṃ tena hataṃ tadāc anv eva ca tato vyomnaḥ puṣpavarṣam avāpatata apsarogītavāditrair nāditaṃ ca manoramamc vimānam āgamat svargān mṛgavyādhaninīṣayāa tad bhūtaṃ sarvabhūtānām abhāvāya kilārjunac tapas taptvā varaṃ prāptaṃ kṛtam andhaṃ svayaṃbhuvāa tad dhatvā sarvabhūtānām abhāvakṛtaniścayamc tato balākaḥ svaragād evaṃ dharmaḥ sudurvidaḥa kauśiko py abhavad vipras tapasvī na bahuśrutaḥc nadīnāṃ saṃgame grāmād adūre sa kilāvasata satyaṃ mayā sadā vācyam iti tasyābhavad vratamc satyavādīti vikhyātaḥ sa tadāsīd dhanaṃjayaa atha dasyubhayāt ke cit tadā tad vanam āviśanc dasyavo pi gatāḥ krūrā vyamārganta prayatnataḥa atha kauśikam abhyetya prāhus taṃ satyavādinamc katamena pathā yātā bhagavan bahavo janāḥe satyena pṛṣṭaḥ prabrūhi yadi tān vettha śaṃsa naḥa sa pṛṣṭaḥ kauśikaḥ satyaṃ vacanaṃ tān uvāca hab satyasya tv avibhāgajñaḥ satyaṃ tebhyaḥ śaśaṃsa saḥc bahuvṛkṣalatāgulmam etad vanam upāśritāḥd iti tān khyāpayām āsa sa tebhyaḥ pārtha kauśikaḥe tatas te tān samāsādya krūrā jaghnur iti śrutiḥa tenādharmeṇa mahatā vāgduruktena kauśikaḥc gataḥ sukaṣṭaṃ narakaṃ sūkṣmadharmeṣv akovidaḥe aprabhūtaśruto mūḍho dharmāṇām avibhāgavita vṛddhān apṛṣṭvā saṃdehaṃ mahac chvabhram ito rhatic tatra te lakṣaṇoddeśaḥ kaś cid eva bhaviṣyatia duṣkaraṃ paramajñānaṃ tarkeṇātra vyavasyatic śrutir dharma iti hy eke vadanti bahavo janāḥa na tv etat pratisūyāmi na hi sarvaṃ vidhīyateb śrutir dhāryeyam ity eke vadanti bahavo janāḥb na tān pārthābhyasūyāmi na ca sarvatra śiṣyatib smṛtir dhāryā iti tv eke vadanti bahavo janāḥb na tu tān pratyasūyāmi nātra sarvaṃ vidhīyatec prabhavārthāya bhūtānāṃ dharmapravacanaṃ kṛtamd evaṃvidhā gatir vīra dharmasyātīva durdṛśād vidyāśīlavayovṛddhān anupāsyānadhītya vād manvādīnāṃ tu kṛtsnaṃ vai ko dharmaṃ vaktum arhatid adharmād eva bhavati dharme pi ca mahān yathād vyādhakauśikayor yadvad dharmādharmaviruddhayoḥd vedo mūlaṃ hi dharmāṇām iti santo yad abruvand jijñāsate hi vidyānāṃ sādhanāny eva tattvavitd vedaṃ brāhmaṇam āsādya puṇyapāpe paraṃtapad sa tu vetti paraṃ dharmam ahiṃsāṃ vetti bhāratad yat syād ahiṃsāsaṃyuktaṃ sa dharma iti niścayaḥd ahiṃsārthāya bhūtānāṃ dharmapravacanaṃ kṛtama dhāraṇād dharmam ity āhur dharmo dhārayati prajāḥc yaḥ syād dhāraṇasaṃyuktaḥ sa dharma iti niścayaḥa ye nyāyena jihīrṣanto janā icchanti karhi citc akūjanena cen mokṣo nātra kūjet kathaṃ canaa avaśyaṃ kūjitavyaṃ vā śaṅkeran vāpy akūjataḥc śreyas tatrānṛtaṃ vaktuṃ satyād iti vicāritamd yaḥ kāryebhyo vrataṃ kṛtvā karmaṇā nopapādayetd na tat phalam avāpnoti evam āhur manīṣiṇaḥd satye sati na pāpebhyo dhanaṃ deyaṃ kadā canaa prāṇātyaye vivāhe vā sarvajñātidhanakṣayec narmaṇy abhipravṛtte vā pravaktavyaṃ mṛṣā bhavete adharmaṃ nātra paśyanti dharmatattvārthadarśinaḥf sarvadā hi vadet tat tu nānṛtaḥ syād vicakṣaṇaḥa yaḥ stenaiḥ saha saṃbandhān mucyate śapathair apic śreyas tatrānṛtaṃ vaktuṃ tat satyam avicāritama na ca tebhyo dhanaṃ deyaṃ śakye sati kathaṃ canac pāpebhyo hi dhanaṃ dattaṃ dātāram api pīḍayete tasmād dharmārtham anṛtam uktvā nānṛtavāg bhaveta eṣa te lakṣaṇoddeśaḥ samuddiṣṭo yathāvidhib yathādharmaṃ yathābuddhi mayā dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiramc tasmin samayasaṃyoge brūhi kiṃ cid anugrahame idaṃ cāparam atraiva śṛṇu hṛtsthaṃ vivakṣitama jānāsi dāśārha mama vrataṃ tvaṃyo māṃ brūyāt kaś cana mānuṣeṣuc anyasmai tvaṃ gāṇḍivaṃ dehi pārthayas tvatto strair bhavitā vā viśiṣṭaḥa hanyām ahaṃ keśava taṃ prasahyabhīmo hanyāt tūbaraketi coktaḥc tan me rājā proktavāṃs te samakṣaṃdhanur dehīty asakṛd vṛṣṇisiṃhaa taṃ hatvā cet keśava jīvalokesthātā kālaṃ nāham apy alpamātramb evaṃ tvaṃ māṃ kṛṣṇa jānāsi sarvaṃb kālaṃ loke hīnadharmo hi jīvanb satyāc cyuto lokam imaṃ tyajeyaṃb tasmāt krodhāt pratikṣapeyaṃ dharmaputramb tvamf evaṃ jñātvā yad dhitaṃ me sadaivaf tathārhasi tvaṃ tu nibodhituṃ ca vāsudeva uvācaa rājā śrānto jagato vikṣataś cakarṇena saṃkhye niśitair bāṇasaṃghaiḥa śarārditaḥ sūtaputreṇa caivab yaś cāniśaṃ sūtaputreṇa vīrab śarair bhṛśaṃ tāḍito yudhyamānaḥb atas tvam etena saroṣamuktob duḥkhānvite nedam ayuktarūpamb akopito hy eṣa yadi sma saṃkhyeb karṇaṃ na hanyād iti cābravīc cab jānāti taṃ pāṇḍava eṣa cāpib pāpaṃ loke karṇam asahyam anyaiḥb tatas tvam ukto bhṛśaroṣitenab rājñā samakṣaṃ paruṣāṇi pārthab bhṛśārditaś cāpi mahāmanasvīc tasmāt pārtha tvāṃ paruṣāṇy avocatkarṇe dyūtaṃ hy adya raṇe nibaddhama tasmin hate kuravo nirjitāḥ syurevaṃbuddhiḥ pārthivo dharmaputraḥb tato vadhaṃ nārhati dharmaputrasb tvayā pratijñārjuna pālanīyāb jīvann ayaṃ yena mṛto bhaved dhib tan me nibodheha tavānurūpamb yadā mānaṃ labhate mānanārhasb tadā sa vai jīvati jīvalokec yadāvamānaṃ labhate mahāntaṃtadā jīvan mṛta ity ucyate saḥa tan mānitaḥ pārthivo yaṃ sadaivatvayā sabhīmena tathā yamābhyāmc vṛddhaiś ca loke puruṣapravīraistasyāvamānaṃ kalayā tvaṃ prayuṅkṣvad yad idaṃ dharmaśāstrārthaṃ vedeṣu ca nidarśanamd śṛṇu pārtha yathā nityo hataḥ syād bhavatā guruḥd hato bhavety evam ukto guruḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥa tvam ity atrabhavantaṃ tvaṃ brūhi pārtha yudhiṣṭhiramc tvam ity ukto hi nihato gurur bhavati bhārataa evam ācara kaunteya dharmarāje yudhiṣṭhirec adharmayuktaṃ saṃyogaṃ kuruṣvaivaṃ kurūdvahaa atharvāṅgirasī hy eṣā śrutīnām uttamā śrutiḥc avicāryaiva kāryaiṣā śreyaḥkāmair naraiḥ sadād avadhena vadhaḥ prokto yad gurus tvam iti prabhuḥd tad brūhi tvaṃ yan mayoktaṃ dharmarājasya dharmavita vadho hy ayaṃ pāṇḍava dharmarājñastvatto yukto vetsyate caivam eṣaḥc tato sya pādāv abhivādya paścācchamaṃ brūyāḥ sāntvapūrvaṃ ca pārthama bhrātā prājñas tava kopaṃ na jātukuryād rājā kaṃ cana pāṇḍaveyaḥc mukto nṛtād bhrātṛvadhāc ca pārthahṛṣṭaḥ karṇaṃ tvaṃ jahi sūtaputram saṃjaya uvācaa ity evam uktas tu janārdanenapārthaḥ praśasyātha suhṛdvadhaṃ tamc tato bravīd arjuno dharmarājamanuktapūrvaṃ paruṣaṃ prasahyaa mā tvaṃ rājan vyāhara vyāharatsuna tiṣṭhase krośamātre raṇārdheb mā vocas tvaṃ kiṃ cid ihādya rājaṃsb tyaktvā yuddhaṃ ya iha vyavasthitas tvamc bhīmas tu mām arhati garhaṇāyayo yudhyate sarvayodhapravīraḥa kāle hi śatrūn pratipīḍya saṃkhyehatvā ca śūrān pṛthivīpatīṃs tānb rathapradhānottamanāgamukhyānb sādipravekān amitāṃś ca śūrānc yaḥ kuñjarāṇām adhikaṃ sahasraṃhatvānadat tumulaṃ siṃhanādamd kāmbojānām ayuta pārvatīyānd mṛgān siṃho vinihatyeva cājaua suduṣkaraṃ karma karoti vīraḥkartuṃ yathā nārhasi tvaṃ kadā citc rathād avaplutya gadāṃ parāmṛśaṃstayā nihanty aśvanaradvipān raṇea varāsinā vājirathāśvakuñjarāṃstathā rathāṅgair dhanuṣā ca hanty arīnc pramṛdya padbhyām ahitān nihanti yaḥpunaś ca dorbhyāṃ śatamanyuvikramaḥa mahābalo vaiśravaṇāntakopamaḥprasahya hantā dviṣatāṃ yathārhamc sa bhīmaseno rhati garhaṇāṃ mena tvaṃ nityaṃ rakṣyase yaḥ suhṛdbhiḥa mahārathān nāgavarān hayāṃś capadātimukhyān api ca pramathyac eko bhīmo dhārtarāṣṭreṣu magnaḥsa mām upālabdhum ariṃdamo rhatia kaliṅgavaṅgāṅganiṣādamāgadhānsadāmadān nīlabalāhakopamānc nihanti yaḥ śatrugaṇān anekaśaḥsa mābhivaktuṃ prabhavaty anāgasama suyuktam āsthāya rathaṃ hi kāledhanur vikarṣañ śarapūrṇamuṣṭiḥc sṛjaty asau śaravarṣāṇi vīromahāhave megha ivāmbudhārāḥd śatāny aṣṭau vāraṇānām apaśyaṃd viśātitaiḥ kumbhakarāgrahastaiḥd bhīmenājau nihatāny adya bāṇaiḥd sa māṃ krūraṃ vaktum arhaty arighnaḥd mahārathānām ayutaṃ supūrṇamd athāśvānām ayutāni ṣaṭ cad padātisaṃghān bahuśo vimṛdyad vīrān hatvā śataśo thāpramādīd prāṇāṃs tyaktvā dustyajān ājimadhyed saṃyuddhe yo vairibhir bhīmasenaḥd yo bhīmaseno nihatārisaṃghaḥd sa mām upālabdhum ariṃdamo rhatid rathāś ca nāgāś ca hayāś ca rājand bhīmenājau nihatāḥ saṃghaśo dyad rājānaś ca bahavo mahābalāḥd sa mām upālabdhum ariṃdamo rhatid dhṛtarāṣṭraputrā balinaś ca yenad mahābalā nihatāḥ prāyaśo vaid śūro yuddheṣv aprativāryavīryaḥd sa mām upālabdhum ariṃdamo rhatid pratāpayaṃs tad balam ugrarūpaṃd yo sau raṇe dhārtarāṣṭrasya vīraḥd ekaḥ sahetāpratisahyapauruṣasd tenāsmi vācyo na tvayā vai kadā citd mahārathā yatra yatraiva yuddhed bhindanti sainyaṃ tava kāmato dyad tatraiva tatraiva raṇe mahātmād dṛḍhaṃ bhīmaḥ parasaṃghān amṛdnātd tenāsmi vācyo na tvayāhaṃ kadā citd mā mā vocaḥ krūram ihādya pārthad nāsmadvidho vai bhavatā tu vācyod yathā bhavān sarvalokasya vācyaḥd evaṃ hi mā te bruvato narendrad kathaṃ na dīryec chatadhādya jihvād aho batedaṃ sunṛśaṃsarūpaṃd bhavān api hy atra karṇād bibhetia balaṃ tu vāci dvijasattamānāṃkṣātraṃ budhā bāhubalaṃ vadantic tvaṃ vāgbalo bhārata niṣṭhuraś catvam eva māṃ vetsi yathāvidho hamd nakulena rājan gajavājiyodhād hatāś ca śūrāḥ sahasā sametyad tyaktvā prāṇān samare yuddhakāṅkṣīd sa mām upālabdhum ariṃdamo rhatid kṛtaṃ karma sahadevena duṣkaraṃd yo yudhyate parasainyāvamardīd na cābravīt kiṃ cid ihāgato balīd paśyāntaraṃ tasya caivātmanaś cad dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ sātyakir draupadeyād yudhāmanyuś cottamaujāḥ śikhaṇḍīd ete dya sarve yudhi saṃprapīḍitāsd te mām upālabdhum arhanti na tvamd tvanmūlam asmābhir idaṃ hi vairaṃd prāptaṃ tathā vyasanaṃ cātighoramd dyūte pramattena kṛtaṃ tvayāsakṛtd kasmād upālabdhum ihārhasi tvamd tvam eva rājan satataṃ pramattasd tvam eva mūḍho bhāratānām asādhuḥd tvāṃ prāpya rājyaṃ ca vinaṣṭam etatd prāptā mahat pāṇḍavāś caiva dāsyamd tvattaḥ kṛte syād vanavāsaduḥkhaṃd rājyasya nāśo hy abhimanyoś ca karṇaḥ phalaṃ prāpsyati dāruṇama adya tvām aham eṣyāmi karṇaṃ hatvā mahīpatec sabhājayitum ākrandād iti satyaṃ bravīmi tea nāhatvā vinivarte haṃ karṇam adya raṇājirātc iti satyena te pādau spṛśāmi āyudhāni ca sarvāṇi sajjyantāṃ vai mahārathea upāvṛttāś ca turagāḥ śikṣitāś cāśvasādinaḥc rathopakaraṇaiḥ sarvair upāyāntu tvarānvitāḥd prayātau svo dya govinda sūtaputrajighāṃsayāa evam ukte mahārāja samaṅgalasvastyayanam āruroha rathottamama tasya rājā mahāprājño dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥc āśiṣo yuṅkta paramā yuktāḥ karṇavadhaṃ pratia taṃ prayāntaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhūtāni bhāratac nihataṃ menire karṇaṃ pāṇḍavena mahātmanāa babhūvur vimalāḥ sarvā diśo rājan samantataḥc cāṣāś ca śatapatrāś ca krauñcāś caiva janeśvarae pradakṣiṇam akurvanta tadā vai pāṇḍunandanama bahavaḥ pakṣiṇo rājan puṃnāmānaḥ śubhāḥ śivāḥc tvarayanto rjunaṃ yuddhe hṛṣṭarūpā vavāśirea kaṅkā gṛdhrā vaḍāś caiva vāyasāś ca viśāṃ patec agratas tasya gacchanti bhakṣyahetor bhayānakāḥa nimittāni ca dhanyāni pārthasya praśaśaṃsirec vināśam arisainyānāṃ karṇasya ca vadhaṃ tathād nimittāni ca śubhrāṇi rutaṃ ca mṛgapakṣiṇāma prayātasyātha pārthasya mahān svedo vyajāyatac cintā ca vipulā jajñe kathaṃ nv etad bhaviṣyatid viṣaṇṇaṃ tu tato jñātvā savyasācinam acyutaḥd saṃcodayati tejasvī madhuhā vānaradhvajama tato gāṇḍīvadhanvānam abravīn madhusūdanaḥc dṛṣṭvā pārthaṃ tadāyastaṃ cintāparigataṃ tadāa gāṇḍīvadhanvan saṃgrāme ye tvayā dhanuṣā jitāḥc na teṣāṃ mānuṣo jetā tvad anya iha vidyatea dṛṣṭā hi bahavaḥ śūrāḥ śakratulyaparākramāḥc tvāṃ prāpya samare vīraṃ ye gatāḥ paramāṃ gatima ko hi droṇaṃ ca bhīṣmaṃ ca bhagadattaṃ ca māriṣac vindānuvindāv āvantyau kāmbojaṃ ca sudakṣiṇama śrutāyuṣaṃ mahāvīryam acyutāyuṣam eva cac pratyudgamya bhavet kṣemī yo na syāt tvam iva kṣamīa tava hy astrāṇi divyāni lāghavaṃ balam eva cac vedhaḥ pātaś ca lakṣaś ca yogaś caiva tavārjunae asaṃmohaś ca yuddheṣu vijñānasya ca saṃnatiḥa bhavān devāsurān sarvān hanyāt sahacarācarānc pṛthivyāṃ hi raṇe pārtha na yoddhā tvatsamaḥ pumānd na cābhimukhato vācyo bhavān etad vaco mayād mānitasya mahādarpo bhaviṣyati raṇe rjunad avaśyam eva vaktavyam atas tvāṃ prabravīmy ahamd atimānāc ca tenātmā mantavyo vai kathaṃ canad jīvamāne raṇe karṇe sūtaputre mahārathed bahunātra kim uktena saṃkṣepāc chṛṇu pāṇḍavad tvatsamaṃ tvadviśiṣṭaṃ vā karṇaṃ manye mahārathamd paramaṃ yatnam āsthāya tvayā vadhyo mahāhaved na hi karṇaṃ raṇe prāpya śakto hi syāt puraṃdaraḥd kṣemī pratyāgamet pārtha tādṛśo sya parākramaḥd tvāṃ tu prāpya mahāraṅge yatnavān api bhāratad nivarteta raṇāt karṇa iti me dhīyate matiḥa dhanurgrahā hi ye ke cit kṣatriyā yuddhadurmadāḥc ā devāt tvatsamaṃ teṣāṃ na paśyāmi śṛṇomi vāa brahmaṇā ca prajāḥ sṛṣṭā gāṇḍīvaṃ ca mahādbhutamc yena tvaṃ yudhyase pārtha tasmān nāsti tvayā samaḥa avaśyaṃ tu mayā vācyaṃ yat pathyaṃ tava pāṇḍavac māvamaṃsthā mahābāho karṇam āhavaśobhinama karṇo hi balavān dhṛṣṭaḥ kṛtāstraś ca mahārathaḥc kṛtī ca citrayodhī ca deśe kāle ca kovidaḥa tejasā vahnisadṛśo vāyuvegasamo javec antakapratimaḥ krodhe siṃhasaṃhanano balīa ayoratnir mahābāhur vyūḍhoraskaḥ sudurjayaḥc atimānī ca śūraś ca pravīraḥ priyadarśanaḥa sarvair yodhaguṇair yukto mitrāṇām abhayaṃkaraḥc satataṃ pāṇḍavadveṣī dhārtarāṣṭrahite rataḥd na bhīṣaye tvāṃ pārthāhaṃ harṣaṃ saṃjanayāmi tea sarvair avadhyo rādheyo devair api savāsavaiḥc ṛte tvām iti me buddhis tvam adya jahi sūtajama devair api hi saṃyattair bibhradbhir māṃsaśoṇitamc aśakyaḥ samare jetuṃ sarvair api yuyutsubhiḥd devair api hi saṃrabdhaiḥ sarvalokeśvarair apid aśakyaṃ taṃ raṇe manye sarvair api yuyutsubhiḥa durātmānaṃ pāpamatiṃ nṛśaṃsaṃduṣṭaprajñaṃ pāṇḍaveyeṣu nityamc hīnasvārthaṃ pāṇḍaveyair virodhehatvā karṇaṃ dhiṣṭhitārtho bhavādyad taṃ sūtaputraṃ rathināṃ variṣṭhaṃd niṣkālikaṃ kālavaśaṃ nayādyad taṃ sūtaputraṃ rathināṃ variṣṭhaṃd hatvā prītiṃ dharmarāje kuruṣvad jānāmi te pārtha vīryaṃ yathāvadd durvāraṇīyaṃ ca surāsuraiś cad sadāvajānāti hi pāṇḍuputrānd asau darpāt sūtaputro durātmāa vīraṃ manyata ātmānaṃ yena pāpaḥ suyodhanaḥc tam adya mūlaṃ pāpānāṃ jaya sautiṃ dhanaṃjayad khaḍgajihvaṃ dhanurāsyaṃ śaradaṃṣṭraṃ tarasvinamd dṛptaṃ puruṣaśārdūlaṃ jahi karṇaṃ dhanaṃjayad ahaṃ tvām anujānāmi vīryeṇa ca balena cad jahi karṇaṃ raṇe śūraṃ mātaṅgam iva kesarīd yasya vīryeṇa vīryaṃ te dhārtarāṣṭro vamanyated tam adya pārtha saṃgrāme karṇaṃ vaikartanaṃ jahi saṃjaya uvācaa tataḥ punar ameyātmā keśavo rjunam abravītc kṛtasaṃkalpam āyastaṃ vadhe karṇasya sarvaśaḥa adya saptadaśāhāni vartamānasya bhāratac vināśasyātighorasya naravāraṇavājināma bhūtvā hi vipulā senā tāvakānāṃ paraiḥ sahac anyonyaṃ samare prāpya kiṃciccheṣā viśāṃ patea bhūtvā hi kauravāḥ pārtha prabhūtagajavājinaḥc tvāṃ vai śatruṃ samāsādya vinaṣṭā raṇamūrdhania ete ca sarve pāñcālāḥ sṛñjayāś ca sahānvayāḥc tvāṃ samāsādya durdharṣaṃ pāṇḍavāś ca vyavasthitāḥa pāñcālaiḥ pāṇḍavair matsyaiḥ kārūṣaiś cedikekayaiḥb māgadhaiḥ pārijātaiś ca dākṣiṇātyaiś ca keralaiḥc tvayā guptair amitraghna kṛtaḥ śatrugaṇakṣayaḥa ko hi śakto raṇe jetuṃ kauravāṃs tāta saṃgatānc anyatra pāṇḍavān yuddhe tvayā guptān mahārathāna tvaṃ hi śakto raṇe jetuṃ sasurāsuramānuṣānc trīṃl lokān samam udyuktān kiṃ punaḥ kauravaṃ balama bhagadattaṃ hi rājānaṃ ko nyaḥ śaktas tvayā vināc jetuṃ puruṣaśārdūla yo pi syād vāsavopamaḥa tathemāṃ vipulāṃ senāṃ guptāṃ pārtha tvayānaghac na śekuḥ pārthivāḥ sarve cakṣurbhir abhivīkṣituma tathaiva satataṃ pārtha rakṣitābhyāṃ tvayā raṇeb hatvā tu balaniṣpiṣṭau bhīṣmadroṇau mahāraṇec dhṛṣṭadyumnaśikhaṇḍibhyāṃ bhīṣmadroṇau nipātitaua ko hi śakto raṇe pārtha pāñcālānāṃ mahārathauc bhīṣmadroṇau yudhā jetuṃ śakratulyaparākramaua ko hi śāṃtanavaṃ saṃkhye droṇaṃ vaikartanaṃ kṛpamc drauṇiṃ ca saumadattiṃ ca kṛtavarmāṇam eva cae saindhavaṃ madrarājaṃ ca rājānaṃ ca suyodhanama vīrān kṛtāstrān samare sarvān evānuvartinaḥc akṣauhiṇīpatīn ugrān saṃrabdhān yuddhadurmadānd tvām ṛte puruṣavyāghra jetuṃ śaktaḥ pumān ihaa śreṇyaś ca bahulāḥ kṣīṇāḥ pradīrṇāśvarathadvipāḥc nānājanapadāś cogrāḥ kṣatriyāṇām amarṣiṇāma govāsadāsamīyānāṃ vasātīnāṃ ca bhāratab nānādeśasamutthāś ca nānādeśasamudbhavāḥb tvāṃ samāsādya bībhatso hatā nāgāś ca saṃyugec vrātyānāṃ vāṭadhānānāṃ bhojānāṃ cāpi mānināma udīrṇāś ca mahāsenā brahmakṣatrasya bhāratac tvāṃ samāsādya nidhanaṃ gatāḥ sāśvarathadvipāḥa ugrāś ca krūrakarmāṇas tukhārā yavanāḥ khaśāḥc dārvābhisārā daradāḥ śakā ramaṭhataṅgaṇāḥa andhrakāś ca pulindāś ca kirātāś cogravikramāḥc mlecchāś ca pārvatīyāś ca sāgarānūpavāsinaḥe saṃrambhiṇo yuddhaśauṇḍā balino dṛbdhapāṇayaḥa ete suyodhanasyārthe saṃrabdhāḥ kurubhiḥ sahac na śakyā yudhi nirjetuṃ tvad anyena paraṃtapaa dhārtarāṣṭram udagraṃ hi vyūḍhaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahābalamc yasya tvaṃ na bhaves trātā pratīyāt ko nu mānavaḥa tat sāgaram ivoddhūtaṃ rajasā saṃvṛtaṃ balamc vidārya pāṇḍavaiḥ kruddhais tvayā guptair hataṃ vibhoa māgadhānām adhipatir jayatseno mahābalaḥc adya saptaiva cāhāni hataḥ saṃkhye bhimanyunāa tato daśa sahasrāṇi gajānāṃ bhīmakarmaṇāmc jaghāna gadayā bhīmas tasya rājñaḥ paricchadame tato nye pi hatā nāgā rathāś ca śataśo balāta tad evaṃ samare tāta vartamāne mahābhayec bhīmasenaṃ samāsādya tvāṃ ca pāṇḍava kauravāḥe savājirathanāgāś ca mṛtyulokam ito gatāḥa tathā senāmukhe tatra nihate pārtha pāṇḍavaiḥc bhīṣmaḥ prāsṛjad ugrāṇi śaravarṣāṇi māriṣaa sa cedikāśipāñcālān karūṣān matsyakekayānc śaraiḥ pracchādya nidhanam anayat paruṣāstravita tasya cāpacyutair bāṇaiḥ paradehavidāraṇaiḥc pūrṇam ākāśam abhavad rukmapuṅkhair ajihmagaiḥd hanyād rathasahasrāṇi ekenaiva tu muṣṭinād lakṣaṃ naradvipān hatvā sametān sa mahābalānd hatvā daśasahasrāṇi saṃnāhaṃ svaśarīrataḥd protsārayati gāṃgeya iti tasyābhavad vratamd nihatya nānānṛpatīn āyudhāny āhave tyajetd tena śūreṇa balinā muktās tv ayutaśaḥ śarāḥa gatyā daśamyā te gatvā jaghnur vājirathadvipānc hitvā nava gatīr duṣṭāḥ sa bāṇān vyāyato mucata dināni daśa bhīṣmeṇa nighnatā tāvakaṃ balamc śūnyāḥ kṛtā rathopasthā hatāś ca gajavājinaḥdA daśame hani saṃprāpte kṛtvā ghoraṃ parākramama darśayitvātmano rūpaṃ rudropendrasamaṃ yudhic pāṇḍavānām anīkāni pravigāhya vyaśātayata vinighnan pṛthivīpālāṃś cedipāñcālakekayānc vyadahat pāṇḍavīṃ senāṃ narāśvagajasaṃkulāma majjantam aplave mandam ujjihīrṣuḥ suyodhanamc tathā carantaṃ samare tapantam iva bhāskaramd padātikoṭisāhasrāḥ pravarāyudhapāṇayaḥe na śekuḥ sṛñjayā draṣṭuṃ tathaivānye mahīkṣitaḥa vicarantaṃ tathā taṃ tu saṃgrāme jitakāśinamc sarvodyogena sahasā pāṇḍavāḥ samupādravana sa tu vidrāvya samare pāṇḍavān sṛñjayān apic eka eva raṇe bhīṣma ekavīratvam āgataḥa taṃ śikhaṇḍī samāsādya tvayā gupto mahārathamc jaghāna puruṣavyāghraṃ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥd mṛtyur jāto vadhīd bhīṣmaṃ śaraughaiḥ pātayan rathāta sa eṣa patitaḥ śete śaratalpe pitāmahaḥc tvāṃ prāpya puruṣavyāghra gṛdhraḥ prāpyeva vāyasama droṇaḥ pañca dināny ugro vidhamya ripuvāhinīḥc kṛtvā vyūhaṃ mahāyuddhe pātayitvā mahārathāna jayadrathasya samare kṛtvā rakṣāṃ mahārathaḥc antakapratimaś cogrāṃ rātriṃ yuddhvādahat prajāḥa adyeti dve dine vīro bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavānc dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ samāsādya sa gataḥ paramāṃ gatima yadi caiva parān yuddhe sūtaputramukhān rathānc nāvārayiṣyaḥ saṃgrāme na sma droṇo vyanaṅkṣyataa bhavatā tu balaṃ sarvaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya vāritamc tato droṇo hato yuddhe pārṣatena dhanaṃjayaa ka ivānyo raṇe kuryāt tvad anyaḥ kṣatriyo yudhib kaś ca śakto raṇe kartuṃ tvad anyaḥ puruṣabruvaḥc yādṛśaṃ te kṛtaṃ pārtha jayadrathavadhaṃ pratia nivārya senāṃ mahatīṃ hatvā śūrāṃś ca pārthivānc nihataḥ saindhavo rājā tvayāstrabalatejasāa āścaryaṃ sindhurājasya vadhaṃ jānanti pārthivāḥc anāścaryaṃ hi tat tvattas tvaṃ hi pārtha mahārathaḥa tvāṃ hi prāpya raṇe kṣatram ekāhād iti karṇo madrādhipaḥ kṛpaḥa tāṃs tvam adya naravyāghra hatvā pañca mahārathānc hatāmitraḥ prayacchorvīṃ rājñaḥ sadvīpapattanāmd droṇaputraṃ kṛpaṃ śalyaṃ bhojam ādhirathiṃ tathād etāṃs tu vai naravyāghra hatvā vīrān mahārathāna sākāśajalapātālāṃ saparvatamahāvanāmc prāpnotv amitavīryaśrīr adya pārtho vasuṃdharāma etāṃ purā viṣṇur iva hatvā daiteyadānavānc prayaccha medinīṃ rājñe śakrāyeva yathā hariḥa adya modantu pāñcālā nihateṣv ariṣu tvayāc viṣṇunā nihateṣv eva dānaveyeṣu devatāḥa yadi vā dvipadāṃ śreṣṭha droṇaṃ mānayato gurumc aśvatthāmni kṛpā te sti kṛpe cācāryagauravāta atyantopacitān vā tvaṃ mānayan bhrātṛbāndhavānc kṛtavarmāṇam āsādya na neṣyasi yamakṣayamd yuddhvā yāmy adya tau pārtha saṃrabdhāv ātatāyinaua bhrātaraṃ mātur āsādya śalyaṃ madrajanādhipamc yadi tvam aravindākṣa dayāvān na canaa dahane yat saputrāyā niśi mātus tavānaghac dyūtārthe yac ca yuṣmāsu prāvartata suyodhanaḥe tatra sarvatra duṣṭātmā karṇo mūlam ihārjunaa karṇād dhi manyate trāṇaṃ nityam eva suyodhanaḥc tato mām api saṃrabdho nigrahītuṃ pracakramed vyanāśeya ca yuṣmāsu acarmitaḥ suyodhanaḥ sica sthirā buddhir narendrasya dhārtarāṣṭrasya mānadac karṇaḥ pārthān raṇe sarvān vijeṣyati na saṃśayaḥa karṇam āśritya kaunteya dhārtarāṣṭreṇa vigrahaḥc rocito bhavatā sārdhaṃ jānatāpi balaṃ tavaa karṇo hi bhāṣate nityam ahaṃ pārthān samāgatānc vāsudevaṃ sarājānaṃ vijeṣyāmi mahāraṇea protsāhayan durātmānaṃ dhārtarāṣṭraṃ sudurmatiḥc samitau garjate karṇas tam adya jahi bhārataa yac ca yuṣmāsu pāpaṃ vai dhārtarāṣṭraḥ prayuktavānb sarvatrānṛjur aprājñaḥ karṇam āśritya vai purāc tatra sarvatra duṣṭātmā karṇaḥ pāpamatir mukhama yac ca tad dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ krūraiḥ ṣaḍbhir mahārathaiḥc apaśyaṃ nihataṃ vīraṃ saubhadram ṛṣabhekṣaṇama droṇadrauṇikṛpān vīrān kampayanto mahārathānc nirmanuṣyāṃś ca mātaṅgān virathāṃś ca mahārathānd prādravanti sma samare diśo bhītābhimanyavea vyaśvārohāṃś ca turagān pattīn vyāyudhajīvitānc kurvantam ṛṣabhaskandhaṃ kuruvṛṣṇiyaśaskarama vidhamantam anīkāni vyathayantaṃ mahārathānc manuṣyavājimātaṅgān prahiṇvantaṃ yamakṣayama śaraiḥ saubhadram āyastaṃ dahantam iva vāhinīmc tan me dahati gātrāṇi sakhe satyena te śapea yat tatrāpi ca duṣṭātmā karṇo bhyadruhyata prabhoc aśaknuvaṃś cābhimanyoḥ karṇaḥ sthātuṃ raṇe grataḥa saubhadraśaranirbhinno visaṃjñaḥ śoṇitokṣitaḥc niḥśvasan krodhasaṃdīpto vimukhaḥ sāyakārditaḥa apayānakṛtotsāho nirāśaś cāpi jīviteb duryodhanaṃ raṇe dṛṣṭvā lajjamāno muhur muhuḥb nāpayāsīt tataḥ pārthaḥ so bhimanyor mahāraṇeb dṛṣṭvā droṇaṃ vadhopāyam abhimanyos tu pṛṣṭavānc tasthau suvihvalaḥ saṃkhye prahārajanitaśramaḥa atha droṇasya samare tat kālasadṛśaṃ tadāc śrutvā karṇo vacaḥ krūraṃ tataś ciccheda kārmukama tataś chinnāyudhaṃ tena raṇe pañca mahārathāḥc sa caiva nikṛtiprajñaḥ prāvadhīc charavṛṣṭibhiḥd tasmin vinihate vīre sarveṣāṃ duḥkham āviśatd prāhasat sa tu duṣṭātmā karṇaḥ sa ca suyodhanaḥa yac ca karṇo bravīt kṛṣṇāṃ sabhāyāṃ paruṣaṃ vacaḥc pramukhe pāṇḍaveyānāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca nṛśaṃsavata vinaṣṭāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kṛṣṇe śāśvataṃ narakaṃ gatāḥc patim anyaṃ pṛthuśroṇi vṛṇīṣva mitabhāṣiṇia lekhābhru dhṛtarāṣṭrasya dāsī bhūtvā niveśanamc praviśārālapakṣmākṣi na santi patayas tavad na pāṇḍavāḥ prabhavanti tava kṛṣṇe kathaṃ canad dāsabhāryāsi pāñcāli svayaṃ dāsī ca śobhaned adya duryodhano hy ekaḥ pṛthivyāṃ nṛpatiḥ smṛtaḥd sarve cāsya mahīpālā yogakṣemam upāsated paśyedānīṃ yathā bhadre vinaṣṭāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ samamd anyonyaṃ samudīkṣante dhārtarāṣṭrasya tejasād vyaktaṃ ṣaṇḍhatilā hy ete narake ca nimajjitāḥd preṣyavac cāpi rājānam upasthāsyanti kauravama ity uktavān adharmajñas tadā paramadurmatiḥc pāpaḥ pāpaṃ vacaḥ karṇaḥ śṛṇvatas tava bhārataa tasya pāpasya tad vākyaṃ suvarṇavikṛtāḥ śarāḥc śamayantu śilādhautās tvayāstā jīvitacchidaḥd adya karṇaṃ raṇe grastaṃ paśyantu kuravas tvayād pratapantam ivādityaṃ svargadvāragataṃ yathād adya te samare vīryaṃ paśyantu kuruyodhinaḥd sūtaputre hate pārtha jānantu tvāṃ mahārathamd adya kaṅkā valā gṛdhrā vāyasā jambukās tathād viprakarṣantu gātrāṇi sūtaputrasya bhāratad adyātirathir ākṣipto nihataś ca tvayā raṇed kurūṇāṃ śokam ādhattāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mudaṃ tathād adya tvāṃ pratinandantu pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sahad yathā vṛtravadhe vṛtte devāḥ sarve śatakratumd adya karṇaṃ raṇe hatvā prāpya caivottamaṃ yaśaḥd viśoko vijvaraḥ pārtha bhava bandhupuraskṛtaḥd nārasiṃhavapuḥ kṛtvā yathā śasto mahāsuraḥd hiraṇyakaśipur daityo viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunād tathā tvam api kṛṣṇāyāḥ śatrutāpanad hatvā śatruṃ raṇe ślāghyaṃ garjantam atipauruṣamd adya cādhirathir viddhas tava bāṇaiḥ samantataḥd manyatāṃ tvāṃ naravyāghra pravaraṃ sarvadhanvināmd gāṇḍīvaprasṛtān ghorān adya pannagārthe yathā purāa taṃ tu śabdam abhiśrutya bhīmaseno mahābalaḥc babhūva paramaprītaḥ pārthadarśanalālasaḥa śrutvaiva pārtham āyāntaṃ bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavānc tyaktvā prāṇān mahārāja senāṃ tava hae tasmin hate hataṃ manye sarvasainyam aśeṣataḥa pratigṛhya ca tām ājñāṃ tava putrasya pārthivāḥc bhīmaṃ pracchādayām āsuḥ śaravarṣaiḥ samantataḥd tasmin raṇe mahārāja maheṣvāsā narās tathāa gajāś bhallaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc caturbhiḥ sārathiṃ hy ārcchad bhīmaṃ pañcabhir eva caa dhvajam ekena ciccheda chatraṃ dvābhyāṃ viśāṃ patec caturbhiś caturo vāhān vivyādha subalātmajaḥd tato hṛṣṭo mahārāja pratāpavānc śaktiṃ cikṣepa samare rukmadaṇḍām ayasmayīma sā bhīmabhujanirmuktā nāgajihveva cañcalāc nipapāta rathe tūrṇaṃ saubalasya mahātmanaḥa tatas tām eva saṃgṛhya śaktiṃ kanakabhūṣaṇāmc paśyatāṃ sarvabhūbhṛtāma sā nirbhidya bhujaṃ savyaṃ pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥc papāta ca tato bhūmau yathā vidyun nabhaścyutāa athotkruṣṭaṃ mahārāja dhārtarāṣṭraiḥ samantataḥc na tu taṃ mamṛṣe bhīmaḥ siṃhanādaṃ tarasvināma sa saṃgṛhya dhanuḥ sajyaṃ tvaramāṇo mahārathaḥc muhūrtād iva rājendra chādayām āsa sāyakaiḥe saubalasya balaṃ saṃkhye tyaktvātmānaṃ mahābalaḥa tasyāśvāṃś caturo hatvā sūtaṃ samutsṛjya dvairathāni samantataḥa tān dṛṣṭvātirathān sarvān dhārtarāṣṭrān parāṅmukhānc javenābhyapatad bhīmaḥ kirañ śaraśatān bahūna te vadhyamānā bhīmena dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ parāṅmukhāḥc karṇam āsādya
