bharatarṣabhab agādhe majjatāṃ teṣāṃ karṇo dvīpo bhavat tadāc samāśvastāḥ sthitā rājan saṃprahṛṣṭāḥ parasparame samājagmuś ca yuddhāya mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanam dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa tato bhagneṣu sainyeṣu rādheya taṃ yāhi prati bhāratamd ghṛṇāṃ tyaktvā prasādaṃ ca bhṛgor astraṃ ca saṃsmarand dṛṣṭiṃ muṣṭiṃ ca saṃdhānaṃ smṛtvā rāmopadeśajamd dhanaṃjayaṃ jaye prepsuḥ pratyudgamya mahārathānd pārthasya prekṣamāṇaḥ samantataḥd dṛśyate vānaro bhīmo vīkṣatāṃ bhayavardhanaḥd etac cakraṃ gadā śaṅkhaḥ śārṅgaṃ kṛṣṇasya ca prabhod dṛśyate pāṇḍavarathe vāhayānasya vājinaḥd etat kūjati gāṇḍīvaṃ vikṛṣṭaṃ savyasācinād ete hastavatā muktā ghnanty amitrāñ śitāḥ śarāḥd viśālāyatatāmrākṣaiḥ pūrṇacandranibhānanaiḥd eṣā bhūḥ kīryate rājñāṃ śirobhir apalāyināmd ete parighasaṃkāśāḥ puṇyagandhānulepanāḥd udyatā raṇaśauṇḍānāṃ pātyante sāyudhā bhujāḥd nirastajihvānetrāntā vājinaḥ sahasādibhiḥd patitāḥ pātyamānāś ca kṣitau kṣīṇā viśerated ete parvataśṛṅgāṇāṃ tulyā haimavatā gajāḥd saṃchinnahastāḥ pārthena prapatanty adrayo yathād gandharvanagarākārā rathā hatanareśvarāḥd vimānānīva puṇyānte svargiṇāṃ nipatanty amīd vyākulīkṛtam atyarthaṃ paśya sainyaṃ kirīṭinād nānāmṛgasahasrāṇāṃ yūthaṃ kesariṇā yathāa eṣā vidīryate senā dhārtarāṣṭrī samantataḥc arjunasya bhayāt tūrṇaṃ nighnataḥ śātravān bahūna varjayan sarvasainyāni tvarate hi dhanaṃjayaḥc tvadartham iti manye haṃ yathāsyodīryate vapuḥa na hy avasthāpyate pārtho yuyutsuḥ kena cit sahac tvām ṛte krodhadīpto hi pīḍyamāne vṛkodarea virathaṃ dharmarājaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā sudṛḍhavikṣatamc śikhaṇḍinaṃ sātyakiṃ ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca pārṣatama draupadeyān yudhāmanyum uttamaujasam eva cac nakulaṃ sahadevaṃ ca bhrātarau dvau samīkṣya caa sahasaikarathaḥ pārthas tvām abhyeti paraṃtapac krodharaktekṣaṇaḥ kruddho tvaritāḥ sma te rjunaṃjighāṃsavo vīratamāḥ samabhyayuḥb śaraiś ca jaghnur yudhi taṃ mahārathāb dhanaṃjayaṃ karṇanideśakāriṇaḥc nadīnadān bhūrijalo mahārṇavoyathā tathā tān samare rjuno grasata na saṃdadhāno na tathā śarottamānpramuñcamāno ripubhiḥ pradṛśyateb na saṃdadhan naiva samuddharañ śarānb na cābhimuñcann aribhiḥ sa dṛśyatec dhanaṃjayas tasya śaraiś ca dāritāhatāś ca petur naravājikuñjarāḥa śarārciṣaṃ gāṇḍivacārumaṇḍalaṃyugāntasūryapratimānatejasamc na kauravāḥ śekur udīkṣituṃ jayaṃyathā raviṃ vyādhitacakṣuṣo janāḥd śarottamān sa prahitān mahārathaiśd ciccheda pārthaḥ prahasañ śaraughaiḥd bhūyaś ca tān ahanad bāṇasaṃghānd gāṇḍīvadhanvāyatapūrṇamaṇḍalamd yathograraśmiḥ śuciśukramadhyagaḥd sukhaṃ vivasvān harate jalaughānd tathārjuno bāṇagaṇān nirasyad dadāha senāṃ tava pārthivendraa tam abhyadhāvad visṛjañ śarān kṛpastathaiva bhojas tava cātmajaḥ svayamb mahāratho droṇasutaś ca sāyakairb avākiraṃs toyadharā yathācalamb jighāṃsavaḥ pātham asahyavikramaṃb yathaiva vahniṃ śalabhā mahārciṣamc jighāṃsubhis tān kuśalaiḥ śarottamānmahāhave saṃjavitān prayatnataḥe śaraiḥ praciccheda ca pāṇḍavas tvaranparābhinad vakṣasi ca tribhis tribhiḥa sa caturbhir aśvāṃś caturaḥ kapiṃ tathāśaraiḥ sa nārācavarair avākirata tathā tu tat tat sphurad āttakārmukaṃtribhiḥ śarair yantṛśiraḥ kṣureṇac hayāṃś caturbhiś caturas tribhir dhvajaṃdhanaṃjayo kirīṭināa śaraiḥ praciccheda tavātmajasyadhvajaṃ dhanuś ca pracakarta nardataḥc jaghāna cāśvān kṛtavarmaṇaḥ śubhāndhvajaṃ ca ciccheda tataḥ pratāpavāna savājisūteṣv asanān saketanāñjaghāna nāgāśvarathāṃs tvaraṃś ca saḥc tataḥ prakīrṇaṃ sumahad balaṃ tavapradāritaṃ setur ivāmbhasā yathāe tato rjunasyāśu rathena keśavaścakāra śatrūn apasavyam āturāna tataḥ prayāntaṃ tvaritaṃ dhanaṃjayaṃśatakratuṃ vṛtranijaghnuṣaṃ yathāc samanvadhāvan punar ucchritair dhvajairathaiḥ suyuktair apare yuyutsavaḥa athābhisṛtya prativārya tān arīndhanaṃjayasyābhi rathaṃ mahārathāḥc śikhaṇḍiśaineyayamāḥ śitaiḥ śarairvidārayanto vyanadan subhairavama tato bhijaghnuḥ kupitāḥ parasparaṃśarais tadāñjogatibhiḥ sutejanaiḥc kurupravīrāḥ saha sṛñjayair yathāsurāḥ purā devavarair ayodhayana jayepsavaḥ svargamanāya cotsukāḥpatanti nāgāśvarathāḥ paraṃtapac jagarjur uccair balavac ca vivyadhuḥśaraiḥ sumuktair itaretaraṃ pṛthaka śarāndhakāre tu mahātmabhiḥ kṛtemahāmṛdhe yodhavaraiḥ parasparamc babhur daśāśā na divaṃ ca pārthivaprabhā ca sūryasya tamovṛtābhavatd śarāndhakāraṃ ca kṛtaṃ mahātmabhisd tadā diśo na prababhuḥ śarārditāḥ saṃjaya uvācaa rājan kurūṇāṃ pravarair balair bhīmam abhidrutamc majjantam iva kaunteyam ujjihīrṣur dhanaṃjayaḥa vimṛdya sūtaputrasya senāṃ bhārata sāyakaiḥc prāhiṇon mṛtyulokāya paravīrān dhanaṃjayaḥa tato syāmbaram āvṛtya śarajālāni bhāgaśaḥc adṛśyanta tathānye ca nighnantas tava vāhinīma sa pakṣisaṃghācaritam ākāśaṃ pūrayañ śaraiḥc dhanaṃjayo mahārāja kurūṇām antako bhavata tato bhallaiḥ kṣurapraiś ca nārācair nirmalair apic gātrāṇi prākṣiṇot pārthaḥ śirāṃsi ca cakarta haa chinnagātrair vikavacair viśiraskaiḥ samantataḥc patitaiś ca patadbhiś ca yodhair āsīt samāvṛtama dhanaṃjayaśarābhyastaiḥ syandanāśvanaradvipaiḥb saṃchinnabhinnavidhvastair vyaṅgāṅgāvayavaiḥ stṛtāb sudurgamā suviṣamā ghorātyarthaṃ sudurdṛśāc raṇabhūmir abhūd rājan mahāvaitaraṇī yathāf gatasattvaiḥ sasattvaiś ca saṃvṛtāsīd vasuṃdharāa īṣācakrākṣabhaṅgaiś ca vyaśvaiḥ sāśvaiś ca yudhyatāmc sasūtair hatasūtaiś ca rathaiḥ stīrṇābhavan mahīd sasūtair hatasūtaiś ca sādihīnaiś ca vājibhiḥd īṣācakrākṣabhagnaiś ca rathaiḥ stīrṇā vasuṃdharāa suvarṇavarmasaṃnāhair yodhaiḥ kanakabhūṣaṇaiḥc āsthitāḥ kṛtavarmāṇo bhadrā nityamadā dvipāḥe kruddhāḥ kruddhair mahāmātraiḥ preṣitārjunam abhyayuḥa catuḥśatāḥ śaravarṣair hatāḥ petuḥ kirīṭināc paryastānīva śṛṅgāṇi sasattvāni mahāgireḥa dhanaṃjayaśarābhyastaiḥ stīrṇā bhūr varavāraṇaiḥb samantāj jaladaprakhyān vāraṇān madavarṣiṇaḥc abhipede rjunaratho ghanān bhindann ivāṃśumāna hatair gajamanuṣyāśvair bhagnaiś ca bahudhā rathaiḥc viśastrapatrakavacair yuddhaśauṇḍair gatāsubhiḥe apaviddhāyudhair mārgaḥ stīrṇo bhūt phalgunena vaia vyasphūrjayac ca gāṇḍīvaṃ sumahad bhairavasvanamc ghoro vajraviniṣpeṣaḥ stanayitnor ivāmbarea tataḥ prādīryata camūr dhanaṃjayaśarāhatāc mahāvātasamāviddhā mahānaur iva sāgarea nānārūpāḥ praharaṇāḥ śarā gāṇḍīvacoditāḥc alātolkāśaniprakhyās tava sainyaṃ vinirdahana mahāgirau veṇuvanaṃ niśi prajvalitaṃ yathāc tathā tava mahat sainyaṃ prāsphurac charapīḍitama saṃpiṣṭadagdhavidhvastaṃ tava sainyaṃ kirīṭināc hataṃ pravihataṃ bāṇaiḥ sarvataḥ pradrutaṃ diśaḥa mahāvane mṛgagaṇā dāvāgnigrasitā yathāc kuravaḥ paryavartanta nirdagdhāḥ savyasācināa utsṛjya hi mahābāhuṃ bhīmasenaṃ tadā raṇec balaṃ kurūṇām udvignaṃ sarvam āsīt parāṅmukhama tataḥ kuruṣu bhagneṣu bībhatsur aparājitaḥc bhīmasenaṃ samāsādya muhūrtaṃ so bhyavartataa samāgamya sa bhīmena mantrayitvā ca phalgunaḥc viśalyam arujaṃ cāsmai kathayitvā yudhiṣṭhirama bhīmasenābhyanujñātas tataḥ prāyād dhanaṃjayaḥc nādayan rathaghoṣeṇa pṛthivīṃ dyāṃ ca bhārataa tataḥ parivṛto bhīmair daśabhiḥ śatrupuṃgavaiḥc duḥśāsanād avarajais tava putrair dhanaṃjayaḥa te tam abhyardayan bāṇair ulkābhir iva kuñjaramc ātateṣv asanāḥ krūrā nṛtyanta iva bhārataa apasavyāṃs tu tāṃś cakre rathena madhusūdanaḥb niyuktān hi sa tān mene yamāyāśu kirīṭināc tatas te prādravañ śūrāḥ parāṅmukharathe rjunea teṣām āpatatāṃ ketūn rathāṃś cāpāni sāyakānc nārācair ardhacandraiś ca kṣipraṃ pārtho nyapātayata athānyair daśabhir bhallaiḥ śirāṃsy eṣāṃ nyapātayatc roṣasaṃraktanetrāṇi saṃdaṣṭauṣṭhāni bhūtalee tāni vaktrāṇi vibabhur vyomni tārāgaṇā ivaa tāṃs tu bhallair mahāvegair daśabhir daśa kauravānc rukmāṅgadān rukmapuṅkhair viddhvā prāyād amitrahā saṃjaya uvācaa taṃ tu yāntaṃ mahāvegair aśvaiḥ kapivaradhvajamc yuddhāyābhyadravan vīrāḥ kurūṇāṃ navatī rathāḥd kṛtvā saṃśaptakā ghorāñ śapathān brāhmalaukikāne parivavrur naravyāghrā naravyāghraṃ raṇe rjunama kṛṣṇaḥ śvetān mahāvegān aśvān kanakabhūṣaṇānc muktājālapraticchannān praiṣīt karṇarathaṃ pratia tataḥ karṇarathaṃ yāntam arīn ghnantaṃ dhanaṃjayamc bāṇavarṣair abhighnantaḥ saṃśaptakarathā yayuḥa tvaramāṇāṃs tu tān sarvān sasūteṣvasanadhvajānc jaghāna navatiṃ vīrān arjuno niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa te patanta hatā bāṇair nānārūpaiḥ kirīṭināc savimānā yathā siddhāḥ svargāt puṇyakṣaye tathāa tataḥ sarathanāgāśvāḥ kuravaḥ kurusattamab kṣipram evābhisaṃkruddhāḥ samare rijighāṃsayāc nirbhayā bharataśreṣṭham abhyavartanta phalgunama tad āyastam amuktāstram udīrṇavaravāraṇamc putrāṇāṃ te mahat sainyaṃ samarautsīd dhanaṃjayaḥa śaktyṛṣṭitomaraprāsair gadānistriṃśasāyakaiḥc prācchādayan maheṣvāsāḥ kuravaḥ kurunandanama tāṃ kurūṇāṃ pravitatāṃ śastravṛṣṭiṃ samudyatāmc vyadhamat pāṇḍavo bāṇais tamaḥ sūrya ivāṃśubhiḥa tato mlecchāḥ sthitair mattais trayodaśaśatair gajaiḥc pārśvato bhyahanan pārthaṃ tava putrasya śāsanāta karṇinālīkanārācais tomaraiḥ prāsaśaktibhiḥc kampanair bhiṇḍipālaiś ca rathasthaṃ pārtham ārdayana tām astravṛṣṭiṃ prahitāṃ dvipasthair yavanaiḥ smayanc ciccheda niśitair bhallair ardhacandraiś ca phalgunaḥa atha tān dviradān sarvān nānāliṅgair mahāśaraiḥc sapatākān sahārohān girīn vajrair ivābhinata te hemapuṅkhair iṣubhir ācitā hemamālinaḥc hatāḥ petur mahānāgāḥ sāgnijvālā ivādrayaḥa tato gāṇḍīvanirghoṣo mahān āsīd viśāṃ patec stanatāṃ kūjatāṃ caiva manuṣyagajavājināma kuñjarāś ca hatā rājan prādravaṃs te samantataḥc aśvāś ca paryadhāvanta hatārohā diśo daśaa rathā hīnā mahārāja rathibhir vājibhis tathāc gandharvanagarākārā dṛśyante sma sahasraśaḥa aśvārohā mahārāja dhāvamānās tatas tataḥb nardantaḥ kūjamānāś ca manuṣyagajavājinaḥc tatra tatraiva dṛśyante patitāḥ pārthasāyakaiḥa tasmin kṣaṇe pāṇḍavasya bāhvor balam adṛśyatac yat sādino vāraṇāṃś ca rathāṃś caiko jayad yudhid asaṃyuktāś ca te rājan parivṛttā raṇaṃ pratid narā nāgā rathāś caiva nadanto rjunam abhyayuḥa tatas tryaṅgeṇa mahatā balena bharatarṣabhac dṛṣṭvā parivṛtaṃ rājan bhīmasenaḥ kirīṭinama hatāvaśeṣān utsṛjya tvadīyān kati cid rathānc javenābhyadravad rājan dhanaṃjayarathaṃ pratia tatas tat prādravat sainyaṃ hatabhūyiṣṭham āturamc dṛṣṭvā yad arjunaṃ bhīmo jagāma bhrātaraṃ pratia hatāvaśiṣṭāṃs turagān arjunena mahājavānc bhīmo vyadhamad abhrānto gadāpāṇir mahāhaved gadāpāṇiṃ tadā bhīmaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhārata bhāratāḥd menire tam anuprāptaṃ daṇḍahastam ivāntakama kālarātrim ivātyugrāṃ naranāgāśvabhojanāmc prākārāṭṭapuradvāradāraṇīm atidāruṇāma tato gadāṃ nṛnāgāśveṣv āśu bhīmo vyavāsṛjatb gajān aśvān hayārohān uddiśyoddiśya bhāratac sā jaghāna bahūn aśvān aśvārohāṃś ca māriṣaa kāṃsyāyasatanutrāṃs tān narān aśvāṃś ca pāṇḍavaḥc pothayām āsa gadayā saśabdaṃ te patan hatāḥd kṣaṇena bhīmaḥ saṃkruddhas tān ninye vai yamakṣayamf tataḥ sa samaraślāghī gajānīkam apātayatf gadayā vyadhamat saṃkhye daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥf gajān sakaṅkaṭān mattān sārohān sapatākinaḥf nyahanal līlayā rājañ śikṣayā ca balena caf te gajā bahvaśobhanta hanyamānā mahāraṇef vinadanto yathā tūrṇaṃ pakṣavanta ivādrayaḥf nipetur urvyāṃ samare bhīmasenena pīḍitāḥf chinnapakṣā yathā kāle vajrarugṇā ivādrayaḥf dantair daśanto vasudhāṃ śerate kṣatajokṣitāḥf bhagnamūrdhāsthicaraṇāḥ kravyādagaṇabhojanāḥf asṛṅmāṃsavasābhiś ca tṛptā māṃsavasāśanāḥf asthīny apy aśnatī tasthau kālarātrīva durdṛśāf sahasrāṇi daśāśvānāṃ hatvā pattīṃś ca bhūyasāf bhīmo bhyadhāvat saṃkruddho gadāpāṇir itas tataḥf gadāpāṇiṃ tato bhīmaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhārata tāvakāḥf menire samanuprāptaṃ kālaṃ daṇḍodyataṃ yathāf sa matta iva mātaṅgaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ pāṇḍunandanaḥf praviveśa gajānīkaṃ makaraḥ sāgaraṃ yathāf vigāhya ca gajānīkaṃ pragṛhya mahatīṃ gadāmf kṣaṇena bhīmaḥ saṃkruddhas tān ninye yamasādanamf gajān sakaṅkaṭān mattān sarohān sapatākinaḥf patataḥ samapaśyāma sapakṣān parvatān ivaa hatvā tu tad gajānīkaṃ bhīmaseno mahābalaḥc punaḥ svaratham āsthāya pṛṣṭhato rjunam anvagāta hataṃ parāṅmukhaprāyaṃ nirutsāhaṃ paraṃ balamc vyālambata mahārāja prāyaśaḥ śastraveṣṭitama vilambamānaṃ tat sainyam apragalbham avasthitamc dṛṣṭvā prācchādayad bāṇair arjunaḥ prāṇatāpanaiḥd narāśvarathamātaṅgā yudhi gāṇḍīvadhanvanād śaravrātaiś citā rejuḥ kadambā iva kesaraiḥa tataḥ kurūṇām abhavad ārtanādo mahāmṛdheb śataśo vadhyamānānāṃ niśitair arjuneṣubhiḥc rathāśvanāgāsuharair vadhyatām arjuneṣubhiḥd kurūṇāṃ tu mahārāja āsīd ārtasvaro mahānd narāśvanāgāsuharān dṛṣṭvā bāṇān kirīṭinaḥa hāhākṛtaṃ bhṛśaṃ tasthau līyamānaṃ parasparamc alātacakravat sainyaṃ tadābhramata tāvakamd tatas tad yuddham abhavat kurūṇāṃ sumahad balamd na hy atrāsīd anirbhinno rathaḥ sādī hayo gajaḥd tataḥ śaradhvastam abhūt kurūṇāṃ sumahad balamd na tatrāsīd anirbhinno ratho vājī naro gajaḥa ādīptaṃ tava tat sainyaṃ śaraiś chinnatanucchadamc āsīt svaśoṇitaklinnaṃ phullāśokavanaṃ yathād tat sainyaṃ bharataśreṣṭha vadhyamānaṃ śitaiḥ śaraiḥd na jahau samaraṃ prāpya phalgunaṃ śatrutāpanamd tatrādbhutam apaśyāma kauravāṇāṃ parākramamd vadhyamānāpi yat pārthaṃ na jahuḥ samare prabhoa tad dṛṣṭvā kuravas tatra vikrāntaṃ savyasācinaḥc nirāśāḥ samapadyanta sarve karṇasya jīvitea aviṣahyaṃ tu pārthasya śarasaṃpātam āhavec matvā nyavartan kuravo jitā gāṇḍīvadhanvanāa te hitvā samare pārthaṃ vadhyamānāś ca sāyakaiḥc pradudruvur diśo bhītāś cukruśuś cāpi sūtajama abhyadravata tān pārthaḥ kirañ śaraśatān bahūnc harṣayan pāṇḍavān yodhān bhīmasenapurogamāna putrās tu te mahārāja jagmuḥ karṇarathaṃ pratic agādhe majjatāṃ teṣāṃ dvīpaḥ karṇo bhavat tadāa kuravo hi mahārāja nirviṣāḥ pannagā ivac karṇam evopalīyanta bhayād gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥa yathā sarvāṇi bhūtāni mṛtyor bhītāni bhāratac dharmam evopalīyante karmavanti hi yāni caa tathā karṇaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ putrās tava narādhipac upālīyanta saṃtrāsāt pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥa tāñ śoṇitapariklinnān viṣamasthāñ śarāturānc mā bhaiṣṭety abravīt karṇo hy abhito mām iteti caa saṃbhagnaṃ hi balaṃ dṛṣṭvā balāt pārthena tāvakamc dhanur visphārayan karṇas tasthau śatrujighāṃsayād viṣphārayitvā durdharṣaś cāpam ādhirathir mahatd tān vidrutān kurūn dṛṣṭvā karṇaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥd saṃcintayitvā pārthasya vadhe dadhre manaḥ śvasand visphārya sumahac cāpaṃ tataś cādhirathir vṛṣaḥe pāñcālān punar ādhāvat paśyataḥ savyasācinaḥa tataḥ kṣaṇena kṣitipāḥ kṣatajapratimekṣaṇāḥc karṇaṃ vavarṣur bāṇaughair yathā meghā mahīdharamd śaraughaiś chādayām āsa mahāmegha ivācalama tataḥ śarasahasrāṇi karṇamuktāni māriṣac vyayojayanta pāñcālān prāṇaiḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ varad pāñcālānāṃ harat prāṇāṃs tamāṃsīva tamonudaḥa tato raṇo mahān āsīt pāñcālānāṃ viśāṃ patec vadhyatāṃ sūtaputreṇa mitrārthe mitraghātinām saṃjaya uvācaa tataḥ karṇaḥ kuruṣu pradruteṣuvarūthinā śvetahayena rājanc pāñcālaputrān vyadhamat sūtaputromaheṣubhir vāta ivābhrasaṃghāna sūtaṃ rathād añjalikena pātyajaghāna cāśvāñ janamejayasyac śatānīkaṃ sutasomaṃ ca bhallairavākirad dhanuṣī cāpy akṛntata dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ nirbibhedātha ṣaḍbhirjaghāna cāśvaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ tasya saṃkhyec hatvā cāśvān sātyakeḥ sūtaputraḥkaikeyaputraṃ nyavadhīd viśokama tam abhyadhāvan nihate kumārekaikeyasenāpatir ugradhanvāc śarair vibhinnaṃ bhṛśam ugravegaiḥkarṇātmajaṃ so bhyahanat suṣeṇama tasyārdhacandrais tribhir uccakartaprasahya bāhū ca śiraś ca karṇaḥc sa syandanād gām apatad gatāsuḥparaśvadhaiḥ śāla ivāvarugṇaḥa hatāśvam añjogatibhiḥ suṣeṇaḥśinipravīraṃ niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥc pracchādya nṛtyann iva sautiputraḥśaineyabāṇābhihataḥ papātaa putre hate krodhaparītacetāḥkarṇaḥ śinīnām ṛṣabhaṃ jighāṃsuḥc hato si śaineya iti bruvan savyavāsṛjad bāṇam amitrasāhama sa tasya ciccheda śaraṃ śikhaṇḍītribhis tribhiś ca pratutoda karṇamc śikhaṇḍinaḥ kārmukaṃ sa dhvajaṃ cacchittvā śarābhyām ahanat sujātama śikhaṇḍinaṃ ṣaḍbhir avidhyad ugrodānto dhārṣṭadyumnaśiraś cakartac athābhinat sutasomaṃ śareṇasa saṃśitenādhirathir mahātmād tato pare bhārata duṣprakampyāḥd pāñcālānāṃ rathasaṃghāḥ sametāḥd pratiśrutā hy antarikṣe gatābhād dhanuḥpravīrās tu rathapravīrāḥa athākrande tumule vartamānedhārṣṭadyumne nihate tatra kṛṣṇaḥc apāñcālyaṃ kriyate yāhi pārthakarṇaṃ jahīty abravīd rājasiṃhaa tataḥ prahasyāśu narapravīrorathaṃ rathenādhirather jagāmac bhaye teṣāṃ trāṇam icchan subāhurabhyāhatānāṃ rathayūthapenaa visphārya gāṇḍīvam athograghoṣaṃjyayā samāhatya tale bhṛśaṃ cac bāṇāndhakāraṃ sahasaiva kṛtvājaghāna nāgāśvarathān narāṃś cad prītāḥ śukāḥ prādravann antarikṣed guhā girīṇām apatan vayāṃsid yan maṇḍalajyena vijṛmbhamāṇod raudre muhūrte bhyapatat kirīṭīa taṃ bhīmaseno nu yayau rathenapṛṣṭhe rakṣan pāṇḍavam ekavīramc tau rājaputrau tvaritau rathābhyāṃkarṇāya yātāv aribhir vimuktaua atrāntare sumahat sūtaputraścakre yuddhaṃ somakān saṃpramṛdnanc rathāśvamātaṅgagaṇāñ jaghānapracchādayām āsa diśaḥ śaraiś caa tam uttamaujā janamejayaś cakruddhau yudhāmanyuśikhaṇḍinau cac karṇaṃ vineduḥ sahitāḥ pṛṣatkaiḥsaṃmardamānāḥ saha pārṣatenaa te pañca pāñcālarathāḥ surūpairvaikartanaṃ karṇam abhidravantaḥc tasmād rathāc cyāvayituṃ na śekurdhairyāt kṛtātmānam ivendriyāṇia teṣāṃ dhanūṃṣi dhvajavājisūtāṃstūṇaṃ patākāś ca nikṛtya bāṇaiḥb teṣāṃ dhvajān vājisūtān patākāsb tūṇīr dhanūṃṣi pracakarta bāṇaiḥc tān pañcabhiḥ sa tv ahanat pṛṣatkaiḥkarṇas tataḥ siṃha ivonnanādaa tasyāsyatas tān abhinighnataś cajyābāṇahastasya dhanuḥsvanenac sādridrumā syāt pṛthivī viśīrṇāity eva matvā janatā vyaṣīdata sa śakracāpapratimena dhanvanābhṛśātatenādhirathiḥ śarān sṛjanc babhau raṇe dīptamarīcimaṇḍaloyathāṃśumālī pariveṣavāṃs tathāa śikhaṇḍinaṃ dvādaśabhiḥ parābhinacchitaiḥ śaraiḥ ṣaḍbhir athottamaujasamc tribhir yudhāmanyum avidhyad āśugaistribhis tribhiḥ somakapārṣatātmajaua parājitāḥ pañca mahārathās tu temahāhave sūtasutena māriṣac nirudyamās tasthur amitramardanāyathendriyārthātmavatā parājitāḥa nimajjatas tān atha karṇasāgarevipannanāvo vaṇijo yathārṇavec uddadhrire naubhir ivārṇavād rathaiḥsukalpitair draupadijāḥ svamātulāna tataḥ śinīnām ṛṣabhaḥ śitaiḥ śarairnikṛtya karṇaprahitān iṣūn bahūnc vidārya karṇaṃ niśitair ayasmayaistavātmajaṃ jyeṣṭham avidhyad aṣṭabhiḥa kṛpo tha bhojaś ca tavātmajas tathāsvayaṃ ca karṇo niśitair raviḥa punaḥ samāsādya rathān sudaṃśitāḥśinipravīraṃ jugupuḥ paraṃtapāḥc sametya pāñcālarathā mahāraṇemarudgaṇāḥ śakram ivārinigrahea tato bhavad yuddham atīva dāruṇaṃtavāhitānāṃ tava sainikaiḥ sahac rathāśvamātaṅgavināśanaṃ tathāyathā surāṇām asuraiḥ purābhavata rathadvipā vājipadātayo pi vābhramanti nānāvidhaśastraveṣṭitāḥc paraspareṇābhihatāś ca caskhalurvinedur ārtā vyasavo patanta caa tathā gate bhīmam abhīs tavātmajaḥsasāra rājāvarajaḥ kirañ śaraiḥc tam abhyadhāvat tvarito vṛkodaromahāruruṃ siṃha ivābhipetivāna tatas tayor yuddham atītamānuṣaṃpradīvyatoḥ prāṇadurodare bhavatc paraspareṇābhiniviṣṭaroṣayorudagrayoḥ śambaraśakrayor yathāa śaraiḥ śarīrāntakaraiḥ sutejanairnijaghnatus tāv itaretaraṃ bhṛśamc sakṛtprabhinnāv iva vāśitāntaremahāgajau manmathasaktacetasaud ālokya tau caiva parasparaṃ tataḥd samaṃ ca śūrau ca sasārathī tadād bhīmo bravīd yāhi duḥśāsanāyad duḥśāsano yāhi vṛkodarāyad tayo rathau sārathibhyāṃ pracoditaud samaṃ rathau tau sahasā samīyatuḥd nānāyudhau citrapatākinadhvajaud bhīmaḥd divīva pūrvaṃ balaśakrayo raṇed diṣṭyāsi duḥśāsana adya dṛṣṭad ṛṇaṃ pratīccheḥ sahavṛddhimūlamd ciroditaṃ taṃ yan mayā te sabhāyāṃd kṛṣṇābhimarśena gṛhāṇa mattaḥd sa evam uktas tu tato mahātmād duḥśāsano vākyam uvāca vīraḥd sarvaṃ smare naiva ca vismarāmid udīryamāṇaṃ śṛṇu bhīmasenad smarāmi cātmaprabhavaṃ cirāyad yaj jātuṣe veśmani rātry ahānid viśvāsahīnā mṛgayāṃ carantod vasanti sarvatra nirākṛtās tud mahad bhayād rātry ahani smarantasd tathopabhogāc ca sukhāc ca hīnāḥd vaneṣv aṭanto girigahvarāṇid pāñcālarājasya puraṃ praviṣṭāḥd māyāṃ yūyaṃ kām api saṃpraviṣṭād yato vṛtaḥ kṛṣṇayā phalguno vaḥd saṃbhūya pāpais tad anāryavṛttaṃd kṛtaṃ tadā mātṛkṛtānurūpamd eko vṛtaḥ pañcabhiḥ sābhipannād hy alajjamānaiś ca parasparasyad smare sabhāyāṃ subalātmajenad saṃjayaḥd dāsīkṛtāḥ stha saha kṛṣṇayā tud tenaivam uktas tu tavātmajenad subālacittena vṛkodaro pid pragṛhya cāpaṃ bhṛkuṭīṃ lalāṭed kṛtvā tu roṣojjvalatāmranetraḥa tato dhvajaṃ sphāṭikacitrakambuṃciccheda vīro nakulaḥ kṣureṇac karṇātmajasyeṣvasanaṃ ca citraṃbhallena jāmbūnadapaṭṭanaddhama athānyad ādāya dhanuḥ suśīghraṃkarṇātmajaḥ pāṇḍavam abhyavidhyatc divyair śarābhighātāc ca ruṣā ca rājand svayaṃ ca bhāsāstrasamīraṇāc cad jajvāla karṇasya suto timātramd iddho yathā jyāhutibhir hutāśaḥa karṇasya putro nakulasya rājansarvān aśvān akṣiṇod uttamāstraiḥb āsīt sughoraṃ bharatapravīrab yuddhaṃ tadā karṇajapāṇḍavābhyāmc vanāyujān sukumārasya śubhrānalaṃkṛtāñ jātarūpeṇa śīghrānd jaghāna cāśvān nakulasya vīrod raṇājire sūtaputrasya putraḥa tato hatāśvād avaruhya yānādādāya carma ruciraṃ cāṣṭacandramc ākāśasaṃkāśam asiṃ gṛhītvāpoplūyamānaḥ khagavac cacāraa tato ntarikṣe nṛvarāśvanāgāṃściccheda mārgān vicaran vicitrānb tato sya pakṣān anayad yamāyab dvisāhasrān nakulaḥ kṣiprakārīc te prāpatann asinā gāṃ viśastāyathāśvamedhe paśavaḥ śamitrāa dvisāhasrā viditā yuddhaśauṇḍānānādeśyāḥ subhṛtāḥ satyasaṃdhāḥc ekena śīghraṃ nakulena kṛttāḥsārepsunevottamacandanās tea tam āpatantaṃ nakulaṃ so bhipatyasamantataḥ sāyakair abhyavidhyata karṇasya putraḥ sahasābhipatya caa raṇe jighāṃsuṃ niśitair anekaiḥb bhūmau carantaṃ nakulaṃ rathasthāḥb samantataḥ sāyakaiḥ pratyagṛhṇanc sa tudyamāno nakulaḥ pṛṣatkairvivyādha vīraṃ sa cukopa viddhaḥd mahābhaye rakṣyamāṇo mahātmād bhrātrā bhīmenākarot tatra bhīmama taṃ karṇaputro vidhamantam ekaṃnarāśvamātaṅgarathapravekānc krīḍantam aṣṭādaśabhiḥ pṛṣatkairvivyādha vīraṃ sa cukopa viddhaḥd sa tena viddho tibhṛśaṃ tarasvīd mahāhave vṛṣasenena rājana tato bhyadhāvat samare jighāṃsuḥkarṇātmajaṃ pāṇḍusuto nṛvīraḥb vitatya pakṣau sahasā patantaṃb śyenaṃ yathaivāmiṣalubdham ājaub avākirad vṛṣasenas tatas taṃb śitaiḥ śarair nakulam udāravīryamb sa tān moghāṃs tasya kurvañ śaraughāṃśb cacāra mārgān nakulaś citrarūpānb athāsya tūrṇaṃ carato narendrab khaḍgena citraṃ nakulasya tasyac tasyeṣubhir vyadhamat karṇaputromahāraṇe carma sahasratārama tasyāyasaṃ niśitaṃ tīkṣṇadhāramasiṃ vikośaṃ gurubhārasāhamc dviṣaccharīrāpaharaṃ sughoramādhunvataḥ sarpam ivograrūpama kṣipraṃ śaraiḥ ṣaḍbhir amitrasāhaścakarta khaḍgaṃ niśitaiḥ sudhāraiḥc punaś ca pītair niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥstanāntare gāḍham athābhyavidhyatd kṛtvā tu tad duṣkaram āryajuṣṭaṃd narair anyaiḥ karma raṇe mahātmād yayau rathaṃ bhīmasenasya rājañd śarābhitapto nakulo mahātmāa sa bhīmasenasya rathaṃ hatāśvomādrīsutaḥ karṇasutābhitaptaḥc āpupluve siṃha ivācalāgraṃsaṃprekṣamāṇasya dhanaṃjayasyad sa bhīmasenasya rathaṃ ca hatvād vavarṣa vai śaravarṣaṃ sughoramd tataḥ kruddho vṛṣaseno mahātmād vavarṣa tāv iṣujālena vīraḥd mahārathāv ekarathe sametaud śaraiḥ prabhindann iva pāṇḍaveyaud tasmin rathe nihate pāṇḍavasyad kṣipraṃ ca khaḍge viśikhair nikṛtted bhīmārjunau vṛṣasenāya kruddhaud vavarṣatuḥ śaravarṣaṃ sughoramd athābravīn mārutiḥ phalgunaṃ tud paśyasvainaṃ nakulaṃ pīḍayantamd ayaṃ ca no bādhate karṇaputrasd tasmād bhavān pratyupayātu kārṇimd sa tan niśamyaiva vacaḥ kirīṭīd rathaṃ samāsādya vṛkodarasyad kapidhvajaṃ keśavasaṃgṛhītaṃd praiṣīd ugro vṛṣasenāya vāhama nakulam atha viditvā chinnabāṇāsanāsiṃviratham ariśarārtaṃ karṇaputrāstrabhagnamc pavanadhutapatākā hrādino valgitāśvāvarapuruṣaniyattās te rathāḥ śīghram īyuḥa drupadasutavariṣṭhāḥ pañca śaineyaṣaṣṭhādrupadaduhitṛputrāḥ pañca cāmitrasāhāḥc dviradarathanarāśvān sūdayantas tvadīyānbhujagapatinikāśair mārgaṇair āttaśastrāḥa atha tava rathamukhyās tān pratīyus tvarantohṛdikasutakṛpau ca drauṇiduryodhanau cac śakuniśukavṛkāś ca krāthadevāvṛdhau cadviradajaladaghoṣaiḥ syandanaiḥ kārmukaiś caa tava naravaravaryās tān daśaikaṃ ca vīrānpravaraśaravarāgryais tāḍayanto bhyarundhanc navajaladasavarṇair hastibhis tān udīyurgiriśikharanikāśair bhīmavegaiḥ kuṇindāḥa sukalpitā haimavatā madotkaṭāraṇābhikāmaiḥ kṛtibhiḥ samāsthitāḥc suvarṇajālāvatatā babhur gajāstathā yathā vai jaladāḥ savidyutaḥa kuṇindaputro daśabhir mahāyasaiḥkṛpaṃ sasūtāśvam apīḍayad bhṛśamc tataḥ śaradvatsutasāyakair hataḥsahaiva nāgena papāta bhūtalea kuṇindaputrāvarajas tu tomarairdivākarāṃśupratimair ayasmayaiḥc rathaṃ ca vikṣobhya nanāda nardatastato sya gāndhārapatiḥ śiro harata tataḥ kuṇindeṣu hateṣu teṣv athaprahṛṣṭarūpās tava te mahārathāḥc bhṛśaṃ pradadhmur lavaṇāmbusaṃbhavānparāṃś ca bāṇāsanapāṇayo bhyayuḥa athābhavad yuddham atīva dāruṇaṃpunaḥ kurūṇāṃ saha pāṇḍusṛñjayaiḥc śarāsiśaktyṛṣṭigadāparaśvadhairnarāśvanāgāsuharaṃ bhṛśākulama rathāśvamātaṅgapadātibhis tataḥparasparaṃ viprahatāpatan kṣitauc yathā savidyutstanitā balāhakāḥsamāsthitā digbhya ivogramārutaiḥa tataḥ śatānīkahatān mahāgajāṃstathā rathān pattigaṇāṃś ca tāvakānc jaghāna bhojaś ca hayān athāpatanviśastrakṛttāḥ kṛtavarmaṇā dvipāḥa athāpare drauṇiśarāhatā dvipāstrayaḥ sasarvāyudhayodhaketavaḥc nipetur urvyāṃ vyasavaḥ prapātitāstathā yathā vajrahatā mahācalāḥa kuṇindarājāvarajād anantaraḥstanāntare patrivarair atāḍayatc tavātmajaṃ tasya tavātmajaḥ śaraiḥśitaiḥ śarīraṃ bibhide dvipaṃ ca tama sa nāgarājaḥ saha rājasūnunāpapāta raktaṃ bahu sarvataḥ kṣaranc śacīśavajraprahato mbudāgameyathā jalaṃ gairikaparvatas tathāa kuṇindaputraprahito paradvipaḥśukaṃ sasūtāśvarathaṃ vyapothayatc tato patat krāthaśarābhidāritaḥsaheśvaro vajrahato yathā giriḥa rathī dvipasthena hato patac charaiḥkrāthādhipaḥ parvatajena durjayaḥc savājisūteṣvasanas tathāpatadyathā mahāvātahato mahādrumaḥa vṛko dvipasthaṃ girirājavāsinaṃbhṛśaṃ śarair dvādaśabhiḥ parābhinatc tato vṛkaṃ sāśvarathaṃ mahājavaṃtvaraṃś caturbhiś caraṇe vyapothayata sa nāgarājaḥ saniyantṛko patatparāhato babhrusuteṣubhir bhṛśama samāgato yatra vṛko mahābalaḥb sa pothito nāgavareṇa vīryavānb parābhinad dvādaśabhiḥ śilīmukhaiḥb vṛkeṇa bāṇābhihato patat kṣitaub sa vāraṇo babhrusutena sārdhamb kuṇindarājasya suto paras tadāb dvipena devāpṛthudaivāvṛdham abhyapīḍayatc sa cāpi devāvṛdhasūnur arditaḥpapāta nunnaḥ sahadevasūnunāa viṣāṇapotrāparagātraghātināgajena hantuṃ śakuneḥ kuṇindajaḥb nināya vaivasvatamandiraṃ raṇec jagāma vegena bhṛśārdayaṃś ca taṃtato sya gāndhārapatiḥ śiro harata tataḥ śatānīkahatā mahāgajāhayā rathāḥ pattigaṇāś ca tāvakāḥc suparṇavātaprahatā yathā nagāstathā gatā gām avaśā vicūrṇitāḥa tato bhyavidhyad bahubhiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥkuṇindaputro nakulātmajaṃ smayanc tato sya kāyān nicakarta nākuliḥśiraḥ kṣureṇāmbujasaṃnibhānanama tataḥ śatānīkam avidhyad āśugaistribhiḥ śitaiḥ karṇasuto rjunaṃ tribhiḥc tribhiś ca bhīmaṃ nakulaṃ ca saptabhirjanārdanaṃ dvādaśabhiś ca sāyakaiḥa tad asya karmātimanuṣyakarmaṇaḥsamīkṣya hṛṣṭāḥ kuravo bhyapūjayanc parākramajñās tu dhanaṃjayasya tehuto yam agnāv iti taṃ tu menirea tataḥ kirīṭī paravīraghātīhatāśvam ālokya narapravīramb mādrīsutaṃ nakulaṃ lokamadhyeb samīkṣya kṛṣṇaṃ bhṛśavikṣataṃ cac tam abhyadhāvad vṛṣasenam āhavesa sūtajasya pramukhe sthitaṃ tadāa tam āpatantaṃ naravīram ugraṃmahāhave bāṇasahasradhāriṇamb tam āpatantaṃ tarasograrūpaṃb kurūttamaṃ bāṇasahasradhāramc abhyāpatat karṇasuto mahārathoyathaiva cendraṃ namuciḥ purātaned tau tatra śūrau rathakuñjarau raṇed parasparasyābhimukhau mahārathaud sasarjatuḥ śarasaṃghān anekānd saṃbhrāntarūpau subhṛśaṃ tadānīma tato dbhutenaikaśatena pārthaṃśarair viddhvā sūtaputrasya putraḥc nanāda nādaṃ sumahānubhāvoviddhveva śakraṃ namuciḥ purā vaia punaḥ sa pārthaṃ vṛṣasena ugrairbāṇair avidhyad bhujamūlamadhyec tathaiva kṛṣṇaṃ navabhiḥ samārdayatpunaś ca pārthaṃ daśabhiḥ śitāgraiḥd pūrvaṃ tathā vṛṣasenena viddhod mahājavaiḥ śvetahayaḥ śarais taiḥd saṃrambham īṣad gamito vadhāyad karṇātmajasyātha manaḥ pradadhrea tataḥ kirīṭī raṇamūrdhni kopātkṛtvā triśākhāṃ bhrukuṭiṃ lalāṭeb mumoca tūrṇaṃ viśikhān mahātmāb vadhe dhṛtaḥ karṇasutasya saṃkhyeb āraktanetro ntakaśatruhantāb uvāca karṇaṃ bhṛśam utsmayaṃs tadāb duryodhanaṃ drauṇimukhāṃś ca sarvānb ahaṃ raṇe vṛṣasenaṃ tam ugramb saṃpaśyataḥ karṇa tavādya saṃkhyeb nayāmi lokaṃ niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥb yamasya yāvad dhi janā vadantib bhavadbhiḥ sarvair mama sūnur hato saub eko ratho madvihīnas tarasvīb ahaṃ haniṣye bhavatāṃ samakṣamb saṃrakṣyatāṃ rathasaṃsthāḥ suto yamb ahaṃ haniṣye vṛṣasenam enamb paścād vadhiṣye tvām api saṃpramūḍhamb ahaṃ haniṣye rjuna ājimadhyeb tam adya mūlaṃ kalahasya saṃkhyeb duryodhanāpāśrayajātadarpamb tvām adya hantāsmi raṇe prasahyab asyaiva hantā yudhi bhīmasenaḥb duryodhanasyādhamapūruṣasyab yasyānayād eṣa mahān kṣayo bhavatb sa evam uktvā vinimṛjya cāpaṃb lakṣyaṃ hi kṛtvā vṛṣasenam ājauc mumoca bāṇān viśikhān mahātmāvadhāya rājan sūtaputrasya saṃkhyea vivyādha cainaṃ daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkairmarmasv asaktaṃ prasabhaṃ kirīṭīc ciccheda cāsyeṣvasanaṃ bhujau cakṣuraiś caturbhiḥ śira eva cograiḥa sa pārthabāṇābhihataḥ papātarathād vibāhur viśirā dharāyāmc supuṣpitaḥ parṇadharo tikāyovāteritaḥ śāla ivādriśṛṅgāta taṃ prekṣya bāṇābhihataṃ patantaṃrathāt sutaṃ sūtajaḥ kṣiprakārīc rathaṃ rathenāśu jagāma vegātkirīṭinaḥ putravadhābhitaptaḥd saṃjayaḥd tam āyāntam abhiprekṣya velodvṛttam ivārṇavamd garjantaṃ sumahākāyaṃ durnivāraṃ surair apid arjunaṃ prāha dāśārhaḥ prahasya puruṣarṣabhaḥd ayaṃ sa ratha āyāti śvetāśvaḥ śalyasārathiḥd yena te saha yoddhavyaṃ sthiro bhava dhanaṃjayad paśya cainaṃ samāyuktaṃ rathaṃ karṇasya pāṇḍavad śvetavājisamāyuktaṃ yuktaṃ rādhāsutena cad nānāpatākākalilaṃ kiṅkiṇījālamālinamd uhyamānam ivākāśe vimānaṃ pāṇḍurair hayaiḥd dhvajaṃ ca paśya karṇasya nāgakakṣaṃ mahātmanaḥd ākhaṇḍaladhanuḥprakhyam ullikhantam ivāmbaramd paśya karṇaṃ samāyāntaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrapriyaiṣiṇamd śaradhārā vimuñcantaṃ dhārāsāram ivāmbudamd eṣa madreśvaro rājā rathāgre paryavasthitaḥd niyacchati hayān asya rādheyasyāmitaujasaḥd śṛṇu dundubhinirghoṣaṃ śaṅkhaśabdaṃ ca dāruṇamd siṃhanādāṃś ca vividhāñ śṛṇu pāṇḍava sarvaśaḥd antardhāya mahāśabdān karṇenāmitatejasād dodhūyamānasya bhṛśaṃ dhanuṣaḥ śṛṇu nisvanamd ete dīryanti sagaṇāḥ pāñcālānāṃ mahārathāḥd dṛṣṭvā kesariṇaṃ kruddhaṃ mṛgā iva mahāvaned sarvayatnena kaunteya hantum arhasi sūtajamd na hi karṇaśarān anyaḥ soḍhum utsahate naghad sadevāsuragandharvāṃs trīṃl lokān sacarācarānd tvaṃ hi jetuṃ raṇe śaktas tathaiva viditaṃ mamad bhīmam ugraṃ mahādevaṃ tryakṣaṃ śarvaṃ kapardinamd na śaktā draṣṭum īśānaṃ kiṃ punar yodhituṃ prabhumd tvayā sākṣān mahādevaḥ sarvabhūtaśivaḥ śivaḥd yuddhenārādhitaḥ sthāṇur devāś ca varadās tavad tasya pārtha prasādena devadevasya śūlinaḥd jahi karṇaṃ mahābāho namuciṃ vṛtrahā yathād arjuna uvācad śreyas te stu sadā pārtha yuddhe jayam avāpnuhid dhruva eva jayaḥ kṛṣṇa mama nāsty atra saṃśayaḥd sarvalokagurur yas tvaṃ tuṣṭo si madhusūdanad codayāśvān hṛṣīkeśa rathaṃ mama mahārathad nāhatvā samare śatruṃ nivartiṣyati phalgunaḥd adya karṇaṃ hataṃ paśya maccharaiḥ śakalīkṛtamd māṃ vā drakṣyasi govinda karṇena nihataṃ śaraiḥd upasthitam idaṃ ghoraṃ yuddhaṃ trailokyamohanamd yaj janāḥ kathayiṣyanti yāvad bhūmir dhariṣyatid evaṃ bruvaṃs tadā pārthaḥ kṛṣṇam akliṣṭakāriṇamd pratyudyayau rathenāśu gajaṃ pratigajo yathād punaś cāha mahātejāḥ pārthaḥ kṛṣṇam ariṃdamamd codayāśvān hṛṣīkeśa kālo yam ativartated evam uktas tadā tena pāṇḍavena mahātmanād jayena saṃpūjya sa pāṇḍavaṃ tadād pracodayām āsa hayān manojavānd sa pāṇḍuputrasya ratho manojavaḥd kṣaṇena karṇasya rathāgrato bhavatd tataḥ samakṣaṃ svasutaṃ vilokyad karṇo hataṃ śvetahayena saṃkhyed saṃrambham āgamya paraṃ mahātmād kṛṣṇārjunau sahasaivābhyadhāvatd śiraḥ karau caiva dhanuś ca pārthad ekeṣuṇā vṛṣasenasya saṃkhyed ciccheda pārtho hy aṅgarājasya sainyaṃd kopāgninā caturaṅgaṃ dadāha saṃjaya uvācaa vṛṣasenaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā śokāmarṣasamanvitaḥc muktvā śokodbhavaṃ vāri netrābhyāṃ sahasā vṛṣaḥa rathena karṇas tejasvī jagāmābhimukho ripūnc yuddhāyāmarṣatāmrākṣaḥ samāhūya dhanaṃjayama tau rathau sūryasaṃkāśau vaiyāghraparivāraṇauc sametau dadṛśus tatra dvāv ivārkau samāgataua śvetāśvau puruṣādityāv āsthitāv arimardanaub rathau caturbhir jaladair bhagamitrāv ivāmbarec śuśubhāte mahātmānau candrādityau yathā divia tau dṛṣṭvā vismayaṃ jagmuḥ sarvabhūtāni māriṣac trailokyavijaye yattāv indravairocanāv ivaa rathajyātalanirhrādair bāṇaśaṅkharavair apic tau rathāv abhidhāvantau samālokya mahīkṣitāma dhvajau ca dṛṣṭvā saṃsaktau vismayaḥ samapadyatac hastikakṣyāṃ ca karṇasya vānaraṃ ca kirīṭinaḥa tau rathau saṃprasaktau ca dṛṣṭvā bhārata pārthivāḥc siṃhanādaravāṃś cakruḥ sādhuvādāṃś ca puṣkalāna śrutvā tu dvairathaṃ tābhyāṃ tatra yodhāḥ samantataḥc cakrur bāhuvalaṃ caiva tathā celavalaṃ mahata ājagmuḥ kuravas tatra vāditrānugatās tadāc karṇaṃ praharṣayantaś ca śaṅkhān dadhmuś ca puṣkalānd rādheyam abhito dadhmuḥ śaṅkhāñ śatasahasraśaḥa tathaiva pāṇḍavāḥ sarve harṣayanto dhanaṃjayamc tūryaśaṅkhaninādena diśaḥ sarvā vyanādayana kṣveḍitāsphoṭitotkruṣṭais tumulaṃ sarvato bhavatc bāhughoṣāś ca vīrāṇāṃ karṇārjunasamāgamea tau dṛṣṭvā puruṣavyāghrau rathasthau rathināṃ varauc pragṛhītamahācāpau śaraśaktigadāyudhaua varmiṇau baddhanistriṃśau śvetāśvau śaṅkhaśobhinaub kṛṣṇaśalyarathopetau tulyarūpau mahārathaub siṃhaskandhau siṃhabhujau raktākṣau hemamālinaub cāpavidyuddhvajopetau pratisaṃrabdhāv anyonyasya jayaiṣiṇaua tāv ubhau prajihīrṣetām indravṛtrāv ivābhitaḥc bhīmarūpadharāv āstāṃ mahādhūmāv iva grahaua tato ntarikṣe sākṣepā vivādā bharatarṣabhac mitho bhedāś ca bhūtānām āsan karṇārjunāntaree vyāśrayanta diśo bhinnāḥ sarvalokāś ca māriṣaa devadānavagandharvāḥ piśācoragarākṣasāḥc pratipakṣagrahaṃ cakruḥ karṇārjunasamāgamea dyaur āsīt karṇato vyagrā sanakṣatrā viśāṃ samapadyanta khecarāṇi vayāṃsi cac   hṛṣṭarūpāḥ samantataḥc munayaś cāraṇāḥ siddhāḥa ratnāni nidhayaḥ sarve vedāś cākhyānapañcamāḥc sopavedopaniṣadaḥ sarahasyāḥ sasaṃgrahāḥa vāsukiś citrasenaś ca karṇataḥa īhāmṛgā vyāḍamṛgā maṅgalyāś ca mṛgadvijāḥb maṅgaḷyāḥ paśavaś caiva siṃhavyāghrās tathaiva cac pārthasya vijayaṃ rājan sarva evābhisaṃśritāḥa vasavo marutaḥ sādhyā rudrā viśve śvinau tathāb arjunasya jaye cāstām aśvināv api sapriyauc agnir indraś ca somaś ca pavanaś ca diśo daśad karṇataḥ samapadyanta śvasṛgālavayāṃsi cad mṛgāś ca paśavaś caiva siṃhavyāghrās tathaiva cad vasavaś ca mahendreṇa marutaś ca sahāgninād agnignī  rudraś ca somaś ca yamo vaiśravaṇas tadāe dhanaṃjayam upājagmur ādityāḥ karṇato bhavanf viśaḥ śūdrāś ca sūtāś ca varṇasaṃkarajāś ca yef sarvasattveṣu te rājan rādheyam abhajaṃs tadāa devās tu pitṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ sagaṇārjunato bhavanc yamo vaiśravaṇaś caiva varuṇaś ca yato rjunaḥd brahma kṣatraṃ ca yajñāś ca dakṣiṇāś cārjunaṃ śritāḥd asurā yātudhānāś ca kravyādāś ca mṛgāṇḍajāḥd rākṣasāḥ saha yādobhiḥ śvasṛgālāś ca karṇataḥa devabrahmanṛparṣīṇāṃ gaṇāḥ pāṇḍavato bhavanb devarṣibrahmarṣigaṇāḥ sarve ca khacarāś ca yec tumburupramukhā rājan gandharvāś ca yato rjunaḥa prāveyāḥ saha mauneyair gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥb sahāpsarobhiḥ śubhrābhir devadūtāś ca guhyakāḥb kirīṭinaṃ saṃśritāḥ sma puṇyagandhā manoramāḥb amanojñāś ca ye gandhās te sarve karṇam āśritāḥb viparītāny aniṣṭāni bhavanti vinaśiṣyatāmb yāny antakāle puruṣaṃ viparītam upadrutamb praviśanti naraṃ kṣipraṃ mṛtyukāle bhyupāgateb te bhāvāḥ sahitāḥ karṇaṃ praviṣṭāḥ sūtanandanamb ojas tejaś ca siddhiś ca praharṣaḥ satyavikramaub manastuṣṭir jayaś cāpi tathānando nṛpottamab īdṛśāś ca naravyāghra tasmin saṃgrāmasāgareb nimittāni ca śubhrāṇi viviśur jiṣṇum āhaveb ṛṣayo brāhmaṇaiḥ sārdham abhajanta kirīṭinamb tato devagaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ siddhāś ca saha cāraṇaiḥb dvidhā bhūtā mahārāja vyāśrayanta narottamaub vimānāni vicitrāṇi guṇavanti ca sarvataḥb samāruhya samājagmur dvairathaṃ karṇapārthayoḥb didṛkṣavaḥ samājagmuḥ karṇārjunasamāgamamb antarikṣe mahārāja devagandharvarākṣasāḥb evaṃ sarveṣu bhūteṣu dvidhābhūteṣu bhāratab āśaṃsamāneṣu jayaṃ rādheyasyārjunasya cab vimānāyutasaṃbādham ākāśam abhavat tadāc īhāmṛgavyāḍamṛgair dvipāś ca rathapattibhiḥa uhyamānās tathā meghair vāyunā ca manīṣiṇaḥc didṛkṣavaḥ samājagmuḥ karṇārjunasamāgamama devadānavagandharvā nāgā yakṣāḥ patatriṇaḥc maharṣayo vedavidaḥ pitaraś ca svadhābhujaḥa tapo vidyās tathauṣadhyo nānārūpāmbaratviṣaḥc antarikṣe mahārāja vinadanto vatasthirea brahmā brahmarṣibhiḥ sārdhaṃ prajāpatibhir eva cac bhavenāvasthito yānaṃ divyaṃ taṃ deśam abhyayātd sametau tau mahātmānau dṛṣṭvā karṇadhanaṃjayaud arjuno jayatāṃ karṇam iti śakro bravīt svayamd jayatām arjunaṃ karṇa iti sūryo bhyabhāṣatad hatvārjunaṃ mama sutaḥ karṇo jayatu saṃyuged hatvā karṇaṃ jayatv adya mama putro dhanaṃjayaḥd iti sūryasya caivāsīd vivādo vāsavasya cad pakṣasaṃsthitayos tatra tayoḥ puruṣasiṃhayoḥd dvaipakṣam āsīd devānām asurāṇāṃ tathaiva cad sametau tau mahātmānau dṛṣṭvā karṇadhanaṃjayaud akampanta trayo lokāḥ sahadevarṣicāraṇāḥd sarve devagaṇāś caiva sarvabhūtāni yāni cad yataḥ pārthas tato devā yataḥ karṇas tato surāḥd rathayūthapayoḥ pakṣau kurupāṇḍavavīrayoḥd tataḥ prajāpatis tūrṇam ājagāma mahīpated dvairathaṃ yudhi taṃ draṣṭuṃ karṇapāṇḍavayos tadād vijitya karṇaḥ svid imāṃ vasuṃdharāmd athārjunaḥ svit pratipadyate khilāmd itīśvarasyāpi babhūva saṃśayaḥd saṃjayaḥd prajāpateḥ prekṣya tayor mahad balamd prajāpatis tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā devabhāgaṃ samāgatamd abravīt tu tato rājan paśyato vai svayaṃbhuvaḥd ubhāv atirathau śūrāv ubhau dṛḍhaparākramaud ubhau sadṛśakarmāṇau vajricakrāyudhopamaud aho bata mahad yuddhaṃ karṇārjunasamāgamed bhaviṣyati mahāghoraṃ vṛtravāsavayor ivaa dṛṣṭvā prajāpatiṃ devāḥ svayaṃbhuvam upāgamanb ko nayor vijayī deva kurupāṇḍavayodhayoḥc samo stu deva vijaya etayor narasiṃhayoḥa tad upaśrutya maghavā praṇipatya pitāmahamc karṇārjunavināśena mā naśyatv akhilaṃ jagatd svayaṃbho brūhi nas tathyam etayor vijayaṃ prabhoa svayaṃbho brūhi tad vākyaṃ samo stu vijayo nayoḥb vyajñāpayata deveśam idaṃ matimatāṃ varaḥb pūrvaṃ bhagavatā proktaṃ kṛṣṇayor vijayo dhruvaḥb evam uktas tu bhagavāñ jaye tābhyām aniściteb ity abravīn mahārāja mahān brahmā prajāpatiḥb dvāv apy etau hi kṛtinau dvāv apy atibalotkaṭaub bhaviṣyaty anayor yuddhaṃ trailokyasya bhayāvahamb tataḥ prajāpatiṃ tatra sahasrākṣo bhyacodayatc tat tathāstu namas te stu prasīda bhagavan mamaa brahmeśānāv atho vākyam ūcatus tridaśeśvaramc vijayo dhruva evāstu vijayasya mahātmanaḥd khāṇḍave yena hutabhuktoṣitaḥ savyasācinād svargaṃ ca samanuprāpya sāhāyyaṃ śakra te kṛtamd karṇaś ca dānavaḥ pakṣa ataḥ kāryaḥ parājayaḥd evaṃ kṛte bhavet kāryaṃ devānām eva niścitamd ātmakāryaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ garīyas tridaśeśvarad mahātmā phalgunaś cāpi satyadharmarataḥ sadād vijayas tasya niyataṃ jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥd toṣito bhagavān yena mahātmā vṛṣabhadhvajaḥd kathaṃ vā tasya na jayo jāyate śatalocanad yasya cakre svayaṃ viṣṇuḥ sārathyaṃ jagataḥ prabhuḥa manasvī balavāñ śūraḥ kṛtāstraś ca tapodhanaḥc bibharti ca mahātejā dhanurvedam aśeṣataḥd pārthaḥ sarvaguṇopeto devakāryam idaṃ yataḥd kliśyante karṇakirīṭinoḥd tasmād āśāṃ gataḥ śakras tūṣṇīṃbhūte pitāmahed vijayaṃ pāṇḍaveyasya vadhaṃ karṇasya cāhavea ity ukto devadevābhyāṃ sahasrākṣo bravīd vacaḥc āmantrya sarvabhūtāni brahmeśānānuśāsanāta śrutaṃ bhavadbhir yat proktaṃ bhagavadbhyāṃ jagaddhitamc tat tathā nānyathā tad dhi tiṣṭhadhvaṃ gatamanyavaḥa iti śrutvendravacanaṃ sarvabhūtāni māriṣac vismitāny abhavan rājan pūjayāṃ cakrire ca tatd ubhayor uttame yuddhe dvairathe dyūta āhṛtec prakurvāte dhvajau yuddhaṃ pratyaheṣan hayān hayāḥd hayā hayān abhyaheṣan spardhamānāḥ parasparama avidhyat puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ śalyaṃ nayanasāyakaiḥc sa cāpi puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ tathaivābhisamaikṣataa tatrājayad vāsudevaḥ śalyaṃ nayanasāyakaiḥc karṇaṃ cāpy ajayad dṛṣṭyā kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥa athābravīt sūtaputraḥ śalyam ābhāṣya sasmitamb uvāca praṇayād rājan sāmapūrvam idaṃ vacaḥc yadi pārtho raṇe hanyād adya mām iha karhi cite kim uttaraṃ tadā te syāt sakhe satyaṃ bravīhi me śalya uvāca hate tvayi hy ahaṃ hanyām ubhau kṛṣṇadhanaṃjayaua yadi karṇa raṇe hanyād adya tvāṃ śvetavāhanaḥc ubhāv ekarathenāhaṃ hanyāṃ mādhavapāṇḍavau saṃjaya uvācaa evam eva tu goviṃdam arjunaḥ pratyabhāṣatac taṃ prahasyābravīt kṛṣṇaḥ pārthaṃ param idaṃ vacaḥa pated divākaraḥ sthānāc chīryetānekadhā kṣitiḥc śaityam agnir iyān na tvā karṇo hanyād dhanaṃjayama yadi tv evaṃ kathaṃ cit syāl lokaparyasanaṃ yathāc hanyāṃ karṇaṃ tathā śalyaṃ bāhubhyām eva saṃyugea iti kṛṣṇavacaḥ śrutvā prahasan kapiketanaḥc arjunaḥ pratyuvācedaṃ kṛṣṇam akliṣṭakāriṇame mamāpy etāv aparyāptau karṇaśalyau janārdanaa sapatākādhvajaṃ karṇaṃ saśalyarathavājinamc sacchatrakavacaṃ caiva diṣṭyā jayasi vārṣṇeya iti karṇe nipātitec adyābhimanyujananīm anṛṇaḥ sāntvayiṣyasie kuntīṃ pitṛṣvasāraṃ ca saṃprahṛṣṭo janārdanaa adya bāṣpamukhīṃ kṛṣṇāṃ sāntvayiṣyasi mādhavac vāgbhiś śūratamo loke sādhuvṛttaś ca pāṇḍavaf abhijño yuddhadharmāṇāṃ tasmāt kṣama mama kṣaṇamf divyāstravid ameyātmā kārtavīryasamo yudhia yāvac cakram idaṃ bhūmer uddharāmi dhanaṃjayac na māṃ rathastho muhūrtaṃ kṣama pāṇḍavad yāvat karomi dhanuṣaṃ sajjaṃ matimatāṃ vara saṃjaya uvācaa athābravīd vāsudevo rathasthorādheya diṣṭyā smarasīha dharmamb dharme hi gṛddhāḥ satataṃ hi pārthāsb tebhyas tato vṛddhim asau dadātib dharmād apetāḥ paribaddhalobhāsb tasmād gatā vai kuravo vināśamc prāyeṇa nīcā vyasaneṣu magnānindanti daivaṃ kukṛtaṃ na tat tata yad draupadīm ekavastrāṃ sabhāyāmānāyya tvaṃ caiva suyodhanaś cac duḥśāsanaḥ śakuniḥ saubalaś cana te karṇa pratyabhāt tatra dharmaḥa yadā sabhāyāṃ kaunteyam anakṣajñaṃ yudhiṣṭhiramb kaitavāt sauvalo jaiṣīd dayāluṃ sarvajantuṣuc akṣajñaḥ śakunir jetā tadā dharmaḥ kva te gataḥd yad bhīmasenaṃ sarpaiś ca viṣayuktaiś ca bhojanaiḥd ācarat tvanmate rājā kva te dharmas tadā gataḥd yad vāraṇāvate pārthān suptāñ jatugṛhe tadād ādīpayas tvaṃ rādheya kva te dharmas tadā gataḥd vanavāse vyatīte ca karṇa varṣe trayodaśed na prayacchasi yad rājyaṃ kva te dharmas tadā gataḥa yadā rajasvalāṃ kṛṣṇāṃ duḥśāsanavaśe sthitāmc sabhāyāṃ prāhasaḥ karṇa kva te dharmas tadā gataḥd yad anāryaiḥ purā kṛṣṇāṃ kliśyamānām anāgasamd vinaṣṭāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kṛṣṇe śāśvataṃ narakaṃ gatāḥd patim anyaṃ vṛṇīṣveti vadaṃs tvaṃ gajagāminīmd upaprekṣasi rādheya kva te dharmas tadā gataḥa rājyalubdhaḥ punaḥ karṇa samāhvayasi pāṇḍavamc gāndhārarājam āśritya kva te dharmas tadā gataḥd yadābhimanyuṃ bahavo yuddhe jaghnur mahārathāḥd parivārya raṇe bālaṃ kva te dharmas tadā gataḥd yady eṣa dharmas tatra na vidyate hid kiṃ sarvathā tāluviśoṣaṇenad adyaiva dharmāṇi vidhatsva sūtad tathāpi naivādya vimokṣyase tvamd nalo hy akṣair nirjitaḥ puṣkareṇad punar yathā rājyam avāpa vīryātd prāptās tathā pāṇḍavā bāhuvīryātd sarve samastāḥ parivṛttalobhāḥd nihatya śatrūn samare pravṛddhānd sasomakā rājyam avāpnuyus ted tathā gatā dhārtarāṣṭrā vināśaṃd dharmābhiguptaiḥ satataṃ nṛsiṃhaiḥd saṃjaya uvācad evam uktas tadā karṇo vāsudevena bhāratad lajjayāvanato bhūtvā nottaraṃ kiṃ cid uktavānd krodhāt prasphuramāṇauṣṭho dhanur udyamya bhāratad yodhayām āsa vai pārthaṃ mahāvegaparākramaḥd tato bravīd vāsudevaḥ phalgunaṃ puruṣarṣabhamd divyāstreṇaiva nirbhidya pātayasva mahābalaa evam ukte tu rādheye vāsudevena pāṇḍavamc manyur abhyāviśat tīvraḥ smṛtvā tat tad dhanaṃjayama tasya krodhena sarvebhyaḥ srotobhyas tejaso rciṣaḥc prādurāsan mahārāja tad adbhutam ivābhavata taṃ samīkṣya tataḥ karṇo brahmāstreṇa dhanaṃjayamc abhyavarṣat punar yatnam akarod rathasarjaned brahmāstreṇaiva taṃ pārtho vavarṣa śaravṛṣṭibhiḥd karṇaś cāpi tato rājan krodharaktāntalocanaḥe tad astram astreṇāvārya prajahārāsya pāṇḍavaḥa tato nyad astraṃ kaunteyo dayitaṃ jātavedasaḥc mumoca karṇam uddiśya tat prajajvāla vai bhṛśama vāruṇena tataḥ karṇaḥ śamayām āsa pāvakamc jīmūtaiś ca diśaḥ sarvāś cakre timiradurdināḥa pāṇḍaveyas tv asaṃbhrānto vāyavyāstreṇa vīryavānc apovāha tadābhrāṇi rādheyasya prapaśyataḥd tatrādbhutaṃ bhārata sūtaputraśd cakre cakre bhūmim anupraviṣṭed yad yodhayat pāṇḍavam ugravegaṃd vivyādha cainaṃ daśabhiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥd tato tividdho bharatapravīraḥd karṇena rājan samare vighūrṇamānaḥ ślathahastagāṇḍivaḥd cacāla bībhatsur amitramardanaḥd kṣiteḥ prakampe ca yathācalottamaḥd tadantaraṃ prāpya vṛṣo mahārathod rathāṅgam urvīgatam ujjihīrṣuḥd rathād avaplutya nigṛhya dorbhyāṃd śaśāka daivān na mahābalo pid tataḥ kirīṭī pratilabhya saṃjñāṃd jagrāha bāṇaṃ yamadaṇḍakalpamd dīpto rjunaḥ prāñjalikaṃ mahātmād tato bravīd vāsudevo pi pārthamd chindhy asya mūrdhānam areḥ śareṇad na yāvad ārohati vai rathaṃ vṛṣaḥd tathaiva saṃpūjya sa tad vacaḥ prabhosd tataḥ kṣuraṃ prajvalitaṃ pragṛhyad jaghāna kakṣām amalārkavarṇāṃd mahārathe rathacakre vimagnea taṃ bhārata diṣṭam etatparyāyasiddhir na sadāsti siddhiḥa etad vaco madrapater niśamyasvaṃ cāpanītaṃ manasā nirīkṣyac duryodhano dīnamanā visaṃjñaḥpunaḥ punar nyaśvasad ārtarūpaḥd saṃjaya uvācad dṛṣṭvā tu sainyaṃ vinivartyamānaṃd putreṇa te madrapatis tadānīmd saṃtrastarūpaḥ parimūḍhacetād duryodhanaṃ vākyam idaṃ babhāṣed dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācad tasmiṃs tu karṇārjunayor vimarded dagdhasya raudre hani vidrutasyad babhūva rūpaṃ kurusṛñjayānāṃd saṃjaya uvācad balasya bāṇonmathitasya kīdṛkd śṛṇu rājann avahito yathā vṛtto mahākṣayaḥd ghoro manuṣyadehānām ājau naravarakṣayaḥd yatra karṇe hate pārthaḥ siṃhanādam athākarotd tadā tava sutān rājann āviveśa mahad bhayamd na saṃdhātum anīkāni na caivātha parākramed āsīd buddhir hate karṇe tava yodhasya kasya citd vaṇijo nāvi bhinnāyām agādhe hy aplavā yathād apāre pāram icchanto hate dvīpe kirīṭinād sūtaputre hate rājan vitrastāḥ śaravikṣatāḥd anāthā nātham icchanto mṛgāḥ siṃhair ivārditāḥd bhagnaśṛṅgā iva vṛṣā bhagnadaṣṭrā ivoragāḥd pratyapāyāma sāyāhne nirjitāḥ savyasācinād hatapravīrā vidhvastā nikṛttā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥd sūtaputre hate rājan putrās te vyadravan bhayātd viśastrakavacāḥ sarve kāṃdiśīkā vicetasaḥd anyonyam avamṛdnanto vīkṣyamāṇā bhayārditāḥd mām eva tūrṇaṃ bībhatsur mām eva ca vṛkodaraḥd abhiyātīti manvānāḥ petur mamluś ca saṃbhramātd hayān anye rathān anye gajān anye mahārathāḥd āhatya javasaṃpannāḥ pādātāḥ prādravan bhayātd kuñjaraiḥ syandanāḥ kṣuṇṇāḥ sādinaś ca mahārathaiḥd padātisaṃghāś cāśvaughaiḥ palāyadbhir bhayārditāḥd vyālataskarasaṃkīrṇe sārthahīnā yathā vaned tathā tvadīyā nihate sūtaputre tadābhavand hatārohās tathā nāgāś chinnahastās tathā narāḥd sarvaṃ pārthamayaṃ lokaṃ saṃpaśyanto bhayāturāḥd tān prekṣya dravataḥ sarvān bhīmasenabhayārditānd duryodhano tha svaṃ sūtaṃ vāhety uktvedam abravītd nātikramiṣyate pārtho dhanuṣpāṇir vyavasthitaḥd jaghanya eva sainyānāṃ śanair aśvān acodayatd jaghanye yudhyamānaṃ hi kaunteyo māṃ na saṃśayaḥd notsaheta vyatikrāntuṃ velām iva mahodadhiḥd adyārjunaṃ sagovindaṃ māninaṃ ca vṛkodaramd nihatya śiṣṭāñ śatrūṃś ca karṇasyānṛṇyam āpnuyāmd tac chrutvā kururājasya śūrārthasadṛśaṃ vacaḥd sūto hemaparicchannāñ śanair aśvān acodayatd rathāśvagajahīnās tu pādātās tava māriṣad pañcaviṃśatisāhasrā yuddhāyaiva vyavasthitāḥd tān bhīmasenaḥ saṃkruddho dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥd balena caturaṅgeṇa parikṣipya nijaghnatuḥd pratyayudhyanta te sarve bhīmasenaṃ sapārṣatamd pārthapārṣatayoś cānye jagṛhus tatra nāmanīd akrudhyata tadā bhīmas tai raṇe pratyupasthitaiḥd so vatīrya rathāt tūrṇaṃ gadāpāṇir ayudhyatad na tān rathastho bhūmiṣṭhān dharmāpekṣī vṛkodaraḥd yodhayām āsa kaunteyo bhujavīryam upāśritaḥd jātarūpaparicchannāṃ pragṛhya mahatīṃ gadāmd avadhīt tāvakān sarvān daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥd padātino pi saṃrabdhās tyaktvā jīvitam ātmanaḥd bhīmam abhyadravan saṃkhye pataṃgā iva pāvakamd āsādya bhīmasenaṃ tu saṃrabdhā yuddhadurmadāḥd vineśuḥ sahasā dṛṣṭvā bhūtagrāmā ivāntakamd śyenavad vyacarad bhīmo gadāhasto mahābalaḥd pañcaviṃśatisāhasrāṃs tāvakānām apothayatd hatvā tat puruṣānīkaṃ bhīmaḥ satyaparākramaḥd dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ puraskṛtya punas tasthau mahābalaḥd dhṛṣṭadyumno pi ca mahān amitragaṇamardanaḥd putraḥ pāñcālarājasya dhanurdharavaro yudhid vipralīnān rathāśvena padātīyān samantataḥd pañcaviṃśatisāhasrān avadhīn niśitaiḥ śaraiḥd śarair nikṛttāḥ samare dhṛṣṭadyumnena tāvakāḥd pañcaviṃśatisāhasrāḥ kālam ārchan padātayaḥd hatvā tat puruṣānīkaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumno mahābalaḥd bhīmasenaṃ puraskṛtya na cirāt pratyadṛśyatad taṃ pārāvatavarṇāśvaṃ kruddhaṃ kruddhāntakopamamd dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ raṇe dṛṣṭvā tvadīyāḥ prādravan bhayātd dhanaṃjayo rathānīkam abhyavartata vīryavānd mādrīputrau tu śakuniṃ sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥd javenābhyapatan hṛṣṭā nighnantaḥ saubalaṃ balamd tasyāśvavārān subahūn vinihatya śitaiḥ śaraiḥd tam abhyadhāvaṃs tvaritās tato yuddham abhūt tadād dhanaṃjayo pi cābhyetya rathānīkaṃ tava prabhod viśrutaṃ triṣu lokeṣu vyākṣipad gāṇḍivaṃ dhanuḥd kṛṣṇasārathim āyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā śvetahayaṃ rathamd arjunaṃ cāpi yoddhāraṃ tvadīyāḥ prādravan bhayātd viprahīnā rathāśvena gajaiś ca parivarjitāḥd pañcaviṃśatisāhasrāḥ kālam ārchan padātayaḥd hatvā tat puruṣānīkaṃ pāñcālānāṃ mahārathaḥd putraḥ pāñcālarājasya dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārathaḥd bhīmasenaṃ puraskṛtya na cirāt pratyadṛśyatad mahādhanurdharaḥ śrīmān amitragaṇasūdanaḥd pārāvatasavarṇāśvaṃ kovidāramahādhvajamd dhṛṣṭadyumnarathaṃ dṛṣṭvā prādravanta bhayād bhṛśamd gāndhārarājaṃ śīghrāstram anusṛtya yaśasvinaud na cirāt pratyadṛśyetāṃ mādrīputrau sasātyakīd cekitānaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca draupadeyāś ca māriṣad hatvā tvadīyaṃ sumahat sainyaṃ śaṅkhān athādhamand te sarve tāvakān prekṣya dravamāṇān parāṅmukhānd abhyadravañ jighāṃsanto vṛṣāñ jitvā yathā vṛṣāḥd senāvaśeṣaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā tava sainyaṃ parāṅmukhamd vyavasthitaṃ savyasācī cukrodha balavat tadād dhanaṃjayo rathānīkam abhyavartata vīryavānd viśrutaṃ triṣu lokeṣu vyākṣipad gāṇḍivaṃ dhanuḥd tata etāñ śarai rājan sahasrān samavārayand rajasā coddhatenātha na sma kiṃ cid vyadṛśyatad anyakārīkṛte loke śarabhūte mahītaled diśaḥ sarvā mahārāja tāvakāḥ prādravan bhayātd bhajyamāneṣu sainyeṣu kururājo viśāṃ pated parān abhimukhāṃś caiva sutas te samupādravatd tato duryodhanaḥ sarvān ājuhāvātha pāṇḍavānd yuddhāya bharataśreṣṭha devān iva purā baliḥd ta enam abhivartanta sahitāḥ samupādravand nānāśastrasṛjaḥ sarve bhartsayanto muhur muhuḥd duryodhano py asaṃbhrāntas tān arīn niśitaiḥ śaraiḥd vyadhamad yudhi rājendra ghorarūpo viśāṃ pated tatrādbhutam apaśyāma tava putrasya pauruṣamd yad enaṃ pāṇḍavāḥ sarve na śekur ativartitumd nātidūrāpayātaṃ tu kṛtabuddhiṃ palāyaned duryodhanaḥ svakaṃ sainyam apaśyac charavikṣatamd tato vasthāpya rājendra kṛtabuddhis tavātmajaḥd harṣayann iva tān yodhān idaṃ vacanam abravītd na taṃ deśaṃ prapaśyāmi pṛthivyāṃ parvateṣu cad yatra yātān na vo hanyuḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kiṃ sṛtena vaḥd alpaṃ ca balam eteṣāṃ kṛṣṇau ca bhṛśavikṣataud yadi sarve tra tiṣṭhāmo dhruvo no vijayo bhavetd viprayātāṃś ca no bhinnān pāṇḍavāḥ kṛtakilbiṣāḥd anusṛtya vadhiṣyanti śreyān naḥ samare vadhaḥd sukhaṃ sāṃgrāmiko mṛtyuḥ kṣatradharmeṇa yudhyatāmd mṛto duḥkhaṃ na jānīte pretya cānantyam aśnuted śṛṇudhvaṃ kṣatriyāḥ sarve yāvantaḥ stha samāgatāḥd yadā śūraṃ ca bhīruṃ ca mārayaty antako yamaḥd ko nu mūḍho na yudhyeta mādṛśaḥ kṣatriyavrataḥd dviṣato bhīmasenasya kruddhasya vaśam eṣyathad pitāmahair ācaritaṃ na dharmaṃ hātum arhathad na hi dharmo sti pāpīyān kṣatriyasya palāyanātd na yuddhadharmāc chreyo nyaḥ panthāḥ svargasya kauravāḥd acireṇa hatā lokaṃ sarve yodhāḥ samāpnutad evaṃ bruvati te putre sainikā bhṛśavikṣatāḥd anavekṣyaiva tad vākyaṃ prādravan sarvatomukhama taṃ dhyānamūkaṃ kṛpaṇaṃ bhṛśārtamārtāyanir dīnam uvāca vākyamc paśyedam ugraṃ naravājināgairāyodhanaṃ vīrahataiḥ prapannama mahīdharābhaiḥ patitair mahāgajaiḥsakṛt praviddhaiḥ gajavājiyodhairmandāsubhiś caiva gatāsubhiś caa balāpaviddhai rathavīrasaṃghaiḥc narāśvanāgaiś ca rathaiś ca marditairmahī mahāvaitaraṇīva durdṛśāa gajair nikṛttāparahastagātrairudvepamānaiḥ patitaiḥ pṛthivyāmb viśīrṇadantaiḥ kṣatajaṃ vamadbhiḥb sphuradbhir ārtaiḥ karuṇaṃ raṇājireb suyodhavarmāyudhapādagoptṛbhiḥb prakīrṇatūṇīrapatākaketubhiḥb suvarṇajālāvatatair bhṛśāhatairb mahī viyad dyaur samare tadvat pārthameghena śāmitaḥb pragṛhya ca yaśo dīptaṃ suyuddhenātmano bhuvib visṛjya śaravarṣāṇi pratāpya ca diśo daśac saputraḥ puruṣavyāghraḥ saṃśāntaḥ pārthatejasāe pratāpya pāṇḍavān rājan pāñcālāṃś cāstratejasāa dadānīty eva yo vocan na nāstīty arthito rthibhiḥc sadbhiḥ sadā satpuruṣaḥ sa hato dvairathe vṛṣaḥa yasya brāhmaṇasāt sarvam ātmārthaṃ na mahātmanaḥc nādeyaṃ brāhmaṇeṣv āsīd sughoṣaumanāṃsy arīṇām avasādayantaua suvarṇajālāvatatau mahāsvanauhimāvadātau parigṛhya pāṇibhiḥc cucumbatuḥ śaṅkhavarau nṛṇāṃ varauvarānanābhyāṃ yugapac ca dadhmatuḥa pāñcajanyasya nirghoṣo devadattasya cobhayoḥc pṛthivīm antarikṣaṃ ca dyām apaś cāpy apūrayatd vitrastāś cābhavan sarve kuravo rājasattamad śaṅkhaśabdena śūrasya mādhavasyārjunasya caa tau śaṅkhaśabdena ninādayantauvanāni śailān sarito diśaś cac vitrāsayantau tava putrasenāṃyudhiṣṭhiraṃ nandayataḥ sma vīraua tataḥ prayātāḥ kuravo javenaśrutvaiva śaṅkhasvanam īryamāṇamc vihāya madrādhipatiṃ patiṃ caduryodhanaṃ bhārata bhāratānāma mahāhave taṃ bahu śobhamānaṃdhanaṃjayaṃ bhūtagaṇāḥ sametāḥc tadānvamodanta janārdanaṃ caprabhākarāv abhyuditau yathaivaa samācitau karṇaśaraiḥ paraṃtapāvubhau vyabhātāṃ samare cyutārjunauc tamo nihatyābhyuditau yathāmalauśaśāṅkasūryāv iva raśmimālinaua vihāya tān bāṇagaṇān athāgatausuhṛdvṛtāv apratimānavikramauc sukhaṃ praviṣṭau śibiraṃ svam īśvarausadasyahūtāv iva vāsavācyutaua sadevagandharvamanuṣyacāraṇairmaharṣibhir yakṣamahoragair apic jayābhivṛddhyā parayābhipūjitaunihatya karṇaṃ paramāhave tadād saṃjaya uvācad hate vaikartane karṇe kuravo bhayapīḍitāḥd vīkṣamāṇā diśaḥ sarvāḥ palāyante sma sarvataḥd vīraṃ tu nihataṃ śrutvā śatrubhiḥ paramāhaved sarve diśo nvakīryanta tāvakā bhayamohitāḥd tato vahāraṃ cakrus te rājan yodhāḥ samantataḥd vāryamāṇā bhayodvignās tava putreṇa bhāratad teṣāṃ tu matam ājñāya putras te bharatarṣabhad avahāraṃ tataś cakre śalyasyānumate nṛpad yodhair mahārathaiḥ sārdhaṃ vṛto bhārata tāvakaiḥd hatāvaśeṣais tvaritaḥ śibirāyaiva dudruved gāndhārāṇāṃ sahasreṇa śakuniḥ parivāritaḥd hatam ādhirathiṃ dṛṣṭvā śibirāyaiva dudruved kṛpaḥ śāradvato rājan nāgānīkena saṃvṛtaḥd mahatā meghakalpena śibirāyaiva dudruved aśvatthāmā tataḥ śūro viniḥśvasya muhur muhuḥd pāṇḍavānāṃ jayaṃ dṛṣṭvā śibirāyaiva dudruved saṃśaptakāvaśeṣeṇa balena mahatā vṛtaḥd suśarmāpi yayau rājan vīkṣamāṇo bhayāturānd duryodhano pi nṛpatir hatasarvasva āturaḥd yayau śokasamāviṣṭaś cintayan vimanā bahud chinnadhvajena śalyas tu rathena rathināṃ varaḥd prayayau śibirāyaiva vīkṣamāṇo diśo daśad tato pare subahavo bhāratānāṃ mahārathāḥd prādravanta raṇaṃ hitvā bhayāviṣṭā vicetasaḥd aśrukaṇṭhā bhayodvignā vepamānāḥ suvihvalāḥd kuravaḥ pradrutāḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā karṇaṃ nipātitamd praśaṃsanto rjunaṃ ke cit ke cit karṇaṃ mahārathāḥd vyadravanta diśo bhītāḥ kuravaḥ kurusattamad teṣāṃ yodhasahasrāṇāṃ tāvakānāṃ mahāmṛdhed nāsīt tatra pumān kaś cid yo yuddhāya mano dadhed hate karṇe mahārāja nirāśāḥ kuravo bhavand jīviteṣv atha rājyeṣu dāreṣu ca dhaneṣu cad tān samānīya putras te yatnena mahatā vibhod niveśāya mano dadhre duḥkhaśokasamanvitaḥd tasyājñāṃ śirasā te pi pratigṛhya viśāṃ pated vivarṇavadanā dīnā nyaviśanta mahārathāḥd yathānurūpaṃ pratipūjya tān athad praśasyamānāv atulaiś ca karmabhiḥd nanandatus tau sasuhṛdgaṇau tadād baliṃ niyamyeva sureśakeśavau saṃjaya uvācaa tathā nipātite karṇe tava sainye ca vidrutec āśliṣya pārthaṃ dāśārho harṣād vacanam abravīta hato balabhidā vṛtras tvayā karṇo dhanaṃjayac vadhaṃ vai karṇavṛtrābhyāṃ kathayiṣyanti mānavāḥa vajriṇā nihato vṛtraḥ saṃyuge bhūritejasāc tvayā tu nihataḥ karṇo dhanuṣā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa tam imaṃ vikramaṃ loke prathitaṃ te yaśovahamc nivedayāvaḥ kaunteya dharmarājāya dhīmatea vadhaṃ karṇasya saṃgrāme dīrghakālacikīrṣitamc nivedya dharmarājasya tvam ānṛṇyaṃ gamiṣyasid vartamāne tu yuddhe vai tava karṇasya cobhayoḥd draṣṭum āyodhanaṃ pūrvam āgato dharmanandanaḥd subhṛśaṃ gāḍhaviddhatvān nāśakat sthātum āhaved tataḥ svaśibiraṃ yātaḥ sa rājā puruṣarṣabhaa tathety ukte keśavas tu pārthena yadupuṅgavaḥc paryavartayad avyagro rathaṃ rathavarasya tamd evam uktvārjunaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ sainikān idam abravīta dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ yudhāmanyuṃ mādrīputrau vṛkodaramc yuyudhānaṃ ca govinda idaṃ vacanam abravīta parān abhimukhā yattās tiṣṭhadhvaṃ bhadram astu vaḥc yāvad āvedyate rājñe hataḥ karṇo rjunena vaid tāvad bhavadbhir yat tais tu bhavitavyaṃ narādhipaiḥa sa taiḥ śūrair anujñāto yayau rājaniveśanamc pārtham ādāya govindo dadarśa ca yudhiṣṭhirama śayānaṃ rājaśārdūlaṃ kāñcane śayanottamec agṛhṇītāṃ ca caraṇau muditau pārthivasya taua tayoḥ praharṣam ālakṣya prahārāṃś cātimānuṣānc rādheyaṃ nihataṃ matvā samuttasthau yudhiṣṭhiraḥd utthāya sa mahābāhuḥ punaḥ punar ariṃdamaḥd vāsudevārjunau premṇā punaś ca pariṣasvajed vāsudevaṃ ca vārṣṇeyaṃ papraccha kurunandanaḥa tato smai tad yathāvṛttaṃ vāsudevaḥ priyaṃvadaḥc kathayām āsa karṇasya nidhanaṃ yadunandanaḥa īṣad utsmayamānas tu kṛṣṇo rājānam abravītc yudhiṣṭhiraṃ hatāmitraṃ kṛtāñjalir athācyutaḥa diṣṭyā gāṇḍīvadhanvā ca pāṇḍavaś ca vṛkodaraḥc tvaṃ cāpi kuśalī rājan mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavaua muktā vīrakṣayād asmāt saṃgrāmāl lomaharṣaṇātc kṣipram uttarakālāni kuru kāryāṇi pārthivaa hato vaikartanaḥ krūraḥ sūtaputro mahābalaḥc diṣṭyā jayasi rājendra diṣṭyā vardhasi pāṇḍavaa yaḥ sa dyūtajitāṃ kṛṣṇāṃ prāhasat puruṣādhamaḥc tasyādya sūtaputrasya bhūmiḥ pibati śoṇitama śete sau śaradīrṇāṅgaḥ śatrus te kurupuṃgavac taṃ paśya puruṣavyāghra vibhinnaṃ bahudhā śaraiḥd hatāmitrām imām urvīm anuśādhi mahābhujad yatto bhūtvā sahāsmābhir bhuṅkṣva bhogāṃś ca puṣkalānd saṃjaya uvācad iti śrutvā vacas tasya keśavasya mahātmanaḥa yudhiṣṭhiras tu dāśārhaṃ prahṛṣṭaḥ pratyapūjayatc diṣṭyā diṣṭyeti rājendra prītyā cedam uvāca haa naitac citraṃ mahābāho tvayi devakinandanac tvayā sārathinā pārtho yat kuryād adya pauruṣamd na tac citraṃ mahābāho yuṣmad bāhuprasādajama pragṛhya ca kuruśreṣṭhaḥ sāṅgadaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ bhujamc uvāca dharmabhṛt pārtha ubhau tau keśavārjunaua naranārāyaṇau devau kathitau nāradena hac dharmasaṃsthāpane yuktau purāṇau puruṣottamaua asakṛc cāpi medhāvī kṛṣṇadvaipāyano mamac kathām etāṃ mahābāho divyām akathayat prabhuḥa tava kṛṣṇa prabhāveṇa gāṇḍīvena dhanaṃjayaḥc jayaty abhimukhāñ śatrūn na cāsīd vimukhaḥ kva cita jayaś caiva dhruvo smākaṃ na tv asmākaṃ parājayaḥc yadā tvaṃ yudhi pārthasya sārathyam upajagmivānd bhīṣmo droṇaś ca karṇaś ca mahātmā gautamaḥ kṛpaḥd anye ca bahavaḥ śūrā ye ca teṣāṃ padānugāḥd tvadbuddhyā nihate karṇe hatā govinda sarvathāa evam uktvā mahārāja taṃ rathaṃ hemabhūṣitamc dantavarṇair hayair yuktaṃ kālavālair mahārathaḥa āsthāya puruṣavyāghraḥ svabalenābhisaṃvṛtaḥc kṛṣṇārjunābhyāṃ vīrābhyām anumanya tataḥ priyama āgato bahuvṛttāntaṃ draṣṭum āyodhanaṃ tadāc ābhāṣamāṇas tau vīrāv ubhau mādhavaphalgunaua sa dadarśa raṇe karṇaṃ śayānaṃ puruṣarṣabhamb yathā kadambakusumaṃ kesaraiḥ sarvato vṛtamb citaṃ śaraśataiḥ karṇaṃ dharmarājo dadarśa hab gandhatailāvasiktābhiḥ kāñcanībhiḥ sahasraśaḥb dīpikābhiḥ kṛtoddyotaṃ paśyate vai vṛṣaṃ tadāb saṃchinnabhinnakavacaṃ bāṇaiś ca vidalīkṛtamc gāṇḍīvamuktair viśikhaiḥ sarvataḥ śakalīkṛtama saputraṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā karṇaṃ rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥb saṃjātapratyayo tīva vīkṣya caivaṃ punaḥ punaḥc praśaśaṃsa naravyāghrāv ubhau mādhavapāṇḍavaua adya rājāsmi govinda pṛthivyāṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ sahac tvayā nāthena vīreṇa viduṣā paripālitaḥa hataṃ dṛṣṭvā naravyāghraṃ rādheyam abhimāninamc nirāśo dya durātmāsau dhārtarāṣṭro bhaviṣyatie jīvitāc cāpi rājyāc ca hate karṇe mahārathea tvatprasādād vayaṃ caiva kṛtārthāḥ puruṣarṣabhac tvaṃ ca gāṇḍīvadhanvā ca vijayī yadunandanae diṣṭyā jayasi govinda diṣṭyā karṇo nipātitaḥf trayodaśa samāstīrṇā jāgareṇa suduḥkhitāḥf svapsyāmo dya sukhaṃ rātrau tvatprasādān mahābhujaa evaṃ sa bahuśo hṛṣṭaḥ praśaśaṃsa janārdanamc arjunaṃ cāpi rājendra dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥd saṃjaya uvācad dṛṣṭvā ca karṇaṃ nihataṃ saputraṃ pārthasāyakaiḥd punar jātam ivātmānaṃ mene kurukulodvahaḥd sametya ca mahārāja kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiramd praśaśaṃsus tataḥ sarve rājāno bhūritejasaḥa tato bhīmaprabhṛtibhiḥ sarvaiś ca bhrātṛbhir vṛtamc vardhayanti sma rājānaṃ harṣayuktā mahārathāḥa nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca pāṇḍavaś ca vṛkodaraḥc sātyakiś ca mahārāja vṛṣṇīnāṃ pravaro rathaḥa dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca pāṇḍupāñcālasṛñjayāḥc pūjayanti sma kaunteyaṃ nihate sūtanandanea te vardhayitvā nṛpatiṃ pāṇḍuputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiramc jitakāśino labdhalakṣā yuddhaśauṇḍāḥ prahāriṇaḥa stuvantaḥ stavayuktābhir vāgbhiḥ kṛṣṇau paraṃtapauc jagmuḥ svaśibirāyaiva mudā yuktā mahārathāḥa evam eṣa kṣayo vṛttaḥ sumahāṃl lomaharṣaṇaḥc tava durmantrite rājann atītaṃ kiṃ nu śocasi vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca evam etan mahac cāsīd yuddhaṃ paramadāruṇama śrutvā tad apriyaṃ rājan dhṛtarāṣṭro mahīpatiḥc papāta bhūmau niśceṣṭaḥ kauravyaḥ paramārtivāne tathā satyavratā devī gāndhārī dharmadarśinīf śuśoca bahulālāpaiḥ karṇasya nidhanaṃ yudhia taṃ pratyagṛhṇād viduro nṛpatiṃ saṃjayas tathāc paryāśvāsayataś caivaṃ tāv ubhāv eva bhūmipama tathaivotthāpayām āsur gāndhārīṃ rājayoṣitaḥb sa daivaṃ paramaṃ matvā bhavitavyaṃ ca pārthivaḥb parāṃ pīḍāṃ samāśritya naṣṭacitto mahātapāḥb cintāśokaparītātmā na jajñe mohapīḍitaḥc tābhyām āśvāsito rājā tūṣṇīm āsīd vicetanaḥd idaṃ mahāyuddhamakhaṃ mahātmanord dhanaṃjayasyādhiratheś ca yaḥ paṭhetd sa samyag iṣṭasya makhasya yat phalaṃd tad āpnuyāt saṃśravaṇāc ca bhāratad makho hi viṣṇur bhagavān sanātanod vahanti taṃ cāgnyanilendubhānavaḥd ato nasūyuḥ śṛṇute paṭhec ca yaḥd sa sarvalokāṃś ca jayet sukhī bhavetd sarvatīrtheṣu yat puṇyaṃ sarvadāneṣu yat phalamd tat phalaṃ labhate martyaḥ karṇākhyānaṃ śṛṇoti hid hiraṇyavastradhānyāni gāṃ savatsām upānahaud tena brahmā ca viṣṇuś ca rudrāś ca vasavas tathād pūjitā munayaḥ sarve pitaraś ca tathāśvinaud yaḥ śṛṇoti sadā bhaktyā karṇākhyānam anuttamamd dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ caturvidhaphalaṃ labhetd tāṃ sarvadā bhaktim upāgatā narāḥd paṭhanti puṇyāṃ varasaṃhitām imāmd dhanena dhānyena yaśasā ca mānuṣād nandanti te nātra vicāraṇāstid ato nasūyuḥ śṛṇuyāt sadā tu vaid naraḥ sa sarvāṇi sukhāni cāpnuyātd viṣṇuḥ svayaṃbhūr bhagavān bhavaś cad tuṣyanti ye yasya narottamasyad vedāvāptir brāhmaṇasyeha dṛṣṭād raṇe balaṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ jayo yudhid dhanajyeṣṭhāś cāpi bhavanti vaiśyāḥd śūdrārogyaṃ prāpnuvantīha sarved tathaiva viṣṇur bhagavān sanātanaḥd sa cātra devaḥ parikīrtyate yataḥd tataḥ sa kāmāṃl labhate sukhī narod mahāmunes tasya vaco rcitaṃ yathād kapilānāṃ savatsānāṃ varṣam ekaṃ nirantaramd yo dadyāt sukṛtaṃ tad dhi śravaṇāt karṇaparvaṇaḥd cintayanto vadhaṃ ghoraṃ sūtaputrasya saṃyuged arjunasya jayaṃ yuddhe cintayānāḥ punaḥ punaḥd pāṇḍavānāṃ maheṣvāsā nyaviśanta paraṃtapāḥd prahṛṣṭamanasaḥ sarve jitvā śatrūn mahārathānd tato yudhiṣṭhiraṃ tatra niviṣṭaṃ vai mudānvitamd sametya sarve pañcālā vardhayanto yathāvidhid arjunas tu rathāt tūrṇam avaruhya mahāyaśāḥd dharmarājasya caraṇau pīḍayām āsa hṛṣṭavatd tam utthāpya mahārāja dharmaputraḥ pratāpavānd sasvaje bharataśreṣṭham upajighrann upaspṛśand nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca pāṇḍavaś ca vṛkodaraḥd abhivādya mahārājam asvajanta sma phalgunamd dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca pāṇḍavānāṃ ca ye rathāḥd vardhayante sma rājānaṃ nihate sūtanandaned tataḥ kṛṣṇo mahārāja sātyakiś cāpi sātvataḥd avardhayetāṃ rājānaṃ nihate sūtanandaned vāsudevaś ca kaunteyaṃ praṇayād idam abravītd adya rājan hatāḥ sarve dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ sarājakāḥd hate vaikartane karṇe rathānāṃ pravare rathed yadi lokās trayaḥ sarve yodhayeyuḥ savāsavāḥd tathāpi durjayaḥ sūtas tava kopāt tu sūditaḥd evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca dharmarājo janārdanamd tava prasādād govinda hataḥ karṇo mahāyaśāḥd pāṇḍavāś ca jayaṃ prāptā nāśitāś cāpi śatravaḥd tvaṃ hi śakto bhayāt trātuṃ yasya kasya cid āhaved tvam asya jagato goptā pāṇḍavānāṃ ca sarvadād tvāṃ samāsādya śakro pi modate divi nityaśaḥd tvaṃ pātā pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ yathaiva jagatas tathād anāścaryo jayas teṣāṃ bhaktir yeṣāṃ tvayi prabhod tvayā nāthena govinda nāthavanto vayaṃ yudhid yathendreṇa purā devās tvayā cāpi janārdanad svapsyāmy adya sukhaṃ kṛṣṇa nidrāṃ lapsye vasan kṣapāmd vigataṃ hi bhayaṃ me dya tvatprasādān na saṃśayaḥd evam uktas tu pārthena keśavaḥ prāha pāṇḍavamd nimittamātraṃ tu vayaṃ tava hy asmin mudāgamed yasya te bhrātaraḥ śūrā bhīmasenādayo nṛpad saṃbandhinaś cendravīryāḥ pārṣatapramukhās tathād arhate ca bhavān vaktuṃ priyaṃ nityaṃ hi maddhitamd priyo hi me tvam etena vacanena narottamad ity ukto dharmarājas tu svarathaṃ hemabhūṣitamd dantavarṇair hayair yuktaṃ kālavālair mahīpatiḥd āsthāya puruṣavyāghraḥ svabalenābhisaṃvṛtaḥd prayayau bahuvṛttāntaṃ draṣṭum āyodhanaṃ pratid saṃbhāṣamāṇau tau vīrāv ubhau pāṇḍavamādhavaud sa dadarśa raṇe karṇaṃ śayānaṃ puruṣarṣabhad gāṇḍīvamuktair viśikhaiḥ sarvataḥ sunipīḍitamd saputraṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā karṇaṃ rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥd praśaśaṃsa naravyāghrāv ubhau pāṇḍavamādhavaud adya rājāsmi sarvasyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ madhusūdanad diṣṭyā jayasi govinda diṣṭyā śatrur nipātitaḥd evaṃ subahuśo rājan praśaśaṃsa janārdanamd arjunaṃ ca kuruśreṣṭho dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥd dṛṣṭvā ca nihataṃ karṇaṃ saputraṃ pārthasāyakaiḥd punar jātam ivātmānaṃ mene kurukulodvahaḥd sametya ca kuruśreṣṭhaṃ kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiramd vardhayanti sma rājānaṃ harṣayuktā mahārathāḥd saṃjaya uvācad evam eṣa kṣayo vṛttaḥ sumahān romaharṣaṇaḥd tava durmantrite rājan diṣṭyā tvam anuśocasid vaiśaṃpāyana uvācad śrutvaitad vipriyaṃ rājā dhṛtarāṣṭro mahīpatiḥd papāta bhūmau niśceṣṭaḥ kauravyaḥ paramāsanātd tathā satyavratā devī gāndhārī divyadarśinīd tatas tūrṇaṃ tu viduras taṃ nṛpaṃ saṃjayas tathād paryāśvāsayatāṃ caitāv ubhāv eva tu bhūmipamd tathaivāśvāsayām āsa gāndhārī rājasattamamd sa daivaṃ paramaṃ mene bhavitavyaṃ ca tat tathād tābhyām āśvāsito rājā tūṣṇīm āste viśāṃ pated evam ākhyāya rājñe ca saṃjayo rājasattamad jagāma śibiraṃ bhūyo hate karṇe mahātmanid sa dṛṣṭvā nihataṃ śalyaṃ rājānaṃ ca suyodhanamd yodhāṃś ca subahūn rājan sainikāṃś ca sahasraśaḥd tathaiva pāṇḍavīṃ senāṃ nihatāṃ prekṣya saṃjayaḥd sauptike drauṇinā rājan hatavājinaradvipānd sa hi dṛṣṭvā hatān sarvān samantād yudhi saṃjayaḥd prayāto hastinapuraṃ śokārto bhayavihvalaḥd hateṣu punar eteṣu prabhūtagajavājiṣud yodhaiś caiva mahārāja nānādeśasamudbhavaiḥd kurukṣetraṃ tu tat sarvaṃ śūnyam āsīj jagatpated nihataiḥ pāṇḍaveyaiś ca dhārtarāṣṭraiś ca saṃyuged yathāviṣayajaṃ vṛttaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya saṃjayaḥd nyavedayata tat sarvaṃ yathāvṛttaṃ yathāvidhid śaśaṃsur nihitaṃ karṇaṃ phalgunena mahātmanād yayatus tatra tau tūrṇaṃ yatrāsīd vīrasaṃkṣayaḥd pradīpahastāḥ śataśaḥ samantāt pratyayur narāḥd punaś ca śibiraṃ prāpto bhrātṛbhir bharatarṣabhaḥd yat kṛtvā tu ca kartavyaṃ sukhāsīnaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
